HBṬ_0.0.1–0.2.4	śrīmat arcaṭa viracitāḥ hetu binduṭīkā namaḥ sarvajñāya jina namaskāreṇa maṅgalam yaḥ san jāta mahā kṛpaḥ vyasaninam trātum samagram janam puṇya jñāna mayam pracitya vipulam hetum vidhūta śramaḥ kṛtsna jñeya visarppi nirmalatara prajñā udaya adrim śritaḥ loke hārddatama upahaḥ jina ravirmūrdhnā namasyāmi tam varam hidhārma kīrtteṣu carviteṣu api carvaṇam niṣpīḍitā api mṛdvīkā mādhuryam hi jahāti kim  nyāya mārgga tulā ārūḍham jagat ekatra yat matiḥ jayet tasya kva gambhīrāḥ giraḥ aham jaḍa dhīḥ kva ca  tathā api manda matayaḥ santi mattaḥ api kecana yān uddiśya mayā api eṣa hetu binduḥ vibhajyate 
HBṬ_0.3.1–0.3.5	 parokṣe ti ādinā prakaraṇa ārambhe prayojanam āha tat ca śrotṛ jana pravṛtti artham iti kecid tat uktam sarvasya eva hiśāstrasya karmaṇaḥ vā api kasyacid yāvat prayojanaṃna uktaṃtāvat tat kena gṛhyatām iti tat ayuktam yatas asya prakaraṇasya idam prayojanam iti pradarśane prayojana viśeṣam prati upāyatām prakaraṇasya niścitya anupāye pravṛtti asambhavāt prekṣāvatām tad arthitayā prakaraṇa śravaṇa ādau pravṛttiḥ syāt iti tad abhidhānasya arthavat tā varṇyate na ca etat yuktam yatas prekṣāvatām pravṛttiḥ prayojana arthinām tad upāye tad bhāva niścayāt yathā kṛṣīvala ādīnām sasya ādi upāye bīja ādāva abīja ādi vivekenā avadhṛta bīja ādi bhāvānām anyathā hi aniścita upāyānām upeya arthanām pravṛttau prekṣāvat tā eva hīyeta upeye tu bhāvini pramāṇa vyāpāra asambhavāt aniścaye api vivecita upāyāḥ pratibandha vaikalyayoḥ asambhave yogyam etat vivakṣitam kāryam niṣpādayitum iti saṃbhāvanayā pravṛttau prekṣā vat tātaḥ na hīyeran 
HBṬ_0.3.6	 niścayaḥ ca pramāṇāt eva na ca prayojana vākyasya prāmāṇyam asti śabdānām bahis arthe pratibandha abhāvāt vivakṣāyām tasya prāmāṇye api yathāvastu pravṛtti niyama abhāvāt na tatas prakaraṇasya prayojana viśeṣam prati upāya tā niścayaḥ samasti na hi ye yathā yam artham vivakṣanti te tathā eva tam anutiṣṭhanti visaṃvādana abhi prāyāṇām anyathā abhidhāyānyathā pravṛtti darśanāt loke sarva tra anāśvāsāt 
HBṬ_0.3.7–0.3.8	 prayojana viśeṣa upanyāsāt prakaraṇasya tad upāya tā viṣayaḥ saṃśayaḥ janyate tatas tad bhāva nirdhāraṇāya kṛṣīvala ādeḥ iva bījāt avadhṛtaye pravṛttiḥ yuktā iti ced na prayojana viśeṣa upāya tā saṃśayasya tad abhidhānāt prāk api bhāvāt tad sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāve tasya nyāya prāpta tvāt anumāna ādi vyutpatti arthānām ca prakaraṇānām darśanāt kim asya anumāna vyutpādanam prayojanam anyat vā na vā kiñcid api iti evam rūpaḥ ca saṃśayaḥ prāk pravarttamānaḥ kena nivāryeta api ca kim idam niṣprayojanam uta prayojana vat asmat abhimatena vā prayojanena tadvat iti jijñāsoḥ pravṛtti sambhave vyarthaḥ eva prayojana vākya upanyāsaḥ tasmāt yat prayojana rahitam vākyam tad arthaḥ vā na tat prekṣāvatā aarabhyate kartum pratipādayitum vā tat yathā daśa dāḍima ādi vākyam kāka danta parīkṣā ca niṣprayojanam ca idam prakaraṇam tad arthaḥ vā iti vyāpaka anupalabdhyā pratyavatiṣṭhamānasya tad asiddha tā udbhāvanā artham ādau prayojana vākya upanyāsaḥ 
HBṬ_0.4.1	 tatra tad vyutpādana artham iti vākyena svayam asya prakaraṇasya prayojanam āha yathāsvam abhidheya pratītiḥ hi vākyasya prayojanam tat ca iha asti padānām avāntara vākyānām ca paraspara saṃsargāt samāsa artha pratīteḥ tathā hi anumānam atra prakaraṇe vyutpādyate iti tat abhidheyam tasya eva tad śabdena sambandhāt yadi api parokṣa artha pratipattau guṇībhūtam anumānam tathā api vaktuḥ abhiprāya anuvidhāyitayā śabda vṛtteḥ tad śabdena parāmṛśyate anyathā pradhāna saṃsparśa upi katham syāt  śabdānām svabhāvataḥ sambhandhā yogāt pakṣa dharmaḥ ityādinā ca anumānasya eva vyutpādanāt tasya vyutpattiḥ aviparīta svarūpa pratītiḥ asya prakaraṇasya prayojanam tasmādhya tvāt atas eva ca anumāna vyutpatti viṣayam prakaraṇa vyāpāram darṣayitum ṇicā nirdiśati tad vyutpādana artham iti tatas ca prakaraṇa prayojanayoḥ sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ 
HBṬ_0.4.2–0.4.3^1	 api uktaḥ bhavati yadi api śabda vṛttena anumāna vyutpatti viṣayasya prakaraṇa vyāpārasya prādhānyam tathā api vastu vṛttena vyutpatteḥ eva pradhāna tā tasyāḥ tad sādhya tvāt itarasya ca tad upāya tvena apradhāna tvāt tasmāt anumāna vyutpattiḥ eva prayojana tayā pratīyate na prakaraṇa vyāpāraḥ iti parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ anumāna āśraya tvāt iti anena tu prakaraṇa arthasya anumāna lakṣaṇasya prayojanam āha na hi vākyasya sva artha pratīti lakṣaṇam phalam asti iti etau atā eva prekṣāvān pravarttate api tu tad abhidheya arthasya puruṣa artha upayogi tve sati 
HBṬ_0.4.2–0.4.3^2	 tat ca iha asti yatas parokṣa arthasya yā pratipattiḥ niścayaḥ tasyāḥ anumānam trirūpa liṅgam kāraṇe kārya upacārāt ananya upāya sādhya tām darśayitum para mata nirāsa artham āśrayaḥ kāraṇam anumānam āśrayaḥ yasya iti sāmānyena vigṛhya tadanu ca kasya anumāna āśraya tvāt iti viśeṣa apekṣāyām yadi api parokṣa artha pratipatti śabda sambhandhe strī tvam gamyate tathā api tat pada saṃskāra velāyām buddhi asaṃnihita tvāt bahis aṅgam iti na strī pratyaya nimittam yathābhūtam iyam brāhmaṇī āvapanam iyam uṣṭrikā iti 
HBṬ_0.5.1–0.5.2	 anena ca sarvā parokṣa artha pratipattiḥ pramāṇa bhūtāḥ anyasmāt tat pratipatti ayogāt trirūpa liṅga āśrayā eva iti uktam bhavati anumāna āśraya tvāt eva iti avadhāraṇāt tatas ca śabda ādīnām sati prāmāṇye anumāna tā anyathā teṣām api vyutpādyatā prasaṅgaḥ nimittasya samāna tvāt tathā hi sarvā parokṣa artha pratipattiḥ pramāṇa bhūtāḥ na svatantrā bhavati tasyāḥ sva artha pratibandha abhāvena niyamena tad saṃvāda ayogāt avisaṃvāda lakṣaṇa tvāt ca pramāṇasya anyatas api asambaddhāt yadi syāt sarvatas sarva pratipatti prasaṅgāt dharmya sambandhe api sarvatra pratītim janayet pratyāsatti vipra karṣa abhāvāt evambhūtaḥ ca trirūpa liṅgam eva arthaḥ bhavati iti sarvā parokṣa artha pratipattiḥ trirūpa liṅga ja tvena anumānāt na bhidyate iti eṣa ca arthaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ kasya  parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ iti prakṛtena saṃbandhāt darśitaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ eva tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ eva ca parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ hetuḥ iti avadhāraṇāt 
HBṬ_0.6.1–0.6.4^1	 artha grahaṇam tu parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ iti anumānasya api sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam prāmāṇyam darśayitum artha kriyā samarthaḥ hi arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam ca evam ātmakam atas eva vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvāt pramāṇa vyavasthāyāḥ iti vakṣyati anyathā anumānāt tatra pravṛttiḥ na syāt artha kriyā arthinaḥ sāmānyasya avastu tve api jñāna mātra lakṣaṇa tvāt tad artha kriyāyāḥ tasyāḥ ca tad utpādya tvena siddha tvāt na hi jātiḥ dāha pāka ādau upayujyate sva lakṣaṇasya eva tatra upayogāt tad sambandhāt tatra pravṛttiḥ iti ced na nityasya anupakāraka tvena kenacid sambhandha abhāvāt sati api ca sambandhe katham anya pratipattau anyatra pravṛttiḥ atiprasaṅgāt samavāyasya sūkṣma tvena anavasita vivekasya avasāyāt bhrāntyā tatra pravṛttiḥ iti ced evam tarhi bhrānti mātram eva astu kim antar gaḍunā sāmānyena 
HBṬ_0.6.1–0.6.4^2–1.1	 nirbbīja bhrānti ayogāt iti ced tāḥ eva vyaktayaḥ tad eka kārya kāriṇyaḥ bhrānteḥ bījam varṇa ākṛti samāna ākāram hi sāmānya jñānam na ca sāmānyam tad rūpam tat katham tat bhrānteḥ bbījam sādṛśya nibandhanā hi bhrāntiḥ iṣyate paraiḥ vyaktyaḥ eva ca asamāna jātīya vyāvṛttāḥ sāmānya ākāra jñāna svarūpāḥ tatas tāḥ eva bhrānti bījam atad rūpa vyāvṛtteḥ tāsu bhāvāt vastu bhūtasya tu sāmānyasya sambhandhā saṃbhavena tāsu bhāva ayogāt ca yaiḥ tu vyakti ātmakam eva sāmānyam kalpitam taiḥ sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam anumānasya prāmāṇyam abhyupagatam eva bhavati sva lakṣaṇa ātmakam tu sāmānyam katham anumāne pratibhāsate vaiśeṣika darśana upagama prasaṅgāt 
HBṬ_1.1.1	 hi kathitam tatra kārya svabhāvayoḥ vidhi sādhana tvāt na pratiṣedhe sādhye vyāpāraḥ anupalabdhitaḥ api na hetu antara abhāva niścayaḥ yatas sā caturddhā avasthitā svabhāva kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhayaḥ viruddha viddhiḥ ca iti tulya yogya tārūpasya eka jñāna saṃsargiṇaḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ anya upalabdhi rūpāḥ abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ iṣyate na ca hetu antaram atyanta abhāva tayā upagatam anukrānta rūpam yadi hi syāt deśa ādi niṣedhaḥ eva asya syāt na atyanta abhāvaḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhī tu siddhe kārya kāraṇa vyāpya vyāpaka bhāve bhavataḥ na ca hetu antare atyantā sattayā aṅgīkṛte prakāraḥ ayam sambhavati tat katham te tad abhāvam gamayiṣyataḥ virodhaḥ api avikala kāraṇasya bhavataḥ anya bhāve abhāvāt avagamyate iti viruddha upalabdhiḥ api asambhavinī sambhave vā kāraṇa anupalabdhi ādīnām katham atyanta niṣedhaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha hetvābhāsāḥ tatas aparaḥ iti tatas 
HBṬ_1.1.2–1.1.3^1	 trividdhāt dhetoḥ apare anye hetvābhāsāḥ yatas tatas tridhā eva saḥ iti evam manyate iha yat yatra niyamyate tad viparyayeṇa tad vipakṣasya vyāptau sa niyamaḥ siddhyati yathā yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva iti sattvasya kṣaṇikeṣu niyamaḥ ucyamānaḥ sattva viparyayeṇa asattvena kṣaṇika vipakṣasya akṣaṇikasya vyāptau siddhyati evam iha api tri tve hetuḥ niyamyamānaḥ hetu viparyayeṇa hetvābhāsa tvena tri saṃkhyā bāhyasya arthasya vyāptau tri sāṃkhyāyām eva niyataḥ bhavati tatas trividha hetu vyatiriktānām arthānām hetvābhāsa tām darśayati tena svabhāva viruddha upalabdhyā kārya svabhāva anupalambha vyatiriktānām arthānām hetu tva abhāva niścayaḥ iti hetu tad ābhāsayoḥ ca paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā eva virodhaḥ hetu lakṣaṇa pratīti kāle eva pratipannaḥ tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānāt eva tad viparītasya anyatayā tad ābhāsatā pratīteḥ parasparam itaretara rūpa abhāva niścayāt 
HBṬ_1.1.3^2	 tatra trividha hetu vyatirikteṣu artheṣu hetvābhāsa tvam upalabhyamānam sva viruddham hetu tvam nirākaroti te ca hetu traya bāhyāḥ arthāḥ na atyanta asattayā upagatā na api hetu tvam teṣu niṣidhyamānam kevalam vyāmohāt hetu tvam anyatra prasiddham eva tatrā aaropitam āśaṅkitam vā tad viruddha upalambhāt apasāryate tat kim ucyate atyanta asaṃbhavinaḥ kathaṃvirodhaḥ iti na ca saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ eva virodhaḥ yena tat nyāyaḥ sarvatra upavarṇyeta na api yat yatra pratiṣidhyate tasya tatra eva virodhaḥ pratipattavyaḥ yena katham asataḥ kenacid virodha gatiḥ iti codyeta na hi na atra śīta sparśaḥ agneḥ iti sādhya dharmiṇī eva śīta sparśasya agninā virodhaḥ api tu sarvatra yathā tu asya anyatra pratīta virodhasya agninā sādhya dharmiṇi niṣedhaḥ 
HBṬ_1.1.4	 tathā hetvābhāsa tva upalambhāt hetu traya bāhyeṣu artheṣu hetu tva nirāsaḥ atyanta asataḥ api ca lākṣaṇikaḥ virodhaḥ pratīyate yathā kṣaṇika tvena akṣaṇika tvasya tasya vastuni kvacid api asambhavāt bhāvena vā yadvat abhāvasya sarva śakti viraha lakṣaṇasya iti alam durmati vispanditeṣu ati ādareṇa iti sthitam etat tri tve hetu tvam niyamyamānam tad viparyayasyā api ca vyāptau satyām tatra niyatam bhavati iti abhiprāyavatā viparyaya vyāptim pradarśayitum idam uktam hetvābhāsāḥ tatas aparaḥ iti 
HBṬ_1.2.1	 tatra etat syāt kṣaṇika vipakṣasya sattva viparyayeṇa vyāptiḥ bādhaka pramāṇa vaśāt avasitāḥ iha tu tri saṅkhyā bāhyānām arthānām hetvābhāsa tvena vyāptiḥ katareṇa pramāṇena avasitā iti atra āha avinā abhauva niyamāt iti trividha hetu vyatirikte liṅga tayā upagate śaṅkhyamāne vā vastuni pakṣa dharma tā sadbhāve api avinā abhāva abhāvāt iti arthaḥ tathā ca vakṣyati na sa trividhāt dhetoḥ anyatra asti iti atra eva niyataḥ ucyate iti avinā abhāva vaikalyam ca hetvābhāsa tvena asiddha viruddha anaikāntika sāmānya dharmeṇa vyāptam prameya tva ādau niścitam iti hetvābhāsa tve sādhye avinā abhāva vaikalyam svabhāva hetuḥ 
HBṬ_1.2.2–1.2.7	 avīna abhāva vaikalyam ca trividha hetu vyatirikta tvāt eva tad anyeṣām vyāpaka anupalabdhitaḥ siddham tathā hi tādātmya tad utpattibhyām avinā abhāvaḥ vyāptaḥ tayoḥ tatra avaśyam bhāvāt tasya ca tayoḥ eva bhāvāt atad svabhāvasya ātad utpatteḥ ca tad anāyatta tayā tad avyabhicāra niyama abhāvāt tat uktam kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinābhāva niyamaḥ adarśanāt na darśanāt avaśyam bhāva niyamaḥ kaḥ parasya anyathā paraiḥ artha antara nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga vat iti 
HBṬ_1.2.8^1	 rūpa ādinā api hi rasa ādeḥ avinā abhāvaḥ na svatas kintu sva kāraṇa avyabhicāra dvārakaḥ iti tad kāraṇa utpattiḥ eva avinābhāva nibandhanam anyathā tad anāyat tasya tad prakāraṇān āyattasya vā tena avinābhāva kalpanāyām sarvasya sarva arthaiḥ avinābhāvaḥ syāt aviśeṣāt eka artha samavāya nimittaḥ rūpa rasa ādeḥ avinā abhāvaḥ iti ced nanu samavāyaḥ api ādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām upavarṇyate sa ca ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ tad ātmānupakāre ati prasaṅgataḥ na sidhyati iti eka sāmagrī adhīnatā eva eka artha samavāyaḥ avaseyaḥ anyaḥ vā vastu bhūtaḥ saṃbandhaḥ asambhavī tathā asambandha parīkṣāyāṃvistarataḥ śāstra kṛta apratipāditam eva iti tatas eva avadhāryam 
HBṬ_1.2.8^2	 nanu asati api janya janaka bhāve tādātmye vā tena eva avinābhāvaḥ na anyena iti atra vastu svabhāvaiḥ eva uttaram vācyam ye evam bhavanti na asmābhiḥ kevalam vayam draṣṭāraḥ iti ced ākasmikaḥ tarhi sa vastūnām svabhāvaḥ iti na kasyacid na syāt na hi ahetoḥ ddeśa kāla dravya niyamaḥ yuktaḥ tat dhi kiñcid kvacid upanīyeta na vā yasya yatra kiñcid āyattam anāyattam vā anyathā viśeṣa abhāva ādiṣṭa deśa kāla dravya vat anya deśa ādi bhāvaḥ kena vāryeta viśeṣa abhāvāt tatas yadi ena avinābhūtam dṛśyate tasya tena avyabhicāra kāraṇam tattva cintakaiḥ abhidhānīyam na tu pāda prasārikā avalambanīyāḥ tat ca avyabhicāra kāraṇam yathā uktāt anyat na yujyate iti tad vikalā na hetu lakṣaṇa bhājaḥ iti tathā ca āha 
HBṬ_1.2.9–1.2.16	 saṃyogi ādiṣu yeṣu asti pratībandhaḥ na tādṛśaḥ na te hetavaḥ iti uktam vyabhicārasya saṃbhavāt iti atra prayogaḥ yasya yena saha tādātmya tad utpattī na staḥ na sa tad avinā bhāvī tathā prameya tva ādiḥ anitya tva ādinā na staḥ ca kenacid tādātmya tad utpattī svabhāva kārya vyatirekiṇām arthānām iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ tu svabhāva hetau antar bhāvitā iti tasyāḥ tādātmya lakṣaṇaḥ eva pratibandhaḥ vyāpaka kāraṇa anupalabdhī tu tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa pratibandha vaśāt eva vyāpya kāryoḥ nivṛttim sādhyataḥ tat uktam tasmāt tanmātra saṃbaddhaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvam eva vā nivartayet kāraṇaṃvā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ iti tat evam hetu lakṣaṇam saṃkhyā niyamaḥ tad upadarśakam ca pramāṇam atra śloke nirdiṣṭam iti 
HBṬ_1.3.1	 athavā tridhā eva saḥ iti sa pakṣa dharmaḥ tri prakāraḥ eva svabhāva kārya anupalambha ākhyaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ na anyaḥ sa tri prakāraḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ eva iti sambhandhaḥ kim kāraṇam  avinā abhau= a niyamāt avinā abhāvasya vyāpteḥ trividhaḥ eva pakṣa dharme niyamāt trividhasya ca pakṣa dharmasya avinābhāva niyamāt tena ca svabhāva kārya anupalambha ātmaka trividha pakṣa dharma vyatiriktā na tad aṃśena vyāptāḥ iti trividhaḥ ca kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi rūpaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ eva iti na tasya ahetu tvam iti uktam bhavati tatas trividha hetu bāhyeṣu avinā abhāva abhāvāt dhetu vyavahāram kurvantaḥ trividhe ca hetau avinā abhau= asya avaśyam bhāva abhāvāt ahetu tvam ācakṣāṇā nirastā bhavati 
HBṬ_1.4.1	 tatra etat syāt hetvābhāsānām api lakṣaṇam abhidhānīyam tatra śiṣyāṇām hetu vyavahāra nivṛttayaḥ iti āha hetvābhāsāḥ tatas aparaḥ iti tatas pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ iti hetu lakṣaṇāt apare anye tad lakṣaṇa vikalāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ gamyante eva iti na tad lakṣaṇam ucyate tathā hi pakṣa dharmaḥ iti ukte yatra pakṣa dharma tā na asti na sa hetuḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ iti vacane yatra tad aṃśa vyāpti virahaḥ viparyaya vyāpteḥ vyāpakasya vā tatra avaśyam bhāva abhāvāt te hetu rūpa vikala tayā hetvābhāsāḥ asiddha viruddha anaikāntikāḥ gamyante eva tathā hi yat lakṣaṇaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ śiṣyasya vyutpāditaḥ tad lakṣaṇa virahite na tad vyavahāram svayam eva pravartayiṣyati atadrūpa parihārena eva tad rūpa pratipattoḥ iti na tatra yatnaḥ phalavān bhavati yat tu anyatra hetvābhāsa vyutpādanam tat manda buddhīn adhikṛtya idam tu prakaraṇam vipula matīn uddiśya praṇītam saṃkṣepataḥ 
HBṬ_1.4.2	 iti vacanāt te eva hi saṃkṣepa uktam yathāvat avagantum kṣamāḥ na manda matayaḥ teṣām vistara abhidhānam antareṇa yathāvat artha pratipatteḥ abhāvāt atas eva artha ākṣipta upanyāsa pūrvakam eva hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇam tatra upavarṇitam iti tat atra vyākhyāne hetu lakṣaṇam hetu sāmkhyā niyamaḥ tasya ca trividhasya hetu tva avadhāraṇam tad ubhaya kāraṇam śliṣṭa nirdeśāt hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇa anabhidhāna kāraṇam ca iti ṣaṣ arthāḥ śloke atra nirdiṣṭāḥ iti 
HBṬ_1.4.3	 kiñcid idam api sādhu dṛśyate tridhā eva kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi bheda bhinnaḥ sa hetuḥ tathā tridhā eva pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatireka rūpa bhedāt tri prakāraḥ eva trirūpaḥ eva tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanena anvaya vyatirekayoḥ abhidhānāt na ābādhita viṣaya tva ādi rūpa antara yogī api sa hetuḥ kutas yatas hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare tatas trividhāt sa vabhāva ādeḥ pakṣa dharma ādi rūpa traya yoginaḥ vai apare anye saṃyogi ādayaḥ abādhita viṣaya tva ādi vyatirikta rūpavantaḥ vā kasmāt  avinā abhā= asya atra eva trividhaḥ eva trirūpaḥ eva ca hetau niyamāt anyatra svabhāva ādi vyatirikte rūpa antara sambhavini vā avinā abhāva abhāvāt iti arthaḥ na hi svabhāva ādi vyatirikte pratibandha nibandhanasyāḥ avinā bhāvasya saṃbhavaḥ tadvati vā rūpa antarasya tathā ca sati eva avinā abhāve rūpa antarasya na sambhavaḥ tathā ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ ityādinā vakṣyati 
HBṬ_1.5.1–1.5.3	 pakṣa dharmaḥ iti atra hetu lakṣaṇe api kriyamāṇe yadi samudāyaḥ pakṣaḥ gṛhyate yaḥ anumāna viṣayaḥ tadā sarvaḥ hetuḥ asiddhaḥ siddhau vā anumāna vaiyarthyam iti āha pakṣaḥ dharmī iti katham punar samudāya vacanaḥ pakṣa śabdaḥ dharmi mātre vartate iti ced avayave samudāya upacārāt pakṣa ākhyasya hi samudāyasya dvau avayavau dharmī dharmaḥ ca tat atra dharmi mātre samudāya upacārāt pakṣa śabdaḥ vartate tat eka deśa tvam ca samudāya upacāra nimittam iti na sādhya dharmiṇaḥ anyatra tad prasaṅgaḥ tat uktam samudāyasya sādhya tvāt dharma mātre ca dharmiṇi amukhye api eka deśa tvāt sādhya tvam upacaryate iti 
HBṬ_1.6.1–1.6.4	 tat etat ācāryīyaṃvyākhyānam īśvarasenena ākṣiptam parihartum pūrva pakṣayan āha prayojana iti ādinā na rtte prayojana ādiṣṭam mukhya śabda artha laṅghanam iti asati prayojane na upacāraḥ yuktaḥ tatas dharmi dharmaḥ iti eva astu iti paraḥ na prayojana abhāvaḥ kutas sarvaḥ ca asau vivāda āśrayaḥ anyaḥ dharmī yaḥ tasya pratiṣedhaḥ arthaḥ prayojanam yasya upacārasya tad bhāva ḥ tasmāt sarva dharmi dharma pratiṣedha artha tvāt upacārasya iti prayojana abhāvāt iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ kaḥ evam sati guṇaḥ iti ced āha evaṃhi upacāre sati cākṣuṣa tva ādi ādi grahaṇāt kākasya kārṣṇyāt ityādi vyadhikaraṇa asiddham parihṛtam hetu tvena nirastam bhavati dharmi dharmaḥ iti tu sāmānyena abhidhānāt teṣām api hetu tā syāt iti 
HBṬ_1.6.5^1	 asati upacāre dharmi grahaṇāt api etat sidhyati tatas anarthakaḥ eva upacāraḥ iti āha paraḥ dharma vacanena api na kevalam dharmi vacanena dharmya āśraya siddhau dharmiṇaḥ āśrayaṇam āśrayaḥ parigrahaḥ tasya siddhiḥ tasyām satyām kim punar ddharmasya dharmyākṣepa nimittam iti ced para āśraya tvāt dharmi paratantra tvāt dharmasya avaśyam asau dharmiṇam ākṣipati tatas dharmi vacanam atiricyamānam viśiṣṭam sādhya dharmiṇam eva pratipādayati na dharmi mātram 
HBṬ_1.6.5^2	 syāt matam dharmi grahaṇāt viśiṣṭaḥ atra dharmī kaścid abhipretaḥ iti gamyate sa tu sādhya dharmī iti kutas iti āha pratyāsatteḥ nyāyāt pratyāsattiḥ ca atra dharmi vacana sāmarthyāt abhipretā iti gamyate vyāptau tu nyāye dharma vacanena api dharmi mātra ākṣepāt dharmi grahaṇa vaiyarthyam pratyāsanna tā ca sādhya dharmiṇaḥ eva tatra prathamam hetu upadarśanāt na pratyāsatteḥ sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ kutas  dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇaḥ api na kevalam sādhya dharmiṇaḥ pratyāsatteḥ kadācid vyāpti darśana pūrvake prayoge dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇī api prathamam hetu sadbhāva upadarśanāt 
HBṬ_1.6.6	 yadi na pratyāsatteḥ sādhya dharmi siddhiḥ pāriśeṣyāt tarhi bhaviṣyati yatas tad aṃśa vyāptyā hetu bhūtayā dṛṣṭānta dharmini dharmasya sattva siddheḥ na hi dṛṣṭāntam antareṇa hetoḥ sādhyena vyāptiḥ pradarśayitum śakyate iti manyate tatas dharmi grahaṇāt vyatiricyamānāt sādhya dharmiṇaḥ eva parigrahaḥ tad aṃśena iti ca tad śabdena dharma vacana ākṣiptaḥ dharmī sambhantsyate iti tad sambhandhana artham api dharmi grahaṇam na aśaṅkanīyam yatra prayojana antaram na sambhavati sa pāriśeṣya viṣayaḥ dharmi vacanasya tu anyat api prayojanam sambhāvyate tat kutas pāriśeṣyāt dharmi vacanāt sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ iti manyamānaḥ siddhāntavādi āha siddhe tad aṃśa vyāptyā dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattve punar ddharmiṇaḥ vacanaṃdṛṣṭānta dharmiṇaḥ eva yaḥ dharmaḥsa hetuḥ iti niyama artham āśaṅkyeta tatas ca cākṣuṣa tva ādayaḥ eva hetavaḥsyuḥ 
HBṬ_1.6.7–1.6.9^1	 na kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ iti aniṣṭam eva syāt tasmāt upacāraḥ kartavyaḥ iti kim punar tarkkaśāstre dṛṣṭam kvacid niyama artha vacanam iti atas āha dṛṣṭam sajātīyaḥ eva ityādi tatra yaḥ san sajātīye iti atrā aacāryīye hetu lakṣaṇe sajātīyaḥ eva sattvam iti avadhāraṇena siddhe api hetoḥ vyatireke kutra  sādhya abhāve yat etat asan= tad atyaye iti asattva vacanam tat niyama artham ācāryeṇa vyākhyātam asatī eva na astitāḥ yathā syāt na anyatra na viruddhaḥ iti tathā iha api dharmi vacanam tatra eva bhāva niyama artham āśaṅkyeta kadā siddhe api dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattve kutas tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanāt kva bhāva niyama artham tatra eva dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sati ca āśaṅkā sambhave kutas  pāriśeṣyāt sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ nanu apakṣa dharmasya ahetutvāt na niyama artha āśaṅkā 
HBṬ_1.6.9^2	 tathā hi sādhya dharmeṇa vyāptaḥ api dharmaḥ yadi kvacid dharmiṇī upalabhyeta tadā tatra eva sva vyāpaka pratītim janayet na anyatra pratyāsatti viprakarṣābhyām yathākramam anupalabdhaḥ tu kvacid dharmiṇi katham gamakaḥ  tathā abhāve vā sarvatra sva vyāpakam gamayet pratyāsatti vipra karṣa abhāvāt eva iti atas āha tasmāt sāmarthyāt ityādi yat idam anantaram sāmarthyam samupavarṇitam asmāt sāmarthyāt arthasya sādhya dharmi parigraha lakṣaṇasya bhavati pratītiḥ paṭudhiyām śrotṝṇām kintu aśabdakam artham svayam anusaratām pratipatti gauravam syāt tad upacāra mātrāt svayam aśabdaka artha abhyūha rahitāt dharmi dharmaḥ iti anena pakṣa dharmaḥ iti samā nirddeśāt 
HBṬ_1.6.10–1.6.11	 pratipatti gauravaṃca parihṛtaṃbhavati pratipatti gauravaṃca iti caśabdena etat āha ye para upadeśam ākāṅkṣanti taiḥ ayam arthaḥ lakṣaṇa vacanāt boddhavyaḥ iti yathālakṣaṇam pratīteḥ apakṣa dharmaḥ na hetuḥ iti kutas iyam āśaṅkā tatas teṣām lakṣaṇa anusāriṇām niyama āśaṅkā parihāra artham ca upacāra karaṇam iti 
HBṬ_1.7.1–1.7.2	 iha vyavaccheda phala tvāt śabda prayogasya avaśyam eva avadhārayitavyam ṣaṣṭhī samāsāt ca pakṣa dharmaḥ iti atra na anyaḥ samāsaḥ sambhavati tathā ca pakṣasya eva dharmaḥ iti evam avadhāraṇāt tad aṃśa vyāptiḥ virudhyate iti viruddha lakṣaṇa tām udbhāvayan āha pakṣasya dharma tve tam pakṣaṃviśeṣaṇam anyatas vyavacchedakam apekṣate iti tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya dharmasya anyatra pakṣīkṛtāt anyasmin sa pakṣe ananuvṛttiḥ tathā hi yaḥ pakṣeṇa viśeṣyate sa pakṣasya eva bhavati na anyasya yathā yaḥ devadattasya putraḥ sa tasya eva putraḥ na yajñadattasya api tatas anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā sādhāraṇa tā na syāt tad aṃśa vyāpti virodhaḥ iti yāvat sādhāraṇa tāyāḥ ca tad aṃśa vyāptyā pratipādanāt tatas yadi pakṣa dharmaḥ na tad aṃśena vyāptiḥ atha tad aṃśa vyāptiḥ na pakṣa dharmaḥ iti vyāhatam lakṣaṇam iti 
HBṬ_1.7.3	 nanu ca tat aṃśavyāptiḥ nāma sādhya dharmasya vyāpakasya tatra hetau sati tad ādhāra dharmiṇi bhāvaḥ eva vyāpyasya vā hetoḥ tatra eva vyāpake sādhya dharme sati eva bhāvaḥ iti sva sādhya avinābhāva lakṣaṇā vakṣyate na ca anayā avaśyam pakṣīkṛtāt anyatra vṛttiḥ ākṣipyate yatas lakṣaṇa vyāghātaḥ āśaṅkyeta tathā hi tatra eva pakṣīkṛte sati eva sādhya dharme hetuḥ varttamānaḥ tad aṃśa vyāptim pratipadyate eva yā eva ca asya sādhya dharmiṇi svasādhya avinā bhāvitā sā eva gamaka tve nibandhanam na anya dharmiṇi sa ca svasādhya avinābhāvaḥ pratibandha sādhaka pramāṇa nibandhanaḥ na sa pakṣe kvacid bahulam vā saha bhāva mātra darśana nibandhanaḥ na hi loha lekhyam vajram pārthiva tvāt kāṣṭha ādi vat iti tat anyatra pārthiva tvasya loha lekhya tā avinā abhāvaḥ api tathā abhāvaḥ bhavati yadi ca pakṣīkṛtāt anyatra eva vyāptiḥ ādarśayitavyā iti niyamaḥ tadā sattvam katham kṣaṇikatām 
HBṬ_1.7.4	 bhāveṣu pratipādayet  yaḥ hi sakala padārtha vyāpinīm kṣaṇika tām icchati tam prati kasyacid sa pakṣasya eva abhāvāt yat api kaiścid jvālā ādeḥ kṣaṇika tvam abhyupagamyate tat api na pratyakṣatas kṣaṇa vivekasya ati sūkṣma tayā anupalakṣaṇāt anyatra eva ca vyāptiḥ ādarśanīyāḥ na sādhya dharmiṇī api iti kaḥ ayam nyāyaḥ  evam hi kālpanika tvam hetu lakṣaṇasya pratipannam syāt na vastu bala pravṛtta tvam tasmāt sva sādhya pratibandhāt hetuḥ tena vyāptaḥ sidhyati sa ca viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā sādhya dharmiṇī api sidhyati iti na kiñcid anyatra anuvṛtti apekṣyāḥ atas eva anyatra uktam yat kvacid dṛṣṭam tasya yatra pratibandhaḥ tadvidhaḥ tasya tat gama kaṃtatrā iti vastu gatiḥ iti 
HBṬ_1.7.5	 yat api anumeye atha tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ iti ādi lakṣaṇam tatra api sādhya dharmavān eva sapakṣaḥ ucyate tatas sati eva sādhya dharme vā asti iti evam param etat tatas ca tad dharmaṇaḥ sādhya dharmiṇaḥ api vāstavam sa pakṣa tvam na vyāvarttate sādhya tvena iṣṭayet chāvi avasthita lakṣaṇena pakṣa tvena tasya nirākarttum aśakya tvāt tasmāt tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanena svasādhya avinābhāvi tvasya pratibandha nibandhanasya anyathā tad ayogāt abhidhānān na avaśyam anyatra vṛttiḥ ākṣiptā iti katham idam āśaṅkitam  satyam na eva idam āśaṅkanīyam yadi sarvasya hetoḥ pakṣīkṛte eva dharmiṇi sva sādhya pratibandhaḥ pramāṇataḥ niścetum śakyeta yathā sattva lakṣaṇasya svabhāva hetoḥ kṣaṇikatāyām sādhyāyām tādātmyam viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā kārya hetoḥ tu pakṣīkṛta dharmiṇā kasyacid svabhāva hetoḥ pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanaḥ pratibandhaḥ 
HBṬ_1.7.6^1	 katham parokṣe sādhya dharme gṛhyeta  tasmāt tasya anyatra eva prasiddhiḥ iti tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya tatra apekṣaṇāt anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā sambhava mātreṇa āśaṅkitāḥ tadā hi anytra āvartamānaḥ sādhya viparīta vyatireka tad ubhaya bahis bhāva ayogāt tad dharmiṇaḥ sādhya vṛtti vyavacchedābhyām sarva saṃgrahāt tatra saṃśaya hetuḥ bhavati syāt matam kvacid āśraye sattāyāḥ prāc pravṛtta pūrva gṛhīta vismṛta pratibandha sādhaka pramāṇa smṛtaye anyatra vṛttiḥ apekṣaṇīyāḥ etat pariharati na ityādi na anyatra ananuvṛttiḥ kutas ayogaḥ asambandhaḥ tad vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt pakṣasya na hi anya yoga vyavacchedena eva viśeṣaṇam bhavati kintu ayoga vyavacchedena api 
HBṬ_1.7.6^2	 yatra dharmiṇi dharmasya sadbhāvaḥ saṃdihyate tatrā ayoga vyavacchedasya nyāya prāpta tvāt atra ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā caitraḥ dhanurdharaḥ iti caitre hi dhanurdhara tvam saṃdihyate kim asti na asti iti tatas caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti tad sadbhāva pratipādikā śrutiḥ pakṣa antaram adhanurdhara tvam śrotuḥ āśaṅka upasthāpitam nirākaroti iti ayoga vyavacchedaḥ atra nyāya prāptaḥ para abhimata vyavaccheda nirācikīrṣayā aaha na anya yoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā iti sambandhaḥ atra api dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathāpārthaḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti sāmānya śabdaḥ api ayam dhanurdhara śabdaḥ sāmarthya ādinā prakṛṣṭa guṇa vṛttiḥ iha pārthe hi dhanurddhara tvam siddham eva iti na ayoga āśaṅkā tādṛśam tu sa atiśayam kim anyatra asti 
HBṬ_1.7.7–1.7.8	 na asti iti anya yoga śaṅkāyām śrotuḥ yadā pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ iti ucyate tadā anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ nyāya prāptaḥ pratipādya āśaṅkā upasthāpitayoḥ eva pakṣayoḥ parasparam virodhāt eka nirdeśena anya yoga vyavacchedasya nyāya bala āyāta tvāt tat iha pakṣe asti ayam dharmaḥ na vā iti saṃśītau pakṣa dharmaḥ iti ukte pakṣasya dharmaḥ eva na adharmaḥ dharmaḥ ca āśrita tvāt viśeṣaṇam tena ayogaḥ vyavacchidyate na anya yoga s tad aṃśa vyāptyā tasya pratipādita tvena dṛṣṭānte saṃdeha abhāvāt tad aṃśaḥ tad dharmaḥ iti tad śabdena pakṣaḥ parāmṛśyate na dharmaḥ dharmasya dharma asambhavāt aṃśaḥ ca dharmaḥ na eka deśaḥ pakṣa śabdena dharmi mātra vacanāt na tad aṃśaḥ tasya ca eka deśa abhāvāt iti 
HBṬ_1.8.1–1.8.2^1	 tasya pakṣa dharmasya sataḥ vyāptiḥ yaḥ vyāpnoti yaḥ ca vyāpyate tad ubhaya dharma tayā pratīteḥ yadā vyāpaka dharma tayā vivakṣyate tadā vyāpakasya gamyasya tatra iti sat saptamī artha pradhānam etat na ādhāra pradhānam dharmāṇām dharma ādhāratvā saṃbhavāt tena ayam arthaḥ yatra dharmiṇi vyāpyam asti tatra sarvu atra bhāvaḥ eva vyāpakasya svagataḥ dharmaḥ vyāptiḥ tatas ca vyāpaka bhāva apekṣayā vyāpyasya eva vyāpta tā pratītiḥ na tu evam avadhāryate vyāpakasya eva tatra bhāvaḥ iti hetu abhāva prasaṅgāt avyāpakasya api mūrtta tva ādeḥ tatra bhāvāt 
HBṬ_1.8.1–1.8.2^2	 na api tatra eve ti prayatna ānantarīyaka tva ādeḥ ahetu tā āpatteḥ sādhāraṇaḥ ca hetuḥ syāt nitya tvasya prameyeṣu eva bhāvāt yadā tu vyāpya dharma tayā vivakṣā vyāpteḥ tadā vyāpyasya vā gamakasya tatra eva vyāpake gamye sati yatra dharmiṇi vyāpakaḥ asti tatra eva bhāvaḥ na tad abhāve api vyāptiḥ iti atra api vyāpyasya eva tatra bhāvaḥ iti avadhāraṇam hetu abhāva prasakteḥ eva na āśritam avyāpyasya api tatra bhāvāt na api vyāpyasya tatra bhāvaḥ eva iti sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ hetu tva prāpteḥ sādhāraṇasya ca hetu tvam syāt prameya tvasya nityeṣu avaśyam bhāvāt iti vyāpya vyāpaka dharmatā saṃvarṇanam 
HBṬ_1.8.3–1.8.5	 tu vyāpteḥ ubhayatra tulya dharma tayā eka ākārā pratītiḥ saṃyogi vat mā bhūt iti pradarśana artham tathā hi pūrvatra ayoga vyavacchedena avadhāraṇam uttaratra anya yoga vyavacchedena iti kutas ubhayatra eka ākāra tā vyāpteḥ  tat uktam liṅge liṅgībhavati eva liṅginī eva itarat punar niyamasya viparyāse asambandhaḥ liṅga liṅginaḥ iti 
HBṬ_1.8.6–1.8.9	 etena ācāryeṇa saṃyoga balāt gamaka tve yaḥ doṣaḥ uktaḥ na ca kenacid aṃśena na saṃyogīhutāśanaḥ dhūmaḥ vāsarvathā tena prāptaṃdhūmāt prakāśanam iti saḥ iha na avatarati iti ākhyātam bhavati tathā hi saṃyogasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt eṣa prasaṅgaḥ na tu vyāpteḥ na hi yādṛśī vyāpaka dharme vyāptiḥ tādṛśī eva vyāpya dharmaḥ iti tathā ca āha 
HBṬ_1.8.10–1.8.12	 sambandhaḥ yadi api dvi ṣṭhaḥ sahabhāvyaṅga liṅginoḥ ādhāra ādheya vat vṛttiḥ tasya saṃyogi vat na tu iti tena vyāpakaḥ vyāpyaḥ na bhavati vyāpyaḥ ca na vyāpakaḥ iti tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ iti vacanāt na saṃyogi pakṣa uktaḥ doṣaḥ nā api ubhayoḥ ggamya gamaka tā prasaṅgaḥ yathā uktāt hetu lakṣaṇāt vyāpakasya eva gamya tva pratīteḥ vyāpyasya eva gamakatā sampratyaya ādi iti 
HBṬ_1.9.1	 yadi tarhi pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ iti etat dhetu lakṣaṇam tatas pakṣa dharma tvam tad aṃśa vyāptiḥ ca iti dvi rūpaḥ hetuḥ syāt anyatra ca tri rūpaḥ uktaḥ tat katham na vyāghātaḥ iti āha etena tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanena anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vāuktaḥ veditavyaḥ iti sambandhaḥ anvaya vyatireka rūpa tvāt vyāpteḥ iti bhāvaḥ tathā hi yaḥ eva yena anvitaḥ yat nivṛttau ca nivṛttate saḥ eva tena vyāptaḥ ucyata iti tad ātmaka tvāt vyāpteḥ vyāpti vacanena anvaya vyatireka abhidhānam tatas vyāpti vacanena rūpa dvaya abhidhānāt na vyāghātaḥ iti 
HBṬ_1.10.1–1.10.2	 tau ca jñāpaka hetu adhikārāt niścitau niścayaḥ ca tayoḥ na ekena eva pramāṇena api tu yathāsvam yasya yat ātmīyam pramāṇam niścāyakam tena yasya ca yat niścāyakam pramāṇam tat uttaratra vakṣyati anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā iti tulya ka kṣatā sūcanā arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ tena sādharmya vaidharmyavatoḥ prayogayoḥ ekena eva dvitīya gateḥ vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tayā vyāvṛtti bhede api paramārthataḥ tādātmyāt na ubhaya upadarśanam iti sūcitam bhavati vyatirekaḥ hi sādhya nivṛttau liṅgasya nivṛtti dharmaka tvam svabhāva bhūtaḥ dharmaḥ iti anvaya rūpa tā vastutas asya na virudhyate pakṣa dharmaḥ ca kim  yathā svaṃpramāṇena niścitaḥ uktaḥ iti sambandhaḥ niścaya prasaṅgena saḥ api atra pratipādyate niścitasya gamaka tvam ākhyātum 
HBṬ_1.10.3	 iti pradarśana arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ pratyakṣeṇa ca svayaṃsu alakṣaṇa ākāra tve api anantara sāmānya vikalpa jananāt prasiddhiḥ upacārataḥ niścayaḥ ucyate pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya anadhigata artha adhigantṛ tva abhāvam darśayitum tena yadi api sāmānya rūpam liṅgam avasthāpyate tathā api sva lakṣaṇa pratītiḥ eva tad vyavasthā nibandhanam iti pratyakṣatas pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmiṇi prasiddhiḥ ucyate etat ca anantaram eva vyaktīkariṣyate anumānataḥ vā asādhya dharmini pakṣa dharmasya prasiddhiḥ niścayaḥ pramāṇa phala bhedāt ca anumānataḥ anumānena niścayaḥ iti āha atra udāharaṇe yathākramam yathāpradeśe dhūmasya dhūma sāmānyasya pratyakṣataḥ niścayaḥ iti 
HBṬ_1.11.1–1.11.3	 yaḥ tu manyate yaḥ pradeśaḥ agni sambandhī saḥ apratyakṣaḥ yaḥ tu pratyakṣaḥ nabhaḥ bhaga rūpaḥ āloka ādi ātmā dhūma vat tayā dṛśyamānaḥ na saḥ agnimān atas katham pradeśe dhūmasya pratyakṣatas prasiddhiḥ tasmāt dhūmaḥ eva dharmī yuktaḥ sa agniḥ ayam dhūmaḥ dhūma tvāt iti evam sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ iti tasya api sa agneḥ dhūma avayavasyāḥ apratyakṣa tvāt paridṛśyamānasya ca ūrddhva bhāga vartinaḥ agninā saha āvṛtteḥ katham dhūma sāmānyasya sādhya dharmiṇi pratyakṣatas prasiddhiḥ  dhūma avayavī pratyakṣaḥ iti ced na avayava vyatirekeṇa tasya abhāvāt loka adhyavasāyataḥ tasya ekatve vā pradeśasya api tāvataḥ kalpitam eka tvam na nivāryate pradeśe eva ca lokaḥ agnim pratipadyate na dhūme deśa kāla ādi apekṣayā eva ca kārya hetuḥ ggamakaḥ yat āha iṣṭam viruddha kārye api deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇam śabde vākṛtaka tvasya pratyaya bheda bhedi tva ādinā anumānena iti 
HBṬ_1.12.1	 atra yathā upavarṇitam pratyakṣataḥ pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmiṇi prasiddhau abhiprāyam apratipadyamānaḥ kumārilaḥ katham pratyakṣeṇa avikalpena sāmānya ātmanaḥ liṅgasya dhūma ādeḥ svrūpa grahaṇam api tāvat yujyate dharmiṇaḥ vā kutas eva tad sambandha grahaṇam iti pratyavatasthe tena hi pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt ca anumāna ādeḥ ddharmaṃpratyanimitta tvam iti etat bhāṣyam 
HBṬ_1.12.2–1.12.12	 katham pratyakṣa pūrva tvam anumāna ādinaḥ bhavet  yadā smṛtya samartha tvāt nirvikalpa indriyasya dhīḥ na ca avikalpya liṅgasya dharmi sambandhayoḥ tathā gṛhītiḥ iti ākṣipya pratyakṣa agrahaṇam yat tu liṅga ādeḥ avikalpanāt tat na iṣṭa tvāt vikalpasya api artha rūpa upakāriṇaḥ asti hi ālocana ājñānaṃprathamaṃnirvikalpakam bāla mūka ādi vijñāna sadṛśaṃśuddha vastu jam tatas paraṃpunarvastu dharmaiḥ jāti ādibhiḥ yayaḥ buddhyā avasīyate sā api pratyakṣa tvena sammatāḥ 
HBṬ_1.12.13	 iti bruvatā saugatānām eva ayam liṅga dharmitad sambandha agrāhaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ doṣaḥ yeṣām avikalpakam eva pratyakṣam na asmākam sa vikalpam api pratyakṣam icchatām iti uktam bhavati tatas tad upavarṇita doṣa pratividhānāyāḥ aaha sa dhūmaṃhi ityādi ayam atra samudāya arthaḥ pratyakṣam hi purovasthitam auttara adharyeṇa dhūma pradeśa ādikam vidhi rūpeṇa dhūma ādi sva lakṣaṇam sakala sajātīya vijātīya vyāvṛttam ca sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ sarvāsām artha mātrāṇām parasparam asaṃkīrṇa rūpa tvāt tad sāmarthya bhāvi yathāsthānam anukurvat pāśca attya vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpa dvayam janayati yena dhūma pradeṣa ākhyau dharma dharmiṇau tayoḥ ca auttara adharyam evam etat na anyathā iti vikalpayati yathā anubhavam abhyāsa pāṭava ādi pratyaya antara sahakāriṇām vikalpānām udayāt tatas dharma dharmiṇoḥ svarūpa niścayaḥ sambandha niścayaḥ ca pratyakṣa nibandhanaḥ 
HBṬ_1.12.14	 sampadyate tathā hi ayam eva dhūma pradeśayoḥ sambandhasya niścayaḥ yaḥ ātrāyam iti adhyavasāyaḥ sa ca avikalpena api pratyakṣeṇa yathā uktena prakāreṇa sampāditaḥ eva na ca auttara adharya avasthitāt vastu dvayāt anyaḥ eva kaścid ādhāra ādheya bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ yatas tasya pratyakṣeṇa ananubhūta tvāt paścāt vikalpanam syāt vastu bhūtasya tasya anyatra niṣedhāt tasmāt ayam tat eva tathā avasthitam artha dvayam āśritya kalpanā samāropitaḥ eva tena sambandhaḥ sambandhi iti bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepābhyām dharma dharmi tayā vyavahāraḥ loke na tu pāramārthikaḥ sāmānya vyavahāraḥ api vijātīya vyāvṛttān eva bhāvān āśritya kalpanā samāropitaḥ eva pratanyate teṣām eva bhinnānām api anubhava dvāreṇa vijātīya vyāvṛtta tayā prakṛtyā eva eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya hetu tvāt tathā ca āha 
HBṬ_1.12.15–1.12.17	 eka pratyavamarśa artha jñāna ādi eka artha sādhane bhede api niyatāḥ kecid svabhāvena indriya ādi vat iti tatas sāmānya vikalpa janana dvārā tad pratibhāsinaḥ dhūma ākārasya vijātīya vyāvṛtta rūpasya sāmānya rūpa tayā pratyakṣeṇa eva gṛhīta tvāt na hi vijātīya vyāvṛttiḥ vyāvṛttāt anyā eva kācid yasyāḥ pratyakṣeṇa agrahaṇam syāt tasmāt yathā paridṛṣṭam dhūma ādi sva lakṣaṇam eva anyatas vyāvṛtta ātmanā vikalpyate iti pratipad tradhyavasāya vaśāt smṛtiḥ eva dvividhaḥ vikalpaḥ pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvī vastutas punar nirviṣayaḥ eva tatas yat āha sāmānyasya ananubhūta tathā 
HBṬ_1.12.18–1.12.24	 smārttam etat abhedena vijñānam iti yaḥ vadet anumāna grāhyam eva tatra ca anavasthā liṅga grāhiṇaḥ api anumānasya tad anya liṅga balena utpatteḥ tasya ca sāmānya rūpa tayā tad anya anumāna māna viṣaya tvāt tathā tad anyasya api iti kasyacid ekasya api liṅginaḥ pratipattiḥ yuga sahasraiḥ api na sambhavati kim aṅga punar ekena puruṣa āyuṣkeṇa iti tathā ca āha sāmānyaṃna anumānena vināyasya pratīyate na ca liṅga vinirmuktam anumānaṃpravarttate asāmānyasya liṅga tvaṃ na ca kenacid iṣyate na ca anavagataṃliṅgaṃkiñcid asti prakāśakam tasya api ca anumānena syāt anyena gatiḥ punar 
HBṬ_1.12.25	 iti āśaṅkya āha sa dhūmaṃhi ityādi evam manyate yasya anumānam antareṇa sāmānyam na pratīyate bhavatu tasya ayam doṣaḥ asmākam tu pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinā api vikalpena prakṛti vibhramāt sāmānyam pratīyate liṅga vikalpasya ca sva lakṣaṇa darśana āśraya tvāt paramparayā vastu pratibandhāt avisaṃvādaka tvam maṇi prabhāyām iva maṇi bhrānteḥ kārya hetu tvam api vikalpa avabhāsinaḥ dhūma sāmānyasya liṅga tayā avasthāpyamānasya kārya darśana āśraya tayā tad adhyavasāyāt ca na hi dhūmasva lakṣaṇasya liṅgatā avasthāpayitum yuktāḥ tasya asādhāraṇasya sa pakṣe vṛtti abhāvāt tad aṃśa vyāpti ayogāt sādhya sādhana saṃkalpe vastu darśanā sambhavāt ca iti 
HBṬ_1.12.26	 yat tu uktam sāmānya lakṣaṇa viṣayam anumānam iti tatra na evam avadhāryate sāmānya lakṣaṇa viṣayam anumānam eva iti pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya api tad viṣaya tvāt tad anyasya ca vikalpasya kintu sāmānya lakṣaṇa viṣayam eva anumānam iti avadhāryate sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tva niṣedha artham iti tatra saha dhūmena vartate iti sa dhūmaḥ pakṣa dharma tā pratipādana artham evam uktam vidhi vikalpasya ca etat eva bījam tam sa dhūmaṃpradeśaṃdṛṣṭavataḥ pratyakṣeṇa iti sambhandhaḥ kīdṛśam artha antara vivikta rūpam artha antaraiḥ sajātīya vijātīyaiḥ viviktam asaṅkīrṇam rūpam asya iti vigrahaḥ sarva bhāvānām sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ svabhāva sāṅkarya abhāvāt anyathā sarvasya sarvatra upayogāt atiprasaṅgaḥ anena pratiṣedha vikalpasya nimittam ākhyātam sāmānya utprekṣāyāḥ ca bījam tat uktam 
HBṬ_1.12.27–1.12.31	 itaretara bhedaḥ asya bījaṃsaṃjñāyat arthakāḥ iti tathā hi artha antara vyāvṛttim paraspara vyāvṛttānām api samānām utpaśyataḥ bhinnam eṣām rūpam tirodhāyāḥ abhinnam svabhāvam āropayantī kalpanā utpadyate asādhāraṇa ātmanā iti artha antara vyāvṛttena svabhāvena na tu yathā kumārilaḥ manyate artha antara vivekaḥ abhāva pramāṇa grāhyaḥ na pratyakṣa avaseyaḥ iti na hi vastu bala bhāvinā pratyakṣeṇa anyathā darśana sambhavaḥ bhrānta tā prasaṅgāt tena ātmanā adṛṣṭavataḥ sataḥ puṃsaḥ anantaram smārttaṃliṅga jñānam utpadyate iti sambandhaḥ smṛtiḥ eva smārttam liṅga pratibhāsi jñānam liṅga jñānam anena pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvini vikalpe yat sāmānyam ābhāti tasya liṅga vyavasthām āha paramārthataḥ kim viṣayam yathā dṛṣṭa bheda parama artha viṣayam 
HBṬ_1.14.1–1.14.4	 darśana vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpānām pramāṇa apramāṇa cintām ārabhate tatra teṣu darśana vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpeṣu tat ādyam yat etat asti hi ālocana ajñānam prathamam iti ādau vikalpa pravṛtteḥ bhavam iti ādyam ākhyātam asādhāraṇa viṣayam sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam darśanam tat eva pramāṇam na vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpau api tasya eva pramāṇa lakṣaṇa yogāt itarayoḥ ca tad asambhavāt tathā hi anadhigata viṣaya tvam artha kriyā sādhana viṣaya tvam ca pramāṇa lakṣaṇam tat darśanasya eva asti tatra ādyam iti apūrva artha vijñāna tvam ākhyātam asādhāraṇa viṣayam iti artha kriyā sādhana viṣaya tvam sva lakṣaṇasya eva artha kriyā sādhana tvāt 
HBṬ_1.15.1^1	 tatra pratiṣedha vikalpasya tāvat pratyakṣa gṛhīta artha viṣaya tayā smṛti tvam pratipādayan āha tasmin asādhāraṇe tathābhūte artha antaraiḥ asaṅkīrṇa rūpe darśanena asaṅkīrṇa rūpa sāmarthya bhāvinā dṛṣṭe adhigate sati tathā hi vyatiriktam api bhāva aṃśāt abhāva aṃśam icchatā bhāva aṃśaḥ svabhāvena asaṅkīrṇa rūpaḥ kalpanīyaḥ anyathā saḥ eva abhāva aṃśaḥ na sidhyet na ca svabhāvena asaṅkīrṇa rūpa tāyām asatyām pṛthak bhūta abhāva aṃśa sadbhāve api sā yuktimatī sva hetu bala āyātasya saṅkīrṇa rūpasya akiñcitkara abhāva aṃśa sambhave api tyāga ayogāt 
HBṬ_1.15.1^2	 na ca tena eva tad vināśanam vināśa hetu ayogasya pratipādayiṣyamāṇa tvāt tena saṅkīrṇa rūpa vināśane ca varam sva hetoḥ eva svabhāvataḥ asaṅkīrṇa rūpāṇām udayaḥ astu kim parivrāj modaka nyāya upagamena tasmāt svabhāvataḥ eva bhāvānām para rūpa vikala tvam abhāva aṃśaḥ na anyaḥ sa ca tathābhūtaḥ darśanena gṛhītaḥ eva tasmin tathābhūte dṛṣṭe sa padārthaḥ yena vastunā asādhāraṇaḥ samāna svabhāvaḥ na bhavati tad rūpa vikala svabhāva tvāt tat asādhāraṇa tām tena tena ātad rūpeṇa asamāna svabhāva tām etat eva vyanakti tatas artha antarāt bhedam vailakṣaṇyam anya rūpam idam na bhavati iti abhilapantī abhimukhayantī 
HBṬ_1.15.2	 dṛṣṭa vailakṣaṇye pravartamāna tayā smṛtiḥ utpannā pratyakṣa balena yadi tu liṅga balena utpadyeta vyavaccheda viṣayā api smṛtiḥ na syāt iti bhāvaḥ kim viṣayāḥ atadavyāvṛtti viṣayā tad śabdena darśana viṣayasya vastunaḥ parāmarśaḥ kṛtaḥ na tat atat vijātīyam atasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ atad vyāvṛttiḥ sā viṣayaḥ yasyāḥ sā tathā yathādṛṣṭaḥ eva artha antarebhyaḥ bhedaḥ mayā api kalpyate iti pratipad tṛ adhyavasāyāt ca evam uktam paramārthataḥ nirviṣaya tvāt sā na pramāṇam na abhāva pramāṇa phalam iti arthaḥ na hi smṛti janaka tvena pramāṇa tā yuktāḥ kasmāt na pramāṇam  yathādṛṣṭasya ākāraḥ abhyāsa pāṭava ādi pratyāya antara sāpekṣaḥ viśeṣaḥ tasya grahaṇāt na hi dṛṣṭam iti eva vikalpena gṛhyate darśana aviśeṣāt sarva ākāreṣu vikalpa udaya prasaṅgāt api tu kaścid eva abhyāsa ādi pratyaya apekṣaḥ iti ākāra grahaṇena ācaṣṭe 
HBṬ_1.15.3	 bhavatu yathā dṛṣṭa ākāra grahaṇam pramāṇam tu kasmāt na bhavati iti parasya tad ukta pramāṇa lakṣaṇa viraham darśayan āha prāk ālocanā jñāna udaya kāle asādhāraṇam asaṅkīrṇa rūpam dṛṣṭvā asādhāranam artha antara rūpam na bhavati iti abhilapataḥ vikalpayataḥ pratiṣedha vikalpasya apūrva artha adhigama abhāvāt apūrva arthvijñāna tā virahāt apūrva artha vijñānam ca pramāṇam bhavatā ucyate iti bhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_1.16.1–1.16.3	 yadi uktena prakāreṇa pratiṣedha vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam vidhi vikalpaḥ tarhi pramāṇam bhaviṣyati na hi tasya apūrva artha vijñāna tva abhāvaḥ sambhavati tad pratibhāsinaḥ anugatasya sāmānya ākārasya asādhārana rūpau alambinā darśanena anadhigamāt tat kutas asya aprāmāṇyam tat uktam tatas paraṃpunar vastu ityādi tat etat kumārila vacanam āśaṅkya vidhi vikalpasya api prāmāṇyam apanudan āha artha kriyā sādhanasya sva lakṣaṇasya ālocanā jñānena darśanāt adṛṣṭasya punar tad sādhanasya artha kriyā sādhanasya svabhāvasya vikalpena apratipatteḥ vidhi vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam yadi api tena anadhigatam sāmānyam adhigamyate iti varṇyate tathā api tat artha kriyā sādhanam na bhavati iti tat adhigantā taimirika ādi jñāna prakhyaḥ vidhi vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam 
HBṬ_1.16.4–1.16.5	 tatas paraṃpunar vastu dharmaiḥ jāti ādibhiḥ yayā adhigame api keśa ādi jñānasya iva na prāmāṇyam atas eva artha kriyā sāmarthya virahiṇā sāmānyena indriyāṇām samprayoga abhāvāt pratyakṣatā api asambhavinī cakāreṇa smṛti tvāt ca iti pūrva ukta kāraṇa samucayaḥ smṛti tvam ca asya uttaratra pratipādayiṣyate anumāna vat iti vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā pratyakṣeṇa artha kriyā sādhane pradeśa ākhye dharmiṇi adhigate api anadhigatasya agneḥ artha kriyā sādhanasya āsāmāni a ākāreṇa parokṣasya sva lakṣaṇa ākāreṇa pratipattum aśakya tvāt pratipattiḥ na evam vidhi vikalpena sāmānya ākāreṇa anadhigatam artha kriyā sādhanam adhigamyate tasya ālocanā jñānena eva adhigamāt tasmin smṛtiḥ eva asau iti na pramāṇam iti 
HBṬ_1.17.1	 artha kriyā sādhana viṣayam eva pramāṇam na itarat iti kutas etat iti ced artha kriyā arthīhi puruṣaḥ yasmāt hita ahita prāpti parihāra arthī sarvaḥ na kākatālīya nyāyena kaścid eva pakṣāvān buddhi purva kārī pramāṇam apramāṇaṃvā pramānāt eva sarvadā pravarteya apramāṇāt mā kadācid vipralambha sambhavāt ubhayam anveṣate na vyasani tayā tatas ayam artha kriyā sādhana viṣayam eva pramāṇam bravīti tasya artha kriyā sādhane pravṛtti aṅga tvāt na itarat tad viparīta tvāt tathā hi pramāṇam avisaṃvādakam apratārakam ucyate loke api yat ca artha kriyā sādhanam anadhigacchat na tatra pravartayati kutas eva tat prāpayet tat katham avisaṃvādaka tayā prekṣā pūrva kārī pramāṇam ācakṣīta  
HBṬ_1.18.1^1	 yadi evam sāmānyam api artha kriyā sādhanam eva tatas tad viṣayaḥ vidhi vikalpaḥ pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti ced āha na ca na eva sāmānyaṃkāñcid tad sādhya tayā upagatām abhinna jñāna abhidhāna lakṣaṇām anyām vā vyakti sādhyām artha kriyām upakalpayati kīdṛśam  sva lakṣaṇa pratipatteḥ vyakti pratipatteḥ ālocanā jñāna saṃjñitāyāḥ ūrddhvam uttarakalām tad sāmarthya utpanna vikalpa vijñāna grāhyam iti tad śabdena sva lakṣaṇa pratipattiḥ sambadhyate tatas param punar vastu iti ādi paraiḥ abhidhānāt evam bravīti darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya pratyakṣa pramāṇa tām nirākartum 
HBṬ_1.18.1^2	 sarvam eva tu sāmānyam na kāñcid artha kriyām upakalpayati yat tu sāmānyam anumāna vikalpa grāhyam tat kāraṇa vyāpaka sambaddha liṅga niścaya dvāra āyātam sambaddha sambandhāt anadhigata artha kriyā sādhana viṣayām artha kriyām upakalpayati iti tad viṣayaḥ vikalpaḥ pramāṇam idam tu na evam adhigata tvāt artha kriyā sādhanasya ālocana ajñānena iti atra udāharaṇam yathā nīlaṃdṛṣṭvā ānīlam iti jñāne pratibhāsamānam iti śeṣaḥ na sāmānyam kāñcid artha kriyām upakalpayati iti prakṛtena sambandhaḥ 
HBṬ_1.18.2–1.18.3	 nanu ca liṅga vikalpa pratibhāsi sāmānyam prakṛtam tat kim anyat udāhriyate  sarvasya darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya para upagatām pratyakṣa pramāṇa tām tulya nyāyatayā nirākartum kām punar nīlam iti vikalpa jñāne darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvini pratibhāsamānam sāmānyam artha kriyām na upakalpayati  yadi vyakti sādhyām tadā anyaḥ api padārthaḥ anyadīyām artha kriyām na upakalpayati iti tasya api anartha kriyā sādhana tvāt avastu tva prasaṅgaḥ atha sva sādhyām tat asiddham abhinna jñāna abhidhāna lakṣaṇāyāḥ svasādhyāyāḥ karaṇāt iti āśaṅkya āha tat eva hi yat tad ālocana ajñānena upalabdham nīla sva lakṣaṇam nīla vyaktiḥ tathāvidha sādhya artha kriyā kāri tathāvidha śabdena sāmānyam atra abhipretam tādṛśa paryāya tvāt asya sādhāraṇa rūpasya ca tādṛśa tvāt tena tathāvidha sādhyām nīla sāmānya sādhyām abhinna jñāna abhidhāna lakṣaṇām artha kriyām kartum śīlam asya sva lakṣaṇasya iti tat tathā uktam 
HBṬ_1.18.4	 evam manyate yathā bhinnāḥ api vyaktyaḥ kayācid pratyāsattyā tad eka kārya pratiniyama lakṣaṇayā tat ekam abhinnam sāmānyam upakurvanti tad apara sāmānya yogam antareṇa api anyathā anavasthā prasaṅgāt tathā abhinna jñāna abhidhāna ātmikām api artha kriyām sādhayiṣyanti kim apramāṇakena pramāṇa bādhitena ca sāmānyena upagatena  tathā hi anumāna ādike jñāne yathāvidham asya aspaṣṭam rūpam pratibhāsate na tathāvidham vyaktiṣu dṛśyamānāḥ upalakṣayāmaḥ ekam eva hi vyakti darśana kāle spaṣṭam nīla ādi rūpam vibhāvayāmaḥ tat katham adṛṣṭa kalpa nayā aatmānam svayam eva vipralabhe mahi  vyakti rūpa saṃsargāt ayaḥ golaka vahni vat avibhāvanam iti ced na sarvatra bheda abheda vyavasthāyāḥ abhāva prasaṅgāt asya uttarasya anyatra api sulabha tvāt na ca sāmānyasya dve rūpe staḥ spaṣṭam aspaṣṭam ca yena ekena darśane pratibhāseta anyena anumāna ādi jñāne padārtha dvaya upagama prasaṅgāt pratibhāsa bhedasya eva sarvatra bhāva bheda vyavasthā nibandhana tvāt sāmānyasya apara sāmānya prasakteḥ niḥsāmānyasya ca asya upagamāt 
HBṬ_1.19.1–1.19.6	 etena etat api nirastam yat āha sarva vastuṣu buddhiḥ ca vyāvṛtti anugama ātmikā jāyate dvi ātmaka tvena vinā sā ca na yujyate na ca atra anyatarā bhrānti rūpa cāreṇa ca iṣyate dṛḍha tvāt sarvadā buddheḥ bhrāntiḥ tad bhrānti vādinām iti yatas yadi indriya buddhim abhipretya ucyate tadā asiddham aspaṣṭasya nīla ādi ākārasya spaṣṭa nīla ādi ābhāsāyām tatra anupalakṣaṇāt spaṣṭasya api ca dvitīyasya anuyāyinaḥ tad bhāve ca vyakti dvaya antarālam api āpnuvataḥ katham tad anugamaḥ  vyaktau ca upalabhyasya sataḥ tatra anupalakṣaṇam kutas  na hi tasya vyakta avyakta rūpa sambhavaḥ eka tvāt tathā ca āha 
HBṬ_1.19.7–1.19.9	 vyaktau ekatra sā vyaktā abhedāt sarvatragāḥ yadi jāti dṛśyeta sarvatra sā api na vyakti apekṣiṇī iti ekatra api ca vyaktau upalabhyamānāyām sakala trailokya vyāpi rūpam sakala sva āśraya vyāpi vā dṛśyeta  na hi ekasyāḥ kiñcid dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam vā nāma kṣaṇikatā ādi vat dṛṣṭāyām api ekatra eva āśraye darśana avasāyaḥ na sarvatra iti ced na vikalpena tad darśana abhyupagamāt na hi niścaya viṣayīkṛtam ca aniścitam ca iti yuktam tatas sarva gata rūpa darśane sarva arthānām darśana prasaṅgaḥ na hi tad darśane tad sahacāriṇaḥ upalabhyasya tad abhinna svabhāvasya ca anupalambhaḥ yuktaḥ tatas katham indriya buddheḥ dvi ātmaka tā  
HBṬ_1.19.10	 atha anumāna ādi buddhim tasyām api sva lakṣaṇa apratibhāsanāt kutas dvi ātmaka tvam  na hi na asu sāmānya grāhiṇīṣu spaṣṭaḥ vyakti ākāraḥ iva lakṣyamāṇaḥ sva lakṣaṇa pratibhāsaḥ tad bhāve api tāsām bhāvāt ākāra antareṇaḥ ca sva jñāne apratibhāsanāt aneka ākāra ayogāt ekasya atiprasaṅgāt ca tasmāt na iyam bhinna artha grāhiṇī abhinnā sāmānya buddhiḥ pratibhāti sva lakṣaṇa udbhāva satī kintu anādi vitatha vikalpa abhyāsa vāsanā janitā satī tathā avabhāsate dṛḍha tvam ca buddheḥ na avināśi tvam kṣaṇika tva abhyupagamāt kintu abādhyamāna tvam na ca asyāḥ tat sambhavati leśataḥ bādhakasya ukta tvāt vistarataḥ tusyāt vāda bhaṅgāt yathāvasaram iha eva tatra tatra vidhāsyamānāt bādhakam avadhāryam tasmāt yathā vyaktyaḥ sāmānya antaram antareṇa tat ekam upakurvanti tathā abhinna jñāna abhidhāne api pravartayiṣyanti iti tat eva nīla sva lakṣaṇam sāmānya sādhya tva upagata artha kriyā kāri 
HBṬ_1.20.1–1.20.6	 yaḥ tu sāmānyam na anyat iṣṭam ced tasya vṛtteḥ niyāmakam viśeṣāt anyat icchanti sāmānyam tena tat dhruvam tāḥ hi tena vinā utpannāḥ mithyā syuḥ viṣayāt ṛte na tu anyena vinā vṛttiḥ sāmānyasya iha duṣyati iti mithyātva prasaṅga doṣaḥ uktaḥ na asautatha āgata samayanayā avadāta buddhīn bādhate sāmānya buddhīnām bādhaka pratyaya nibandhanasya mithyātvasya upagata tvāt tathā hi 
HBṬ_1.20.7–1.20.14	 kasmāṭ sāsnādi matsu eva go tvam yasmāt tad ātmakam tādātmyam asya kasmāt ced svabhāvāt iti gamyatām iti vacanāt vyakti svabhāvam ca sāmānyam na ca asādhāraṇam vyakti udaya vināśayoḥ ca na udaya vyaya yogi iti ayuktam viruddha dharma adhyāsataḥ bheda prasaṅgāt iti āha ca tādātmyaṃced mataṃjāteḥ vyakti janmani ajāta tā nāśe anāśaḥ ca kena iṣṭaḥ tadvat cā ananvayaḥ na kim  vyakti janmani ajātā ced āgatān āśraya antarāt prāk āsīt na ca tad deśe sātayā saṅga tā katham  vyakti nāśe na ced naṣṭa āgata avyakti antaraṃna ca 
HBṬ_1.20.15	 tarhi adhigacchan vikalpaḥ pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti āha tat ca nīla sva lakṣaṇam tena ātmanā nīla sādhya artha kriyā kāriṇā svabhāvena dṛṣṭam eva ālocanā pratyayena tatas niṣpādita kriye karmaṇi aviśeṣa ādhāyi vikalpa jñānam katham pramāṇam syāt  atha matam sāmānyam eva tarhi adhigacchan nīla vikalpaḥ pramāṇam astu tat ca sāmānyam artha kriyā kāri yatas nīla sādhyam eva artha kriyām nīlena saha sambhūya kariṣyati vyakti svabhāvāni eva hi sāmanyāni iti āha na ca na eva tat sva lakṣaṇa grahaṇa uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ nīla vyakti darśana uttara kālam bhavana śīlasya liṅga grahaṇa uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ tu pūrva uktena prakāreṇa vyakti sādhya artha kriyā sāmānyasya kalpitasya vyavasthāpayitum śakyate iti bhāvaḥ nīla vikalpasya viṣayeṇa nīla sāmānyena nīla sādhya artha kriyā rañjana ādikā kriyate tasya vyakti svābhāvya ayoge sati kalpita rūpasya tad asambhavāt na ca nitya svabhāva tām ābibhrāṇena nīla vikalpasya viṣayeṇa nīla sādhyāḥ anyā vā artha kriyā kriyate krama yaugapadya virodhāt iti manyate 
HBṬ_1.22.1	 tat evam nīlam dṛṣṭvā nīlam iti jñāne pratibhāsamānam sāmānyam na kāñcid artha kriyām upakalpayati iti prasādhya anartha kriyā kāri viṣayasya api vikalpasya pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt ati vyāptiḥ iti tatra apūrva artha vijñānam iti pramāṇa laksaṇemī māṃsakaiḥ viśeṣaṇam upādeyam iti darśayan āha tasmāt yatas evam anartha kriyā sādhana viṣaya tayā darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya prāmāṇyam ayuktam tasmāt asmat abhimatam pramāṇam avisaṃvādi jñānam iti pramāṇa lakṣaṇam vyudasya anadhigata artha viṣayaṃpramāṇam tatra apūrva artha vijñānam pramāṇam iti api etasmin api āhopuruṣikayā anyasmin pramāṇa lakṣaṇe kriyamāṇe ati vyāpti parihārāya viśeṣaṇīyam viśeṣaṇam upādeyam katham viśeṣaṇīyam anadhigate sva lakṣaṇaḥ iti anena hi viśeṣaṇena anumāna vikalpasya ca prāmāṇyam sidhyati ālocanā jñāna pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ ca vikalpasya prāmāṇyam vyudasyate iti sarvam sustham 
HBṬ_1.22.2	 tat evam vidhi vikalpasya anartha kriyā sādhana viṣaya tayā anadhigata sāmānya adhigame api prāmāṇyam nirākṛtya ca śabda samuccitam smṛti tvam pratiṣedha vikalpena sādhāraṇam prāmāṇya kāraṇam darśayan āha adhigate tu sva lakṣaṇe ālocanā jñānena tad sāmarthya janmā sva lakṣaṇa adhigama bala bhāvī vikalpaḥ tad anukārī sākṣāt anutpatteḥ darśana saṃskāra āvedha vaśāt ca aspaṣṭa nīla sva lakṣaṇa ākāra anukārī dṛśya vikalpyayoḥ ca ekīkaraṇāt evam ucyate vastutas tu na kiñcid asau anukaroti sa smṛtiḥ eva kutas kāryataḥ tad viṣaya tvāt na paramārthataḥ kāryam atra sva lakṣaṇe puruṣasya pravartanam tad adhyavasāyaḥ ca yatas ca kāryataḥ tad viṣaya tvāt smṛtiḥ eva atas na pramāṇam darśana bala utpannaḥ vikalpaḥ tathā hi smṛteḥ api anubhūta sva lakṣaṇa aṃśa viṣayāyāḥ na paramārthataḥ tad viṣaya tvam sva lakṣaṇasya indriya buddhau iva sphuṭa rūpa tayā smṛtau apratibhāsanāt kintu yathā uktāt kāryataḥ eva tat ca vidhi vikalpe api samānam iti katham asau smṛtiḥ na syāt iti 
HBṬ_1.23.1	 tatra etat syāt nanu anumāna vikalpaḥ smṛti rūpaḥ api pramāṇam iṣyate tathā hi yat eva anagni vyāvṛttam vastu mātram mahānasa ādau anubhūtam āsīt tat eva pradeśa viśeṣe dhūma darśanāt smaryate tadvat vidhi vikalpaḥ api pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti atas āha anādhigatasya vastunaḥ rūpasya anadhigateḥ iti evam manyate yat mahānasa ādau anagni vyāvṛttam vastu mātram prāk anubhūtam na tat tad deśa ādi sambandhi tayā eva anumāna vikalpena smaryate kintu yatra pradeśe prāk ananubhūtam tad sambandhi tayā tatas sādhya dharmi dṛṣṭānta dharmi grāhi darśana dvayān adhigatasya anagni vyāvṛttasya vastu rūpasya ayoga vyavacchedena adhigamāt yuktam asya prāmāṇyam na tu darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya tad viparīta tvāt iti 
HBṬ_1.24.1	 yadi nāma anadhigatam vastu rūpam na adhigacchati pramāṇam tu kasmāt na bhavati iti ced āha vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvāt ityādi vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvam ca pramāṇa vyavasthāyāḥ pramāṇa vyāpāra viṣayam abhipretya ucyate na ālambhana lakṣaṇam anyathā anumānasya parikalpita sāmānya ālambhana tayā vastu adhiṣṭhāna tva abhāvāt avyāpinī pramāṇa vyavasthā syāt yadi vastu adhiṣṭhānā pramāṇa vyavasthā katham viprakṛṣṭa viṣayāyāḥ anupalabdheḥ prāmāṇyam iti ced tatra api pradhāna ādi vikalpasya eva bhāvānupādāna tayā sādhya tvāt tasyāḥ api vastu adhiṣṭhāna tā asti eva iti adoṣaḥ 
HBṬ_1.24.2	 athāḥ vatu adhiṣṭhānā eva pramāṇa vyvasthe ati kutas etat iti āha artha kriyāyām sukha duḥkha lakṣaṇāyām yat yogyam śaktam tad viṣaya tvāt tad arthinām artha kriyā arthinām pravṛtteḥ prāpti tyāga lakṣaṇāyāḥ yadi nāma artha kriyā yogye tad arthinām pravṛttiḥ tathā api katham vastu adhiṣṭhānā pramāṇa vyavasthā  artha kriyā yogya adhiṣṭhānā hi tathā sati syāt iti ced āha artha kriyāyām yat yogyam tad lakṣaṇam eva hi vastu tatas artha kriyā yogya adhiṣṭhāna tvena vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvam katham na syāt iti bhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_1.24.3	 idam ca vastu āśrayeṇa pramāṇa vyavasthā pratipādanam anadhigate sva lakṣaṇaḥ iti ukte kadācid paraḥ brūyāt vastu mātra nibandhanāḥ hi pramāṇa vyavasthā na sva lakṣaṇa āśraya eva tatas yadi api anadhigatam sva lakṣaṇam na adhigacchati tathā api anadhigata vastu rūpam adhigacchataḥ vikalpasya prāmāṇyam bhaviṣyati iti tad asiddha tā udbhāvanā artham uktam anadhigata vastu rūpā iti ādi tad asiddha tā udbhāvane ca anadhigata vastu rūpa adhigantuḥ eva prāmāṇyam na itarasya iti kutas iti paryanuyoge artha kriyā yogyā iti ādi uktam tathā ca vastu viṣayam api prāmāṇyam bruvatā sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam eva uktam bhavati tasya eva artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt sāmānyasya ca tad viparīta tvāt iti manyate 
HBṬ_1.24.4	 punar api anubhava uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ nīla vikalpasya prāmāṇyam apanetum upacaya hetum āha tatas api yathā uktāt vikalpāt na kevalam nīla sva lakṣaṇa anubhavāt vastuni eva sva lakṣaṇaḥ eva tat adhyavasāyena sva lakṣaṇa adhyavasāyena anyathā tatra pravṛtti ayogāt puruṣasya pravṛtteḥ adhigate sva lakṣaṇe tad sāmarthya janmā vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam iti sambandhaḥ pūrvam anadhigata vastu rūpa an adhigateḥ aprāmāṇyam uktam adhunā tu adhigatasya eva adhigamāt iti vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tayā upapattyoḥ bhedaḥ yat vā kāryataḥ tat viṣaya tvāt iti yat uktam tat eva upacaya hetu vyājena sphutīkṛtam 
HBṬ_1.25.1^1	 yadi nāma tat adhyavasāyena vastuni eva puruṣasya pravṛttiḥ tathā api anadhigata sāmānya grāhiṇaḥ asya darśanāt pṛthak prāmāṇyam kim iti na iṣyate iti ced āha pravṛttau sva lakṣaṇaḥ eva satyām pratyakṣeṇa ālocanā jñāna ākhyena abhinna yogakṣema tvāt yogaḥ aprāptasya viṣayasya pariccheda lakṣaṇā prāptiḥ kṣemaḥ tad artha kriyā anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇam paripālanam abhinnau yogakṣema avasthā iti sa tathā uktaḥ tatra vikalpasya nirvikalpa pratyakṣeṇa abhinnaḥ yogaḥ sva lakṣaṇa adhyavasāyataḥ abhinnaḥ kṣemaḥ ālocanā vijñānāt iva vikalpāt api sva lakṣaṇaḥ eva pravṛtteḥ 
HBṬ_1.25.1^2	 ayam asya abhiprāyaḥ yadi vikalpaḥ nirvikalpa cetasaḥ prameya antara viṣayaḥ tadā tatra eva puruṣam pravartaya tu tad sādhyām artha kriyām adhigantum na eva vā pravartayet tad viṣaya tva abhimatasya sāmānyasya abhinna jñāna lakṣaṇāyāḥ eva artha kriyāyāḥ upagamāt vikalpa udayāt eva ca tad siddheḥ na hi nīla anubhavāt prameya antara viṣayāḥ pīta ādi pratyayāḥ puruṣam nīla vastuni pravartayanti sādhita artha kriyā vā kvacid api iti tasmāt ālocanā jñānāt na eva ayam prameya antara viṣayaḥ viśeṣeṇa yaiḥ evam vyākhyāyate 
HBṬ_1.25.2–1.25.3	 nirvikalpaka bodhena dvi ātmakasya api vastunaḥ prahaṇam iti tatas nīla darśanasya eva nirvikalpasya prāmāṇyam yuktam na tat abhinna upayogasya smṛteḥ iva vikalpasya api darśanāt pṛthak eva anyathā niṣphalām pramāṇa antara kalpanām kurvataḥ smṛti icchā dveṣa prayatna ādi pramāṇam anuṣajyate iti pramāṇānām iyattā viśīryeta iti 
HBṬ_1.26.1^1	 yadā ekasmin eva nīla ādi vastuni dhārāvāhīni indriya jñānāni utpadyante tadā pūrveṇa abhinna yogakṣema tvāt uttareṣām indriya jñānānām aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ na ca evam atas anekāntaḥ iti pramāṇa saṃplava vādī darśayan āha pūrva pratyakṣa kṣaṇena ityādi etat pariharati na uttareṣām prāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ kutas  nānā yogakṣema tvāt tathā hi pratikṣaṇam viṣaya pariccheda lakṣaṇaḥ yogaḥ tad artha kriyā anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇaḥ ca kṣemaḥ paripālana rūpaḥ bhidyate tatas vipakṣe vṛtti abhāvāt na hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ kadā nānā yogakṣema tvam  kṣaṇa viśeṣa sādhya arthavāñchāyām yadā kṣaṇa viśeṣa sādhye arthe hita ahita lakṣaṇe vāñchā prāpti parihāret śā yoginām para upakāram uddiśya bhavati kasyacid kathañcid kvacid upayogāt tadā 
HBṬ_1.26.1^2	 yathā darśana mārgge duḥkhe dharma jñāna kṣāntiḥ daśānām anuśayānām vāsanām nirodhayati tad viruddha āśaya utpādanāt duḥkhe dharma jñānam kleṣa vivikta tā lakṣaṇām nirvāṇa prāptim utpādayati anuśaya viruddha āśaya dārḍhya utpādanāt tatas eṣām grāhakāṇi para citta jñānāni pṛthak eva pramāṇāni para hita ādhāna dīkṣāvatām ca samasta vastu vistara vyāpi jñāna āloka avabhāsita antarātmanām bhagavatām kaścid eva artha kṣaṇaḥ kasyacid eva para arthasya anugrāhakaḥ vibandhakaḥ vā iti sarva bhāvān pratikṣaṇam vīkṣamāṇānām adhyakṣa cetasām tad viṣa yakṣaṇānām bhinna artha kriyāsu upayogataḥ nānā yogakṣema tvāt tat yadi pratiksaṇam ksaṇa viveka darśinaḥ adhikṛtya ucyate tadā bhinna upayogi tayā pṛthak prāmāṇyāt na anekāntaḥ atha sarva padārtheṣu ekatvā adhyavasāyinaḥ sāṃvyavahārikān puruṣān abhipretya ucyate tadā sakalam eva nīla santānam ekam artham sthira rūpam tat sādhyām 
HBṬ_1.26.2	 ca artha kriyām eka ātmikām adhyavasyanti iti prāmāṇyam api uttareṣām aniṣṭam eva iti kutas anekāntaḥ iti darśayan āha sādhāraṇe hi iti tad santāna varttinām sarva kṣaṇānām eka tvena adhyavasitānām vyavahartṛbhiḥ yat sādhāraṇam pratikṣaṇam anya anyakāraṇa tayā vibhinnam api paramārtha taḥ viparyāsāt ekatayā abhiniviṣṭam rañjana ādikam nīla ādika kāryam tatra na teṣām uttareṣām jñāna kṣaṇānām sāmarthyasya artha prāpaṇa śakteḥ bhedaḥ pūrva pratyakṣa kṣaṇa viṣayaḥ eva tebhyaḥ api pravṛtteḥ ādyasya eva tatra prāmāṇyam tathā hi artha kriyā arthinām tad sādhana prāpaṇa samarthe jñāne pramāṇa vyavahāram kurvatām aviklava dhiyām artha kriyā sādhana bhedāt eva prāmāṇya bheda vyavahāraḥ jñāneṣu yuktaḥ anyathā smṛti ādeḥ api prāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ katham apākriyeta  ādriyeta vā niṣphalā pramāṇa vyavasthā prekṣāvatā iti  
HBṬ_1.26.3	 keṣām iva sādhāreṇe kārye na sāmarthya bhedaḥ iti āha apara apare ca te dhumāḥ ca taiḥ pramitāḥ ca te sannikṛṣṭa agnayaḥ ca teṣu iva tad viṣayāṇām iva anumān jñānānām agni mātra sādhye arthe sandhukṣaṇa ādike vāñchite tad artha kriyā sādhana prāpaṇa vyakti bheda abhāvāt tathā prāmāṇya bhedaḥ na yuktaḥ viduṣām tathā atra api yadā tu pañcatapaḥ taptu kāmaḥ bhavati tadā apara apara dhūma pramita sannikṛṣṭa agni viṣayāṇām api anumānānām sāmarthya bhedāt prāmāṇyam anivāritam eva 
HBṬ_1.27.1–1.27.3	 tat evam yathā nīlam dṛṣṭvā nīlam iti jñānam iti udāharaṇe nīla vikalpasya prāmāṇyam nirākṛtya prakṛte yojyan āha etena nīla sva lakṣaṇa darśana uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ nīla vikalpasya prāmāṇya nirākareṇa tat na iṣṭa tvāt vikalpasya api artha rūpa upakāriṇaḥ iti bruvata akumārilena pradeśa ādi darśana uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ dharmi vikalpasya tathā sambandha pratipatti kāle agni sva lakṣaṇa darśana sāmarthya bhāvinaḥ agni sāmānya viṣayasya sādhya dharma vikalpasya dhūma ālocanā jñāna pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ dhūma sāmānya avabhāsinaḥ liṅga vikalpasya ādi grahaṇāt dharma dharmi sambandha vikalpasya ca pramāṇa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ dharmya ādi svarūpa mātra viṣaya ālocana ākhya pratyakṣa pūrvakasya 
HBṬ_1.27.4–1.27.9	 na ca avikalpya liṅgasya dharmi sambandhayoḥ tathā gṛhītiḥ iti ākṣepa bhayāt yat abhyupagatam prāmāṇyam tat pratyuktam pratyākhyātam pūrvakam eva sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam darśanam yat pareṇa ālocanā jñānam iti vyavahṛtam tat pramāṇam na tu tad bala bhāvī vikalpaḥ yathā uktena nyāyena iti sthitam etat pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmiṇi pratyakṣataḥ anumānataḥ vā aprasiddhiḥ niścayaḥ iti tat evam pratyakṣataḥ pakṣa dharma niścayam bruvatā prasaṅgena darśana pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya prāmāṇya nirākaraṇāt pratyakṣaṃkalpanā apoḍham iti pratipāditam 
HBṬ_1.28.1	 yadi evam kasmāt anumāna vyutpādana artham idam ārabhyate iti uktam na sāmānyena samyak jñāna vyutpādana artham iti  saṅkhī ā ādi vipratipattiḥ api atra tad viṣayāḥ nirastā eva parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ anumānam eva āśrayaḥ kasmāt yatas pakṣa dharmaḥ eva tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ eva ca hetuḥ kāraṇam tasyāḥ na anyaḥ iti abhidhānāt parokṣa artha viṣayam sarvam pramaṇam anumāne antar bhāvitam iti saṅksepataḥ saṅkhyā vipratipattiḥ samyak jñāna viṣayāḥ nirastāḥ tathā vyāpaka aṃśasya gamya tva pratīteḥ tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanena sāmānya viṣayam anumānam na sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam iti ākhyātam tasya asādhāraṇa tvāt asādhāraṇasya ca vyāpaka tva ayogāt vikalpa aviṣaya tvāt ca tatra tad ādyam asādhāraṇa viṣayam iti ācakṣāṇena sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam eva pratyakṣam uktam darśanam eva pramāṇam iti ākhyānāt pramāṇam eva phalam iti sūcitam 
HBṬ_1.28.2–1.28.3	 tasya artha pratīti rūpa tvāt tathā tasya dvidhā prayogaḥ iti vakṣyamāṇa tvāt para artha anumānam kathayiṣyate tasya trirūpa liṅga ākhyāna rūpa tvāt saṅkṣepataḥ ca anumāna vyutpādanam api abhimatam tat ca sarvatra asti eva iti kasmāt anumāna vyutpādana artham iti uktam  satyam prādhānyāt tu tad grahaṇam tathā hi pradhāna puruṣa artha upayoginaḥ tattvasya catur ārya satya lakṣaṇasya anumānataḥ eva niścayāt tasya prādhānyam tathā pratyakṣe api viṣaye vivāda sambhave na anumānāt anyat nirṇaya nibandhanam iti atas api asya prādhānyam pravartaka tvāt ca prādhānyam asya tathā hi yad anubhūta phalam sukha duḥkha sādhanam anubhūyamāna phalam vā dṛśyamānam na tad pravṛtti viṣayaḥ niṣpanna tvāt phalasya tasmāt yat anāgata phalam sukha duḥkha sādhanam pratyakṣam api tatra api anumānam eva pravartakam na hi tasya anāgate sukha duḥkhe prati yogyatām pratyakṣam nirddhārayati phalasya parokṣa tvāt tat uktam na hi apratyakṣe kārye kāraṇa bhāva gatiḥ iti 
HBṬ_1.28.4	 tasmāt pūrva anubhūta sukha duḥkha sādhana sādharmyāt pratyakṣa viṣayasya api vastunaḥ anāgata phala yogya tā niścayaḥ na pratyakṣatas tathā ca āha tat yathā dṛṣṭa sādharmyāt tathā aprasādhitam na anumeya tām atipatati iti katham tarhi dvayoḥ api pravartaka tvam  na hi ābhyām arthaṃparicchidya pravartamānaḥ artha kriyāyāṃvisaṃvādyate iti uktam sukha duḥkha sādhanasya jala anala ādeḥ svarūpasya pratyakṣatas prasiddheḥ phalam anāgatam prati yogyatāyāḥ anumānataḥ iti ubhayoḥ api pravartaka tvam samyak jñāna pūrvaka tvam ca hita ahita prāpti parihārayoḥ uktam na tu anāgata phalam prati yogyatāyāḥ pratyakṣataḥ aniścayāt na hi arvāk darśinām bhāvi phala yogya tāyāḥ tatas niścayaḥ tatas prādhānyāt anumāna grahaṇam iti alam ati vistareṇa iti 
HBṬ_1.29.1^1	 tatra svabhāva kārya anupalambhānām pakṣa dharma niścayaḥ tulya upāya sādhya tayā abhedena eva uktaḥ anvaya vyatireka niścayasya tu bhinna upāya sādhya tayā bhedena eva nirddeśaḥ kāryaḥ iti svabhāva hetau tāvat anvaya niścayam sva pramāṇa nibandhanam darśayan āha anvaya niścayaḥ api na kevalam pakṣa dharma niścayaḥ uktaḥ kintu anvaya niśayaḥ api svabhāva hetau ucyate iti śeṣaḥ sādhana dharmasya yat bhāva mātram sattā mātram mudgara ādi nimitta antara anapekṣam tasya anubandhaḥ anugamanam vyāptiḥ tasya siddhiḥ yā sa svabhāva hetau anvaya niścayaḥ 
HBṬ_1.29.1^2	 kasya sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandha siddhiḥ  sādhya dharmasya sādhyaḥ ca asau asiddha tvāt dharma dharmi samudaya eka deśa tvāt dharmaḥ ca iti tathā uktaḥ yatra yatra sādhana dharmasya bhāvaḥ tatra tatra sādhya dharmasya api nimitta antara anapekṣaḥ bhāvaḥ iti etasya arthasya siddhiḥ svabhāva hetau anvaya niścayaḥ katham punar sādhya dharmaḥ sādhana dharma bhāva mātram anubadhnāti  tad bhāva tayā sa sādhana dharmaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ yasya tasya bhāvatayā tad bhāva tayā yaḥ hi sādhana dharmaḥ sādhya dharmasya svabhāvaḥ sa katham tam na anubadhnīyāt nīrūpa tva prasaṅgāt  
HBṬ_1.30.1	 nanu tad svabhāva tve bheda abhāvāt katham sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ iti āha vastutas paramārthataḥ sādhya sādhana saṃkalpa kāle tu paramparayā tat tad vyāvṛtta padārtha nibandhanāyām kalpanā buddhau bhedena pratibhāsanāt sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ na vihanyate na hi asau pāramārthikam sādhya sādhana dharmayoḥ ddharmiṇaḥ ca kṛtaka tva ādau bhedam avalambhate sambandha abhāvena sādhya sādhana bhāva ayogāt 
HBṬ_1.30.2	 eka artha samavāyaḥ kṛtaka tva anitya tva ādeḥ sambandhaḥ iti ced na tasya api tatas artha antara tve ayam anayoḥ asmin arthe samavāyaḥ iti sambandha abhāvasya tad avastha tvāt sambandha antara kalpanāyām ca anavasthā prasaṅgāt samavāyāt vṛtti kalpanāyām ca kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ nitya abhimateṣu api ātma ādiṣu varteran yaḥ eva hi kṛtaka tva ādeḥ śabde samavāyaḥ yat balāt tatra eva tat vartate saḥ eva nitya abhimateṣu api tasya eka tvena upagata tvāt iti ātma ādau vṛttiḥ kṛtaka tva ādeḥ kena nivaryeta  atha yaḥ eva abhūtvā bhavana dharmā bhūtvā ca abhavana dharmāḥ asthira rūpaḥ bhāvaḥ tatra eva kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ vartante iti vyavasthāpyate sā eva tarhi abhūtvā bhavana svabhāva tā bhūtasya ca asthira svabhāva tā tad viparīta rūpa samāra upa vyavaccheda viṣayayāyāḥ kalpanā buddheḥ nibandhanam kim na iṣyate  tayā eva parama artha abhedavatoḥ ddharmayoḥ sādhya dharmiṇi vṛtteḥ kim antarāla gaḍunā kṛtaka tva ādinā 
HBṬ_1.30.3	 vyatirekavatā upagatena  tathā hi na sattā mātreṇa kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ sādhya dharma pratipatti nibandhanam teṣām sadā sannihita tvena anavaratam tad dharma pratīti prasaṅgāt kintu vikalpa pratibhāsinaḥ eva sa ca vikalpaḥ sva pratibhāsinam eva ākāram bahīrūpatayā adhyavasitam anusaran kṛtakān iti ādi rūpa tām vastunaḥ pratipadyate paramārthataḥ asaṃsparśe api tad rūpasya paramparayā tad upādāna tvāt vyatiriktāḥ tu dharmāḥ tad utpatti nimitta mātra tayā parikalpyante tat varam yat eva tad kalpanā nibandhanam tat eva tathāvidha vikalpa prasava nimittam astu tasya avaśyam abhyupagamanīya tvāt tad abhyupagame ca caritārthāḥ vyatirekavantaḥ dharmāḥ iti alam tad kalpanayā avaśyam ca vyatiriktā anitya tā dvāreṇa api vastunaḥ eva anavasthāyinam ātmānam pratipadyante tad anurūpa artha kriyā arthitayā pravṛtteḥ anyathā vyatiriktā anitya tayā nitya tvāt tad avagama artha tvena ayam anitya sādhya artha kriyā arthī nityam 
HBṬ_1.30.4	 śabda ādikam āśaṅkamānaḥ kim anitya tā vicāram prati āhita āsthaḥ  vyatiriktāyām ca anitya tāyām avagatāyām tatra eva pravartatām kim iti nitye śabda ātmani  tad dvāreṇa pratipatteḥ iti ced tat kim anena vyavadhinā  varam avyavahitasya eva pratipattiḥ astu tena eva artha tvāt iti tat etat atipracarccyamānam ati gahanam sampadyate iti āstām tāvat 
HBṬ_1.30.5	 ye api jaiminīyām anyante yeṣām atyanta vyatirekavantaḥ dharmāḥ teṣām eva ayaṃnaiyāyika ādīnām doṣaḥ asmākam tu kathañcid bheda abhedavatām dharmāṇām tad svabhāvatayā na eṣa doṣaḥ iti teṣām api vastutas sādhana dharma rūpa tā upagame sādhya dharmasya kathañcid bheda abhyupagame na kiñcid phalam utpaśyāmaḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvasya kalpita bheda dvāreṇa api upapatteḥ na ca aikātmye kathañcid api bhedaḥ yuktaḥ ekasmāt svabhāvāt abhedāt tatas api tayoḥ kathañcid bheda abhedau staḥ eva iti ced na anavasthā prasaṅgāt tathā hi dharmayoḥ tad eka svabhāvāt api bhedavatoḥ tena svabhāvena kathañcid abheda nimittam abhinnaḥ aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tathā tenā api aparaḥ iti anantā eva bhinna abhinna svabhāva paramparā syāt na ca kalpanā buddhau ananta ubhaya rūpa svabhāva paramparā pratibhāsate iti kim iti tat kalpanayā aatmānam vipralabhante bhavantaḥ  kathañcid ca bheda upagamāt 
HBṬ_1.30.6	 katham bheda pakṣa bhāvinām doṣāṇām anavasaraḥ  yam ca ātmānam purodhāya imau dharmāu ayam dharmī iti vyavasthāpyate yadi tena bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva iti kutas anekānta vādaḥ  atha abhedaḥ tadā ayam sādhana dharmaḥ ayam sādhya dharmaḥ dharmī ca ayam iti katham pāramārthikam tritayam sidhyet  tasmāt tad tad para rūpa vyāvṛtti samāśrayāyām kalpanā buddhau bhedavatām iva dharma dharmiṇām pratibhāsanāt sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ tanmātra anubandhaḥ tu vastutas tad tad svabhāva tayā eva yuktaḥ iti manyamānena vastutas tad bhāva tayā iti uktam 
HBṬ_1.31.1	 kā punar asau vastutas tad bhāva tā yayā hetu bhūtayā sādhya dharmasya sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandhaḥ sidhyati iti āha sā vastutas tad bhāva tā sādhyasya viparyayaḥ vipakṣaḥ tatra hetoḥ yat bādha kaṃpramāṇam tad viparīta dharma pratyavasthāpakam yena bādhyamānaḥ hetuḥ tatra na pravartate viruddhayoḥ ekatra sahabhāva asambhavāt tasya yā vṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttiḥ tad sādhya tvāt ca vastutas tad bhāva tāyāḥ sā bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttiḥ uktāḥ tasyām hi satyām vipakṣāj nivṛttaḥ hetuḥ sādhya dharmavatī eva dharmiṇi vartate iti sādhya dharmasya anartha antarasya sādhana dharma svabhāva tā sidhyati tayā āca vastutas tad bhāva tayā sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandhaḥ sādhya dharmasya sidhyati iti anvaya niścayaḥ yatra yatra sādhana dharmaḥ tatra sādhya dharmaḥ iti evam rūpaḥ jāyate 
HBṬ_1.31.2–1.31.3	 atra udāharaṇam yathā yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva avadhārena vyāptim āha sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandhanasya ca etat rūpam ākhyātam nimitta antaram antareṇa sat iti eva kṛtvā kṣaṇikam iti upadarśanāt sa ca vastutas tad bhāva tayā sidhyati iti tad siddhi upāyam bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttim darśayati akṣaṇika tve kṣaṇika viparyaye sati artha kriyā virodhāt arthasya kāryasya kriyā niṣpattiḥ tasyāḥ virodhāt tad lakṣaṇam sā artha kriyā lakṣaṇam yasya vastu tvasya artha kriyā sāmarthya ātmanaḥ tat tathā uktam artha kriyā hi tad sāmarthya rūpam vastu tvam lakṣyate tat evam vidham vastu tvam hīyate nivartate tad viparyaya rūpasya asattvasyā aakarṣaṇāt etat ca bādhakam pramāṇam vyāpaka anupalabdhi rūpam uttaratra avasara prāptam svayam eva vakṣyati tad anayā bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttayā sādhya dharmasya vastutas sādhana dharma svabhāva tā sidhyati tayā ca vastutas tad bhāva tayā sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandhaḥ iti 
HBṬ_1.32.1	 evam svabhāva hetau viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā tādātmya siddhitaḥ anvaya niścayam pratipādya kārya hetau pratipādayan āha kārya hetau anvaya niścayaḥ iti prakṛtam kaḥ punar asau kārya kāraṇayoḥ bhāvaḥ  kārya tvam kāraṇa tvaṃca tasya yā siddhiḥ pratītiḥ sā kārya hetau anvaya niścayaḥ yathā ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ bhavati tathā upadarśayan āha yathā ityādi yathāśabdaḥ upadarśana arthaḥ idam dhūma ādikam asya agneḥ upalambhe sati upalabhyate iti sambandhaḥ anena kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau pratyakṣa vyāpāram āha na ca kevalam pratyakṣam kārya kāraṇa bhāvam asandigdham sādhayati kintu prāc pravṛttān upalambha sahāyam iti darśāyitum āha upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam anupalabdham iti yadi tat dhūma ādikam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu 
HBṬ_1.32.2	 dṛśya ātmakam sat na upalabdham bhavati agni ādi sāmagrī sannidhānāt prāk tad agni ādi sāmagryām upalabhyamānāyām upalabhyamānam tat kāryam sidhyati na tu upalambha pratyaya antar vaikalyāt anupajāta upalabdhi yogya rūpam sat tad deśa sannihitam api anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tayā agni ādi sāmagrī sannidhānāt prāc anupalabdham iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya ca anupalambhena agni ādi sāmagrī sannidhānāt prāc anya tā āgamanam tad deśa kāla saṃ= nihitāt kaṭakuṭī ādeḥ utpattiḥ tad deśe cā asannidhānam iti tritayam apākriyate etāvadbhiḥ ca prakāraiḥ atat kāryatā bhavantī bhavet tatas anupalambhenā atad kārya tā śaṅkā nirāsāt tad bhāve bhāva grāhi pratyakṣa nibandhanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ asandigdhaḥ sidhyati 
HBṬ_1.32.3^1	 na ca agni indhana ādi bhāve niyata sannidheḥ adṛśya ātmanaḥ kutaścid dhūmasya bhāvaḥ syāt iti āśaṅkanīyam agni indhana ādi bheda anuvidhānāt dhūmasya candana aguru karpūra keśa ūrṇa ādīn dhana bhede tad anurūpa bhedasya asya darśanāt alpa mahat indhana vikāra kāriṇaḥ ca agneḥ tad anurūpasya na ca agni indhana ādi sannidhau adṛśya ātmanaḥ niyata sannidhāna tā yuktāḥ pratibandha abhāvāt pratibandhe vā tad kāryatā tad kāraṇa tā vā syāt tad kārya tve na agni indhana samparkkā anantaram dhūma janma syāt tad bhāva abhāva anuvidhānāt eva ca asya api tad kāryatvam tat ca dhūme api samānam na api indhana ādi kāraṇa tvam adṛśya ātmanaḥ indhana ādeḥ sva hetoḥ eva vṛkṣa ādeḥ bhāva darśanāt tatra api tathā abhāva kalpanāyām tat eva uttaram vācyam 
HBṬ_1.32.3^2	 punar codye saḥ eva parihāraḥ anavasthā ca etena ekasāmagrī adhīna tā api pratyuktāḥ tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt eva ca dhūmasya tat kāraṇam kalpeta tat ca agni ādau api tulyam tat api tatra kāraṇam astu iti ced na agni ādi bhāve avaśyam bhāvinaḥ anyasya api kāraṇa tva kalpanāyām nimitta abhāvāt kārya vyatireka nibandhana tvāt kāraṇa bhāva kalpanāyāḥ tathā agni indhana ādeḥ eva anyatara abhāve abhavataḥ bhavatu vā anyasya api tad bhāve niyata sannidheḥ kāraṇa tā na tu tāvatā agni ādeḥ kāraṇa tva hāniḥ yatas dhūma darśanāt tad niścayena pravṛttau tad visaṃvādaḥ syāt na hi sarva sattva karma ādhipatya janita tve api jagat vaicitryasya dṛṣṭa kāraṇa hānitas tad kārya darśanāt vā pravṛttānām atad prāptiḥ iti alam atiprasaṅgena 
HBṬ_1.32.4	 kim rūpaḥ punar asau kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anupalambha sahāya pratyakṣa nibandhanaḥ iti āha tad bhāve bhāvaḥ tad abhāve abhāvaḥ ca iti yaḥ eva hi kāraṇa abhimatasya bhāve bhāvaḥ eva kārya tvena abhimatasya bhāvaḥ tad abhāve kāraṇa tva abhimatasyāḥ abhāve abhāvaḥ eva kārya tvena abhimatasya abhāvaḥ ca saḥ eva kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na anyaḥ 
HBṬ_1.32.5	 sa hi tābhyām anyaḥ bhavan svabhāvataḥ apratipanna kārya kāraṇa rūpayoḥ vā bhavet yat vā svabhāvena eva kārya kāraṇa ātmanoḥ yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā sarvatra eva akārya kāraṇa bhūte api vastuni bhavet tad niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt tatas sarvam sarvasya kāryam syāt svabhāvena ca atad rūpasya anya yoge api na tad rūpa tā na hi bhāvāḥ pratiniyata rūpatyagena anya yoge api rūpa antaram ābhajante yatas na anya yogaḥ teṣām pūrva rūpam nāśayati vināśa hetu ayogāt vakṣyamāṇakāt nā api apūrvam utpādayati tasya tatas artha antara tva prasaṅgāt na hi teṣu niṣpanneṣu aniṣpannaḥ bhinna hetukaḥ vā tad svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ ayam hi bhedaḥ bheda hetuḥ vā viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ kāraṇa bhedaḥ ca tatas ced na bhedaḥ anya nimitta abhāvāt ekam dravyam viśvam syāt ityādi prasajyeta pratibhāsa bhedaḥ api hi itaretara abhāva rūpa tayā viruddha dharma adhyāsa tām na atikrāmati tatas ca pūrvake vastunī 
HBṬ_1.32.6–1.32.7	 tad avasthe eva iti na tayoḥ anya yoge api kārya kāraṇa rūpa tā āpattiḥ atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā svabhāvataḥ eva tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa rūpa tvāt anyaḥ tad bhāvaḥ katham na vaiyarthyam anubhavet  kārya kāraṇa buddhī api tad bhāva bhāvi tva mātra nibandhane na artha antara nimitte tasya upapalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya kārya kāraṇa rūpa vivekinā rūpa antareṇa apratibhāsanāt tathāvidhāsya api grahaṇa kalpanāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tāyām katham kārya kāraṇa bhāva buddhī tad nibandhane  na hi tat artha antaram sva sattā mātreṇa tad buddhī pravartayati sadā sannihita tvena asya tayoḥ sarva dā udaya prasaṅgāt na ca viśeṣaṇam agṛhītam viśeṣye sva viśiṣṭa pratyaya nibandhanam iti ayuktā asya anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tā na ca dṛṣṭasya api anupalakṣaṇam yuktam kārya kāraṇa buddhyoḥ tad nibandha natā upagamāt na hi yad nimittaḥ yaḥ anyatra atad buddhi bhāji tad vyavasāyaḥ sa tad anupalakṣaṇe yuktaḥ devadatte daṇḍi vyavasāya vat 
HBṬ_1.32.8	 daṇḍa anupalakṣaṇe na ca artha antarasya kārya kāraṇābhyām sambandhaḥ ghaṭate sambandha antara kalpanāyām anavasthā prasakteḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva abhyupagame kārya kāraṇābhyām asahabhāvitā sadbhāvasya tatas ca kārya kāraṇa kāle tasya asannidhānāt katham kārya kāraṇa buddhi hetu tāḥ  niruddhayoḥ adhyāhṛtya tad pratyaya kalpanāyām ca kalpita viṣayaḥ eva kārya kāraṇa tā adhyavasāyaḥ syāt na vastu viṣayaḥ sa ca viśiṣṭa bhāva abhāva nibandhanaḥ abhyupagataḥ eva iti kim artha antara kalpanayā  kalpita viṣaya tve tad vyavasāyasya tasyāḥ vaiyarthyāt kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca ayaugapadyāt na hi tābhyām asau janyate pratyeka janyaḥ ca katham kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  yadā ca kāraṇena janyate tadā kim sva kārya sahitaḥ janyate atha kevalaḥ  kevalaḥ api kim sva kāryāt prāk atha paścāt  yadi sva kārya sahitaḥ tad ā ubhayoḥ anyatas eva bhāvāt parasparam asambandhaḥ iti kārya sambandhi tā asya hīyeta atha 
HBṬ_1.32.9	 kevalaḥ sva kāryāt prāk tadā kṣaṇikatayā kāraṇasya tam eva janayitvā dhvaṃsāt katham sva kārya kriyā  tasyām ca asatyām katham tad apekṣam asya kāraṇa tvam  tasmin ca asati katham akāraṇena kārya kāraṇa sambandhaḥ janyate  atha sva kāryam kṛtvā paścāt janyeta tadā api sva kārya kāle eva vinaṣṭa tvāt asataḥ tad uttara kāla bhāvi kārya kāraṇa bhāva jananam kutas  tad bhāvaḥ ca sambandhaḥ ucyate 
HBṬ_1.32.10–1.32.11	 janyatāyām vā yadi samagrāḥ svarūpataḥ eva tām janayanti kārye kaḥ eṣām śakti vyāghātaḥ yatas anyatra kalpyate tatra api apara sāmagrī yoga apekṣāyām ca anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ tatas samagrāḥ eva janakāḥ teṣām ca kāraṇa tvam ekaika apāye kārya vyatirekataḥ samunnīyate iti āha satsu api anyeṣu tad sāmagrī antarggateṣu hetuṣu janakeṣu pratyekam teṣām vyañjanaka tvāt asya abhāve janakatvena nirddhāryamāṇa tayā vivakṣitasya abhāve na bhavati iti anena anupalambhasya viṣayaḥ uktaḥ pratyakṣa vṛttiḥ tu pūrva uktā evā anupalambha rahitā tad bhāve bhāva grāhiṇī saṃbandhyate 
HBṬ_1.32.12	 tathā ca ayam api tad bhāve bhāvaḥ tad abhāve abhāvaḥ ca kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kim sādhanaḥ iti āha pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanaḥ pratyakṣa pūrvakaḥ anupalambhaḥ tad vivikta anya padārtha grāhi pratyakṣa ātmakaḥ sādhanam asya iti pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ yaḥ tu anupalambha sāpekṣeṇa pratyakṣeṇa sādhyate iti prāk uktaḥ saḥ anupalambha pūrvakam pratyakṣam sādhanam asya iti anupalambha pratyakṣa sādhanaḥ iti vaktavyaḥ tasya kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya anvaya vyatireka ātmanaḥ siddhiḥ niścayaḥ yathā uktābhyāṃ pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kārya hetau anvaya niścayaḥ iti sambadhyate 
HBṬ_1.32.13	 nanu ca anvaya niścayaḥ nāma kārya hetoḥ sarvatra kāryasya bhavataḥ sva kāraṇa sattayā a nugamanam iti evam avasāyaḥ tat katham kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ evā asau ucyate iti āśaṅkya kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nibandhana tvāt anvaya niścayasya kāraṇe kārya upacārāt ananya upāya sādhya tām darśayitum darśana mātra nibandhanam ye tam icchanti tat mata niṣedha artham asau evam uktaḥ iti darśayan āha kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva hi kārya kāraṇa bhāve sati eva hi yasmāt artha antarasya sādhyāt vyatiriktasya yaḥ tu avyatiriktaḥ tasya viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā tādātmya niścayāt eva anvaya niścayaḥ iti pūrvam uktam eva iti artha antara grahaṇam tasya artha antarasya evaṃsyāt katham  yatra nāma kvacid dhūmaḥ tatra avaśyam agniḥ iti niyamena agneḥ tatra bhāvaḥ iti evam rūpaḥ anvaya niścayaḥ yaḥ tu akārya kāraṇa bhāve api rasasya artha antarasya rūpeṇa anvaya niścayaḥ
