HBṬ_1.32.14–1.32.15	 saḥ eka sāmagrī adhīna tayā tasya sva kāraṇa vyabhicāra dvārakaḥ eva iti adoṣaḥ atha yadi nāma kāryam agneḥ dhūmaḥ tathā api kim iti yatra asau tatra avaśyam agniḥ bhavati yatas kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nibandhanaḥ anvaya niścayaḥ ucyate iti āha agneḥ bhāve eva sattāyām eva hiḥ yasmāt bhāvaḥ sattā dhūmasya kāryatvam iti tasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāve sati eva yathā uktaḥ anvaya niścayaḥ iti yadi hi yatra dhūmaḥ tatra avaśyam agniḥ na syāt tadā agnim antareṇa api asya bhāvāt agni bhāvaḥ eva bhāva lakṣaṇam kārya tvam hīyeta 
HBṬ_1.33.1	 idānīm anupalabdhau anvaya niścayam āha anupalabdhau api na kevalam svabhāva kārya hetvoḥ anvaya niścayaḥ uktaḥ kintu anupalabdhau api anvaya niścayaḥ ucyate kim rūpaḥ asau iti āha asat avyavahārasya sādhya dharmasya yogyatāyāḥ ca sādhya tvāt tad yogya tā asat vyavahāraḥ abhipretaḥ tasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya yā anupalabdhiḥ tad anya upalabdhi rūpā tanmātre nimitta antara anapekṣaṇī yā vṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ asat vyavahārasya tasyāḥ sādhanam siddhiḥ anupalabdhau anvaya niścayaḥ kutas punar asat vyahārasya tanmātre vṛttiḥ bhavati iti āha nimitta antara abhāva upadarśanāt iti yadā hi asat vyavahārasya yathā ukta anupalabdhi vyatiriktam buddhi vyapadeśa artha kriyā viraha ādikam nimittam na bhavati iti sādhyate tadā yathā ukta anupalabdhi mātre asya vṛttiḥ siddhā bhavati tayā ca anupalabdhau anvaya niścayaḥ anyathā hi nimitta antara apekṣā śaṅkāyām 
HBṬ_1.33.2–1.33.4	 satyām api yathā ukta anupalabdhau na avaśyam asat vyavahārasya bhāvaḥ iti kutas anvaya niścayaḥ syāt  nimitta antara abhāvaḥ tu vistara tovāt anyāya uktaḥ iti tatas eva avadhāryaḥ athavā sat vyavahārasya yad nimittam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya sattvam tat asat vyavahāra nimittāt anya tvāt nimitta antaram tatra anupalabdheḥ abhāvaḥ upadarśyate yena pramāṇena tat evam uktam tena sati vastuni tasyāḥ asambhava niścayāt anupalabdhau anvaya niścayaḥ tat ca tad vyatireka cintāyām darśayiṣyāmaḥ tat evam trayāṇām api hetūnām tathāsvam pramāṇena anvaya viniścayaḥ uktaḥ svabhāva hetau viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā tādātmya siddhi nibandhana tvāt kārya hetau pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nimitta tvāt anupalabdhau nimitta antara abhāva prasādhaka māṇataḥ tad abhāva siddhi hetu tvāt ca iti 
HBṬ_1.34.1–1.34.2^1	 samprati trayāṇām api hetūnām sva sva pramāṇa nibandhanam vyatireka niścayam pratipādayitu kāmaḥ āha vyatireka niścayaḥ api na kevalam anvaya niścayaḥ yathāsvam pramāṇa nibandhanaḥ tayoḥ uktaḥ api tu vyatireka niścayaḥ api kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ yathāsvam pramāṇa nimittaḥ ucyate kaḥ punar asau sādhya abhāve abhāva siddhiḥ yau atada ātmaka tad ātmakau hetū kāraṇa vyāpaka rūpa sādhyasya sādhakau sādhya abhāve ca abhāva siddhiḥ tayoḥ kena pramāṇena  kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyām kārya hetau kāraṇa anupalabdhyā sādhya abhāve abhāva niścayaḥ svabhāva hetau vyāpaka an upalabdhyā 
HBṬ_1.34.1–1.34.2^2	 kadā punar te anupalabdhī sādhike tasya bhavataḥ  kārya kāraṇa vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau satyām kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ kārya hetau sādhya abhāve abhāvasya sādhikā viparyaye ca bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā tad bhāvatā siddhitaḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau satyām vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ svabhāva hetau sādhya abhāve abhāvasya sādhikā iti tat evam bruvatā ubhayatra tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa pratibandha niścayāt eva dvayoḥ api anvaya vyatirekayoḥ niścayaḥ iti uktam bhavati atas eva anyatra kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt 
HBṬ_1.34.3	 vā ityādi uktam kīdṛśībhyām dṛśya viṣayābhyām dṛśyaḥ viṣayaḥ yayoḥ te tathā ukte yadi kāraṇa vyāpakau upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptau bhavataḥ tadā tad anupalabdhī sādhya abhāve abhāvam sādhyate iti yāvat kadā punar tayoḥ dṛśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam apekṣyate iti āha uddiṣṭa viṣayasya uddiṣṭaḥ kathitaḥ viṣayaḥ ādhāraḥ vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇaḥ yasya sādhya abhāve abhāvasya tasya upadarśane kriyamāṇe tatra api kasmāt dṛśya viṣaya tā apekṣyate iti ced āha anupalabdhi ityādi anyathā yadi dṛśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam anupalabdhyoḥ na apekṣyate yadā anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam viṣayam vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta rūpam upādatte tadā anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptau tatra kāraṇa vyāpakau= api bhavataḥ iti anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya kāraṇasya vyāpakasya vā kvacid viprakṛṣṭe viṣaye sumeru ādau abhāva asiddha ih 
HBṬ_1.34.4–1.34.5	 katham ābhyām sādhya abhāve abhāva siddhiḥ syāt kāraṇa vyāpaka an upalabdhyoḥ eva asiddha tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ atha anuddiṣṭa viṣayasya api abhāvasya upadarśane anupalabdhyoḥ daśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam kim iti na apekṣyate iti āha anuddiṣṭa viṣayam anuddiṣṭaḥ viṣayaḥ vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta rūpaḥ yasmin sādhya abhāve hetvabhāva khyāpane tat pratibandha mātra siddhau satyām dṛśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam antareṇa api yasmāt sidhyati iti tasmāt na tatra anuddiṣṭa viṣaye vyatireka sādhane anupalabdhyoḥ dṛśya viṣaya tā viśeṣaṇam apekṣyate aṅgīkriyate tathā hi aśeṣa padārtha parigraheṇa sāmānyena api bruvataḥ yaḥ yatra pratibaddha svabhāvaḥ tādātmya tad utpattibhyām sa tad abhāve avaśyam eva na bhavati iti niḥsvabhāva tvā ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt tat uktam 
HBṬ_1.34.6–1.34.14	 svabhāve api avinābhāvaḥ bhāva mātra anurodhini tad abhāve svayaṃbhāvasya abhāvaḥ syāt abhedataḥ tathā kāryaṃdhūmaḥ huta bhujaḥ kārya dharma anuvṛttitaḥ sa bhavan tad abhāve api hetumat tāṃvilaṅghayet iti tatas tatra dṛśya viṣaya tā apekṣyamāṇān upakārikā eva iti na tayā kiñcid iti bhāvaḥ pratibandha mātra siddhau iti anena ye pratibandham hetoḥ na varṇayanti kintu adarśana mātrāt eva vyatirekam āhuḥ teṣām tad asambhavam ca darśayati tathā hi asati pratibandhe yadi sarve sādhya virahiṇaḥ arthāḥ dṛśyāḥ bhavanti tadā teṣu anupalabdhasya sādhanasya abhāvaḥ śiṣyeta tat āha kumārilaḥ api gatvā aga tvātu tān deśān yadi arthaḥ na upalabhyate tadā anya kāraṇa abhāvāt asan iti avagamyate iti 
HBṬ_1.34.15	 deśa ādi viprakarṣi tayā tu adṛśya tve sati api tatra hetau anupalambha mātrasya sambhavāt sandigdhaḥ asau aśeṣe sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ vyatirekaḥ tathāvidhasya eva yatra yatra sādhya abhāvaḥ tatra tatra sādhana abhāvaḥ iti vīpsā padābhyām abhidhānāt anvaya niścayaḥ api prāk pratibandha nibandhanaḥ eva varṇitaḥ tatas tena api pareṣām darśana nibandhanām anvaya siddhim icchatām abhāvaḥ asya api kathitaḥ eva sarva arthānām hetumatām sādhya dharmavattayā draṣṭum aśakya tvāt anumātṛbhiḥ aśeṣa deśa ādi viṣayasya ca sādhya anugamasya yatra yatra hetuḥ tatra tatra sādhyam iti vīpsayā pratipādanāt na ca katipaya deśa ādausādhana dharmasya sādhya dharmeṇa sahabhāvasya bhūyas darśane api vyāptiḥ sidhyati asati pratibandhe kvacid bahulam tathā adṛṣṭānām api anyathā tu asya api sambhavāt tad asambhave bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt 
HBṬ_1.35.1	 anupalabdhim adhikṛtya adhunā aaha vyatireka niścayaḥ anupalabdhau ucyate iti śeṣaḥ kim ātmakaḥ asau iti āha upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāt vidyamāna upalambha pratyaya antarāt dṛśya svabhāvāt ca sataḥ vidyamānāt sādhya abhāva rūpa āt anupalambhasya tad vivikta upalambha ātmanaḥ yaḥ abhāvaḥ sataḥ yat grāhakam pratyakṣam tad bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ tasya darśanam darśyate pratyāyyate anena iti darśanam upadarśakam pramāṇam tad ātmakaḥ anupalabdhau vyatireka niścayaḥ tad hetu tvāt ca tat pramāṇam tathā ucyate yadi hi sannihitā anya upalambha pratyayaḥ dṛśya svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ vidyamānaḥ api na upalabhyeta katham asau dṛśya svabhāvaḥ syāt  yaḥ hi satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu san pratyakṣaḥ eva bhavati saḥ eva dṛśya svabhāvaḥ ākhyāyate tasmāt tathāvidhe sannihite avaśyam pratyakṣa vṛttyā bhavitavyam anyathā asya na kadācid 
HBṬ_1.35.2	 api pratyakṣatā syāt viśeṣa abhāvāt iti prayogaḥ yat yat mātra nimittam tat tasmin sati niyamena bhavati tat yathā bīja ādi sāmagrī mātra nimittaḥ aṅkuraḥ yathā ukta upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tā mātra nimittam ca sati vastuni tathāvidhe pratyakṣam iti svabhāva hetuḥ etena pramāṇena svabhāva anupalabdhau sādhya abhāve abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ vyatirekaḥ niścīyate etat ca pramāṇam anvaya niścayasya api nimittam anena eva nimitta antare anupalabdheḥ abhāva upadarśanāt kāraṇa vyāpaka an upalabdhyoḥ tu vakṣyamāṇayoḥ pratibandha dvaya siddhi upāyaḥ eva anvaya vyatireka niścaya nibandhanam sa ca kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ upadarśitaḥ eva iti pṛthak na uktaḥ tathā hi kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ abhāvaḥ kārya vyāpya abhāvābhyām avaśyam anvitaḥ kārya vyāpya abhāva vyatireke ca tad bhāva lakṣaṇe avaśyam vyatiricyate kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ bhāvāt anyathā kārya vyāpyayoḥ ahetuka tva niḥsvabhāvatā prasaṅgāt iti na kiñcid pṛthak abhidhānena iti 
HBṬ_1.36.1	 tat etau atā granthena pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ iti vyākhyātam adhunā tridhā eva saḥ iti etat vyākhyātum āha etad lakṣaṇaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ san yaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ iti etad lakṣaṇam yasya saḥ etad lakṣaṇaḥ tridhā eva saḥ saḥ iti etasya vyākhyānam hetuḥ iti  tridhā eva iti asya vivaraṇam tri prakāraḥ eva iti tān hetūn svena svena nāmnā kīrttayati svabhāvaḥ kāryam anupalabdhiḥ ca iti cakāraḥ hetu tva samuccaya arthaḥ iti śabdaḥ samāptim sūcayan avadhāraṇa artham eva sphuṭayati yathā anitye kasmiṃścid śabda ādau sādhye sattvam iti svabhāva hetu upadarśanam agnimati pradeśe sādhye dhūmaḥ iti kārya hetoḥ pradarśanam abhāve ca abhāvasya vyavahāre ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ iti anupalabdheḥ upanyāsaḥ 
HBṬ_1.37.1	 kasmāt punar trividhaḥ eva hetuḥ iti āśaṅkya trividha hetu vyatiriktānām arthānām hetvābhāsa tayā hetu viruddhayā vyāpteḥ triṣu eva hetu tvam niyatam bhavati iti hetvābhāsa tām pramāṇavatīm tad vyatirekiṇām darśayan āha atra eva svabhāva kāryā anupalabdhi ākhye trividha hetau avinā abhāvasya niyamāt iti trividha hetu vyatirikteśu artheṣu avinā abhāvāḥ abhāvāt iti arthaḥ tatas ca avinā abhāva vikala tvāt svabhāva kāryānupalabdhi vyatirekiṇaḥ arthāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ prameya tva ādi vat iti uktam bhavati avinā abhāva abhāvaḥ ca trividha hetu vyatirikta tvāt eva tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ avinā abhāva vyāpikayoḥ abhāvāt vyāpaka anupalabdhitaḥ avagataḥ 
HBṬ_1.38.1	 atha kaḥ ayam avinābhāvaḥ kasya ca asau katham vā atra eva niyataḥ ucyate iti atas āha yathā ukta avyāptiḥ vyāpakasya tad kāraṇa tayā tad bhāva tayā ca yatra tat vyāpyam kāryam svabhāvaḥ vā sannihitaḥ tatra bhāvaḥ eva vyāpyasya vā kāryasya svabhāvasya vā yatra tad kāraṇa svabhāva ākhyam vyāpakam sannihitam tatra eva dharmiṇi na tad abhāve api bhāvaḥ iti yā vyāpaka vyāpya dharma tayā vyāptiḥ uktā sā yathā ukta avyāptiḥ avinābhāvaḥ kasya  pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmi dharmasya saḥ evam rūpaḥ avinābhāvaḥ trividhāt yathā uktāt hetoḥ anyatra tad vyatirekiṇī arthe na asti yatas atra ca trividhe asti tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ avinā abhāvena vyāptayoḥ bhāvāt kṛtaka tva anitya tva vadanayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvāt iti tasmāt atra eva trividhe hetau tad anyatra abhāva mukhena niyataḥ ucyate tat anena hetvābhāsāḥ tatas aparaḥ iti asya avinā abhauva niyamāt iti upapatti sahitasya arthāḥ 
HBṬ_1.38.2–1.38.3	 pradarśitaḥ yathā ca trividhāt hetoḥ anyatra avinābhāvaḥ na asti tathā prāk eva uktam yadi vā svabhāvāt anyaḥ arthaḥ artha antaram tat ca kāryāt api anyat kāraṇam anubhayam vā anupalabdheḥ api anyat yathā uktāyāḥ anupalabdhi mātram upalabdhiḥ vā pratiṣedhyasya tad anyasya api viruddhasya aviruddhasya vā tatra artha antaram yadi anantara kāryam tasya arvāt garśibhiḥ itara vivekena lakṣayitum aśakya tvāt aliṅga tvam kārya darśanāt viveka avasāye api sādhya siddhi uttara kāla bhāvī pakṣa dharmatāvasāyaḥ anvaya anugamanam ca vyartham vyavahita kāryam api kāraṇam na kāryasya liṅgam antarāla pratibandha vaikalya sambhavena vyabhicārāt tat uktam 
HBṬ_1.38.4–1.38.7	 sāmagrī phala śaktīnām pariṇāma anubandhini anaikāntika tā kārye pratibandhasya sambhavāt iti yogyatā anumāne tu na artha antaram liṅgam na api anubhayam apratibandhena gamakatva ayogāt katham kṛttikā udaya vijñānāt rohiṇī āsattiklṛptiḥ iti ced nanu sā api na eva asati pratibandhe yuktāḥ viśeṣa abhāvena sarvatas sarva pratīti prasaṅgāt iti ukta tvāt tasmāt nakṣatra cakrasya saṅkrānti hetuḥ eva kāla vyavadhānena kaścid kalpayitavyaḥ yathā bhūta saṃakṣobhaḥ paścāt kāla bhāvinaḥ varṣasya iti hetu dharma anumānena kārya liṅga jā eva kalpayitavyā 
HBṬ_1.38.8	 anupalabdhi mātram api sāmśaya hetuḥ pramāṇa nivṛttau api artha abhāva asiddheḥ upalabdhiḥ api pratiṣedhyasya katham abhāvam sādhayet  abhrānta upalambhasya abhāva ayogāt viruddha upalabdhiḥ tu pratiyogi abhāvam sādhayati kintu sa virodhaḥ tad bhāve sati anya anupalambhāt eva siddhaḥ iti tad dvāreṇa anupalabdhiḥ eva prayuktā bhavati anyathā aniṣiddha upalabdheḥ abhāva asiddheḥ aviruddha upalabdhiḥ punar pratiṣedhe anaikāntikī sahabhāva sambhavāt aviruddhānām na ca aparaḥ prakāraḥ sambhavati iti nāvinā abhāvaḥ anyatra vidyate iti 
HBṬ_2.1.1–2.1.2	 idānīm svabhāva hetoḥ tāvat lakṣaṇam āha tatra hetu traye svabhāva hetoḥ tāvat lakṣaṇam ucyate sādhyate yena tat sādhanam tat ca asau dharmaḥ ca tasya bhāvaḥ tad bhāvaḥ saḥ eva sādhana dharma bhāva mātram tasya anvayaḥ sa yasya asti sādhya dharmasya avayave samudāya upacārāt tasmin svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ sādhya dharmasya śruta tvāt tasya eva svabhāvaḥ iti gamyate katham punar asau sādhya dharma svabhāvaḥ yāvatā bhedena pratīyate iti atas āha aparasmāt aparasmāt ca asataḥ akṣaṇikāt ca yā vyāvṛttiḥ tasyāḥ yaḥ bhedaḥ avadhi bheda upakalpitaḥ tena hetu bhūtena sādhya dharmāt sādhana dharmasya yaḥ bhedaḥ tasmin sati api vastutas paramārthataḥ liṅga svabhāvaḥ eva sādhya dharma svabhāvaḥ eva tathā hi yaḥ eva asataḥ vyāvṛttaḥ saḥ eva akṣaṇikāt api tatas ekasmāt dharmiṇaḥ bheda abhāvāt sādhya sādhana dharmau api paramārthataḥ na eva bhidyeta iti 
HBṬ_2.2.1	 yadi vastutas liṅgi svabhāvaḥ eva sādhana dharmaḥ tat kasmāt sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anvayini iti sādhya dharmaḥ viśeṣyate  yaḥ hi yasya svabhāvaḥ sa katham tanmātra anvayī na syāt  nīrūpa tva prasaṅgāt atad svabhāva tā vā iti atas āha hetuḥ svabhāvaḥ yasya sādhya dharmasya tasmin hetu svabhāve sādhya dharme sati anvaya vyabhicāra abhāvāt sādhana dharma bhāva mātrasya yaḥ anvayaḥ tasya vyabhicāra abhāvāt sambhave vyabhicāre ca viśeṣaṇam yuktam atra tu sambhavaḥ eva na vyabhicāraḥ iti viśeṣaṇam ayuktam eva tathā api svabhāva hetu lakṣaṇe kriyamāṇe yat etat sādhya dharmasya tanmātra anvayena sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anugamanena viśeṣaṇam tat parama tāpekṣam naiyāyika ādīnām vipratipatteḥ tad mata apekṣam na tu sva mata apekṣam 
HBṬ_2.2.2–2.2.3	 tām eva para vipratipattim darśayan āha pare hi naiyāyika ādayaḥ artha antara nimittam janakāt arthāt anyaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ vegavat dravya yoga ādiḥ tad nimittam te hi evam āhuḥ vegavat dravya yogāt avayaveṣu karmāṇi utpadyante tebhyaḥ avayava vibhāgaḥ tatas tad saṃyoga vināśaḥ tadā ārabdham kārya dravyam api naśyati iti evam artha antaram nimittam tatas eva artha antara nimittam apekṣamāṇam kṛtaka tva ādi bhāve api abhāvāt atadbhāva mātra anvayinam tasya kṛtaka tva ādeḥ bhāvaḥ sattā sā eva tanmātram tasya anvayaḥ sa yasya asti sādhya dharmasya anitya tva lakṣaṇasya tad viparītam api kṛtaka tva ādeḥ svabhāvam icchanti yatas tatas viśeṣaṇam kṛtam tena ca viśeṣaṇena tathāvidhasya artha antara nimittasya vināśasya ātad svabhāva tām āha lakṣaṇe viśeṣaṇa kāraḥ sva sattā mātra bhāvini eva svabhāva tvam na anyatra iti viśeṣaṇena sūcanāt 
HBṬ_2.3.1–2.3.2	 tathā tasmin artha antara nimitte sādhye hetoḥ kṛtaka tva ādeḥ vyabhicāram anaikāntika tām ca āha atra udāharaṇam yathā hetumati vināśe sādhye kṛtakatva asya hetoḥ atad svabhāva tā vyabhicāraḥ ca iti nanu ca kṛtaka tva svabhāva tā anitya tāyāḥ bheda upagamāt na iṣṭā eva paraiḥ tat kim ucyate atadbhāva mātra anvayinam api svabhāvam icchanti iti  evam manyate vyatiriktau api kṛtaka tva anitya tva ākhyau dharmau abhyupagacchadbhiḥ avaśyam abhūtvā bhavanam bhūtvā ca abhavanam anavasthāyi svabhāva tvam abhyupagantavyam anyathā aatma ādiṣu api kṛtaka tva anitya tve viśeṣa abhāvāt bhavetām tatas yat eva abhūtvā bhavanam bhūtvā abhavanam ca anavasthāyi tvam upādīyate bhāvasya tayoḥ eva tad darśana bala utpanna kṛtaka tva anitya tva bheda avabhāsi kalpanā dvāreṇa sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ astu kim vyatirikta dharma kalpanayā  kalpayitvā api vastu ātmanaḥ eva artha kriyā nibandhana tayā tad arthibhiḥ cintya tvāt tat uktam sat asat pakṣa bhedena śabda arthānapavādibhiḥ 
HBṬ_2.3.3–2.3.6	 vastu eva cintyate hi atra pratibaddhaḥ phala udayaḥ artha kriyā asamarthasya vicāraiḥ kiṃtad arthinām  ṣaṇḍhasya rūpa vairūype kāminyāḥ kiṃparīkṣayā  iti tasmāt dṛṣṭāḥ api bhāvāḥ kenacid ātmanā tad anya vyāvṛttena kathañcid niścitāḥ tad anyena api atad rūpa vyāvṛttena ātmanā bhrānti kāraṇa sadbhāvāt aniścīyamānāḥ niścitā niścitayaḥ rūpayoḥ pramāṇa antarataḥ pratibandha avasāya puras varttinaḥ anumānataḥ niścīyaṃte iti anitya tā svabhāva bhūtasya eva kṛtaka tvasya vināśam prati liṅgatā yuktāḥ tathā ca vināśa svabhāvaḥ eva kṛtaka tva ākhyaḥ hetuḥ taiḥ atha ukta nyāya ādiṣṭaḥ bhavati tasyāḥ atanmātra anvayitve artha antara nimitta tayā viśeṣaṇena atad svabhāva tā kathyate 
HBṬ_2.3.7	 syāt matam kṛtaka tvena sākṣāt hetumān vināśaḥ anumīyate tatas prāk pradhvaṃsa abhāva viśeṣaṇā sattā tad samavāyaḥ vā anitya tā vyavasthāpyate atas eva ātma ādiṣu anitya tā prasaṅga abhāvaḥ vināśaḥ iti ca bhāva abhāvam pradhvaṃsa lakṣaṇam manyāmahe kṛtaka tvam tu sva kāraṇa sattā samavāyam tasya viśeṣaṇena vināśa asvabhāvatā khyāpane na kiñcid aniṣṭam iti 
HBṬ_2.3.8	 tat ayuktam tathāvidhasya vināśasya hetumattā virodhāt svayam eva ca etat ācāryaḥ vakṣyati na ca tena anumitena kiñcid tasya artha kriyā sāmarthya vikala tvāt sukha duḥkha sādhane jñātvā yathārham pratipitsavaḥ hi kiñcid parīkṣante na vyasani tayā tasmāt anena asthira svabhāva tā eva bhāvasya anumātavyā sā eva ca hetumatī kalpanīyāḥ anyathā bhāva vilakṣaṇasya pradhvaṃsa abhāvasya mudgara ādeḥ udaye api tasya bhāve anupayogāt sa bhavaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti katham tad viśeṣaṇā sattā tad samavāyaḥ vā anitya tā syāt  avicalita rūpasya ca bhāvasya mudgara ādi kṛta pradhvaṃsa abhāva viśeṣaṇau sattā samavāyau yadi anitya tā kim na ātma ādeḥ api iti prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva sva kāraṇa samavāyaḥ api ca abhūtvā bhavanam anicchataḥ na sidhyati abhūtvā bhavataḥ eva ca yā sattā sā eva kṛtaka tvam varṇyate na ca sattā samavāyayoḥ nitya tayā upagatayoḥ niratiśaya tvāt prāk pradhvaṃsa abhāvau viśeṣaṇam yujyate abhūtvā 
HBṬ_2.3.9	 bhavana upagame ca tat eva kṛtaka tvam asthira svabhāva tā ca vināśaḥ astu kim niṣphalayā apramāṇikayā pramāṇa bādhitayā artha antara kalpanayā  evam kṛtaka tva vināśayoḥ tādātmya upagamaḥ avaśyam bhāvī pareṣām api tatas vināśasya āsthāyitva lakṣaṇasya artha antara nimittatā upagame kṛtaka tvasya atad svabhāva tā viśeṣaṇena khyāpyate tad niṣpattau aniṣpannasya bhinna hetukasya ca tad svabhāva tva ayogāt 
HBṬ_2.3.10–2.3.11	 tathā tasmin sādhye kṛtaka tvasya vyabhicāraḥ tathā hi ye yatra hetu antara apekṣiṇaḥ na te tatra avaśyam bhāvinaḥ yathā vāsasi rāgaḥ hetu antara apekṣī ca kṛtakeṣu api bhāveṣu pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ iti viruddha vyāpta upalabdhiḥ nanu vāsasi rāgasya parimita hetu tvāt tasya ca sva kāraṇa āyatta sannidhāna tvāt tad āśrayasya ca vidhura pratyaya upanipātena asthira tayā na avaśyam bhāvitāḥ yuktā eva na punar vināśasya tad hetūnām ānantyāt avaśyam kasyacid ghaṭa ādiṣu sannidheḥ na ca vināśasya āśrayam prāk tad hetu sannidheḥ kecid upaghnanti yatas tad abhāvāt vināśaḥ na ārabhyeta iti 
HBṬ_2.3.12	 tat ayuktam yatas yadi api bahulam vināśa kāraṇāni santi tathā api teṣām sva kāraṇa āyatta sannidhi tvāt tathā tad kāraṇānām ca sannihitānām api virodhinām api ānantyāt tad bhāve tad śakti pratibandhāt na avaśyam hetavaḥ phalavantaḥ iti kaścid na vinaśyet api iti vyabhicāraḥ na nivartate nanu ayam vāsasi rāgaḥ sa apekṣaḥ api yadi sarvatra upalabhyeta tatas kim avaśyambhāvī na syāt  syāt yadi tathā upalambhyeta sa tu anyathā api gṛhyate yadi evam na tarhi sarvatra upalabdhasya vināśasya anyathā bhāva śaṅkayā manasi khedaḥ ādhātavyaḥ kim vā punarbhavān samasta vastu vistara vyāpi jñāna ālokaḥ  yena evam vadati tathā abhāve vā katham anumāna vṛttiḥ dṛṣṭe na vaiphalyam aśnuvīta  kasyacid tu hetu kṛta vināśa darśane api hetu āyatta janmanām anyathā api darśanāt upajāta āśaṅkaḥ deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭeṣu katham tathā abhāvam niścinvīta  kṛtakam api ca ayam 
HBṬ_2.3.13–2.3.16	 bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇam vināśam nityam upaiti tad vināśa upagame bhāvasya unmajjana prasaṅgāt na ca asya ghaṭa ādeḥ iva vināśa hetuḥ upalabhyate kaścid iti tat uktam ghata ādiṣu yathā dṛṣṭa ahetavaḥ dhvaṃsa kāriṇaḥ na evaṃnāśasya saḥ ahetuḥ tasya saṃjāyate katham  iti tatas kṛtaka tvasya vināśe sādhye tena eva vyabhicāraḥ kim na iṣyate  
HBṬ_2.3.17	 bhāvānām ayam aikāntikaḥ eva dharmaḥ iti ced kutas punar etat vasitam  teṣām anyathā bhāvasya anupalambhāt iti ced nanu ayam anupalambhaḥ bhavan api ātma ādeḥ anivarttakaḥ sattāyāḥ katham anyatra anyathā bhāvam nivarttayati  tasya anumānena upalambhāt iti yadi ucyate tadā tatra api anumāne vipakṣe vṛttim anupalambhaḥ eva hetoḥ katham nivarttayati iti yat kiñcid etat tasmāt sādhu uktam hetumati vināśe kṛtaka tvasya asvabhāva tām vyabhicāram ca āha iti alam ati jalpitena iti 
HBṬ_2.4.1	 idānīm yadi api sva artha anumānam prakṛtam tathā api kaścid prayoga darśana abhyāsāt prayoga bhaṅgya eva pratipadyate iti sva artha anumāne api tad sambhavāt prasaṅgena para artha anumānam ca vyutpādayitum āha tasya svabhāva hetoḥ dvidhā trailakṣaṇya pratipādakaḥ vacana udāhāraḥ prayogaḥ tam eva darśayati samānaḥ dharmaḥ yasya tasya bhāvaḥ tena sādharmyeṇa ekaḥ prayogaḥ aparaḥ visadṛśaḥ dharmaḥ yasya tasya bhāvaḥ tena vaidharmyeṇa 
HBṬ_2.4.2–2.4.3	 yathākrama m anayoḥ udāharaṇam āha yathāyat sat yat yat sat iti vīpsā pradhānaḥ yat śabdaḥ tat sarvam iti tad śabdaḥ api vīpsā pradhānaḥ eva atra sarva grahaṇena ca aśeṣa parigrahāt bahis vyāpteḥ nirāsaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādayaḥ iti yasya sattva kṣaṇika tvayoḥ pratibandha prasādhakam pramāṇam ghaṭa ādau pravṛttam tam prati tatra smṛti samādhāna artham dṛṣṭānta vacanam na sādhya siddhi artham dṛṣṭānta mātrataḥ sādhya siddheḥ abhāvāt na hi ekasya tathā bhāve sarvaḥ tathā bhavati atiprasaṅgāt san= ca śabdaḥ iti pakṣa dharma upasaṃhāraḥ vaidharmya prayogasya udāharaṇam tathā ityādi tathā śabdaḥ samuccaye vaidharmyeṇa ca prayogaḥ udāhriyate atra api sarva grahaṇam vibhakti vipariṇāmena sambandhanīyam kṣaṇika tva abhāve sarvasmin sattva abhāvaḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.4.4^1	 prayoga dvaye api sarva grahaṇasya phalam darśayan āha sarvasmin sādhana dharmavati dharmiṇi na dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇī eva sādhya dharmasya upasaṃhāraṇam upasaṃhāraḥ ḍhaukanam tena yā vyāptiḥ vyāpakasya tatra bhāvaḥ eva ityādi rūpā tasyāḥ pradarśanam pratipādanam tat eva lakṣaṇam yayoḥ tau tathā uktau tatas ca ye sādhya dharmiṇam parihṛtya bahis vyāptim pradarśayanti te yadi api dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sādhya dharmeṇa sādhana dharmaḥ vyāptaḥ tāvatā asya sarvatra tathā abhāva abhāvāt sādhya siddhiḥ ayuktā iti nirastāḥ bhavanti sarvatra vā sādhya dharmeṇa sādhana dharmasya vyāptiḥ tad bhāve sā tathāvidhā eva kid na pradarśyate yena asamarthā bahis vyāptiḥ ākhyāyate  
HBṬ_2.4.4^2	 na hi sa śyāmaḥ tad putra tvāt paridṛśyamāna putra vat iti tad putra tvasya śyama tvena sādhyāt bahis paridṛśyamāna putre vyāpti pradarśane api sādhya siddhiḥ bhavati tasmāt yā eva sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyāptiḥ pramāṇa siddha pratibandha nibandhanā sādhya siddhau samarthā sā eva tad smṛtaye pradarśanīyāḥ na ca sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyāpti pradarśane api dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī api tadā eva pratīyate yatas pakṣa dharma upadarśana uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ anumānasya smṛti tvam syāt tasyāḥ sādhya dharmiṇi sādhya dharmāvinābhūta sādhana dharma pratīti nibandhana tvena tad upadarśanāt prāk asambhavāt tad pūrvikāyām ca vyāptau anantaram viśeṣa viṣayam anumānam katham smṛtiḥ syāt iti 
HBṬ_2.5.1–2.5.2	 nanu ca sādharmya prayogasya vyāpti pradarśana lakṣaṇa tvam yuktam sādhana dharme sati sādhya dharmasya avaśyam bhāvita apradarśanāt vaidharmya prayogasya tu katham  tatra hi kevalam sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ kathyate na tu hetau sati sādhyasya bhāvaḥ eva iti na eṣa doṣaḥ na hi atra sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ darśyate tasya hetu rūpa tā virodhāt vastu dharmaḥ hi sattva ādikaḥ hetuḥ tasya ātmanaḥ eva abhāvaḥ katham hetu svarūpam bhaviṣyati yatas tri rūpaḥ hetuḥ bhavet kintu nivṛttau nivṛtti dharmaka tvam svagataḥ dharmaḥ upadarśyate vaidharmya prayogeṇa tathāvidhe ca sādhana dharme avaśyam tayā sādhya dharmasya bhāvaḥ pratīyate eva anyathā tad nivṛttau nivṛtti dharmaka tvasya eva ayogāt iti na vyāpti pradarśana lakṣaṇa tvam vaidharmya prayogasya na yujyate 
HBṬ_2.6.1	 nanu dvividhe api prayoge pratijñā prayogaḥ na upadarśitaḥ tat katham tad artha avagatiḥ  tad artha pratyāyanāya ca sādhana prayogaḥ abhimataḥ iti atas āha atra anayoḥ prayogayoḥ pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātra sāmarthyāt eva vakṣyamāṇakāt pratijñā arthasya dharma dharmi samudāya lakṣaṇasya sādhyasya pratīteḥ hetoḥ na pratijñāyāḥ prayogaḥ upadarśitaḥ paraḥ sāmarthyam anavabudyamānaḥ āha apradarśite vacanena prameye sādhye katham na kathañcid tad pratītiḥ pratijñā artha pratītiḥ iti evam ced yadi manyase tadā sva artha anumāna kāle svayam param pratipādakam antareṇa pratipattau prameyasya kaḥ upadarśayitā na eva kaścid svayam eva tu sādhyāvinābhūta sādhana dharma darśanāt prameyam pratipadyate tathā para artha anumāne api tatas eva tad pratītiḥ astu kim pratijñā vacanena  
HBṬ_2.6.2	 yadi svayam pratipatti kāle na kaścid prameyasya upadarśayitā katham tarhi tad pratipattiḥ iti atas āha pradeśa stham sādhya dharmiṇi sthitam dhūmam sādhana dharmam upalabdhavataḥ pratyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭavataḥ sataḥ tasya dhūmasya agninā sādhya dharmeṇa pramāṇataḥ pratibandha niścaya balāt prāk pratipannāyāḥ vyāpteḥ avinā abhāvasya smaraṇe sati tad sāmarthyāt eva pakṣa dharma grahaṇa vyāpti grahaṇa sāmarthyāt eva pratijñā prayoga rahitāt agniḥ atra iti evaṃrūpā pratijñā artha pratītiḥ bhavati 
HBṬ_2.6.3	 syāt matam tatra api asya karṇa piśācikā ādiḥ prameyam kathayati eva iti atas āha na ca na eva tatra sva artha anumāna kāle kaścid karṇa piśācika ādiḥ adṛśyaḥ agniḥ atra iti evam asmai pratipattre prameyam nivedayati kathayati yadi bhavān satya vādī na evam vaktum arhati tathā hi vayam api pradeśa stha dhūma darśanāt tasya agninā vyāpti smaraṇa sāpekṣāt agnim pratipadyāmahe na ca asmabhyam kaścid nivedayati agniḥ atra iti bhavati ca tad pratipattiḥ tathā tad anyasya api sā yukta rūpā eva iti 
HBṬ_2.6.4	 yadi api na kaścid nivedayati tathā api svayam eva prameyam vyavasthāpya tad pratipattaye liṅgam anusariṣyati iti ced āha na api na kevalam na kaścid nivedyati svayam api prāk eva liṅga vyāpārāt na pratipadyate kiñcid agni ādikam kasmāt iti ced pramāṇam hetum antareṇa vinā agniḥ atra iti evam pratīteḥ nimitta abhāvāt trirūpaḥ hi hetuḥ parokṣa artha pratīteḥ nimittam tad abhāve sā katham bhavet  atha liṅgam antareṇa api evam pratītiḥ bhavati iti brūyāt tadā pratīta aviṣyamāṇāyām liṅgasya vaiyarthyam tasya anumeya pratipatti artha tvāt tena vinā tad pratipattau katham asya niṣprayojana tā na syāt  
HBṬ_2.6.5	 atyanta mūḍha tām ca parasya darśayan āha svayam eva svatantraḥ eva agniḥ atra iti vyavasthāpya katham svatantraḥ vyavasthapayati  akasmāt pramāṇam antareṇa vyavasthāpanāt tad pratipattaye nird nimitta vyavasthāpita prameya pratipatti artham paścāt liṅgam tad nimittam anusarati iti kaḥ ayaṃpratipatteḥ kramaḥ paripāṭiḥ  tathā hi prathamam liṅga anusaraṇam tatas sādhya pratipattiḥ iti vipaścitām kramaḥ ayam tu apūrvaḥ anumātā yaḥ tad viparyayam āśrayate iti upahasati yat tat loke gīyate śiraḥ muṇḍayitvā nakṣatram pṛcchati iti tad tulya tvāt asya kramasya tasmāt pakṣa dharma grahaṇa vyāpti smaraṇa sāmarthyāt eva svayam pratipadyate tat ca pratipādakam kathitam eva iti na kiñcid prameya nirddeśena 
HBṬ_2.6.6	 yadi nāma sva artha anumāna kāle svayam eva sādhyam pratipadyate tat yuktam eva liṅgasya api tatra svayam eva pratipatteḥ para artha anumāne tu paratas yathā liṅgam pratyeti tathā prameyam api paratas eva pratyetavyam atas yuktaḥ eva pratijñā prayogaḥ iti atas āha pareṇa api na kevalam svayam eva prāk vyavasthāpyamānam plavate pareṇa api vādinā tat prameyam ucyam ānaṃplavate eva tad vacanasya sandigdha artha abhidhāyaka tayā sādhya niścaya anaṅga tvāt prameya gāmbhīryān avagāhinaḥ paramparayā api atad sambaddhasya vivakṣā mātra nibandhana tayā upari eva avasthāpanāt kasmāt plavate iti ced upayoga abhāvāt na asya sādhya pratītim prati kaścid upayogaḥ tad pratyāyana samarthasya anabhidhānāt iti yāvat 
HBṬ_2.6.7	 paraḥ tu upayoga mātram kadācid brūyāt iti āśaṅkya āha viṣaya upadarśanam hetoḥ yaḥ viṣayaḥ sādhyam tad upadarśanam pratijñā vacanasya upayogaḥ ced matam atra āha tena eva viṣayeṇa tāvat śabdaḥ krame viṣayasya upadarśyamānasya arthavat tāyām tad upadarśanam pratijñā vacanasya prayojanam bhavet viṣayeṇa eva tu darśyamānena kaḥ arthaḥ kim prayojanam  
HBṬ_2.6.8	 nanu sādhya pratītiḥ sādharmya vat prayoga ādi pratītiḥ ca viṣaya upadarśanasya arthaḥ tatas tad upadarśanam pratijñā vacanasya prayojanam tathā hi asati sādhya nirdeśe yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti ukte kim ayam sādharmyavān prayogaḥ uta vaidharmyavān iti na jñāyeta ubhayam hi atra aśaṅkhyate kṛtaka tvena anitya tve sādhye sādharmyavān nitya tvena akṛtaka tve vā vaidharmyavān iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ akṛtakaḥ vā iti tu pratijñā vacane sati ubhayam asandigdham avagamyate hetu viruddha anaikāntika pratītiḥ ca na syāt pratijñā pūrvake tu prayoge anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti hetu bhāvaḥ pratīyate nityaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti viruddha tā prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti anaikāntika tvam hetoḥ ca trairūpyam na gamyate tasya sādhya apekṣayā vyavasthānāt sati pratijñā vacane avayave samudāya upacārāt sādhya dharmī pakṣaḥ iti tatra vṛttasya kṛtaka tvasya pakṣa dharma tvam sādhya dharma sāmānyena 
HBṬ_2.6.9	 ca samānaḥ arthaḥ sa pakṣaḥ iti tatra varttamānasya sa pakṣe sattvam na sa pakṣaḥ asapakṣaḥ iti sādhya dharma virahiṇī avṛttasya āsa pakṣe api asattvam pratīyeta iti āśaṅkya āha yadi pratītiḥ sādhyasya niścaya lakṣaṇā sādharmya vat prayoga ādeḥ ca svarūpa avadhāraṇa ātmikā anyathā pratijñā vacanam antareṇa na syāt tadā yat uktam sādhya siddhi artham sādharmya vat prayoga ādi jñāna artham ca viṣaya upadarśanam iti tat sarvaṃśobheta yāvatā sva artha anumāna kāle pratijñā vacanam antareṇa api pakṣa dharma grahaṇa sambandha smaraṇataḥ sādhya siddhi lakṣaṇā bhavati eva pratītiḥ iti ākhyātam eva tadvat para arthe api anumāne bhaviṣyati yatas evam tasmāt eṣa pratijñā prayoga vādī yadā svayam sādhyam pratyeti tadā svayam sādhyasya pratītau viṣayaḥ upasthāpyate yena pratijñā vacana dvāreṇa puṃsā kenacid tena vinā api 
HBṬ_2.6.10	 pratiyan sādhyam niścinvan liṅga sāmarthyāt eva yadā asmābhiḥ pratipādyate tadā asmān kāryiṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā avyaktam pratijñā prayoga lakṣaṇam mūlyaṃmṛgayate kaḥ iva parva brāhmaṇaḥ iva yathā dakṣiṇām antareṇa api anyadā aurdvarathikaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ bhuñjānaḥ anyadā śrāddha ādi parvaṇi arthinam śraddhālum bravīti yadi me ghṛtapūram ghṛtapūram prati rūpakam dadāsi tatas aham bhuñje na anyathā iti tena tulyaḥ bhavān api iti 
HBṬ_2.6.11	 kiñca yat api bravīṣi para artha anumāna kāle yathā liṅgam pareṇa anabhidhīyamānam na pratyeti pratipādyaḥ tathā sādhyam api iti tadā etat yujyate yadi asau vādi vacana mātreṇa liṅgam api niścitya tad anusāreṇa sādhyam avagacchet para prati iti arthinaḥ ca tadā vayam api pratijñām kid na prayuñjmahe liṅga vacana rahitām  asmad vacanasya eva tam prati pramāṇa tayā tatas eva anumeya pratīteḥ tad vacanasya caritārtha tvāt na ca etat asti yatas asmad vacanāt api na kevalam sva artha anumāna kāle asmad vacanam antareṇa iti api śabdaḥ kintu yadā api asmad vacanam pravṛttam tadā api na eva asmad vacanāt liṅgam api pratyeti kutas eva sādhya siddhaye anusariṣyati  api tu svayam asya yadi tat liṅgam kutaścid pramāṇataḥ siddham bhavati asmad vacanena tu kevalam tatra smṛti samādhāna m ātra kriyate tadā svayam siddham eva liṅgam anusṛtya sādhyam pratyeti na asmad vacanāt 
HBṬ_2.6.12	 pānīyam api pibati iti tasmāt kaḥ anayoḥ pratijñā vacanā vacana ātmikayoḥ avasthayoḥ viśeṣaḥ  ubhayatra svayaṃsiddha liṅga sāmarthyāt eva sādhya pratīteḥ na kaścid tatas sva para artha anumānayoḥ svayaṃsiddha liṅga anusaraṇam tatas sādhya pratītim ca prati viśeṣa abhāvāt pratijñopanyāsaḥ para artha anumāne api vyarthaḥ eva liṅgam api hi tāvat atra na abhidhīyate yadi tat pūrva prasiddham svayam anusmaret kim aṅgaḥ sandigdha artha abhidhāyakam pratijñā vacanam upādīyate  
HBṬ_2.6.13	 syāt matam yadi nāma sādhya siddhau pratijñā vacanasya na upayogaḥ tad arthaḥ asya prayogaḥ mā bhūt sādharmya vat prayoga ādi jñāna artham tu tad upādānam avasthitam eva tasya anyathā prati iti abhāvāt iti atas āha dṛṣṭāca sādharmya vat prayoga ādeḥ pratijñā vacanam antareṇa api pratītiḥ tatas tad arthaḥ api pratijñā upanyāsaḥ na śobhate 
HBṬ_2.6.14	 kutas punar sādharmya vat prayoga ādeḥ asati sādhya nirdeśe pratītiḥ iti āha pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātrāt iti evam manyate na eva hi kaścid yat kṛtakam tat anityam etāvat mātram abhidhāyā aaste sādhana nyūna tayā eva asya parājayāt kintu avaśyam hetoḥ ddharmiṇī upasaṃhāram karoti iti tatra yadi kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti brūyāt tadā sādharmya vat prayoga pratītiḥ atha nityaḥ ca iti abhidadhyāt tadā vaidharmyavataḥ iti sambandha vacana pūrvakāt pakṣa dharma vacanāt prayoga dvaya avagatiḥ 
HBṬ_2.6.15	 hetu viruddha anaikāntikāḥ api pakṣa dharma vacana mātreṇa na pratīyante yadā tu sambandha vacanam api kriyate tadā katham apratītiḥ  tathā hi yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti pakṣa dharma vacane sati ukte hetuḥ avagamyate vidhīyamānena ānūdyamānasya vyāptaḥ yat kṛtakam tat nityam iti abhidhāne viruddhaḥ viparyaya vyāpteḥ yat kṛtakam tat prayatna anantarīyakam iti pradarśane vyabhicārāt anaikāntika adhyavasāyaḥ 
HBṬ_2.6.16	 trairūpyam api hetoḥ gamyate eva yatas vyāpti pradarśana kāle vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ sādhyatayā avagamyate yatra ca vyāpyaḥ dharmaḥ dharmiṇī upasaṃhriyate sa vyāpaka dharma viśiṣṭa tayā avagamyamānaḥ sādhya samudāya eka deśa tayā pakṣaḥ iti upasaṃhṛtasya vyāpya dharmasya pakṣa dharma tva avagatiḥ sā ca vyāptiḥ yatra dharmiṇī upadarśyate sa sādhya dharma sāmānyena samānaḥ arthaḥ sa pakṣaḥ pratīyate iti sa pakṣe sattvam avagamyate sāmarthyāt ca vyāpaka nivṛttau vyāpya nivṛttiḥ yatra avasīyate saḥ asapakṣaḥ iti asapakṣe api asattvam api niścīyate iti yadi pakṣa ādibhiḥ api jñātaiḥ kiñcid prayojanam na tu vyavahartaṇām pakṣa ādi saṅketa apekṣā parokṣa artha gatiḥ bhavati tathā hi yat kvacid dṛṣṭam tasya yatra pratibandhaḥ tad vidaḥ tasya tat gamakam tatra iti hi loke vastu gatiḥ bhavati na pakṣa ādi saṅketa grahaṇa apekṣā tatra yatheṣṭaṃśa astra kāra āgamaka rūpa pratipattaye sva saṅketena anyathā 
HBṬ_2.6.17	 vā lakṣaṇam praṇayantu na tu vyavahāra kāle tad anusaraṇam kvacid upayujyate tad saṅketa pratipāditam eva tu yathoktam gamakam rūpam upayogi vyavahartṛṛṇām tat ced pratipannam tāvatā eva sādhya siddhiḥ san jātāḥ iti pakṣa sa pakṣa ādi saṅketā parijñāne api na kiñcid plūyate atas eva ācārya pādaiḥ nnāntarīya kārya darśanam tad vidaḥ anumānam iti gamaka rūpa mātram eva pakṣa ādi saṅketa anapekṣam pratipāditam sva prajñāparādhāt tu tatra api kaiścid asantaḥ eva doṣāḥ prakīrtyante iti kim atra brūmaḥ  tasmāt sādharmya vat prayoga ādi jñāna artham api pratijñā vacanam pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātre eva yathā uktena prakāreṇa pratīteḥ ayuktam iti kaḥ tasya pratijñā vacanasya upayogaḥ na eva kaścid 
HBṬ_2.6.18–2.6.19^1	 svayam ca ayam vādī yena krameṇa anumeyam pratipannavāmḥ tam ullaṅghya para pratipattaye krama antaram āśrayan para vañcaka tayā dhūrttaḥ eva pratīyate na sat dhṛttaḥ iti upadarśayan āha sva niścaya vat ityādi yathā aatmanaḥ niścayasya utpādanam kṛtam tathā eva anyeśām api niścaya utpādanāya ca para hita nirataiḥ sādhanam ucyate tatra etasmin nyāye sati svayam ayam vādī prameyasya upadarśanena upadarśakena vacanena vinā api sva artha anumāna kāle pratipadya prameyam param saṃśayita ādikam pratipādayan sva pratipannam prameyam avabodhayan apūrvam sva pratipatti kāle pūrvam yaḥ prameya pratipattau kramaḥ upāyaḥ anubhūtaḥ tasmāt anyam āśrayate iti kim atra krama antara āśrayeṇa kāraṇam 
HBṬ_2.6.18–2.6.19^2	 na eva kiñcid para vyāmohanam muktvā tathā hi yadi sva pratipatti kramaḥ pratīti nibandhanam kim tad parityāgena krama antara āśrayaṇam  katham tena svayam pratipannavān asi iti  yatas evam tasmāt na prameyasya sādhyasya vacanena pratijña ākhyena kiñcid prayojanam kutas  anyathā api vinā api tena pratipatteḥ sādhya pratīteḥ utpatteḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
HBṬ_2.7.1	 evam pratijñām sādhana vākyāt apanīya aparam api upanaya nigamana ādikam para parikalpitam sādhana vākyāt apanetum uktam eva nyāyam atidiśan āha etena anyathā api pratipatteḥ utpatteḥ iti nyāyena upanaya nigamana ādikam ādi grahaṇāt saṃśaya jijñāsā ādikam pratyuktam pratyākhyātam tatra udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhāraḥ na tathā iti vā asādhyasya upanayaḥ pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanaṃnigamanam iti anayoḥ lakṣaṇam sādhya nirddeśaḥ pratijñāḥ iti tu pratijñāyāḥ etena iti etat eva darśayati etau atā eva pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātrā eva upanaya ādi rahitena sādhya pratīteḥ bhāvāt utpatteḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.7.2	 atra uddyota karaḥ prāha pratijñā tāvat viṣaya nirddeśa artham avaśya karttavyā yatas lokaḥ prathamam karma cchedya ādikam nirūpayati tatas kuṭhāra ādikam sādhanam vyāpārayati upanayena api yāvat dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭa sāmarthyaḥ hetuḥ ddharmiṇi na upasaṃhriyate tāvat kutas sādhya pratītiḥ  sva artha anumāna dṛṣṭaḥ ca pratyavamarśa pratyaya arthaḥ anena darśyate tathā hi sva artha anumāne prathamam pradeśe dhūmam paśyati tatas yatra yatra aham dhūmam adrākṣam tatra tatra agnim api iti vyāptim smarati tatas dhūmaḥ ca atra iti punar pratyavamṛśati sa pratyavamarśa arthaḥ para artha anumāne upanayena ucyate nigamanam api avaśya abhidhānīyam yatas yadi api pūrvam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti uktam na tu tāvatā asya niścayaḥ jātaḥ samprati tu pramāṇa bala āyātaḥ arthaḥ tad sampratyaya artham anena nigamyate aśeṣa pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ ca anena upasaṃhriyate tathā hi āgamaḥ pratijñā 
HBṬ_2.7.3	 hetuḥ anumānam dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratyakṣam upamānam upanayaḥ tat etasya pramāṇa catuṣṭayasya api vyāpāraḥ nigamanena upasaṃhriyate iti katham asya na sāphalyam iti etat āśaṅkya āha ḍiṇḍikarāgaṃparityajya ḍiṇḍikāḥ nagna ācāryāḥte niṣphalam upari upari nāma lekhane prasaktāḥ tatas teṣām iva pareṇa ukte tasya upari mayā avaśyam ayukta tayā niṣphalam api abhidhānīyam iti asthāna abhiniveśam tyaktvā akṣiṇī nimīlya bahis vikṣepam upasaṃhṛtya cintaya tāvat kim iyatā pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātrakeṇa vākyena sādhyasya pratītiḥsyāt na vā iti yāvatā yāvān eva para artha anumāne arthaḥ abhidhānīyaḥ iti asmābhiḥ anujñāyate tāvān eva anyūna anatiriktaḥ sva artha anumāne api pratīti hetuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasya kaḥ iha śakteḥ vyāghāt yena asau para artha anumāne api pratītim na kuryāt bhāve pratīteḥ kiṃprapañca mālayā 
HBṬ_2.7.4	 pratijñā upanaya nigamana lakṣaṇayā bāla pratāraka tad upayoga upavarṇa lakṣaṇayā vā  tathā hi ḥ pratijñā upanaya nigamana prayoge api yadi pramāṇa niścitā svasādhya vyāptiḥ sādhana dharmasya na syāt sādhya dharmiṇi vā sadbhāvaḥ tadā asya na eva pratīti hetu tā tad sambhave tu pratijña ādi abhāve api sva artha anumānaḥ iva gamaka rūpā vaikalyāt sā na nivāryate iti kim asthāna nirbandhena iti  na hi sādhya dharma ākṣepaṇa sāmarthya virahe sādhana dharmasya vādi vacana mātrāt sādhya niścayaḥ yuktaḥ hetu upanyāsa vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt tasya tad ākṣepa sāmarthye vā pratijñā vacanasya iti 
HBṬ_2.7.5	 yat tu uktam viṣaya pradarśanāya pratijñā iti atra śāstra kṛtā eva dattam uttaram yaḥ ca sādhanam prayuṃkte tena aham anena sādhanena amuṣmin sādhye pratītim sādhayiṣyāmi iti karma nirūpya eva tat prayuktam iti na laukika nyāya atikramaḥ anyathā yadi sādhanāt yasya sādhya pratītiḥ upajāyate tena eva karma nirūpaṇīyam katham tad abhāve sva artha anumāne sādhya siddhiḥ sādhana nibandhanā syāt  yaḥ ca agni dhūmayoḥ sambandham cetasi vyavasthāpya kva agniḥ kva agniḥ iti agnim paryeṣate sa pradeśe dhūma darśana mātrāt eva agnim pratipadyate iti katham sva artha anumāne pratyavamarśa pratyayaḥ syāt  atha kadācid asau dṛṣṭaḥ tatra iti para arthe api asya upādānam tadā dadhi ādikam api bhuktvā kadācid dhūmāt agnim pratipannavān iti kid na dadhi bhojana ādeḥ api kādācid kasya upādānam  
HBṬ_2.7.6–2.7.7	 yat punaruktam āgamaḥ pratijñāḥ iti tatra yadi vādi vacanam eva āgamaḥ tadā tatas eva sādhya siddheḥ hetu ādi upādānam anarthakam atha pratijñā arthasya āgame pāṭhāt āgamaḥ pratijñā tadā na kvacid āgame paṭhyate atra pradeśe agniḥ iti katham āgama tvam pratijñāyāḥ  hetuḥ anumānam iti api ayuktam na hi pakṣa dharma tva mātram hetuḥ tasya tri rūpa tvāt dṛṣṭāntaḥ api na sarvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ iti katham dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratyakṣam bhavet  upamānam tu pramāṇam eva na bhavati katham tat vyāpāraḥ upasaṃhriyeta nigamanena  yadi ca avaśyam dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭa sāmarthyaḥ hetuḥ ddharmiṇi upaneyaḥ tadā upanayaḥ eva astu kim kṛtaka tvāj iti pakṣa dharma nirddeśena  saḥ eva dṛṣṭa sāmarthyam hetum upasaṃhariṣyati pakṣa dharma tām ca darśayiṣyati iti na kiñcid tena tatas yatra ca pratijñāyāḥ prathamatas eva prayogaḥ na iṣyate tatra tasyāḥ punarvacanam kutas nigamanam bhaviṣyati  iti āha iti tasmāt iyān eva pakṣa dharma sambhandha vacana mātra ātmakaḥ sādhana vākye prayogaḥ jyāyāt na pañca avayava ātmakaḥ iti sthitam 
HBṬ_2.8.1–2.9.1	 atra sādhana vākye na kevalam pratijña ādi prayogaḥ na yuktaḥ para upagataḥ pūrvam hetuḥ prayoktavyaḥ paścāt dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti krama niyamaḥ api na kaścid kutas sarvathā yadi pūrvam hetuḥ paścāt vyāptiḥ atha pūrvam vyāptiḥ paścāt pakṣa dharmaḥ prayujyate tathā api gamaka tvāt nanu tasya dvidhā prayogaḥ iti ayuktam uktam yatas trividhaḥ hetuḥ anvayī vyatirekī anvaya vyatirekī ceti naiyāyikāḥ tatas tasya tridhā prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām ca iti vaktavyam iti atas āha sambandha vacane api na kevalam krama niyamaḥ na yuktaḥ kintu artha bhedaḥ api na kaścid ubhayatra api trirūpa sadbhāvāt tatas sarve eva hetuḥ anvaya vyatirekī na tu anvayī vyatirekī vā kaścid dhetuḥ asti iti bhāvaḥ tat kutas traividhyam prayogasya syāt iti manyate kutas punar artha bhedaḥ na asti iti ced āha ubhayathā sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca prayoge yadi api vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tayā dharma bhedaḥ pratīyate tathā api tad bhāvasya eva sādhana dharmasya sādhya svabhāvatāyāḥ eva sādharmya vaidharmya prayogābhyām khyāpanāt 
HBṬ_2.9.2	 nanu sādharmya prayoge hetu bhāve sādhyasya bhāvaḥ vaidharmye ca sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ śabdāt avagamyate na tādātmyam tat kim ucyate tad bhāvasya eva khyāpanāt iti atas āha na hi ityādi yadi sādharmya prayoge tad bhāvaḥ na ākṣipyeta tadā sādhanasya atad svabhāvasya bhāve kim iti ekāntena avaśyan tayā sādhyasya bhāvaḥ  kādācid kaḥ tu bhavatu nāma  yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti ekānta bhāvaḥ ca hetau sati sādhyasya vyāptyā sādharmya prayoge abhidhīyate sa ca tādātmyam antareṇa anartha antarasya na sambhavati iti sāmarthyāt tadā ākṣipati 
HBṬ_2.9.3	 katham iva atad svabhāvasya bhāve na ekāntena anya bhāvaḥ iti āha kṛtaka tvā iti ādi yadi prayatna ānantarīyaka tvām antareṇa api kṛtaka tvasya bhāvāt atad svabhāva tvam anitya tve api ayam eva vṛttāntaḥ tatas ca tādātmya virahāt prayatna ānantarīyaka tvasya anitya tvena anvayaḥ na syāt tad nivṛttau vā nivṛttiḥ iti katham tatas tat pratīyate  na eṣa doṣaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka padārtha svabhāvasya eva anitya tvasya tena sādhanāt tatra ca tādātmya sadbhāvāt anvaya vyatirekau anivāritau anitya tva kṛtaka tva mātra apekṣayā tu tādātmya virahaḥ asya abhihitaḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.9.4	 nanu agni nivṛttau atad svabhāvasya api dhūmasya nivṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā anvayaḥ ca iti āha kāryasya iti anvaya vyatirekayoḥ hi pratibandhaḥ nibandhanam tena tayoḥ vyāpteḥ tad abhāve tayoḥ api abhāvāt tatra artha antarasya dhūmasya agnau tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ pratibandaḥ anvaya vyatireka nimittam asti iti bhavetām tau yatra tu anartha antarasya tau ucyete tatra avaśyam tādātmyena bhavitavyam iti abhiprāyaḥ atra udāharaṇam yathā anayoḥ eva kṛtaka tva prayatna ānantarīyaka tvayoḥ viparyayeṇa na eka nivṛttau anya nivṛttiḥ yat prayatna anantarīyakam na bhavati tat kṛtakam api na bhavati iti evaṃrūpā yatas evam tasmāt anvaya vyatirekayoḥ yathālakṣaṇam hetu bhāve sādhyasya avaśyam bhāvaḥ sādhya abhāve ca hetoḥ avaśyam abhāvaḥ iti ekaḥ api sādharmya mukheṇa vaidharmya mukheṇa vā prayuktaḥ dvitīyam ākṣipati sva vyāpaka pratibandha ākṣepāt tasya api ca itareṇa vyāpteḥ tasmāt ubhayatra trairūpya pratīteḥ 
HBṬ_2.9.5–2.9.6	 ekasya śabdataḥ aparasya arthataḥ iti sambandha vacane api prayogaḥ eva vidhi mukhena pratiṣedha mukhena vā bhidyate na arthaḥ iti siddhim tatas tasya dvidhā prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca na tu sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām api tad arthasya anyatareṇa eva prakāśanāt sarvaḥ hetuḥ anvayavyatireki eva vastutas na kaścid anvayī vyatirekī vā nāma iti etat upasaṃharan āha iti na ekatra anvaya mukhena vyatireka mukheṇa vā sādhana vākye dvayoḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ prayogaḥ sākṣāt śabdena pratipādanam iṣyate vaiyarthyāt pratīta pratyāyane prayojana abhāvāt 
HBṬ_2.9.7	 tām eva arthataḥ aparasya pratītim sphuṭayan āha tad svabhāvatayā ityādi yadi tad svabhāvatayā sādhyena hetoḥ anvayaḥ sidhyati tatas eva tad abhāve abhāvaḥ api sidhyati eva tad svabhāvasya tad abhāve svayam nairātmyena bhāva ayogāt tathā tad svabhāvatayā sādhya abhāve sādhanasya abhāva siddhau ca satyām tatas eva sādhyena hetoḥ anvayasya api siddheḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.9.8–2.9.9^1	 yaiḥ tu vyākhyāyate sādharmyavati prayoge tad abhāvaḥ eva vipakṣe hetoḥ abhāva khyātiḥ yathā syāt na anyatra vipakṣe viruddhe vā hetu abhāva prasaṅgāt viruddhataḥ eva vyavaccheda prasaṅāt ca iti niyama khyāpana arthaḥ vyatireka prayogaḥ iti sa tad arthaḥ api ayuktaḥ kutas anya viruddhayoḥ api na kevalam tad abhāvasya vipakṣa tvāt yasya hi anyaḥ eva vipakṣaḥ anya dharma yogī vā anyaḥ na vivakṣita dharmān āśrayaḥ viruddhaḥ eva vā saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇena eva virodhena na paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā api vipakṣaḥ tasya anitya tvāt anyān ātma ādi dharmavati arthe kṛtaka tva ādi vṛtteḥ hetu abhāva prasaṅgaḥ 
HBṬ_2.9.8–2.9.9^2	 auṣṇye ca sādhye agni lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ viruddhāt eva śītāt na anuṣṇa śītāt api anyatas vyavaccheda prasaṅgāt na ekāntena auṣṇyam agniḥ grasayet iti tasya ayam doṣaḥ syāt tam pratyācāryeṇa uktam yadi ekasya vipakṣa tvam iṣyate tadā tad abhāvasya eva iṣyatām na viruddhasya anyasya vā tasya anyatra api vivakṣita dharmān āśraye viruddhe ca bhāvāt tad abhāvam antareṇa tayoḥ anya viruddha tva ayogāt na tu asmākam trividham api vipakṣam icchatām vivakṣita dharmān āśrayam cā anyam iti bhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_2.10.1	 yadi svabhāva hetau anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sādhana dharmasya sādhya svabhāva tā nibandhanam iti anvayena vyatirekeṇa vā sādharmya vaidharmyavatoḥ prayogayoḥ abhidhīyamānena tādātmya ākṣepa dvāreṇa arthāt itarākṣepaḥ ucyate tadā pramāṇa siddhā eva tad svabhāva tā tayoḥ nibandhanam na śabda mātrataḥ pratīyamāna iti abhiprāyavān āha katham idam ityādi yena iti sataḥ naśvara svabhāva tvena sattva lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ kṣaṇika tva svabhāva tvena iti yāvat pṛcchataḥ ca ayam abhiprāyaḥ iha dvividhāḥ santaḥ kṛtakāḥ ca ghaṭa ādayaḥ akṛtakāḥ ca ākāśa ādayaḥ tatra ye tāvat akṛtakāḥ te sat akāraṇa vat nityam iti nitya lakṣaṇa yogāt anityāḥ eva na bhavanti kutas eva kṣaṇikāḥ iti na sattvasya kṣaṇika tva svabhāva tā ye api santaḥ kṛtakāḥ teṣām api mudgara ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyitayā vināśasya sa hetuka tvāt tad hetu asannidhau= 
HBṬ_2.10.2–2.10.5	 vināśāt kṛtaka ātmanaḥ api sattvasya kṣaṇika tva svabhāva tā na samasti eva iti na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sambhavaḥ iti avaśyam ca vināśaḥ daṇḍa ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyī dṛṣṭa tvāt tathā hi abhighāta agni saṃyoga nāśa pratyaya sannidhim vinā asaṃsarggitāṃyāti na vināśaḥ ghaṭa ādibhiḥ anyatra api ca anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam eva hetumattā vyavahāra nibandhanam abhyupeyatesaugataiḥ api tat iha api asti iti kid na tad vyavahāraḥ pravarttyate iti 
HBṬ_2.10.6	 nanu ca anvaya niścayam pratipādayatā bādhaka pramāṇa vṛtti vaśāt tad svabhāva tā pūrvam eva pratipāditāḥ anvaya niścayaḥ api svabhāva hetau ityādi vicanāt tat kutas asya pūrva pakṣasya avasaraḥ  satyam kintu pūrva ācāryaiḥ kṛtaka tvasya kṣaṇikatāyām sādhyāyām paraiḥ kṛtakānām ante a vaśyam hetu nibandhana vināśa upagamāt tad hetu ayoga pratipādanena anapekṣā vināśam prati viparyaye bādhakam pramāṇam tādātmya prasādhakam uktam tat prasaṅga mukhena kṛtaka lakṣaṇasya eva sattvasya tad ātmatām gamayati na anyasya iti darśayitum artha kriyā virodha lakṣaṇam tu sarvasya sattvasya iti vastu mātreṇa prāk uktam api vipañcayitum pūrva pakṣa upanyāsaḥ akṛtaka lakṣaṇam tu sattvam na sambhavati eva niyāmakam hetum antareṇa deśa kāla svabhāva niyama ayogāt tatas pūrva ācāryaiḥ na tasya eka aṅga vaikalyāt eva sat akāraṇa vat nityam iti nitya tā sambhava 
HBṬ_2.10.7	 iti na tad ātma tām prati yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ śāstra kāraḥ tu sāmānyena sattvasya kṣaṇika svabhāva tām kṛtaka lakṣaṇasya api ca deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭasya api vastu sthityā eva tad ātmatām artha kriyā virodhena na para upagata avaśyam bhāvi vināśasya ahetuka tayā viśeṣa abhāvāt utpanna mātrasya abhāva prasaṅgena pratipādayiṣyati 
HBṬ_2.11.1–2.11.2	 tatra pūrva ācārya uktam sarvasya sataḥ kṛtakasya avaśyam ante hetu kṛtaḥ vināśa iti yaḥ paraiḥ iṣyate tam pratyanapekṣa tvam kyāpayitum upakramate vināśa hetu ayogāt iti yadi tarhi nāśasya hetuḥ na asti sa teṣām kṛtakānām satām avaśyam bhāvī vināśaḥ kutas  na hi ākasmikaḥ kaścid svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ iti āha svabhāvataḥ eva bhavati asmāt kāryam iti bhāva śabdaḥ hetu vacanaḥ tena sva hetubhyaḥ eva naśvarāḥ naśana śīlāḥ sūcī agre sarṣapāḥ iva anavasthāyinaḥ sva ātmani bhāva ajāyante na eṣām kṛtaka lakṣaṇānām satām bhāvānām sva hetubhyaḥ niṣpannānām anyatas abhighāta ādeḥ vināśa utpattiḥ kutas tasya abhighāta agni saṃyoga ādeḥ tad hetu tayā upagatasya asāmarthyāt tathā hi agni saṃyoga ādi kāle tritayam lakṣayāmaḥ tat eva kāṣṭha ādikam vināśyam aṅgāra ādikam avasthā antaram kāṣṭha ādi nivṛtti lakṣaṇam ca abhāvam tuccha rūpam na aparam yatra agni saṃyoga ādeḥ vyāpāraḥ cintyeta etāvat 
HBṬ_2.11.3–2.11.4	 yām ca vastu gatau na kvacid atra vināśa hetoḥ sāmarthyam yujyate yatas na hi vināśa hetuḥ bhāvasya indhana ādeḥ sva hetubhyaḥ sthira rūpasya utpannasya svabhāvam eva asthiḥ ātma tā lakṣaṇam karoti kutas tasya indhana ādeḥ sva hetubhyaḥ eva nirvṛtteḥ na hi sthira ātmanaḥ nirvṛttasya anyathā bhāvaḥ tad ātmā śakyate kartum tasya hetu antarāt paścāt bhavataḥ artha antara tva prasaṅgāt tasya eva anyathā tva ayogāt tatra hetu vyāpārasya kalpayitum aśakya tvāt athavā tritaye samīkṣyamāṇe yat tāvat vināśyam kāṣṭha ādi na tad svabhāvam eva agni saṃyoga ādiḥ vināśa hetuḥ karoti tasya sva hetubhyaḥ eva nirvṛtteḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.12.1–2.12.6	 kumārilaḥ tu manyate na agni saṃyoga ādinā bhāva svabhāvaḥ eva kriyate kintu indhana ādeḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ sa ca indhana ādi rūpa vikalam aṅgāra ādikam uttaram bhāva antaram eva tat uktam na astitā payasaḥ dadhni pradhvaṃsa abhāva lakṣaṇam iti tathāvidhasya ca abhāvasya hetumat ta upagamaḥ na eva virudhyate tathā ca āha kaścid bhāva antara vinirmuktaḥ bhāvaḥ atra anupalambha vat abhāvaḥ sammataḥ tasya hetoḥ kin na samudbhavaḥ  iti 
HBṬ_2.12.7	 tat etat kaumārilam darśanam apanudan āha na api ityādi yadi uttaram kārya ātmakam bhāva antaram eva abhāvaḥ tadā agni saṃyoga ādayaḥ aṅgāra ādi janmani vyāpriyante iti iṣṭam eva asmākam kintu bhāva antara karaṇe abhyupagamyamāne agni ādīnām indhana ādau avyāpārāt tad avastham eva indhana ādikam tatas ca yathā agni saṃyogāt prāk indhana ādeḥ upalabdhiḥ anyā ca tad sādhyā artha kriyā tathā aṅgāra ādi utpattau api upalabdhi ādeḥ prasaṅgaḥ 
HBṬ_2.12.8	 nanu bhāva antarasya pradhvaṃsa abhāva rūpa tāyām tad utpattau indhana ādīnām pradhvaḥ tatvāt asatām katham tathā upalabdhi ādi prasaṅgaḥ  satyam evam manyate sarvasya indhana ādeḥ anyasya gavā ādeḥ api tathā abhāvaḥ mā bhūt iti aṅgāra ādeḥ dhvaṃsa vyavasthāyām nibandhanam abhidhānīyam tasmin sati tad nivṛttiḥ iti ced aho vacana kauśalam yatas nivṛtteḥ tuccha svabhāva tā anaṅgīkaraṇāt tat eva bhāva antaram aṅgāra ādikam nivṛttim brūṣe tat ayam arthaḥ sampannaḥ aṅgāra ādi bhāve aṅgāra ādi bhāvāt aṅgāra ādikam dhvaṃsaḥ kāṣṭha ādeḥ iti na ca aṅgāra ādi bhāve tad bhāvaḥ sva ātmani hetu bhāva ayogāt agni ādibhyaḥ ca tad utpāda vacanāt indhana ādi upamarddena aṅgāra ādi bhāvāt asya dhvaṃsa rūpa tā iti ced kaḥ ayam upamarddaḥ nāma  yadi nivṛttiḥ sā aṅgāra ādi lakṣaṇā eva iti na pūrvasmāt viśiṣyate tasmāt svarasataḥ nivarttate kāṣṭha ādiḥ 
HBṬ_2.12.9–2.12.11^1	 agni ādibhyaḥ tu aṅgāra ādi janma iti eva bhadrakam anyathā kāṣṭha ādeḥ tathā upalabdhi ādi prasaṅgaḥ katham na syāt api ca yadi bhāva antaram pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ ye ete anupajāta vikārāḥ pradīpa buddhi ādayo dhvaṃsante teṣām katarat bhāva antaram pradhvaṃsaḥ vyavasthāpyate  te api avyakta tām ātma bhāvam ca vikāram eva dhvaṃsam samālambantaḥ iti ced na pradīpa ādeḥ bhāva rūpa avyakta tā bhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt yadi hi śakti rūpa tā āpattiḥ avyakta tā tadā śakteḥ kārya darśana unnīyamāna rūpa tvāt tad abhāve katham pradīpa ādayaḥ śakti ātmanā avasthitāḥ kalperan  
HBṬ_2.12.9–2.12.11^2	 atha upalabdhi yogya tā vikala ātma tā āpattiḥ avyaktiḥ atra api tad ātmanā avasthitau na eva pramāṇam asti na ca apramāṇakam ādriyante vacaḥ vipaścitaḥ ātmanaḥ ca asattvāt katham tad bhāvaḥ buddhi ādīnām vikāraḥ pariṇāmaḥ ca  anyatra vihita pratikriya tvāt na iha pranyate iti alam prasaṅgena syāt matam bhāva antareṇa aṅgāra ādinā aavṛta tvāt indhana ādeḥ tathā upalabdhi ādayaḥ na bhavanti iti atas āha na api ityādi svabhāva antaram anyasya indhana ādeḥ āvaraṇam api na yujyeta tad avasthe avicalita rūpe tasmin indhana ādau satya āvaraṇasya api na kevalam anupalabdhi ādeḥ ayogāt 
HBṬ_2.13.1	 na kevalam bhāva svabhāvaḥ bhāva antaram vā vināśa hetunā na kriyate bhāva abhāvaḥ api na kriyate iti āha na api ityādi kutas iti ced abhāvasya vidhinā paryudāsena vivakṣitāt bhāvāt anyatayā kāryatva upagame kriyamāṇe kim indhana ādi rūpaḥ eva asau atha artha antaram iti vyatireka avyatireka vikalpa anatikramāt tatra ca uktaḥ eva doṣaḥ 
HBṬ_2.13.2–2.13.7	 nanu prasajya pratiṣedha ātmā tuccha rūpaḥ asau agni ādi janyaḥ abhyupeyate tad bhāve ca indhana ādīnām naiḥsvābhāvyāt kutas pūrva doṣa avasaraḥ  sa ca avaśyam agni ādi bhāva abhāva anuvidhāyitayā tad kāryaḥ tad bhāva vyavahārasya anyatra api tad nibandhana tvāt tat uktam san bodha gocara prāptaḥ tad bhāve na upalabhyate naśyan bhāvaḥ kathaṃtasya na nāśaḥ kārya tām iyāt prāk abhūtvā abhavan bhāvaḥ hetubhyaḥ jāyate yathā bhūtvā api na bhavan tadvat hetubhyaḥ na bhavati ayam iti 
HBṬ_2.13.8	 atas āha bhāva pratiṣedha iti ādi ayam abhiprāyaḥ yadi anapekṣita bhāva antara saṃsarggaḥ cyuti mātram eva tuccha rūpam dhvaṃsaḥ tadā tatra kāraka vyāpāraḥ na eva sambhavati bhavana dharmiṇī eva tad sambhavāt tasya api abhūtvā bhāva upagamāt kārya tā na virudhyate iti ced na bhavana dharmaṇaḥ bhāva rūpa tā prāpteḥ abhāva tu ahāneḥ yatas bhavati iti bhāvaḥ maṇyate na aparam aṅkura ādeḥ api bhāva śabda pravṛtti nimittam artha kriyā sāmarthyam iti ced sarva sāmarthya virahiṇaḥ tarhi asya katham pratīti viṣaya tā  na hi akāraṇam pratīti viṣayaḥ atiprasaṅgāt tad aviṣayasya vā katham hetumat ta avagatiḥ vastu tāḥ vā  yena ucyate tuccha rūpam eva tat vastu iti pratīti janaka tve vā katham na sāmarthya sambandhi tā  sat iti pratyayāḥ aviṣayasya katham bhāvatā iti ced kārya tā api asya katham  sva hetu bhāve bhāvāt iti ced katham tarhi sat pratyayāḥ aviṣaya tā  tathā hi yadi sva hetu bhāve bhavati iti 
HBṬ_2.13.9	 pratīyate sat ityādi pratīyeta yatas asti iti sat iti vadanti vidvāṃsaḥ na ca asti bhavati bhāvaḥ san= iti śabdānām artha bhedaḥ parama arthaḥ kaścid abhāva ātmaka tayā eva bhavati asau iti ced na vyāhata tvāt yatas na bhavati iti abhāvaḥ ucyate sa katham bhavati iti vyapadiśyate  pratiṣṭhitena kenacid rūpeṇa sva jñāna ātmani apratibhāsanāt na bhāvaḥ iti ced atyanta parokṣāṇām cakṣuḥ ādīnām abhāvatā prasaṅgaḥ na teṣām jñāna hetu rūpa tayā pratibhāsanāt iti ced na asya api bhavitṛ rūpa tayā avabhāsanāt sarva rūpa vivekasya ca katham bhūtyā sambandhaḥ  kenacid rūpeṇa unmajjanam hi bhavanam jñāna viṣaya tayā asya api ca tad hetu rūpa tayā avabhāsanasya tulya tvāt ahetoḥ ca viṣaya tva ayogāt asmākam tu abhāva buddhayaḥ sva vāsanā paripāka anvayāḥ nirviṣayāḥ eva abhāvasya ca bhavitṛ tve katham paryudāsāt prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ bhidyeta asat rūpasya vidhānena paryudāsāt sa bhidyata 
HBṬ_2.13.10	 iti ced na asat rūpasya bhavana virodhāt bhavati iti hi bhūtyā sat tayā abhisambadhyate tatra katham sat rūpasya vidhānam  paryudāsaḥ eva ekaḥ nañarthaḥ ca syāt sarvatra vidheḥ prādhānyāt saḥ api vā na bhavet yadi hi kiñcid kutaścid nivartyeta tadā tad vyatireki saṃspṛśyeta tad paryudāsena tat ca na asti sarvatra nivṛttiḥ bhavati iti ukte vastu antarasya eva kasyacid vidhānāt tathā anena vastu antaram eva uktam syāt na tayoḥ vivekaḥ aviveke ca na paryudāsaḥ aprastuta abhidhānam ca syāt bhāva nivṛttau prastutāyām asat ātmanaḥ vastu antarasya eva vidhānāt na ca asya sva rūpeṇa asat ātmaka tvam sva rūpeṇa api asataḥ kāryatva virodhāt para rūpeṇa tu sarvam eva vastu asat ātmakam iti na asya ghaṭa ādeḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ bhavatu vā ayam abhāvaḥ agni ādibhyaḥ tad bhāve kim iti na upalabhyante kāṣṭha ādayaḥ  tathā hi agni ādīnām anya kriyāyām caritārtha tvāt anivṛttāḥ eva tebhyaḥ indhana ādayaḥ prāgvat upalabhyeran tad upamarddena 
HBṬ_2.13.11	 dhvaṃsasya utpatteḥ iti ced katham tad upamarddaḥ  na tāvat pradhvaṃsa abhāvena indhana sattā kāle tasya abhāvāt na agni ādibhiḥ dhvaṃsa āvirbhāvaḥ eva teṣām vyāpāra upagamāt na ca utpannaḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ indhana ādīn vihanti yaugapadya prasaṅgāt dhvaṃsena vināśane ca vikalpa trayasya tad avastha tvāt tatas ca anavasthā saḥ eva dhvaṃsaḥ indhana ādeḥ agni ādi janmā nivṛttiḥ atas asya anupalabdhiḥ iti ced katham anyaḥ anyasya nivṛttiḥ  atiprasaṅgāt yadi ca ayam hetumān tad bhedāt ātma bhedam kim na anubhavati  śāli yava aṅkura ādayaḥ api kāraṇa bhedāt eva ātma bhedam atyanta vilakṣaṇam anubhavantaḥ adhyakṣataḥ eva avasīyante na tu evam anapekṣita bhāva antara saṃsarggaḥ cyuti mātra lakṣaṇaḥ dhvaṃsaḥ tasya abhighāta agni saṃyoga ādi kāraṇa bhede api tuccha rūpa tayā eka rūpasya sva jñāna ātmani avabhāsanāt na hi bhāva śūnyatām vihāya aparam tatra kiñcid rūpam īksāmahe vistarataḥ ca etad kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhau vicāritam 
HBṬ_2.13.12	 iti āstām tāvāt iha tasmāt agni ādi saṃyoga kāle na tasya kiñcid bhavati na bhavati eva kevalam iti eva upagantum yuktam yatas na ayam kasyacid bhāvena naṣṭaḥ nāma kintu yatas svayam asthira rūpa tayā bhūtaḥ tatas naṣṭaḥ nāma tena na asyāḥ abhavanam anyat vā kiñcid bhavati tathā ca bhavana dharmaṇaḥ kasyacid abhāvāt bhāvam bhavantam kutaścid na karoti iti kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ eva agni saṃyoga ādeḥ syāt eva ca sati karttā agni saṃyoga ādiḥ na bhavati iti akartuḥ ahetu tvam iti tasmāt na vināśa hetuḥ kaścid 
HBṬ_2.14.1	 na kevalam asāmarthyāt vināśa hetu ayogaḥ kintu vaiyarthyāt ca tat eva āha yadi svabhāvataḥ naśvaraḥ naśana śīlaḥ sva ātmani anavasthāyī sthātum aśaktaḥ yathā sūcī agre sarṣapaḥ tasya na kiñcid nāśa kāraṇaiḥ kim kāraṇam  svayaṃnāśāt tad svabhāva tayā eva asthira svabhāva tayā eva na hi prakṛti eva sthātum aśakte sūcī agre sarṣape tad asthitaye prayāsaḥ phalavān bhavet 
HBṬ_2.14.2–2.14.3	 atra eva vyāptim ādarśayati yaḥ hi ityādi na punar tad bhāve tad svabhāva tve janakāt hetoḥ hetu antaram apekṣate na hi prakāśa ādayaḥ ityādinā dṛṣṭānta vivaraṇam tad ātma tāyāḥ hetu antara anapekṣaṇena vyāptim tādātmya sādhakena pramāṇena darśayati tad ā ātmanaḥ yaḥ yasya svabhāvaḥ tad svabhāvasya tādātmya abhāve hetu antaram apekṣamāṇasya sva hetoḥ niṣpannasya api tad svabhāva tva abhāve nairātmyasya niḥsvabhāva tāyāḥ prasaṅgāt tadvat prakāśa ādi vat na punar paścāt tad ātmatāyām asthiti dharma ātma tāyām hetu antaram apekṣate iti pramāṇa phalam asthiti dharma āced naśvara svabhāvaḥ ced svabhāvataḥsva hetubhyaḥ niṣpannaḥ bhāvaḥ iti pakṣa dharma upasaṃhāraḥ viruddha vyāpta upalabdhiḥ ca iyam hetu antara apekṣā anapekṣayoḥ paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā virodhāt hetu antarā anapekṣayā ca tat svābhāva tāyāḥ vyāpta tvāt 
HBṬ_2.15.1	 atra ca parasya vacanau akāśam āśaṅkya āha bīja ādi vat ityādi syāt etat ityādinā etat eva vibhajate kevalāna janayanti iti kutas iti ced salila kṣiti ādeḥ sva hetu vyatiriktasya aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvānām api bīja ādīnām tad ātma tāyām apekṣaṇāt tatas ca na punar tad bhāve hetu antaram apekṣante iti anekāntaḥ tadvat bhāvaḥ api indhana ādiḥ sva hetoḥ naśvara ātmā niṣpannaḥ api vināśe vinaśvara ātma tāyām syāt iti dārṣṭa antikam na bīja ādi vat anekāntaḥ kutas tad svabhāvasya aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvasya bīja ādeḥ aṅkura ādi jananāt tad ātma tāyām hetu antara anapekṣaṇāt yaḥ ca kṣiti ādikam apekṣamāṇaḥ na janayati kuśūla ādi avasthaḥ tasya ajanakasya ca atad svabhāva tvāt aṅkura ādi janana svabhāva tva abhāvāt tatra tad ātmatā lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ na vartate eva iti na tena anekāntaḥ 
HBṬ_2.16.1	 nanu pratyabhijñā pratyakṣate eva bīja ādiḥ eka svabhāvaḥ lakṣyate tatra kutas ayam janana svabhāva tva ajanana svabhāva tva lakṣaṇaḥ bhedaḥ yatas anekāntaḥ na syāt na ca apramāṇam pratyabhijñā tatra apūrva artha vijñānam ityādi pramāṇa lakṣaṇa yogāt sat samprayogeṇa indriyāṇām bhāvataḥ ca pratyakṣam eva pratyabhijñānam na ca pratyakṣāt gariṣṭham pramāṇam asti yatas tad viṣayasya bheda siddhyā bādhām anubhavat apramāṇam etat syāt iti āśaṅkya āha atas eva janakatvā janaka tvāt eva viruddha dharma adhyāsāt tayoḥ avasthayoḥ janakā janaka avasthayoḥ bīja ādeḥ vastu bhedaḥ svabhāva bhedaḥ niśceyaḥ adhyavasātavyaḥ yathā hi śāli bījam tad aṅkura janana svabhāvam tad bhāve śāli aṅkura bhava darśanāt pratyakṣatas avagamyate yava bījam ca atad janana svabhāvam tad bhave śāli aṅkura anupalabdhyā tad vivikta yava bīja grāhi pratyakṣa rūpayā 
HBṬ_2.16.2	 pratīyate tathā atra api avasthā dvaye śālibījasya tad aṅkura viviktā vivikta avasthā agrāhi pratyakṣa balāt eva sva aṅkura jana kājanaka svabhāva tā kinna niścīyate  iṣyate eva avasthayoḥ bhedaḥ avasthāvataḥ tu abhedaḥ iti ced na tasya avasthā rūpa vivekinā rūpa antareṇa pratyakṣe pratibhāsana prasaṅgāt na hi yat anātma rūpa vivekena sva jñāne na pratibhāsate tasya pratyakṣatā yuktāḥ avasthātadvatoḥ svabhāva bheda abhāvāt katham rūpa antareṇa pratibhāsanam iti ced nanu avasthābhyaḥ anavāpta rūpa bhedasya avasthānām iva ātmanaḥ tad bhede sati abhedaḥ na saṅgacchate tatas ca asya avasthānām iva ātma bhedam anubhavataḥ katham avasthātṛ tvam  avasthā bhede api abhinna rūpasya tathā vyavasthānāt kathañcid bhedasya api bhāvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced yadi yam ātmānam purodhayaḥ ayam avasthātā avasthāḥ ca imāḥ iti bhaṇyate tena avasthā tadvatoḥ bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva iti kathañcid iti andha padam etat tatas asya pratyakṣatāyām anātma rūpa vivekinā 
HBṬ_2.16.3^1	 rūpa antareṇa avabhāsana prasaṅgaḥ na nivarttate atha tena ātmanā abhedaḥ avasthāvat bheda prasaṅgaḥ avasthātuḥ tadvat avasthānām abhedasya vā tayoḥ api kathañcid bheda abhedau iti ced tayoḥ tarhi avasthāta dvat ātmanoḥ bhedavatoḥ kathañcid abheda nimittam rūpa antaram iṣṭam syāt tathā ca tasya api tābhyām kathañcid bhedaḥ anyathā tad eka svabhāvāt atyantam abhedāt avasthā tadvatoḥ parasparam atyantam bheda abhedau prasajyeyātām rūpa antarasya kathañcid bhede tad nibandhanam aparam rūpam tathā asya api tat anyat iti aparimita rūpa tā eva ekaikasya vastunaḥ samāsajyeta 
HBṬ_2.16.3^2	 na ca aparimita rūpa pratibhāsi pratyakṣam anubhavāmaḥ ananubhavantaḥ ca katham tat kalpanayā aatmanā eva ātmānam vipralabhemahi  tasmāt avasthā rūpa vivekena upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalambhāt aparimita rūpa tā prasaṅgāt ca kathañcid bheda abhedavataḥ avasthātuḥ asattvam eva tāḥ ca avasthāḥ jana kājanaka svabhāva bhedavatyaḥ pratyakṣatas eva avagamyante iti tad eka tva adhyavasāyi pratyabhijñānam tad bādhām anubhavat katham pramāṇam syāt  yatas bīja ādīnām aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvānām api tad ātmatāyām hetu antara apekṣaṇāt prāktanasya hetoḥ anaikāntika tā bhavet 
HBṬ_2.16.4	 bhavatu vā avasthātā kaścid tasya api etat eva bhedam sādhayati tathā hi tayoḥ janakā janaka avasthayoḥ iti saptamī dvivacanam etat tadā bhavati tat ayam arthaḥ janaka avasthāyām ajanaka avasthāyām ca vastunaḥ dharmi lakṣaṇasya bheda svabhāva nānātvam atas eva jana kājanaka svabhāva tvāt eva pratyakṣau= asitāt niśceyaḥ niścaya lakṣaṇaḥ tatra vyavahāraḥ kartavyaḥ viṣayasya viruddha dharma adhyāsa lakṣaṇasya darśanāt iti 
HBṬ_2.16.5	 na ca śakyate vaktum avasthāḥ eva aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvāḥ na avasthātā iti tasya sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇasya asattva prasaṅgāt tatas yat eka rūpa tayā pratyabhijñānam bhaveṣu tat pūrva uttara kālayoḥ jana kājanaka svabhāva bheda vyavasthāpaka pratyakṣa nibandhanām anubhavat bādhām katham iva pramāṇam syāt  tad pratibhāsinaḥ ca abhinna rūpasya alīka tve akṣa samudbhavām api vṛttim anubhavataḥ asya sat samprayoga ja tvā abhāvāt taimirika ādi dhiyām iva kutas pratyakṣatā  na ca artha kriyā nibandhanam rūpam apāsya bīja ādeḥ aparaḥ paramārthataḥ svabhāvaḥ asti yasya adhigamāt pratyabhijñānam pramāṇam bhavet artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt parama artha sataḥ tasmāt sadṛśa apara bhāva nibandhanaḥ eva ayam keśa kadalī stamba ādiṣu iva ākāra sāmya tā mātra apahṛta hṛdayānām bhrāntaḥ eva tattva adhyavasāyaḥ mantavyaḥ tatas sataḥ api pratikṣaṇam bhedasya anupalakṣaṇam 
HBṬ_2.16.6	 bālānām yadā tu vidhura pratyaya upanipātāt visadṛśa apara bhāva prasavaḥ tadā a sya tattva adhyavasāyī pratyabhijñā pratyayaḥ na bhūtim avalambate na ca tad eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya janaka tvāt aparam sādṛśyam bhedāḥ aviśeṣe api ca sva hetu balāyāt aprakṛti vaśāt kecid eva eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya lakṣaṇām artha jñāna ādi lakṣaṇām vā artha kriyām kurvanti na aparaḥ iti vipañcitaṃpramāṇa vārtikaḥ eva śāstra kṛtā iti na iha prapañcyate 
HBṬ_2.17.1^1	 avaśyam ca bīja ādeḥ janakā janaka avasthayoḥ vastu bhedaḥ yathā uktaḥ avagantavyaḥ iti darśayitum anumānam abhedasya bādhakam āha bhāvānām bīja ādīnām sva kārya janakaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasya teṣu satsu anyathātva abhāvāt kadācid ajanakatva asambhavāt tad svabhāvasya aṅkura ādi janaka svabhāvasya paścāt iva salila ādi kāraṇa sannidhānaḥ iva prāk api kuśūla ādi avasthiti kāle api sva kārya janana prasaṅgāt tatha hi salila ādi sannidhāne api bīja ādiḥ sva rūpeṇa eva kāryam karoti na para rūpeṇa yaḥ ca asya tadā kārya janakaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa ced prāk api asti saḥ eva ayam iti pratyabhijñāyām puras avasthāyinaḥ janaka svabhāvasya prācya rūpa abheda adhyavasāyāt tatas kim iti prāk api tat kāryam na kuryāt iti  prayogaḥ yat yadā yat janana svabhāvam tat tadā tat janayati eva 
HBṬ_2.17.1^2–2.17.2	 ajanakasya janakatva svabhāva virodhāt anyasya api vā tad svabhāvatā āpatteḥ yathā tat eva bīja ādikam salila ādi sannidhi kāle kuśūla ādi avasthāsu api ca idam bīja ādikam sva kārya janana svabhāvam eva pratyabhijñayā vyavasthāpyate iti svabhāva hetu prasaṅgaḥ na ca janayati tasmāt na tad janana svabhāvam iti viparyaya prayogaḥ yat yadā yat janana svabhāva nirvarttyam kāryam na janayati na tat tadā tad janana svabhāvam tat yathā śāli aṅkura janana svabhāva nirvartyam kāryam ajanayat kodrava bījam na janayati ca salila ādi kāraṇa sannidheḥ prāk tad kārya janana svabhāva nirvarttyam sva kāryam bīja ādikam iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ tatas anumānataḥ api bādham anubhavat pratyabhijñānam katham pramāṇam syāt  nanu ca anena bādhyamānasya anumānasya aprāmāṇyāt katham bādhaka tvam  aniścita pramāṇa bhāvena kutas bādhā  na api itaretara āśraya tvam na hi pratyabhijñānasya aprāmāṇyāt etat anumānam pramāṇam kintu sva sādhya pratibandhāt sa ca viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa balāt niścitaḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.18.1	 na pratyakṣāt anyat gariṣṭham pramāṇam iti ced na pratyabhijñāyāḥ pratyakṣa tva asiddheḥ na hi iyam anumānena pratyakṣa ātmikā satī bādhyate iti brūmahe kim kṛtam ca pratyakṣasya garīyaḥ tvam  tat dhi arthasya asambhave abhāvāt pramāṇam ucyate tat ca anumānasya api artha pratibaddha liṅga janya tayā samānam iti na asya kaścid viśeṣaḥ yadi ca anumāna virodham aśnuvānā api pratyabhijñā pramāṇam tadā aakārasya sāmyāt tat eka tām pratiyatī nīla itara kusuma ādeḥ pratītiḥ kim na pramāṇam  na hi kusuma phala ādi kārya darśana unnīyamānaḥ bhedaḥ pratyakṣataḥ tathā abhāvam anubhavati vistarataḥ ca pratyabhijñā prāmāṇya nirāsaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhau eva vihitaḥ iti āstām tāvat iha 
HBṬ_2.18.2–2.18.3	 yatas evam uktena prakāreṇa janakājanaka avasthayoḥ bīja ādeḥ vastu bhedaḥ tasmāt yaḥ a nyaḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ yad antaram aṅkura ādi kārya prasavaḥ saḥ eva aṅkura janana svabhāvaḥ kārya darśana unnīyamāna rūpa tvāt tad janana svabhāva tāyāḥ yadi tarhi saḥ eva aṅkura janana svabhāvaḥ pūrva bhāvinām avasthā bhedānām atajjanana bhāva tvāt katham teṣu tad kāraṇa vyapadeśaḥ aṅkura arthibhiḥ vā tad upādānam iti atas āha pūrva bhāvinaḥ tu kuśūla ādi avasthiti kāla bhāvinaḥ tu avasthā viśeṣa aaṅkura kāraṇasya antyasya avasthā viśeṣasya kāraṇāni pratyaya antara upadhīyamāna viśeṣebhyaḥ paramparayā tebhyaḥ tad utpatteḥ atas teṣu upacārataḥ kāraṇa vyapadeśaḥ aṅkura arthibhiḥ ca upādānam yatas tad svabhāvasya bīja ādeḥ jananam na hetu antara apekṣam yat ca ajanakam apekṣate na tasya tad janana svabhāva tvam iti tasmāt na anā ikāntaḥ bīja ādi vat tad svabhāva tvāt iti asya hetoḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
HBṬ_2.18.4	 tat evam yadā tāvat pratyabhijñānam pratyakṣa pramāṇa tayā sthairya siddhaye paraiḥ ucyate bīja ādi vat anekāntam pratipādayitum tadā tasya uktena prakāreṇa pratyakṣa anumānābhyām bādhyamāna tvāt tad ātmatā na asti iti kutas tatas ekatā bhāvānām  yatas anekāntaḥ syāt iti pratipāditam yadā tu pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt pūrva apara kālayoḥ eka svabhāvā bīja ādayaḥ iti hetutayā ucyate paraiḥ tadā ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ na ca sa pakṣe kvacid varttate iti āha kṣaṇikeṣu bhāveṣu asmābhiḥ iṣyamāṇeṣu ekya abhāvāt iti sambandhaḥ 
HBṬ_2.19.1	 atha yasya api kṣanikāḥ bhāvāḥ tasya api bīja ādīnām pratikṣaṇam aikya abhāve api viśeṣa anupalakṣaṇāt antyakṣaṇa vat sarveṣām janaka svabhāvānām api tad bhāvam prati salila ādi apekṣa tvāt tad avastham anaikāntika tvam iti āśaṅkya āha apara apara utpatteḥ kṣaṇikaiḥ api na anekāntaḥ aparebhyaḥ aparebhyaḥ ca pratyayebhyaḥ pratikṣaṇam utpatteḥ kṣaṇikānām bhinna śakti tvāt antyakṣaṇa vat janaka svabhāva tā virahāt kutas taiḥ api anekāntaḥ syāt na hi kāraṇa bheda upadhīyamāna janmanām viśeṣa anupalakṣaṇe api abhinna svabhāva tā yuktāḥ hetu bhedān anuvidhāne ahetuka tā prasaṅgāt tathā ca vakṣyati apara apara pratyaya yogena pratikṣaṇam bhinna śaktayaḥ santanvantaḥ saṃskārāḥ yadi api kutaścid sāmyāt samāna rūpāḥ pratīyante tathā api bhinnaḥ eva eṣām svabhāvaḥ tena kiñcid eva kasyacid kāraṇam iti 
HBṬ_2.19.2	 yat uktam tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti asya anekāntam udbhāvayan āha paraḥ te bīja kṣiti ādayaḥ antyāḥ ante bhavāḥ pratyekam aṅkura janane samarthāḥ khaṇḍaśas kāraṇebhyaḥ kārya utpāda abhāvāt bhavadbhiḥ iṣyante iti kinna janayanti pratyekam  tatas ca eṣām ekaḥ eva kaścid aṅkuram janayati tad anye tu tad svabhāvāḥ api na janayanti iti tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti anekāntaḥ tadvat kuśūla ādi avasthāḥ api bīja ādayaḥ aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvāḥ api na janayiṣyanti iti taiḥ anekāntaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti manyateparaḥ 
HBṬ_2.19.3	 atra āha iti yat evam tvam manyase pareṇa sāmānyena abhidhānāt sāmānyena eva uttaram āha janayanti eva na atra sva kārya janane anyathā bhāvaḥ ajanaka tvam āśaṅkanīyam kutas svabhāvasya avaiparītyāt yadi hi na janayeyuḥ janana svabhāvāḥ eva na syuḥ tad svabhāvāḥ ca iṣyante iti avaśyam janayanti tathā ca kutas anaikāntaḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_2.20.1	 pratyekam antyānām janaka tve kāryasya ekena jananāt apareṣām upayogasya nirviṣaya tvāt ajananam eva iti manyamānaḥ āha paraḥ teṣu antyeṣu sahakāriṣu saha yugapad karaṇa śīleṣu samartha svabhāveṣu tad kārya kriyā yogyeṣu abhyupagamyamāneṣu satsu kāryasya ekena eva janita tvāt kaḥ aparasya upayogaḥ na eva kaścid tat kim ucyate janayanti eva iti  etat pariharati na vai na eva bhāvānām bīja ādīnām kācid prekṣā pūrva kāritā buddhi pūrva kāri tā yatas prekṣā pūrva kāri tvāt ayam asmāsu anyatam ekaḥ api samarthaḥ kārya janane kim atra asmābhiḥ karttavyam iti ālocya apare nivarteran audāsīnyam bhajamānāḥ tad kārya janane na vyāpriyeran yasmāt te bīja ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ nirabhiprāya vyāpārāḥ paryālocanā śūnya vyāpārāḥ ekatas utpadyamāne kārye sarve eva vyāpriyante bhavana dharmaṇi ca kārye teṣām prāgbhāva 
HBṬ_2.20.2–2.20.3	 eva vyāpāraḥ tad anyasya ayogāt yadi hi vyāpṛtāt anyaḥ eva vyāpāraḥ tadā tatas eva kārya utpādāt vyāpāravataḥ kāraka tvam eva hīyate tasya asau vyāpāraḥ tatas tasya kāraka tvam iti ced nanu evam vyāpāra upayogasya kārya anupayogini tatra upacārāt pāramārthikam asya kāraka tvam hīyeta kaḥ ca asya vyāpāreṇa sambandhaḥ  samavāyaḥ ced na tasya prāk eva nirasta tvāt samavāyāt ca vyāpāravat tve anyasya api tad kārya anupayoginaḥ tad bhāva prasaṅgaḥ samavāyasya iha iti buddhi hetoḥ ekatvena sarvatra samāna tvāt abhimatena eva vyāpṛtena tad vyāpāra utpādanāt na ati prasaṅgaḥ iti ced nanu tena tad utpādanam tatra samavāyāt eva ucyate sa ca sarvatra samānaḥ yena ca pariśrameṇa vyāpāram janayati tena kāryam eva kid na utpādayati yena vyavadhānam āśrīyate yathā ca sva sannidhi mātreṇa eva ayam vyāpāram janayati na vyāpāra antareṇa anavasthā prasaṅgāt tathā tatas eva kāryam api iti ukta prāyam 
HBṬ_2.20.4–2.20.5	 tasmāt bhāvini kārye prāgbhāvaḥ eva kāraṇasya vyāpāraḥ sa ca sarveṣām asti iti sarve eva kārya utpattau vyāpriyante iti vyapadiśyante tat api kāryaṃsarvebhyaḥ eva jāyate sarveṣām bhāvaḥ eva tad bhāvāt na hi kāryasya kāraṇa abhimata bhāvaḥ eva bhāvam antareṇa aparam janma tathā abhāve hi tatra eva kāraṇa vyāpārāt kārya kriyā eva eṣām na sambhavet tatas ca satsu api kāraṇeṣu katham asya bhāvaḥ upalabdhiḥ vā syāt  tad sambandhinaḥ janmanaḥ karaṇāt iti ced na asatā tena sambandha ayogāt svatas eva sattve vā janma artha anupapatteḥ janma kāle ca upalabhyasya ātmanaḥ prāk api bhāvāt tathā upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ rūpa antareṇa bhāve na tasya bhāvaḥ syāt rūpa bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt bhāva bhedasya tasmāt upalabdhi ātmanaḥ janmanaḥ prāc anupalambhāt asattvam tatas asya janma sambandhi tā kutas  tasmāt kāryam eva abhūtvā hetu bhāve bhavati iti bhāvaḥ eva asya tatas janma iti sarvebhyaḥ tat jāyate 
HBṬ_2.20.6^1	 nanu ekasya api tad janane sāmarthyāt apareṣām tatra sannidhi lakṣaṇaḥ vyāpāraḥ vyarthaḥ eva iti na tatra apareṣām bhāvaḥ saṅgacchate iti ced āha sva hetoḥ kṣiti bīja salila ādi sāmagrī lakṣaṇasya pariṇāmaḥ kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣavataḥ pratikṣaṇam upadhīyamāna atiśayasya kṣaṇa antarasya prasavaḥ tatas upanidhiḥ kārya deśe sannidhānam dharmaḥ yeṣām te tathā abhavantaḥ kārya deśe sannidhīyamānāḥ na upālambham arhanti ekasya api etad kārya karaṇe samartha tvāt kim atra bhavantaḥ sannihitāḥ iti na paryanuyogam arhanti na hi tad apara sannidhim antareṇa tatra ekasya api bhāvaḥ upapadyate kutas tad prakṛte tad prakṛti tvāt iti bhāva pradhānaḥ nirddeśaḥ 
HBṬ_2.20.6^2	 kṣiti bīja salila ādi sāmagrī pariṇāma janya svabhāva tvāt ekaikasya samarthasya tad bhāve kutas kevalasya sambhavaḥ  sāmagrī śabda vācyaiḥ kāraṇa bhedaiḥ samartha sva sva lakṣaṇa antara ārambhāt tatas ca pratikṣaṇam upadhīyamāna atiśayasya utpādāt kevalānām ca tad janana svabhāva vaikalyāt tad apara pratyaya yoga janya svabhāva tvāt samartha janakasya hetoḥ etat ca yathāvasaram tatra tatra vyaktīkariṣyati tasmāt yad sāmagrī janya svabhāvaḥ yaḥ bhāvaḥ sa tatra eka abhāve api kāraṇa vaikalyāt na sambhavati iti eka sāmagrī janmanām sahabhāvaḥ niyataḥ sarveṣām teṣām bhāvaḥ eva kāryasya bhāvāt sarve eva janayanti iti tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti atra na anekāntaḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.20.7	 yena abhiprāyeṇa te antyāḥ samarthāḥ kid na janayanti iti uktam tam prakaṭayan āha samarthāḥ ityādi siddhānta vādi api janayanti eva iti yat abhiprāyavata uktam tam ādarśayati na tatra eva ityādi etat eva vyācaṣṭe tasya eva ityādi ayam abhiprāyaḥ idam atra samartham idam asamartham iti pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanābhyām anvaya vyatirekābhyām vyavahriyate anya nimitta abhāvāt tau ca anvaya vyatirekau ekatra eva kārye dṛśyete na apara aparatra iti tasya eva ekasya janane samarthāḥ gamyante iti na aparā para jananam te tu yat avasthāḥ janayantaḥ dṛśyante kim tad janana svabhāvāḥ tadā eva āhosvit prāk api iti atra vivādaḥ tatra prāk api tad svabhāva tve paścāt iva prāk api janana prasaṅgaḥ iti pratikṣaṇam bhedaḥ ucyate iti 
HBṬ_2.21.1–2.21.2	 punar anyathā akṣapaṇaka jaiminīyāanekāntam udbhāvayantaḥ āhuḥ bhinnaḥ paraspara vyāvṛttaḥ svabhāvaḥ yeṣām tebhyaḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ saha kāribhyaḥ yugapad kartṛbhyaḥ ekasya vijñāna lakṣaṇasya kāryasya utpattau satyām bahūni bhinna svabhāvāni kāraṇāni kāryam tu ekam abhinna svabhāvam iti na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ syāt tatas cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ na bhinnena ātmanā ekasya kāryasya janakāḥ eṣṭavyāḥ kintu abhinnam eṣām eka kārya janakam sāmānya bhūtam rūpam upeyam yena abhinnam kāryam janayanti tat ca samagra avasthāyām eva tat kāryam janayati na vyagra avasthāyām na ca ekaika abhāve tasya abhāvaḥ sāmānya ātmanaḥ kadācid abhāva virodhāt na ca tadā asyāḥ ajanaka svabhāva tā janakājanaka rūpavataḥ samagra itara avasthāyoḥ bheda prasaṅgāt tathā ca sāmānya ātmanā hāniḥ tatas yat asya samagreṣu cakṣuḥ ādiṣu janakam rūpam tat ekaika abhāve api vidyate na ca janayati iti tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti anekāntaḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.22.1	 siddhānta vādi āha na yathāsvam ityādi evam manyate kim punar idam kāraṇam abhimatam bhavataḥ  yadi pratyekam cakṣuḥ ādikam tat ayuktam sāmagrī janya svabhāva tvāt kāryasya tasyāḥ eva kāraṇa tvāt nanu tad avasthāyām pratyekam eva sāmagrī śabda vācyānām janana svabhāva tva abhyupagamāt pratyekam eva cakṣuḥ ādikam kāraṇam yadi evam kaḥ ayam niyamaḥ yat anekasmāt bhavatā anekena bhavitavyam viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt ekena eva tat kāryam karoti iti kutas avasitam  tad bhāve bhāvāt iti ced anekatra api samānam etat tat uktam tasya eva ekasya janane samarthāḥ na anyasya iti na aparā para jananam iti na ca anekasmāt bhavat anekam prāpnoti yatas na asmākam bhavatām iva kāraṇam eva kārya ātma tām upaiti yatas aneka pariṇateḥ aneka rūpa tvāt kāryasya aneka tā syāt kintu apūrvam eva keṣucid satsu bhavati tat ca aneka bhāvaḥ eva bhāvāt tat kāryam ucyate tasya kuto 
HBṬ_2.22.2	 aneka tā prasaṅgaḥ  yat tu abhinnam rūpam janakam ucyate tasya eka sthitau api bhāvāt tad kārya janana svabhāvāt ca tatas kārya prasava prasaṅgaḥ tad anya sannidhau tasya viśeṣa abhāvāt tadā api vā na janayet tasmāt yeṣu bhāva abhāvavatsu kāryam bhāva abhāva vat dṛśṭam te eva viśeṣāḥ janakāḥ iti kutas anekāntaḥ  
HBṬ_2.22.3	 atha sāmagrīm kāraṇam āśritya ucyate na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ syāt iti tat na yathāsvam yasyāḥ sāmagryāḥ yaḥ ātmīyaḥ svabhāvaḥ tad bhedena tad viśeṣa upayogataḥ tasya vijñāna lakṣaṇasya kāryasya viśeṣāḥ sāmagrī bhedāt bhinnāḥ svabhāvāḥ teṣu upayogataḥ tad upayogaiḥ bhinna sāmagrī vyāpāraiḥ kāryāḥ ye svabhāva viśeṣāḥ kāryāṇām viśiṣṭāḥ svabhāvāḥ teṣām asaṅkarāt paraḥ para vyāvṛtta rūpa tvāt sāmagrī bhedāt bhinna rūpa tā eva kāryāṇām iti kathat na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ syāt  tathā hi ekā sāmagrī manaskāra tat sādguṇya ādi lakṣaṇā tatas vikalpa vijñāna mātram jāyate aparā manaskāra indriya mātra lakṣaṇā tatas bhrānta indriya vijñāna sambhavaḥ tad anyā viṣaya indriya manaskāra ātmikā tatas api abhra anta vijñāna sambhūtiḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.22.4–2.22.6	 bhinna sāmagrī janmanām kārya svabhāva viśeṣāṇām asāṅkaryāt asti eva sāmagrī lakṣaṇa kāraṇa bhedāt kāryāṇām bhedaḥ iti nanu yadā viṣaya indriya manaskārebhyaḥ vijñāna sambhavaḥ tadā teṣām upayoga viṣayasya eka tvāt katham asāṅkaryam  tathāvidhasya sāṅkaryasya iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ tat uktam tatra eva ekatra sāmarthyāt ityādi katham tarhi teṣām tad janaka tvam  yadi tad bhedāt na bhidyate kāryam kim nu vai samagrāṇām anyāni a kārya jananena janaka tvam yatas tad bhāve tat na syāt janaka tvam hi eṣām tad bhāvaḥ eva kasyacid bhāvāt tatra ekasya anekasya vā bhāve teṣām eka aneka janaka tvam ucyate 
HBṬ_2.23.1	 nanu ekasyāḥ sāmagryāḥ anekasya bhāve sāmagrī antara janyebhyaḥ bhavatu bhedaḥ parasparataḥ tu katham  tad atad rūpa hetu ja tvāt dhi bhāvāḥ tat atad rūpaṇi iṣyante tatra yadā cakṣū rūpamanaskārebhyaḥ vijñāna janma tadā cakṣu ūrū pakṣaṇayoḥ api bhāvāt vijñānena abhinna hetu ja tvāt tayoḥ vijñāna ātma tā vijñānasya vā tad rūpa tā katham na prasajyeta  āha ca 
HBṬ_2.23.2–2.23.4	 tat atad rūpiṇaḥ bhāvāḥ tad atad rūpa hetu jāḥ tad rūpa ādi kim ajñānaṃvijñāna abhinna hetu jam iti na eṣa doṣaḥ teṣām yathāsvam svabhāva bhedena nimitta upādāna tayā tad upayogāt manaskāraḥ hi vijñānasya upādāna kāraṇam cakṣuṣaḥ tu sva vijñāna janana yogyasya janmani sahakāri kāraṇam evam itaratra api yathāyogam vācyam tatas anyādṛśī sāmagrī cakṣuḥ kṣaṇasya janikā anyādṛśī ca vijñānadeḥ iti tad vailakṣaṇyāt eva kāryāṇām vailakṣaṇyam 
HBṬ_2.23.5–2.23.6^1	 syāt etat sarveṣām anvaya vyatirekau anuvidhīyete tadā cakṣuḥ ādi kṣaṇaiḥ iti kutas ayam bhedaḥ iha upādāna bhāvena idam upayujyate anyatra tu saha kāri bhāvena iti  bodha rūpa tā ādeḥ anukārān anukārābhyām tad bhāve vyabhicāra avyabhicārataḥ ca tathā hi vijñānam manaskārasya bodha rūpa tām anukaroti na cakṣuḥ ādeḥ jaḍa ādi bhāvam evam anyat api pratyeyam niyamena ca vijñāna mātra bhāve samanantara pratyayasya vyāpāraḥ na cakṣuḥ ādeḥ cakṣuḥ kṣaṇa antara udaye ca pūrva bhāvinaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ na sva vijñāna yogya tā hetoḥ samanantara pratyayasya
