HBṬ_2.23.5–2.23.6^2	 evaṃrūpasya api vācyam tasmāt avasthā bhede api yat eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya nibandhana tayā sva santati patita kārya prasūti nimittam tat upādānakāraṇam yat santāna antare prāc avastha apekṣa viśeṣa udaya nibandhanam tat sahakāri kāraṇam sa ca iyam bhāvānām sva hetu paramparā āyātā prakṛtiḥ yayā kiñcid kāryam sva santāna vyavasthā nibandhanam janayanti aparam ca santāna antara vyapadeśa nibandhanam iti tasyāḥ eva sāmagryāḥ avāntara viśeṣa kṛta tvāt cakṣū rūpa vijñā na kṣaṇānām parasparataḥ vailakṣaṇyam na virudhyate 
HBṬ_2.24.1–2.24.2	 tasmāt yadi kāraṇa bhedāt kāraṇa aneka tvāt kāryasya bhedaḥ aneka tvam tadā pratibandha abhāvāt anekāntaḥ na ca tat abhyupagamyate iti na kācid kṣatiḥ atha sāmagrī lakṣaṇasya kāraṇasya bhedaḥ sāmagrī antarāt vailakṣaṇyam kāryasya api bhedaḥ atad kāraṇebhyaḥ bhinna svabhāva tā ucyate tadā tasya iha bhāvāt katham na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ syāt iti abhiprāyavatā na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ na syāt kutas  yathāsvam iti ādi abhihitam 
HBṬ_2.24.3	 ubhayam ca etat kāryeṣu pramāṇa paridṛṣṭam iti darśayan āha yathā ityādi mṛd piṇḍa ādibhyaḥ hi bhavataḥ ghaṭasya na kāraṇa aneka tve api aneka rūpa tā nā api sāmagrī antara janyāt abhinna svabhāvatā iti udāharaṇa arthaḥ tatra sāmagryantara janyāt tāvat bhedam darśayati mṛd piṇḍāt ityādi iha mṛd piṇḍa kulāla sūtrāṇi vyagra svabhāvāni kāraṇa antara sahitāni iṣṭakā ādi lakṣaṇāni tad anya janyebhyaḥ bhinna svabhāvāni yāni kāryāṇi sādhayanti tebhyaḥ vilakṣaṇam eva samagrāṇi ghaṭa ātmakam kāryam janayanti tathā hi kulāla ādi nirapekṣaḥ mṛd piṇḍaḥ tad anya janyāt vṛkṣa ādeḥ vilakṣaṇam eva upādāna bhāvena mṛd ātmakam kāryam janayan dṛṣṭaḥ kulāla ādi sahitaḥ api tad ātmakam eva ghaṭam tad kāraṇa āhita viśeṣaḥ ca kevala mṛd piṇḍāt bhinna svabhāva tayā tad kāryāt api iṣṭaka ādeḥ vilakṣaṇam eva karoti evam kulāla ādikam 
HBṬ_2.24.4	 api tad anya upādāna sahitam saha kāri bhāvena yat kāryam karoti tad vilakṣaṇam eva mṛd piṇḍa sahitam tad kāranā hita viśeṣam ghaṭa ātmakam kāryam janayati iti samudāya arthaḥ tatra mṛd piṇḍāt bhinnaḥ svabhāvaḥ ghaṭasya ye tad anya upādāna kāraṇa tayā mṛd svabhāvāḥ na bhavanti vṛkṣa ādayaḥ tebhyaḥ bhavati kulālāt mṛd piṇḍa upāda anāhita atiśayāt saha kāri bhāvena upayujyamānāt tasya eva ghaṭasya mṛd piṇḍa upādāna tayā mṛdā ātmanaḥ sataḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ pṛthu budhnā udara ādi ākāraḥ tad ātma tayā tad anyebhyaḥ yeṣām mṛd piṇḍa s tad anya nimitta sahitaḥ upādānam iṣṭakā ādīnām tebhyaḥ bhinnaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhavati sūtrāt mṛd piṇḍa kulāla kāraṇa āhita viśeṣāt tasya eva ghaṭasya mṛd saṃsthāna viśeṣa ātmanaḥ mṛd piṇḍa kula ālayoḥ tad janana svabhāva tvāt ghaṭasya tad rūpa yogāt tayoḥ ca sūtra kāraṇa upahita viśeṣayoḥ tad nirapekṣā avasthātaḥ 
HBṬ_2.24.5–2.24.6^1	 bhinna ātmaka tayā cakra ādeḥ vibhaktaḥ vicchinnaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhavati tasmāt anukrānta kāraṇa traya janyaḥ ghaṭaḥ tad anyasmāt ekaika kāryāt dvi dvi kāryāt ca bhinna svabhāvaḥ eva jāyate iti sāmagrī bhedāt bhinnāni eva kāryāṇi parasparam asaṅkīrṇa svabhāvāni bhavanti iti tad upayoga kārya viśeṣa asaṅkaraḥ siddhaḥ tasya ca ekaika tad avasthā bhā vi kāraṇa bheda anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyitayā khaṇḍaśas anutpādāt ca tat ekaika janya tve api vastutas tad ekaika sajātīya kāraṇa antara sannidhau= adṛṣṭasya viśeṣasya itara sannidhau tad darśanāt tat janyaḥ ayam iti tattva cintakaiḥ vivecyate 
HBṬ_2.24.5–2.24.6^2	 yatas kārya viśeṣa arthinaḥ aneka kāraṇa parigraham kurvanti paraspara āhita upakāra kārya paramparayā vāñchita kārya janana yogya kāraṇa sāmagrī bhāva artham yatas evam sāmagrī bhedāt bhinnāni eva iṣṭakā cakrā vibhakta ghaṭa tad vibhakta ghaṭa lakṣaṇāni kāryāṇi bhavanti tat tasmāt evam uktena prakāreṇa kulālāt mṛd piṇḍa rahitāt anya sāmagrī antarbhūtāt na mṛd svabhāva tā kasyacid kāryasya mṛd piṇḍa kāraṇa upakṛta ātmanaḥ eva tasya tad viśeṣa hetu tvāt na mṛdaḥ kevalāyāḥ tad sāmagrī bahirbhūtāyāḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ kulālopādāna upakṛta tāyāḥ eva mṛd saṃsthāna viśeṣa ātmaka kārya hetu tvāt 
HBṬ_2.25.1	 tat evam sāmagrī bhedāt bhedam kārasya udāharaṇe pratipādya sahakāriṇām aneka tve api aneka ātma tā viraham pratipādayan āha na ca tayoḥ mṛd kula alayoḥ sahitayoḥ paraspara upādāna upakṛta ātmanoḥ yaḥ śakti viśeṣaḥ pratyaya antara sahita avasthātaḥ viśiṣṭā yogya tā tad viṣayasya tad anya avasthā viṣayāt bhede sati api yathā tad anyasmāt bhedaḥ evam svabhāvena na bhedaḥ svarūpataḥ api na nānātvam na aneka ātmaka tā kāryasya tābhyām janitaḥ yaḥ viśeṣaḥ mṛd saṃsthāna viśeṣa ātmakaḥ saḥ eva tad anya sāmagrī janyāt bhidyate iti bhedaḥ asya 
HBṬ_2.25.2	 katham punar etat jñāyate tad anyasmāt iva svabhāvataḥ api asya bhedaḥ na asti iti atas āha mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ ityādi yadi hi mṛd kula alayoḥ tad avasthā bhāvinoḥ śakti viśeṣa viṣayaḥ mṛd saṃsthāna viśeṣa ātmakaḥ bhedaḥ tad anyasmāt iva svarūpataḥ bhidyeta tadā mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ aparaspara ātma tayā paraspara ātma tā viraheṇa kāraṇena saṃsthāna viśeṣeṇa mṛd na pratibhāseta na mṛd svabhāvena ca saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ yathā tad anya rūpeṇa na hi yaḥ yasya svabhāvaḥ na bhavati sa tena ātmanā sva grāhiṇi jñāne pratibhāsate rūpa rasavat jñānam vā tad rūpa vikala artha sāmarthyena utpadyamānam tad rūpam anukartum yuktam bhrānta tā prasaṅgena tad vaśāt artha vyavasthāna abhāva prasakteḥ tasmāt mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ eka ātma tā eva iti na kāraṇa aneka tvāt kāryasya aneka ātmaka tā aikāntikī yatas bhinna svabhāvebhyaḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ saha kāribhyaḥ eka kārya utpatti virodhāt 
HBṬ_2.25.3	 eka rūpa tayā teṣām sādhāraṇa eka kārya kriyā bhinna rūpa tayā vā sādhāraṇa kārya karaṇam iyeta etat ca eka sāmagrī apekṣayā eka kārya kartṛ tvam ucyate paramārthataḥ tu tad sāmagrī antarggatānām sajātīyasyāḥ api kṣaṇa antarasya ārambhāt sāmagrī antara avayava tvena ca kārya antarasya api yathā eka pratyaya janitam kiñcid ekam na asti tathā aneka pratyaya janitam api iti kāraṇa aneka tvāt kārya aneka tva upagame api na kācid kṣatiḥ tatas eka kārya apekṣayā aneka tva prasañjane sandigdha vyatireka tā sāmānyena sādhane siddha sādhyatā iti ca 
HBṬ_2.26.1	 nanu ca mṛd saṃsthāna viśeṣayoḥ eka svabhāva tve api ahrīka ādibhiḥ saṅkhī ā ādi bhedāt bhedaḥ iṣyate tat katham aneka pratyaya janitasya ekatve etat udāharanām syāt  sarvatra eva hi dravya paryāyayoḥ saṅkhyā saṃjñā lakṣaṇa kārya bhedāt bhedaḥ deśa kāla svabhāvā bhedāt ca abhedaḥ iṣyate yathā ghaṭasya rūpa ādīnām ca tathā hi ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ bahavaḥ iti saṅkhyā bhedaḥ ghataḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti saṃjñā bhedaḥ anuvṛtti lakṣaṇam dravya vat nityam ca vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇāḥ bhedāḥ kṣaṇikāḥ ca jaiminīyasya tu kecid kāla antara sthāyinaḥ api iti lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ ghaṭena udaka āharaṇam kriyate rūpa ādibhiḥ punar vastu rāgaḥ iti kārya bhedaḥ evam sarvatra dravya paryāyayoḥ saṅkhī ā ādibhiḥ bhedaḥ deśa ādibhiḥ tu abhedaḥ iti mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ kathañcid bhedāt mṛd kulālābhyām janitasya kāryasya aneka tā asti eva yathā tu ekatā tathā tābhyām tasya abhinna ātma janyata eva iti 
HBṬ_2.26.2–2.26.3	 yat aneka kāraṇam tat anekam eva yat punar ekam tat sahakāriṇām abhinna rūpa janya tayā eka kāraṇam eva iti na vyabhicāraḥ iti tat ayuktam svabhāvataḥ bheda anabhyupagame anyathā bheda asiddheḥ anekasmāt eka kārya utpatteḥ abhādhanāt svabhāvataḥ bheda upagame vā aparaspara ātma tayā mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ saṃsthāna mṛd svabhāva viśeṣābhyām tayoḥ apratibhāsanam durnnivāram yadi hi svabhāvataḥ na bhedaḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ saṅkhī ā ādi bhedāt api na eva bhedaḥ na hi para rūpāḥ bhidyamānāḥ api saṅkhyā ādayaḥ ātma bhūtam abhedam bādhitum samarthāḥ 
HBṬ_2.26.4	 saṅkhyā bhedaḥ tāvat asamarthaḥ ekasmin api dravye bahu tvena vyavahāra darśanāt yathā guravaḥ iti na ca bahuvacanasya niyamena adarśanāt rūpa ādayaḥ atra nimittam rūpa ādi nimitta tve hi guruḥ iti na kadācid eka vacanam syāt sambhavi dharmi rūpa mātram abhidheya tvena vivakṣitam iti ced na tasya ekatvena vivakṣāyām kārtsnya gauravayoḥ apratīti prasaṅgāt vrīhayaḥ iti ca jāti vacane dharmiṇaḥ rūpa ādīnām ca anabhidhānāt na kiñcid uttaram ubhaya rūpasya ca vastunaḥ guru śabda vācya tvāt katham sambhavinaḥ dharmi rūpasya ekatvena vivakṣā  tatas ca ekaḥ guruḥ iti sāmāna adhikaraṇī adarśanāt paryāyāḥ api eka saṃkhyā viṣayāḥ te ca paryāya rūpeṇa bhidyante tat katham saṃkhyā bhedāt bheda siddhiḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.26.5	 saṃjñā api saṅketa nibandhanāḥ sa ca icchā āyatta vṛttiḥ iti kutas tatas artha bhedaḥ  ekasmin api saṃjñā bheda dṛṣṭeḥ katham asya bheda nimitta tā  yathā indraḥ śakraḥ purandaraḥ iti atra api indanāt śakanāt dāraṇāt ca śakti bhedaḥ gamyate iti ced na samastasya kārya kartṛ tvāt na hi śaktiḥ eva indati śaknoti dārayati ca kim tarhi  dharmi rūpam api tayoḥ eka svabhāva upagamāt śaknoti ādi padaiḥ tad vācinām sāmāna adhikaraṇī adarśanāt ca na ca askhalat vūtti pratyaya viṣaya tvāt upacāra kalpanā yuktā iti yeṣām ca paryāyāṇām na kācid artha anugama mātrā tatra kim vaktavyam  
HBṬ_2.26.6	 lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ api ahetuḥ asiddha tvāt na hi ekaḥ bhāvaḥ kvacid api anvayī siddhaḥ iti tathā hi na kūṭastha nitya tayā nityam dravya mahrīkaiḥ iṣyate pariṇāma nityatā upagamāt sā ca pūrva uttara kṣaṇa prabandha vṛttyā na hi asya paryāyāṇām iva ucchedaḥ tad rūpeṇa paryāyāḥ eva paryāya rūpeṇa nirudhyante na tu dravyam iti nityam abhyupagamyate na ca iyam kūṭastha nitya tā vā dravye sambhavati paryāya vyatiriktasya dravyasya asiddheḥ tasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya tad viveka anupalakṣaṇāt paryāyeṣu eva tulya rūpa kārya kartṛṣu dravya abhimānaḥ manda matīnām na punar tat tatas vilakṣaṇam upalakṣyate 
HBṬ_2.26.7	 kārya bhedaḥ tu asmān prati asiddhaḥ eva rūpa ādīnām eva keṣāñcid tad kārya kartṛ tvāt tathā api abhyupagyamya ucyate kāryam hi dvividham bhinna kālam abhinna kālam ca tatra pūrvam bhavati bheda nibandhanam yadi iha sambhavet tat tu na sambhavati dharma dharmiṇoḥ tulya kāla tvāt abhinna kālaḥ tu kārya bhede anaikāntikaḥ vibhakta pariṇāmeṣu paṭa ādiṣu sambhavāt paṭa ādayaḥ api hi vibhakta pariṇāmāḥ anekam kāryam kurvantaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ na ca dharmi rūpeṇa bhidyante ekasya aneka kiyā virodha abhāvāt ca na hi atra kāraṇam eva kārya ātma tām upaiti yatas ekasya kāraṇa ātmanaḥ eka kārya rūpa tā upagame tad anya rūpa abhāvāt tad anya kārya ātma tā upagatiḥ na syāt kintu apūrvam eva kasyacid bhāve prāk avidyamānam bhavat tad kāryam tatra viṣaya indriya manaskārāṇām itaretara upādāna āhita rūpa bhedānām sannidhau viśiṣṭa svetarakṣaṇa bhāve pratyekam tad bhāva abhāva anu vidhānāt aneka kriyā upagamaḥ 
HBṬ_2.26.8–2.26.9	 na virudhyate yatas eka kriyāyām api tasya tad bhāva bhāvitā eva nibandhanam sā ca aneka kriyāyām api samānā iti nanu ca tad sannidhau vijñāna lakṣaṇa kārya sambhavāt tad janana svabhāva tā eva eṣām avadhriyate kārya svabhāva apekṣayā kāraṇasya janaka rūpa tā avasthānāt tatas vijñāna janana svabhāvebhyaḥ pratyekam katam tad anya kārya sambhavaḥ  tad bhāve vā teṣām tad anya janana svabhāva tā syāt tatas ca vijñānam eva na kuryuḥ tad anya janana svabhāva tvāt 
HBṬ_2.26.10	 na eṣa doṣaḥ teṣām aneka kārya kriyā svabhāva tvāt tathā hi te tad avasthāyām pratyekam viśiṣṭa sajātīyeta rakṣāṇa janana ātmakāḥ teṣām tad sattā nantarya darśanāt tatra vijñāna janana svabhāva tā eva iti tasya ajanana svabhāva tā vyavacchidyate tasyāḥ eva pratiyogi tvāt na anya janana svabhavatā na ca atas teṣām aneka ātma tā syāt ekasya eva ātma atiśayasya aneka kārya hetu tvāt na hi tad anya apekṣayā viparyaya vyāvṛttim upādāya anekena śabdena abhidhīyamānam vastu aneka rūpa tām pratipadyate prativiśiṣṭasya ekasya eva ātmanaḥ tathā abhidhānāt yathā rūpam sa nidarśanam sa pratigham iti na hi atra svabhāva bheda nibandhanāḥ dhvanayaḥ sāmāna adhikaraṇya abhāva prasaṅgāt tad nimittānām ekatra bhāvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na teṣām tad eka upakāra anapekṣiṇām tad ayogāt apekṣāyām vā katham ekam aneka kāryam na syāt  anekena eva ātmanā upayogāt iti ced na 
HBṬ_2.26.11	 sāmāna adhikaraṇya abhāva doṣasya tādavasthya prasaṅgāt na ca nīla ādīnām ātma bhedam adhyakṣam īkṣāmahe na api kārya bhedāt eva ātma bheda anumānam pratibanda abhāvāt tad grāhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt pratyakṣataḥ aneka kāryāṇām api bhāvānām eka ātma tayā eva upalakṣaṇāt pradīpa ādīnām na anumānataḥ tatra api viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt ekasya aneka kriyā anabhyupagame ca yaḥ ayam rūpa rasa gandha sparśa viśeṣāṇām kvacid sahabhāva niyamaḥ pramāṇa paridṛṣṭaḥ sa na syāt bhinna nimittānām sahabhāva niyama ayogāt tad nimittānām api tad eka kāraṇān āyatta janmanām niyata sāhitya asambhavāt tad eka dharmi svabhāva tayā ekatra sahabhāva niyamaḥ iti ced na ekasya aneka svabhāva tāyāḥ eva cintya tvāt anekena eka svabhāva tām ca anubhavataḥ tadvat aneka tāyāḥ durnivāra tvāt anyathā dharma dharmiṇām katham na aikāntikaḥ bhedaḥ  tathā hi yam ātmānam purodhāyāḥ ayam 
HBṬ_2.26.12–2.26.13	 dharmī paryāyāḥ ca ete iti vyavasthāpyate yadi tasya bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva iti anekasya api eka kārya tā na syāt na hi paraspara upādāna kṛta upakāra anapekṣāḥ viṣaya indriya manaskārāḥ saha eka kārī a ārambhiṇaḥ yuktāḥ na ca ekam eva kiñcid kvacid janayati tatas ca sarvatra kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva utsīdet anekasya ekasya ca eka aneka kriyā virahāt prakāra antara abhāvāt ca 
HBṬ_2.26.14	 na api ahetukam eva viṣvam deśa kāla prakṛti niyamāt tasmāt eka sāmagrī adhīna janmanām eva sahabhāva niyamaḥ bhāvānām eka kārya kriyā niyamaḥ vā tatas ca sva santā nakṣaṇam itara upādānam ca yugapad upakurvataḥ katham ekasya aneka kārya tā na syāt  tatas katham kārya bhedāt bhedaḥ kalpyeta  dravya paryāyāṇām ca eka svabhāva tām ācakṣāṇaḥ ekasya aneka kārya tām pratikṣipati iti katham na unmattaḥ  svabhāvasya eva vastu tvāt anyathā tasya niḥsvabhāvatā prasaṅgāt eka svabhāva tve ca dravya paryāyāṇām tad kārya bhedaḥ eka vastu nibandhanaḥ eva iti kārya bhedāt bhedam abhidadhānaḥ sphuṭam ahrīkaḥ eva ayam iti upekṣām arhati 
HBṬ_2.27.1	 vaiśeṣikaḥ api dravyasya ekasya dravya guṇa karmaṇām samavāyikāraṇa tām bruvāṇaḥ karmaṇaḥ ca ekasya saṃyoga vibhāga saṃskāra nimitta tām ekasya aneka kārya kriyām pratikṣipan sva kṛtānta kopena eva pratihataḥ na ca atra śakti bhedaḥ nibandhanam yatas tad eka upakāra nirapekṣāḥ katham etāḥ śaktayaḥ niyata artha ādhārāḥ  na punar anavayavena vyaktīḥ vā aśnu vīran  tatas yatas eva asyāḥ aatmā atiśāyāt aneka śakti upakāra tatas eva aneka kārya kriyā api iti alam ati vistāriṇyā kathaya iti 
HBṬ_2.28.1	 deśa kāla svabhāva abhedāt abhedaḥ tu yaḥ abhyupagamyate saḥ api anupapannaḥ eva tathā hi deśa kālayoḥ abhede api rūpa rasa gandha sparśāḥ paryāya rūpeṇa bhidyante tatas katham abheda siddhiḥ  svabhāvaḥ api yadi dravya paryāyayoḥ dvayoḥ api pratyekam anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti rūpa tā tadā padārtha dvayam syāt ghaṭa paṭa vat na tu ekam dvi rūpam iti kathan tasmāt abheda siddhiḥ  na ca anuvṛtti vyāvṛttī svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ tayoḥ anuvarttamāna vyāvarttamāna adhīna tvāt tatas ca anuvarttamāna vyāvarttamānayoḥ svabhāvaḥ anyaḥ vaktavyaḥ na tu tayoḥ anuvṛtti vyāvṛttī eva svabhāvaḥ bhāva tvena bhavitṛ adhīna tvāt na hi smṛtiḥ smarttuḥ svabhāvaḥ bhavati anuvṛtti vyāvṛttyoḥ ca svabhāva tve lakṣaṇāt svabhāvasya bhedaḥ vaktavyaḥ mṛd ā ādi rūpa tā svabhāvaḥ iti ced atra api abhedaḥ iti yadi sādṛśyam ucyate tat bhedaḥ eva sambhavati sādṛśyasya sadṛśa adhikaraṇa tvāt tatas ca padārtha dvayam 
HBṬ_2.28.2	 eva syāt na tu ekam dvi rūpam iti atha aikyam dvitīya rūpa rahita tā abhedaḥ aṅgīkriyate katham tarhi dvi rūpa tā  rūpa śabdena hi atra svabhāvaḥ abhidhīyate tasya ca aikye katham dvi rūpa tā  vipratiṣiddham hi etat eka svabhāva tā dvi rūpa tā ca iti atha punar svabhāvataḥ aikyam na upeyate katham tarhi saḥ ekaḥ iti ucyate anekaḥ san  na tāvat eka kāraṇa janya tvāt sarvatra upādāna nimitta kāraṇa bhedena hetu bheda siddheḥ na api eka kārya kartṛ tvāt ekasya api vibhakta pariṇāma avibhakta pariṇāma kārya bhedāḥ abhyupagamāt eka abhidhāna abhidheya tvāt api na ekatvam ekasya api aneka paryāya sambhavāt yogya tvāt ca viśvasya kṛta akṛtānām eka abhidhāna abhidheya tvasya kvacid asambhavāt śakti bhedāt ca viṣaya bhedam bruvāṇam prati abhihitam na api eka vijñāna viṣaya tvāt ekam ekatra api aneka vijñāna prasūteḥ tathā hi śaśāṅka udayam bahavaḥ nirīkṣante tasya katham eka tvam abhyupagatam  bahūnām ca eka vijñāna viṣaya tva sambhavāt 
HBṬ_2.28.3–2.28.4	 nīla pīta ādīnām eka tā prasaṅgaḥ sarvathā idam na kathañcid api saṅgacchate yat uta ekasya dvairūpyam iti vijñānam tu nīla praticchāyatayā utpadyamānam pīta ādi pratibhāsa vyavacchedena prativiśiṣṭam khyāpyate na punar asya bhāvataḥ dve rūpe staḥ atha punar dravya paryāyayoḥ sammūrcchita tvāt narasiṃha vat ekam śabala rūpa tvāt dvi rūpam ucyate tat ayuktam nara siṃghahasya śabala rūpa tva asiddheḥ sa hi aneka paramāṇu saṅghāta rūpaḥ te ca paramāṇavaḥ pratyekam nara siṃha rūpāḥ na bhavanti ūrdhva bhāgaḥ tasya siṃha rūpaḥ aghaḥ bhāgaḥ tu nara rūpaḥ jāti antaram ca saḥ eva nara siṃhābhyām syāt na śabala rūpaḥ vicitram hi rūpam śabalam ucyate 
HBṬ_2.28.5–2.28.6	 vicitra tā ca nānā svabhāva tā nānā svābhāvye ca eka tvam kutas iti kevalam aneka tve api bahuṣu eka kārya darśanāt senā ādi vat eka vyavahāra darśana kṛtaḥ ayam viparyāsaḥ jaḍa matīnām tat evam tāvat pratyekam ahetu tvam deśa kāla svabhāvānām eka tva prasādhane samuditānām api vyabhicāri tvam paryāyaiḥ tathā hi paryāyāḥ abhinna deśa kāla svabhāvāḥ ca paryāya rūpeṇa ca bhidyante pūrva uktāt ca dharma dharmiṇoḥ niṣedhāt na ubhaya vāda sambhavaḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.29.1–2.29.8	 āha ca dravya paryāya rūpa tvāt dvairūpyaṃvastunaḥ kila tayoḥ eka ātmaka tve api bhedaḥ saṃjñā ādi bhedataḥ indriya jñāna nirbhāsi vastu rūpaṃhi gocaraḥ śabdānāṃna eva tat kena saṃjñā bhedāt vibhinna tā parama artha eka tāna tvaḥ ityādi vacanāt tathā śabdena avyāpṛta akṣasya buddhau apratibhāsanāt arthasya dṛṣṭau iva tad śabdāḥ kalpita gocarāḥ 
HBṬ_2.29.9–2.29.15	 kalpitasya eva tad bhedaḥ saṃjñā bhedāt bhavet yadi vyāvṛtti bhedaḥ kāścid syāt vastunaḥ na kathaṃcana saṃkhyā bhedaḥ api na eva anyaḥ mataḥ vacana bhedataḥ tatas api kalpitasya eva kathañcid syāt vibhinna tā yeṣām vastu vaśā vācaḥ ityādeḥ na tu vastunaḥ bhedaḥ eva viśīryeta tat eka avyatirakataḥ abhedasya aparityāge bhedaḥ syāt kalpanā kṛtaḥ 
HBṬ_2.29.16–2.29.23	 tasyāḥ avitatha bhāve vāsyāt abhede mṛṣā artha tā anyonya abhāva rūpāṇām aparābhāva hetukaḥ eka bhāvaḥ yatas tasmāt na ekasya syāt dvi rūpa tā tasya bhedaḥ api tābhyāṃced yadi yena ātmanā āca te dharmī dharmaḥ tad anyaḥ ca yadi bhedaḥ tad ātmanā bhedaḥ eva atha tatra api tebhyaḥ anyaḥ parikalpyate teṣām abheda siddhi arthaṃprasaṅgaḥ pūrvavat bhavet dharmitvaṃtasya ca evaṃsyāt tad tantra tvāt tad anyayoḥ 
HBṬ_2.29.24	 atra vaiśeṣika matam āśaṅkya āha anyat eva ityādi saṃsthānam hi avayava sanniveśaḥ ucyate sa ca saṃyoga lakṣaṇa tvāt guṇa rūpaḥ tatas mṛd dravyāt asya anya tvam dravya guṇayoḥ asaṃkīrṇa svabhāva tvāt tena yadi mṛd piṇḍasya mṛdā ātma tāyām vyāpāraḥ kulālasya tad saṃsthāna viśeṣe kathyate tadā tayoḥ atyanta bhedāt kāraṇa aneka tvāt kārya anekatvam prāptam iti siddhānta vādi āha uktam atra iti mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ svabhāva bhede dūṣaṇam uktam mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ aparaspara ātma tayā iti ādikam iti na saṃsthānasya mṛd dravyāt anya tvam tatas mṛd piṇḍa upāda ana āhita atiśayena tad kārya kṣaṇa sahakāriṇā kulālena tad upādāna upakṛta ātmanā tad kārya kṣaṇa sahakāriṇā mṛd piṇḍena ca pratyekam sakalam eva mṛd saṃsthāna ātmakam kāryam kriyate iti na kāraṇa an eka tve api aneka tvam asya atra eva upacaya hetum āha api ca 
HBṬ_2.29.25	 ityādi yat tat ghaṭa gatam saṃsthānam yadi tata mṛdaḥ bhinnaṃsyāt tadā kulālaḥ pṛthak eva kim iti na karoti  na hi bhinnānām āvaśyakam apṛthak karaṇam kulālaḥ ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām tasya saṃsthānasya guṇa ātmanaḥ kāraṇa tayā gamyate iti sa pṛthak api tat kāryāt paraḥ āha guṇasya itiādi dravya āśrayya aguṇavān saṃyoga vibhāgeṣu akāraṇam anapekṣaḥ iti guṇa lakṣaṇāt sarvadā guṇaḥ dravya pratantraḥ sa katham kadācid pṛthak kriyeta  vaiśeṣikaḥ eva bauddhīyaṃcodyam āśaṅkya āha tad saṃsthānaḥ ityādi yadi svabhāvena eva tasya guṇa ātmanaḥ saṃsthānasya kriyāvat guṇavat ityādi vacanāt ādhāra svabhāvam tat mṛd dravyam saṃsthānam vā tathāvidham kapāla ādheya ātmakam tadā kim iti kulāla vyāpāram apekṣate  svatas eva kim na bhavati iti ca udaka abhiprayaḥ 
HBṬ_2.29.26	 evam ca udyam āśaṅkya vaiśeṣikaḥ parihāram āha na tatas ityādi yat tat mṛd dravyam pṛthu vudhna udara ādi ākāram ca saṃsthānam tayoḥ yaḥ sambandhaḥ ādhāra ādheya lakṣaṇaḥ tatra yā yogya tā tām dvayam api etat kulālāt yatas pratilabhate tasmāt kulālam apekṣate kulāla anapekṣāyām doṣam āha anyathā yadi tayoḥ paraspara sambandha yogya tāyām kulāla apekṣā na syāt tadā svabhāvataḥ eva mṛd piṇḍasya tathāvidha saṃsthāna sambandha yogya tvam bhavet tasmin ca sati vastunaḥ eva tad saṃsthāna sambandha yogya tā lakṣaṇā dharmatā asti iti kulāla sannidheḥ prāk api saṃsthāna viśeṣeṇa sambandhaḥ syāt iti vaiśeṣikīyaḥ ca udya parihāraḥ 
HBṬ_2.31.1	 siddhānta vādi āha evam ityādi yadi paraspara sambandha yogya tāyām kulālam apekṣate evam tarhi sāyogya tā mṛd dravyasya kulālāt bhavati iti āpannam na ca anayoḥ mṛd dravya yogyatayoḥ svabhāvasya bhedaḥ nānātvam yadi hi syāt tadā yogyatāyāḥ dravyāt pṛthak karaṇam prāgvat prasajyeta atha yogyatāyāḥ api yogya pāratantryāt apṛthak siddhim brūyāt tadā tasyāḥ api vastu dharma tayā eva prāk api samāveśaḥ mā bhūt iti dravyeṇa saha sambandha yogya tāyāḥ anyā yogyatā kulālāt bhavati iti eṣṭavyāḥ sā api pṛthakkaraṇa prasaṅgāt dravyāt bhinna svabhāvāḥ na upagantavyā pṛthakkaraṇa prasaṅge vā punar saḥ eva parihāraḥ tadīyaḥ punar tat eva uttaram iti anavasthā prasaṅgāt avaśyam abhinna svabhāva tā kapāla ātmam amṛd dravya yogya tayoḥ abhyupagantavyā kim evam sati siddham bhavati iti atas āha asti tāvat ityādi mṛd piṇḍa kulālābhyām 
HBṬ_2.31.2	 kapāla dravyasya saṃyoga viśeṣa sambandha yogyasya ārambhāt yadā eka svabhāva tve api ekasya aneka pratyaya upādheya viśeṣa tā tadā siddhaḥ āsmākīnaḥ pakṣaḥ tatas ca kim asmākam mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ eka svabhāva tva sādhanāya ati nirbbandhanena  yadi yogyatām api āśritya aneka pratyaya janya tve api eka tvāt nānātva prasaṅga abhāvaḥ sidhyati kāryasya na kiñcid dravya guṇavāda nirākaraṇena iha prayojanam anyatra eva tad nirākaraṇasya kṛta tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ nirbandha grahaṇena ca mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ aparaspara ātma tayā saṃsthāna mṛd svabhāva viśeṣābhyām tayoḥ apratibhāsana prasaṅgāt iti anayā upapattyā sādhitam eva anayoḥ eka tvam yukti antarāṇām sambhave api tad abhidhāna lakṣaṇaḥ nirbbandhaḥ na kriyate prakṛta siddheḥ anyathā api bhāvāt iti ācaṣṭe 
HBṬ_2.32.1	 tat evam sāmagrī bhedāt sāmagryantara janyebhyaḥ bhedaḥ sahakāriṇām aneka tve api ca kāryasya ekatvam aviruddham iti pratipādya upasaṃharan āha tena sahakāriṇaḥ ityādi yena pratyaya antara pracaye tad vikala sāmagryāḥ sāmagryantaram sampadyate tat ca pūrva sāmagrī janyāt bhinnam kārya antaram eva janayati eka sāmagrī vyapadeśa viṣayāṇām ca sahakāriṇām aneka tve api anekasya eka kriyā virodha abhāvāt tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyinaḥ ca kāryasya ekasya darśanāt svabhāvataḥ eka tvam sādhitam tena kāraṇena saha karaṇa śīlāḥ eka sāmagrī antarggatāḥ pratyayāḥ sāmagrī antaraiḥ saha na eka upayoga viṣayāḥ ekaḥ upayogasya viṣayaḥ yeṣām te na bhavanti sāmagrī antaraiḥ eva saha bhinna upayoga aviṣaya tvasya nyāya balāt pratīteḥ anena yat prāk vikalpitam yadi kāraṇa śabdena sāmagrī bhaṇyate tadā tad bhedāt asti eva ātad sāmagrī janyebhyaḥ kāryasya bhedaḥ iti kim ucyate 
HBṬ_2.32.2	 na kāraṇa bhedāt bhedaḥ syāt iti etat udāharaṇa upadarśitam nigamitam atha kāraṇa śabdena sāmagrī vyapadeśa viṣayāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ ucyante tadā tad bhedāt aneka tva lakṣaṇāt kāryasya aneka tva lakṣaṇaḥ bhedaḥ neṣyate eva anekasya eka kriyā virodha abhāvāt ekasya anekatas utpatti darśanāt ca iti mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ eka ātmaka tā upadarśitam nigamayati kārya svabhāvasya mṛd saṃthānātmanaḥ eka tve api nānātva abhāve api vastutas paramārthataḥ kalpanā buddhau mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ bhinnayoḥ iva pratibhāsane api iti 
HBṬ_2.32.3	 evam udāharaṇe sāmagrī bhedāt kāryāṇām bhedaḥ na eka sāmagrī viṣaya pratyaya bhedāt aneka tvam kāryasya iti pratipādya prakṛte cakṣuḥ ādau yojayan āha yathā aiha udāharaṇe kāraṇa bhedaḥ sāmagrī bhedaḥ kulāla vikala mṛd piṇḍa tad sahita sūtra adhika sāmagrī tritaya lakṣaṇaḥ bhinneṣu nānā svabhāveṣu viśeṣeṣu iṣṭakā ādi cakrā vibhakta ghaṭa tad vibhakta ghaṭa lakṣaṇeṣu upayogāt na eka kāryaḥ kintu bhinna kāryaḥ eva tathā tena eva prakāreṇa cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ vijñānasya utpattau sāmagrī antarāt sāmagrī lakṣaṇa kāraṇa bhedaḥ aneka kāryaḥ iti unneyaḥ 
HBṬ_2.32.4	 etat eva vibhajan āha tathā hi ityādi yā cakṣūḥ uparahitā samanantara pratyaya ākhya vijñāna lakṣaṇā pratyaya antara sāpekṣā sāmagrī tatas vijñānasya vikalpakasya itarasya vā tad upādeya tvena yā bodha rūpa tā upalabdhā sā cakṣuḥ vijñānasya api bhavati tasya eva cakṣuḥ vijñānasya kidṛśasya  upalambha ātmanaḥ sataḥ bhavataḥ jāyamānasya tadā eva tad eka kārya pratiniyatasya cakṣuḥ indriyasya sannidhānāt samanantara pratyaya upādāna upakṛtāt tatas rūpa grahaṇa pratiniyamaḥ rūpa ākāra tā pratiniyamaḥ śabda ādi ākāra vivekavataḥ eva kāryasya cakṣuḥ sahita samanantara pratyaya sāmagryāḥ janaka tvāt viṣayāt viṣaya adhikāt samanantara pratyayāt indriyāt ca tena viṣayeṇa tulya rūpa tā na kevalā eva rūpa pratibhāsitā bhrānta vijñānasya iva iti viṣaya indriya manaskāra lakṣaṇa sāmagrī kāryam evam pradarśitam tat anyat eka dvaya janyam tu kāryam 
HBṬ_2.32.5	 svayam abhyūhyam atra abhinna tve api vastutas kāryasya cakṣuḥ vijñāna lakṣaṇasya kāraṇānām viṣaya indriya manaskārāṇām bhinnebhyaḥ svabhāvebhyaḥ kevalānām eṣām yaḥ svabhāvaḥ tatas bhinnāḥ eva ātat janyebhyaḥ api viśeṣāḥ bodha rūpa tā ādi lakṣanāḥ bhavanti atad janya apekṣayā ca eka ātmakāḥ api bahu tvena nirdiṣṭāḥ yatas evam iti tasmāt na kāraṇa bhede api yathā eka sāmagryantarggata pratyaya bhede api abhedaḥ na evam sāmagrī lakṣaṇa kāraṇa bhede api abhedaḥ sāmagrī antarasjanyebhyaḥ kārya viśeṣasya viśiṣṭasya kāryasya iti 
HBṬ_2.32.6	 tena yat ucyate yadi sahakāriṇām bhede api abhinnam kāryam bhavati sāmagrī bhede api abhinnam astu atha sāmagrī bhedāt bhinnam bhavati sahakāri bhedāt api kim iti bhinnam na bhavati viśeṣa abhāvāt iti tad apāstam bhavati tathā hi paraspara upasarppaṇa ādi āśrayāt pratyaya viśeṣāt eka kārya uddeśena itara itara santāna upakārāt ca sahakāriṇām pratiniyata śaktīnām udayāt ekam kāryam samājāyate sāmagryantarasya tu kārya antara prabhava śakti nibandhanebhyaḥ hetu antarebhyaḥ svabhāva bhedavataḥ bhāvāt bhinna kārya prasūtiḥ iti kutas viśeṣa abhāvaḥ  
HBṬ_2.33.1	 nanu ca sarvam kāryam sa ādhāram yathā upādāya rūpam tat dhi bhūtebhyaḥ jāyamānam tāni eva āśrayate iti bhavadbhiḥ iṣyate tathā anyat api vijñāna ādikam kāryam atas anena api kiñcid kāraṇam āśrayaṇīyam tasya ca kāraṇasya pūrvam janaka tvam paścāt kāryam pratyādhāra bhāvaḥ eva na jananam tatas tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti anekāntaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti atas āha te eva ete ye anantaram uktāḥ kāraṇa śakti bhedāḥ kāraṇānām śakti viśeṣāḥ kīdṛśāḥ yathāsvam yeṣām kāraṇa śakti bhedānām sahakāri lakṣaṇānām yat ā ātmīyam sāmagryantara janyāt prativiśiṣṭam kāryam tasya janane avyavadheyāḥ vyavadhātum pratibandhum aśakyā śaktiḥ yeṣām tad bhāvaḥ tayā avyavadheya śakti tayā avaśyam kārya kāri śakti tayā pratyupasthitāḥ udyuktāḥ santaḥ sāmagrī kāryasya eka pratyaya janitasya kasyacid 
HBṬ_2.33.2–2.33.3	 abhāvāt sarvam sāmagryāḥ eva kāryam iti kṛtvā sāmagrī kāryasya svabhāva sthiti āśrayaḥ iti ucyante kasmāt punar avyavadheya śakti tā kṣaṇika tvāt na hi kṣaṇikasya śaktiḥ pratibandhum śakyate svabhāva antara utpādane yāvat pratibandhakaḥ vyāpriyate tāvat kṣaṇikasya sva kāryam kṛtvā eva nirodhāt katham punar asamāna kālam kāraṇam ādhāraḥ yujyate  iti atas āha tathā hi ityādi yasmāt tat vijñāna lakṣaṇam kāryam tebhyaḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ samastabhyaḥ bodha rūpa tayā tad anyasmāt tad ajanyāt prativiśiṣṭa svabhāvam ekam khaṇḍaśas kāryasya anutpādāt ekaikasmāt sakalasya eva bhāvāt ekam jātam tasmāt te ādhārāḥ ucyante na hi janakāt anyaḥ eva upakārakaḥ na ca anupakārakaḥ ādhāraḥ atiprasaṅgāt tatas bhinna kālasya ādhāra bhāvaḥ na virudhyate yat api bhūtānām upādāya rūpam pratyāśraya tvam ucyate tat api sva deśasya asya janaka tvam eva iti na kiñcid prāk janakam bhūtvā paścāt sthāpaka tām upaiti yatas anekāntaḥ syāt iti 
HBṬ_2.34.1	 punar anyathā tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti anekānta udbhāvanam parasya āśaṅkya āha apratirodha śaktikeṣu avidyamānaḥ pratirodhaḥ pratibandhaḥ yasyāḥ śakteḥ sā yeṣām apratirodha śaktika tvam ca anantara kārya tvāt ye hi utpannāḥ kāla kṣepeṇa kāryam kurvanti teṣām syāt api śakti pratibandhaḥ na tu ye udaya anantaram eva kāryam kurvanti anena kṣaṇa kṣayiṇām upaghātaka abhāvam āha anugrāhaka viraham api āha anādheya viśeṣeṣu tat ca anādheya viśeṣa tvam kṣaṇikeṣu iti anena āha na hi kṣaṇikānām viśeṣaḥ ādhātum śakyate viśeṣa ādhāyakena tad sahabhāvinā tad anantaram tad utpādanāt tadā ca tasya nirodhāt teṣu evaṃvidheṣu pratyayeṣu para sparaṃkaḥ sahakāra arthaḥ yena sahakāriṇaḥ ucyante  nanu anādheya viśeṣa tvena eva sahakāri tva abhāvaḥ pratipāditaḥ iti kim artham idam apratirodha śaktikeṣu iti  na hi śakti pratirodhakaḥ 
HBṬ_2.34.2	 sahakārī bhaṇyate satyam sarvathā tu tatra akiñcitkara tva jñāpana artham etat uktam śakti pratibandha ka apanayanena ca upakāri tva kalpanām sahakāriṇām nirasyati tasmāt atiśaya ādhāyinaḥ sahakāriṇaḥ asambhavāt kṣaṇikānām sva hetu mātra pratibaddham eva janaka tvam tat ca evam vidham sarvadā asti na ca kevalāḥ janayanti iti tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti anekāntaḥ eva iti manyate 
HBṬ_2.34.3	 etat pariharati na vai na eva atiśaya utpādanam sahakriyā yatas tad abhāvāt sahakāriṇaḥ na syuḥ kva punar atiśaya utpādanam sahakriyā pratiyayānām na bhavati  sarvatra na hi kvacid api saha bhāvinām atiśaya utpādana lakṣaṇā sahakriyā sambhavati kā tarhi sahakriyā iti āha eka artha karaṇam eka kārya niṣpādanam yat bahūnām api sambhāvanāyām nyāya balāt evaṃvidhām eva sarvatra sahakriyām sambhāvayāmaḥ na anyām iti atra udāharaṇam yathāantyasya anantara aṅkura ādi kāryasya kāraṇa kalāpasya pratyaya sāmagryāḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.35.1	 syāt etat aupacārikam etat sahakāri tvam atiśaya utpādanam eva tu mukhyam iti atas āha tat eva eka kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇam mukhyaṃsa hakāri tvam na atiśaya utpādana lakṣaṇam tasya eva gauṇa tvāt etat ca uttaratra vakṣyate kutas etat iti āha tasya eva anyasya vivakṣita kāryam prati kāraṇa tvāt kāraṇasya ca sahakāri vyapadeśaḥ na akāraṇasya yatas saha yugapad sarvantar sahakāriṇaḥ ucyante antyaḥ ca kāraṇa kalāpaḥ evaṃvidhaḥ iti yathā ca antyasya eka artha kāraṇam sahakāri tvam evam pūrvasya api kāraṇa kalāpasya uttarottara viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa antara ārambhiṇaḥ iti avaseyam antyasya udāharaṇa tayā nirddeśāt tasmāt sarvam kāryam aṅkura ādikam viśeṣa lakṣaṇam vā aneka pratyaya janyam iti sarvatra eka artha kriyā eva ca upacīyamāna apacīyamāna kārya kāriṇaḥ kāraṇa kalāpasya sahakāri tvam na viśeṣa utpādanam iti 
HBṬ_2.35.2	 syāt etat eka artha karaṇam api tatra sahakāri tvam astu atiśaya utpādana lakṣaṇam api iti atas āha tatra ca kṣaṇe antye viśeṣasya karttum aśakya tvāt na atiśaya utpādanam api sahakāri tvam kutas viśeṣasya karttum aśakya tvam iti atas āha ekasya anaṃśasya svabhāvasya avivekāt na hi tatra ayam anāhita atiśayaḥ bhāgaḥ sva hetubhyaḥ jātaḥ ayam tu sahakāribhiḥ āhita atiśayaḥ iti vivekaḥ asti yadi nāma avivekaḥ viśeṣaḥ tu kim iti na kriyate iti atas āha svabhāva antara utpatti lakṣaṇa tvāt viśeṣa utpatteḥ nirbhāge ca kutas svabhāva antarasya vyavasthā  
HBṬ_2.35.3	 syāt matam bhinna svabhāvaḥ eva antyasya viśeṣaḥ astu iti atas āha bhāva antaraḥ ityādi yadi bhāva antara lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ bhavet tadā tasya antya tvam eva hīyeta hīyatām kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced tatas ca anantya tvāt na sākṣāt kāraṇaṃsyāt yatas evam tasmāt na kāraṇasya mukhyasya saha kāribhyaḥ sakāśāt viśeṣasya utpattiḥ iti eka artha kriyā eva sahakāri tvam iti 
HBṬ_2.35.4	 nanu asatyām saha kāribhyaḥ viśeṣa utpattau kārya janane sāmarthyam eṣām na yujyate iti atas āha te samarthāh ityādi yadi hi te svabhāvena asamarthāḥ utpadyeran tadā eṣām saha kāribhyaḥ sāmarthya utpattiḥ abhyupagamyeta yāvatā te antyāḥ svabhāvena eva samarthāḥ pratyayāḥ sahita ajāyante kṣaṇa mātra vilambinaḥ yeṣām eka kṣaṇa niyata tvāt tatas prāk paścāt pṛthak tu abhāvaḥ na asti yebhyaḥ ca anantaram eva kāryam utpadyate na kāla antareṇa tatra teṣu evaṃvidheṣu eka artha kriyā eva sahakāri tvam na atiśaya utpādana lakṣaṇam 
HBṬ_2.35.5	 svabhāvataḥ sāmarthyasya bhāva virodhāt parasparataḥ ca anabhyupagamāt samarthasya janma eva ayuktam iti manvānaḥ paraḥ āha samarthaḥ kutas ityādi siddhānta vādi āha sva kāraṇebhyaḥ iti parama tāpekṣayā tu svabhāvataḥ iti uktam paraḥ hi utpannasya kāraṇasya saha kāribhyaḥ sāmarthyam icchati iti tat niṣedha param svabhāvataḥ iti vacanam na tu svabhāvataḥ kiñcid jāyate tasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt 
HBṬ_2.36.1	 eka artha kriyā niyamaḥ eva kṣaṇikānām ayuktaḥ kevalānām api aṃti akṣaṇa sarūpāṇām darśanāt tathā hi idam evaṃrūpam na evam ca iti darśana adarśanābhyām vibhajyate tatra yādṛśāḥ kṣiti ādayaḥ tad anya pratyaya sannidhau upalabhyante tādṛśāḥ eva kevalāḥ api tatas tad anya sahitāḥ iva kevalāḥ api samartham aṅkura janane svam svam kṣaṇa antaram ārabheran tatas kevalasya api aṅkura ādi janana svābhāvyāt ajananāt ca tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti anekāntaḥ eva iti manyamānaḥ paraḥ āha tāni sva kāraṇāni kṣiti bīja ādīni enam samartham aparasya anyasya pratyayasya sannidhānaḥ eva kim kasmāt anayanti na kevalāni  sahitānām eva sarvadā sambhavāt iti ced āha kadācid kasmiṃścid kāle anyathā api kevalāḥ api syuḥ bhaveyuḥ tathā hi dṛśyante eva adhyātika bāhyāḥ kvacid kārye yādṛśāḥ yat sahitāḥ tādṛśāḥ eva tat rahitā 
HBṬ_2.36.2	 api iti janayan tu kevalāḥ api sambhavantaḥ samartham kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced āha tatas ca kevalānām api samartha janakānām sambhavāt ekaḥ api na kevalam anekaḥ kvacid deśa ādau samarthaḥ utpannaḥ kṣiti bīja ādiḥ aṅkura ādi kāryam janayet yadi tad svabhāvasya avaśyam janaka tvam na ca kevalaḥ janayati tad svabhāva sambhave api tatas anekāntaḥ iti paraḥ 
HBṬ_2.36.3	 etat pariharan āha aparāparaḥ ityādi aparaiḥ ca aparaiḥ ca kuśūla tad apanetṛ puruṣa prayatna piṭaka ādi prakṣepa kṣetra nayana prakiraṇa ādibhiḥ pratyayaiḥ yaḥ yogaḥ tena kāraṇena pratikṣaṇaṃbhinna śaktayaḥ na kadācid pūrva apara kāla bhāvinaḥ eka śaktayaḥ apara apara pratyaya yoga lakṣaṇa hetu bhede api abhinna śakti tāyām ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt anyatra api ca śāli yava bīja ādau śakti bhedasya hetu bheda nibandhana tvāt 
HBṬ_2.36.4	 saṃskārāḥ sametya sambhūya ca pratyayaiḥ kriyamāṇāḥ santanvantaḥ santānena bhavantaḥ yadi api kutaścid sāmyāt varṇena saṃsthānena anyena vā kenacid prakāreṇa sādṛśyāt eka ākāra parāmarśa pratyaya janana lakṣaṇāt samānam rūpam eṣām iti sarūpāḥ sadṛśāḥ pratīyante pratyabhijñāyante tathā api kṛtrima kṛtrimāṇām iva maṇi muktā ādīnām apara apara pratyaya yoga lakṣaṇa sāmagrī bhedāt bhinnaḥ eva visadṛśaḥ eva na pratyabhijñāna vaśāt abhinnaḥ tulya rūpaḥ eṣām bīja ādīnām svabhāvaḥ yatas evam tena bhinna svabhāva tvena bhinna śakti tayā vā apara apara sāmagrī janya tvena kṣaṇānām siddhayā kiñcid eva kṣiti bīja ādikam kasyacid eva kāryasya aṅkura ādeḥ tad janana samarthasya vā kāraṇam na sarvam sarvasya tathā ca vyagrāṇām kṣiti bīja ādinām aṅkura janana svabhāva tā 
HBṬ_2.36.5–2.36.6	 samartha kṣaṇa janana svabhāva tā vā na asti eva iti tad svabhāvasya jananāt ajanakasya ca ātad svabhāva tvāt iti atra na anekāntaḥ yatas yaḥ yad svabhāvaḥ sa sva hetoḥ eva utpadyamānaḥ tādṛśaḥ bhavati na punar tad bhave hetu antaram apekṣate iti atra anekāntaḥ syāt iti pratyabhijñānasya ca sarūpa tā viṣayasya sāmagrī bhedāt anumita bhinna śakti svabhāva tvena bādhyamāna tayā prāmāṇya abhāvāt na tatas sarūpa tā siddhiḥ kṣaṇa kṣayiṇām iti pūrvam ca atas eva tayoḥ avasthayoḥ vastu bhedaḥ niśceyaḥ iti ādinā ekatva aviṣayam pratyabhijñānam nirastam adhunā tu tulya svabhāvatā viṣayam iti bhedaḥ etat api tatra apara apara utpatteḥ iti anena uktam eva vipañcana artham tu punar iha upanyastam 
HBṬ_2.37.1	 kiñcid eva kasyacid kāraṇam iti uktam tatra kim kasya kāraṇam iti śakya paricchedam api ādhyātmikeṣu tāvat darśayan āha tatra ityādi tatra teṣu pratikṣaṇam śakti svabhāveṣu kṣaṇikeṣu bhāveṣu vyavadhānam vyavadhīyate yena tad ādiḥ yeṣām ati dūra atyāsanna tva ādīnām te avidyamānāḥ yasmin deśe saḥ avyavadhāna ādiḥ deśaḥ yasya saḥ avyavadhāna ādi deśaḥ rūpam indriyam ca ādī yasya manaskāra ādeḥ sa rūpa indriya ādiḥ sa ca asau kāraṇa kalāpaḥ ca sāmagrī lakṣaṇaḥ tathā uktaḥ avyavadhāna ādi deśaḥ ca asau rūpa indriya ādi kāraṇa kalāpaḥ ca sa vijñāna janane samarthaḥ hetuḥ na anyaḥ tad bhāvaḥ eva tasya bhāvāt anya bhāve api ca abhāvāt etad mātra nibandhana tvāt ca samartha asamartha vyavasthāyāḥ yaḥ teṣām indriya ādīnām paraspara upasarppaṇasya anyonya ḍhaukanasya ādi grahaṇāt vyavadhāna apanayanā 
HBṬ_2.37.2–2.37.3	 sāmagrī adhīna tvena asaṃbhavāt iti imam evaṃvidham hetu phala bhāva pratiniyamam niravadyam ādhyātmakeṣu darśitam anyatra api atidiśan āha anena nyāyena ityādi yaḥ ayam anantaram hetu phala bhāva pratiniyame nyāya uktaḥ saḥ aanyatrāḥ api sarvatra draṣṭavyaḥ sarvatra iti vacanāt akṣaṇikeṣu api pratītiḥ mmā bhūt iti āha pratikṣaṇam ityādi yāḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe anyāḥ ca anyāḥ ca svabhāva bhedān vayinyaḥ śaktayo bhavanti tatra ayam eka artha kriyā pratiniyamaḥ sahakāriṇām draṣṭavyaḥ na tu ye sthira eka svabhāvāḥ bhāvāḥ paraiḥ kalpyante teṣu api sthairyam santāna āśrayeṇa api vyapadiśyeta iti eka grahaṇam kṣaṇe api eka tvam asti iti sthira grahaṇam 
HBṬ_2.38.1	 kasmāt punar sthira eka svabhāveṣu na iṣyate iti āha svabhāvaḥ ityādi kāmam bhāvaḥ svayam na bhavet na tu svatas eva svabhāvasya anyathātvam sambhavati tatas ca sthiraḥ padārthaḥ yadi kārya utpādana samartha svabhāvaḥ tatas asya akriyā na upapadyate iti sarvadā eva kuryāt atha asamartha svabhāvaḥ tadā api kriyā anupapannā sarvadā eva na kuryāt iti bhāvaḥ yat tu kadācid karoti kadācid naḥ iti etat na labhyate tatas ca akṣaṇikānām tad kārya kriyā samartha svabhāva tve sahita asahita avasthayoḥ eka rūpa tvāt kevalānām api tad kārya kriyā prasaṅgena kutas eka artha kriyā pratiniyama lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam sambhavet  
HBṬ_2.38.2–2.38.3	 atra paraḥ āha anya sahitaḥ ityādi yadi api kevalasya api akṣaṇikasya samarthaḥ svabhāvaḥ tathā api anya sahitaḥ karoti na kevalaḥ ayam api hi asya svabhāvaḥ yat anya sahitena sva kāryam karttavyam na samartha svabhāvena api satā kevalena iti siddhānta vādi āha kiṃkevalasya ityādi anya sahitena eva sva kāryam karttavyam na kevalena iti etat kevalasya asamartha svabhāva tve yujyate na anyathā iti manyamānasya praśnaḥ paraḥ tu anavagata abhiprāyaḥ āha samarthaḥ iti kevalasya api akṣaṇikasya samarthaḥ eva svabhāvaḥ anyathā asya akṣaṇika tā eva hīyeta iti siddhānta vādi āha kid na karoti iti na hi samarthasya akriyā sahitasya avasthāyām iva yujyate iti sahitasya eva kriyām icchatā kevalasya asamartha svabhāva tā eva upagantavyā 
HBṬ_2.38.4	 atha matam kevalasya yadi śiraḥ chidyate tathā api na karoti iti atas āha akurvan ityādi kārya anumeyam hi sāmarthyam na ca kevalasya kadācid api kārya kriyā asti iti katham sāmarthyam kalpyate  na ayam niyamaḥ yat samartha svabhāvena avaśyam eva kāryam karttavyam anyathā api darśanāt iti manyamānaḥ āha paraḥ kuvinda ādayaḥ ityādi siddhāntavādi apasan āha krīḍana śīlaḥ ityādi devānāṃpriyaḥ ṛjuḥ mūrkhaḥ vā sukha saṃvardhita tvāt ramaṇa svabhāvaḥ krīḍanam bāla dharmaḥ tat sādharmyeṇa prajñā vaikalyam darśayati sukha edhita tvena śāstreṣu anabhiyogam yaḥ hi anabhiyuktaḥ durvuddhiḥ ca sa kṛtam api vastu vismaraṇa prakṛti tvāt punar punar kārayati iti punar pratividhāpayati kva punar etat prativihitam iti āha tathā hi ityādi bīja ādi vat anekāntaḥ iti anena prastāvena nirlloṭhitam eva etat 
HBṬ_2.38.5	 tat evam akṣaṇikasya samartha svabhāva tve sahitasya eva kārya kriyā svabhāva tva virodhāt kevalasya akriyā anupapanna iti pratipādya upasaṃharan āha tasmāt tad svabhāvasya kārya kriyā samarthasya anyathātvāsambhavāt kadācid asamartha tva abhāvāt tad dharmaṇaḥ kārya kriyā dharmaṇaḥ tathā abhāvaḥ kārya kriyā antya avasthāvat sahita avasthāyām iva anivāryaḥ 
HBṬ_2.39.1	 syāt matam kevalaḥ ayam akṣaṇikaḥ asamarthaḥ eva tatas kevalaḥ na karoti sahita avasthāyām tu asya sāmarthyam saha kāribhyaḥ jāyate tatas sahitaḥ eva karoti iti atas āha antya avasthāyāṃsāmarthya utpattau kīdṛśasya prāk asamarthasya sataḥ tasya sāmarthyasya yasya tat upajāyate tad svabhāva tve mīmāṃsaka ādibhiḥ iṣyamāṇe na hi teṣām samarthyasya sāmarthyasya ca svabhāva bhedaḥ abhimataḥ kathañcid tad bhede api tad svabhāva tayā eva pratīyamāna tvāt iti te manyante apūrva utpattiḥ eva sā apūrvasya eva vastunaḥ sā utpattiḥ yā tad svabhāvasya sāmarthyasya na hi eka svabhāva tve sāmarthyam eva apūrvam upajātam na samarthaḥ iti yuktam tayoḥ svabhāva bheda prasaṅgāt viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt 
HBṬ_2.39.2	 nanu pratīyamāne eva sāmarthya tadvatoḥ utpatti anupattī eka svabhāva tā ca katham nihnotum śakyate iti ced na apramāṇena pratīteḥ anyathā pratīti anusāriṇā bhavatā dvi candra ādayaḥ api na nihnotavyāḥ bādhaka pramāṇa sambhavāt te apahnūyante iti ced iha api vastunaḥ eka svabhāvasya utpatti anupattī paraspara viruddhe bādhike kim neṣyete  vyavasthitasya eva vajra upala ādeḥ ddharmiṇaḥ tad svabhāvam sāmarthyam utpannam iti ca pūrva apara kālayoḥ apratibhāsamāna vivekaḥ katham pratīyāt  
HBṬ_2.39.3	 vijñāna ādi kāryasya anutpatti yaugapadya udaya prasaṅgāt cakṣuḥ ādi sānnidhye prāk asat tat sāmarthyam utpannam krama vat ca iti niścayaḥ iti ced yadi evam eka ākāratayā pūrva apara kālayoḥ vikṛtam pratyabhijñānam upajāyamānam apūrva sāmarthya pratibhāsa vivikta upala ādi grāhy api anumānāt arthāpattitaḥ vā bādhām anubhavat na pramāṇam iti upagatam syāt tathā utpatti anutpattyoḥ eka svabhāvatāyām virodhāt samarthasya eva apūrvasya utpattiḥ sadṛśa apabhāva graha kṛta ś cārvāk darśanānām eka tva vibhramaḥ lūna punar jjāteṣu iva keśa nakha ādiṣu iti kim na iṣyate  
HBṬ_2.40.1	 atha sāmarthyam sahakāri pratyaya sānnidhya lakṣaṇam eva iti atad svabhāvam iti na apūrva utpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti naiyāyika ādayaḥ manyeran atra āha atad svabhāva tve sāmarthyasya iṣyamāṇe sa bīja ādiḥ padārthaḥ prāk iva tad rūpā parityāgāt paścāt api akārakaḥ eva kutas  sāmarthyam iti ākhyā yasya padārtha antarasya sahakāri pratyaya sānnidhya lakṣaṇasya saḥ eva atiśaya śabda vācyaḥ iti naiyāyikaiḥ abhyupagamāt tatas eva tad bhāva bhāvi tvena kārya utpatteḥ te api sahakāriṇaḥ pratyayāḥ yadi akṣaṇikāḥ teṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ anivārita eva iti kṣaṇikatā eva eka artha kriyā pratiniyama lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam icchataḥ abhyupeyāḥ 
HBṬ_2.40.2	 punar api akṣaṇikānām eka artha kriyā pratiniyamam nirākartum upacaya hetum āha api ca ityādi yaḥ asau akṣaṇikaḥ bhāvaḥ sakaleṣu sahakāriṣu sva kāryam karoti itīṣyate sa tadā eva tāvat kasmāt karoti  yena hi kāraṇena tad kārya kriyā svabhāva tvena tadā karoti tena eva sthira svabhāva tvāt prāk api kuryāt tatas kutas asya eka artha kriyā pratiniyamaḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_2.40.3	 kāca anyām ṛgyate yuktiḥ yathātat dṛśyate tathā iti sarvatra iyam apratihatā yuktiḥ iti manyamānaḥ kumārilaḥ prāha kurvan dṛṣṭaḥ ityādi yatas tadā eva kāryam kurvan dṛṣṭaḥ mayā tena darśana balena karoti iti brūmaḥ kim atra anyayā upapattyā abhihitayā  prāk tat kurvan na dṛṣṭaḥ tena na karoti iti eka artha kriyā pratiniyamaḥ sidhyati akṣaṇikānām api iti bhāvaḥ hi kāryam karoti tad janana svabhāva tayā na darśana balena adṛṣṭasya api sva kārya karaṇāt atas na idam uttaram sambadhyate iti upahasan āha aho mahā sāmarthyam ityādi mahā prabhāvasya bhavataḥ mahā sāmarthyam darśanam yasmāt etat bhāvān kārya karaṇa svabhāva vikalān api yadi kārya karaṇa svabhāva tvāt bhāvāḥ kāryam kuryuḥ tadā etat eva uttaram kim na uktam  yatas kārya karaṇe darśanam uttarīkṛtam iti kṛtvā svabhāva mātreṇa ātma sattā mātreṇa 
HBṬ_2.40.4	 nānā prākāreṣu vyāpāreṣu niyuṅkte tat katham mahā sāmarthyam na syāt  na ca atra me kācid akṣamā kintu yadi nāma kiñcid kāranam kathañcid anādṛtasya vā vyākṣiptasya vā atrabhavataḥ iti pūjā vacanam darśanasya viṣaya tām atikrāmet tadā hantaḥ iti dainya udbhāvanam etat aprasavaḥ dharmaḥ asya tat idam aprasava dharmakam tatas apeta santānam syāt iti iyam asmākam cintā cittam dunoti 
HBṬ_2.40.5	 paraḥ āha na vai vayam ityādi na eva vayam kārya karaṇa svabhāva rahitānām bhāvānām asmat darśana vaśāt kāṛya kriyāṃbrūmaḥ kintu svabhāvena eva te bhāvāḥ tad kārya karaṇa svabhāvāḥ tatas sva kāryam kurvanti tān paśyantaḥ kevalaṃjānīmahe te ete kāraka svabhāvāḥ iti darśanasya hi yathā avasthita vastu vijñāne vyāpāraḥ na avidyamāna svabhāva kriyāyām iti 
HBṬ_2.40.6	 siddhānta vādi āha satyam idam api asti kim vayam nyāya anurāgitayā nyāyyam vacanam upalakṣayāmaḥ uta bhavān eva sarvadā nyāyya vacana rahitaḥ api kathañcid nyāyyam uktavān iti sañjāta paritoṣaḥ pṛcchati kim tat iti āha svabhāvaḥ teṣām bhāvānām kārya kriyā dharmā kārya karaṇa dharmā tena kāraṇena samastāh samagrāḥ pratyayāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ yeṣām teṣām akṛtvā kāryam na upekṣā pattiḥ na audāsīni apratipattiḥ iti satyam idam api asti bhavataḥ nyāyyam vacanam iti kintu idam asi praṣṭavyaḥ saḥ akṣepa kriyā dharma asvabhāvaḥ kiṃteṣāṃtadaiva antya āvasathāyām samagra avasthāyām yad anantaram kāryam utpadyate tadā eva utpannaḥ āhosvit prāk api paraspara viraha avasthāyām api āsīt  
HBṬ_2.40.7	 tatra tadā eva utpanne tad svabhāva tve apūrva utpattiḥ eva atad svabhāva tve saḥ akārakaḥ eva iti prāc ukta doṣa bhayāt paraḥ āha āsīt kutas pracyutaḥ ca utpannaḥ ca pracyuta utpannaḥ tasya pratiṣedhaḥ apracyutaḥ anutpannaḥ sthiraḥ ekaḥ svabhāvaḥ yeṣām bhāvānām teṣām kasmiṃścid kāle kasyacid svabhāvasya tatra upalabdhasya abhāva virodhāt kṣaṇikeṣu eva hi ekadā dṛṣṭaḥ svabhāvaḥ anyadā na bhavet tadā tasya anya tvāt na apracyuta anutpanna pūrva apara rūpeṣu sthireṣu bhāveṣu iti 
HBṬ_2.40.8–2.40.9	 atra āha tat kim idānīm ityādi syāt matam na eva idam anena vākyena sadṛśam asmat vākyam iti āha kaḥ vā asya ityādi yadi etat anena tulyam na bhavati tadā sakala sahakārī avasthāyāḥ prāk api ayam akṣepa kriyā svabhāvaḥ avila mvita kārya karaṇa svabhāvaḥ kāryaṃca na karoti iti asya bhāṣitasya arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti naiyāyikāḥ tu manyante bhāvānām sahakāri sannidhāna asannidhāna apekṣayā kāraka ākāraka svabhāva vyavasthā na svabhāvataḥ tena ayam apracyuta utpanna sthira eka svabhāva tve api na prāk api sva kārya janana svabhāvaḥ kintu sannihita sakala sahakāri pratyayaḥ eva iti tat matam āśaṅkamānaḥ āha sahitaḥ ityādi 
HBṬ_2.40.10	 etat nirasyati anyaḥ tarhi ityādi yadi nāma sahitasya sva kārya janana svabhāva tā kevalasya ca tad viparīta rūpa tā anya tvam tu kasmāt bhavati iti atas āha svabhāva bhedaḥ ityādi svabhāva bhedaḥ eva hi bhāva bhedasya lakṣaṇam sa ced tad kārya jana kājanaka rūpa tayā bhidyate śāli yava bīja ādīnām iva katham iva bhāva bhedaḥ na syāt  na hi svabhāvāt anyaḥ bhāvaḥ yatas tad bhede api na bhidyeta niḥsvabhāvatā prasaṅgāt 
HBṬ_2.40.11–2.40.12^1	 nanu ca uktam svatas jana kājanaka svabhāva tā virahāt pratyaya antara bhāva ādi apekṣa tvāt janakājanaka rūpa tāyāḥ tad bhede api kutas bhāva bheda prasaṅgaḥ  tasya apara apekṣa svabhāva bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt iti atas āha na hi sa sāhitye api ityādi tadā etat uttaram bhāvatkam sambadhyeta yadi bhāvaḥ yaḥ asau paraḥ sahakāritva abhimataḥ sannidhīyate tad rūpeṇa karttā syāt na svarūpeṇa na ca etat asti tathā abhāve hi paramārthataḥ saḥ eva paraḥ karttā syāt tatra tu kartṛ tva vyapadeśaḥ kalpanā nirmitaḥ eva bhavet 
HBṬ_2.40.11–2.40.12^2	 na ca kalpanā anuvidhāyin yaḥ artha kriyāḥ na hi māṇavakaḥ dahana upacārāt ādhīyate pāke tatas ca na asya anupakāriṇaḥ bhāvam apekṣeta kāryam iti tad rahitebhyaḥ eva saha kāribhyaḥ bhavet yat vā tebhyaḥ api na bhavet teṣām api para rūpeṇa kartṛ tve svayam akāraka tvāt tatas sarveṣām evam svayam akāraka tve para rūpeṇa api akāraka tvāt sarvathā kāraka uchedaḥ eva iti na kiñcid kutaścid jāyeta tasmāt sva rūpeṇa eva bhāvaḥ sva kāryasya karttā na para rūpeṇa iti na asya uttarasya avakāśaḥ tatas anyaḥ sahitaḥ anyaḥ ca kevalaḥ iti etat avicalam eva iti 
HBṬ_2.40.13	 atha yena svarūpeṇa ayam janakaḥ tat asya sahita asahita avasthayoḥ sarvadā asti tadā svarūpam ca sva kārya janakam asya sthira svabhāvasya prāk api sahita avasthāyāḥ tat eva yat sahita avasthāyām akṣepa kriyā svabhāvam iti tasmāt na kathaṃcid kārya kriyā virāmaḥ athavā kadācid paraḥ brūyāt sva hetubhiḥ eva ayam pratyaya antara apekṣaḥ sva kārya janana svabhāvaḥ janitaḥ iti kevalaḥ na karoti na ca asya sahita asahita avasthayoḥ svabhāva bhedaḥ pratyaya antara apekṣa sva kārya janana svabhāva tāyāḥ sarvadā bhāvāt iti atas āha na hi sa sāhitye api ityādi sva rūpeṇa eva asya kartṛ tvāt tasya ca prāk api bhāvāt pratyaya antara apekṣāyāś ca tatas labhyasya ātma atiśayasya abhāvena ayogāt upakāra lakṣaṇa tvāt asya anyathā ati prasaṅgāt kevalasya kārya karaṇam anivāryam iti akurvataḥ katham sahita avasthāyāḥ na bhedaḥ syāt iti bhāvaḥ pratyaya antara apekṣa sva kārya karaṇa svabhāvaḥ iti api para rūpeṇa ākārasya 
HBṬ_2.40.14	 pratyaya antara sannidhāna upalakṣita kāle kāraka tvam na prāk iti ayam arthaḥ tatas ca kadācid kārya kriyā svabhāvaḥ na sarvadā iti bruvatā katham sarvadā kārya janana svabhāva tā asya uktā bhavati  nanu evam svabhāva bhedaḥ eva asya tad atad kālayoḥ samarthitaḥ syāt tasmāt na akṣaṇikānām eka artha kriyā pratiniyama lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam iti sthitam 
HBṬ_2.40.15	 paraḥ samāna doṣa tām āpādayan āha yasya api ityādi su bodham yadi nāma kṣaṇikaḥ tathā api kinna bhavati iti āha uktaṃyādṛśasya saha kāribhiḥ apṛthak bhāvinaḥ kriyā te samarthāḥ eva svabhāvataḥ antyāḥ pratyayāḥ saha jāyante kṣaṇikāḥ yeṣām prāk paścāt pṛthak bhāvaḥ na asti iti atra sa katham eka kṣaṇa bhāvī ekasmin eva antye kṣaṇe bhavana śilaḥ anyathā abhavet antya kṣaṇāt prāk paścāt pṛthak vā bhavet yaḥ cā anyathā bhavati saḥ eva antyakṣaṇa bhāvī sahakāri santāna upakṛta svabhāvaḥ a kṣepa kriyā dharmā na bhavati iti na ayam akṣaṇika pakṣa uditaḥ prasaṅgaḥ kṣaṇika pakṣe kutas  kāraka ākārakayoḥ ityādi kārakaḥ antyaḥ akārakaḥ tad anyaḥ tayoḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa bhinnaḥ api bheda avivakṣaya eka tvena uktaḥ tathā kārakasya 
HBṬ_2.40.16	 yaḥ hetuḥ upāntyaḥ akārakasya api yaḥ hetuḥ tad anyaḥ sa bhinnaḥ api abheda vivakṣayā eva eka tvena uktaḥ tena kāraka ākārakayoḥ yau svabhāvau tayoḥ ekatra dharmiṇi virodhāt tathā tayoḥ svabhāvayoḥ janakau yau hetū ekaḥ kāraka svabhāva janakaḥ anyaḥ ca ākāraka svabhāva janakaḥ tayoḥ api ekatra dharmiṇi virodhāt anya tve sati akāraka svabhāva janaka hetoḥ utpannasya ākārakasya svabhāvasya anya tvāt yaḥ ca bhavati saḥ eva na bhavati iti na ayaṃprasaṅgaḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.41.1	 aparaḥ tu anyathā sthira rūpeṣu eka artha akriyā pratiniyamam kalpitavān tam upanyasyati yaḥ api manyate ityādi bhāvasya hi akṣepa kriyā dharmā eva sarvadā svabhāvaḥ na tu yathā kecid bruvate sahakāri sannidhāna apekṣā vastūnām kāraka svabhāva vyavasthā na svatas iti svatas akārakātve para rūpeṇa kāraka tva ayogāt kāraka vyavasthā uccheda prasaṅgāt saḥ evaṃvidha svabhāvaḥ na kadācid sāhityam sva kārya karaṇe apekṣate yatas anyaḥ sahitaḥ anyaḥ ca kevalaḥ kāraka ākāraka svabhāva bhedāt syāt sa tarhi sarvadā tad svabhāvaḥ kāryam kin na karoti iti ced kāryasya pratyaya antara apekṣa svabhāvatayā tasmin sarvadā janakatvena avasthite api kevalāt abhāvāt tena atra kāryam eva aparādhyati yat tasmin kevale janakatayā avasthite api pratyaya antarāṇi apekṣate iti tatas tad ā ātmanaḥ kāryasya sahitebhyaḥ eva bhāvāt eka artha kriyā lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam akṣaṇikānām 
HBṬ_2.41.2	 api upapadyate iti siddhānta vādī pūrva doṣa anatikramam asya darśayan āha tasya api evaṃvādināḥ kathaṃsa nitya abhimataḥ bhāvaḥ kevalaḥ karoti eva akṣepa kriyā dharmā eva sa tasya svabhāvaḥ iti vacanāt kāryam ca sahitebhyaḥ eva bhavati sāmagrī janya svabhāva tvāt tasya iti vacanāt tasmāt kevalāt na bhavati iti tad avasthaḥ virodhaḥ yaḥ pūrvam uktaḥ tathā hi yadi akṣepa kriyā dharmā tadā avaśyam anena kāryam kartavyam na ced avaśyam karoti katham akṣepa kriyā svabhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_2.41.3	 akṣepeṇa kārya darśanāt akṣepa kriyā svabhāva tā avagamyate na anyathā iti para abhiprāyā śaṅkayā aaha na kevalaḥ ityādi na evam mayā uktam kevalaḥ karoti eva iti kintu akṣepa kriyā svabhāvaḥ iti atra āha katham idānīm ityādi yadi karoti eva iti na iṣyate katham akṣepa kriyā svabhāvaḥ iti kathyate  atha tathā ucyate tadā nanu etat eva anena vacasā paridīpitam abhihitam bhavati kim tat  karoti eva iti saḥ eva hi akṣepa kriyā svabhāvaḥ yaḥ karoti eva yaḥ tu na avaśyam karoti sa katham tad rūpaḥ syāt  yat api uktam kāryasya eva ayam aparādhaḥ yat tasmin janakatayā avasthite pratyaya antarāṇi apekṣate iti tat api ayuktam yatas kāryam ca ayam akṣaṇikaḥ bhāvaḥ kevalaḥ api samarthaḥ san param pratyaya antaram apekṣamāṇaṃkatham upekṣeta na eva anupekṣamāṇena kim karttavyam  āha param pratyaya antaram anādṛtya tiraskṛtya etat kāryam prasahya 
HBṬ_2.41.4	 haṭhāt kuryāt kaḥ evam sati asya guṇaḥ bhavati iti ced āha evaṃhi param anādṛtya haṭhāt sva kāryam kurvatā anena kevalena api samarthena satā yat tad ātmanaḥ kevalasya api sāmarthyam tat darśitam prakāśitam bhavati anyathā anya sahitasya eva karaṇāt kevalasya ca kadācid api akaraṇāt na ayam kevalaḥ api samarthaḥ iti pareṣām buddhiḥ syāt tatas ayam tiraskṛta prabhāvaḥ iva katham bhrājeta  tasmāt ayuktam ucyate kāryam pratyaya antara apekṣam iti 
HBṬ_2.41.5	 kārya apekṣayā api virodhasya tādavasthyam darśayan āha kāryaṃparam ityādi kāryasya para apekṣām bruvan kevalāt kāraṇāt anutpattim asya kathayasi sa kevalaḥ api samarthaḥ iti idam vadan tatas kevalāt utpattim kāryasya brūṣe ete ca ekasya eva kāryasya tatas eva ekasmāt kāraṇāt utpatti anutpattī paraspara viruddhe katham ekatra kārya ākhye dharmiṇi syātām viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt ekatra te bruvāṇaḥ mātā ca vandhyā ca iti anena sadṛśam brūṣaḥ iti na pūrva ukta doṣān mucyase yatas evam api bruvāṇaḥ viruddham eva brūte na ca lakṣayati tat tasmāt ayam akṣaṇika vādī kṣaṇika pakṣasya anavadya tayā tad vādinām nirddoṣa tā sampatsu amarṣa lakṣaṇa īrṣyā eva śalyam antar duḥkha hetu tvāt tena vitudyamānāni vyathyamānāni marmāṇi yasya saḥ yam īrṣyā śalya vitudyamāna marmā varākaḥ asvastha citta tayā viruddha abhidhānam 
HBṬ_2.41.6–2.41.7	 api alakṣayan viklavam ākulam pūrva apara asambaddham vikrośati viroditi iti kṛtvā asvastha citta vacaneṣu anādarāt tad doṣa udbhāvanasya sutarām duḥkha utpādanena kṣata kṣāra niṣeka tulya tvāt upekṣām eva vipaścitām kṛpā dhanānām arhati iti tat evam akṣaṇikeṣu na kathañcid eka artha kriyā pratiniyama lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam sambhavati iti pratipādya upasaṃhāran āha tasmāt idam ityādi yeṣām hi sthira rūpa tayā pṛthak api bhāvaḥ sambhavati teṣām akṣaṇikānām pṛthak kevalānām kārya karaṇa sambhavena hetunā saha eva kurvanti iti sahakāri tva niyama ayogāt idam eka artha kriyā lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam kṣaṇikānām eva teṣām sva hetu pariṇāma upanidhi dharmāṇām paraspara upādāna sahakāri pratyaya eka sāmagrī janyānām pṛthak asambhavāt 
HBṬ_2.42.1^1	 nanu atiśaya utpādana lakṣaṇam api sahakāri tvam bhāveṣu dṛśyate tat katham uktam prāk sarvatra na eva atiśaya utpādanam sahakriyā kim tarhi bahūnām eka artha karaṇam eva iti atas āha yatra tu santāna upakāreṇa ityādi eka artha kriyā lakṣaṇam eva sahakāri tvam sarvatra na kvacid atiśaya utpādanam sambhavati yatra tu santāna upakāreṇa pūrva pūrva pratyayebhyaḥ viśiṣṭa viśiṣṭatara uttara uttarakṣaṇa jananena bhāvāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ vivakṣita kāryasya hetu tām pratipadyante yathā taṇḍula ādibhyaḥ odana ādi janmani dahana udaka ādayaḥ bīja ādibhyaḥ ca aṅkura ādi janmani pṛthivī ādayaḥ tatra viśeṣa utpādane pratyayānām sahakriyā ucyate loke 
HBṬ_2.42.1^2	 santāna āśrayeṇa pūrva kṣaṇebhyaḥ dvitīya ādi viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa lakṣaṇam santāna ākhyam kāryam āśritya pūrva uttara kṣaṇayoḥ eka tva adhyavasāyena tasya eva ayam atiśayaḥ iti na dravya āśrayeṇa aupacārikam eva na tu pāramārthikam pūrva pūrvakṣaṇebhyaḥ tu sva hetu pariṇāma upanidhi dharmabhyaḥ uttarottara viśeṣa utpattau pūrva kāraṇa kalāpasya eka artha kriyā lakṣaṇam eva tatra paramārthataḥ sahakāri tvam iti na kācid kṣatiḥ iti kasmāt dravya āśrayeṇa atiśaya utpādanam na iṣyate  kṣaṇike dravye vastuni viśeṣasya anutpatteḥ tasya ananta rakṣaṇa bhāva rūpa tvāt 
HBṬ_2.42.2–2.42.5	 yadi tarhi kṣaṇike taṇḍula ādi dravye viśeṣaḥ na utpadyate anantaram api asau mā bhūt tatas yathā para sparataḥ viśeṣam anāsādayantaḥ api kṣaṇikāḥ sahitāḥ eva kurvanti na kevalāḥ evam akṣaṇikāḥ api tena eṣām eka artha kriyā lakṣaṇam eva sahakāri tvam bhaviṣyati na ca śakyam vaktum yaḥ yasya prāk akārakaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa paścāt api iti tathā hi prabhāsvarāt apavarakam praviṣṭasya indriyam artha pratipattim akurvat api paścāt kurvāṇam upalabhyate tat uktam na hi praviṣṭa mātrāṇām uṣṇāt garbhagṛha ādiṣu arthāna pratibhānti iti gṛhyante na indriyaiḥpunar iti 
HBṬ_2.42.6	 atas āha na hi taṇḍula ādīnām ityādi viśeṣa anutpattau sannidhānasya api asannidhāna tulya tvāt dahana ādi bhāve api taṇḍula ādibhyaḥ na odana janma syāt tathā prabhāsvarāt apavarakam praviṣṭasya yadi indriyam sva upakāribhyaḥ atiśayam krameṇa na pratipadyate tadā prāk iva paścāt api artha pratipattim na eva janayet tasmāt yat asambhavi kāryam yatra dṛśyate tasya tatas anya tvam eva śāli bījāt iva kodrava bījasya iti niratiśayāt anya tvam eva sa atiśaya tayā tad kārya kāriṇaḥ iti evam tāvat yatra saha kāribhyaḥ krameṇa kāryam bhavati tatra atiśaya utpādana lakṣaṇam aupacārikam sahakāri tvam eka artha kriyā lakṣaṇam eva tu mukhyam tatra api iti pratipāditam 
HBṬ_2.42.7	 yatra tu akṣepeṇa eva artha sannidhi mātreṇa sahakāriṇaḥ kāryam kurvanti kim tatra api santāna āśrayam atiśaya utpādanam asti iti atas āha akṣepa kāriṣu ityādi ye hi avyavadhāna ādi deśāḥ indriya ādayaḥ sva hetubhyaḥ jātāḥ teṣu avilambita kāriṣu na viśeṣa utpattiḥ parasparataḥ sambhavati kṣaṇika tvāt iti uktam prāk 
HBṬ_2.42.8	 yadi na viśeṣa utpattiḥ tadā katham nirviśeṣāḥ jñānasya kāraṇī bhavanti iti atas āha tatra yathāsvam yasya ye ātmīyāḥ pratyayāḥ taiḥ paraspara upasarppaṇa vyavadhāna ādi viraha ādeḥ āśraya bhūtaiḥ ye jātāḥ yogyaḥ ca asau= ati āsanna tva ati vipra karṣa virahāt deśaḥ ca saḥ ādiḥ yasya avyavahita deśa ādeḥ tatra avasthānam avasthā yeṣām te saha svabhāva niṣpattyā svabhāva niṣpattiḥ vidyate iti eva kṛtvā jṇāna hetu tāṃ pratipadyante tatra kim parasparataḥ viśeṣa utpattyā prārthitayā  yadi hi sva hetubhyaḥ eva paraspara upasarppaṇa ādya aśrebhyaḥ sva kārya janana kṣamā yogya deśa ādi avasthāna lakṣaṇa viśeṣa yoginaḥ na utpadyeran tadā eṣām parasparataḥ viśeṣa utpattiḥ prārthyeta na tu sva hetubhyaḥ eva tathāvidhānām utpattau yatas evam iti tasmāt tatra teṣu akṣepa kāriṣu indriya ādiṣu eka artha kriyā eva mukhyam sahakāri tvam na santāna āśrayeṇa 
HBṬ_2.42.9–2.42.10	 vyavasthāpyamānam atiśaya utpādana lakṣaṇam gauṇam iti atha viśeṣa utpādana lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam katham na vyavasthāpyate  tat api hi loke pratīta tvāt vyavasthāpanīyam eva iti atas āha yatra tu kārye na avyavadhānādi deśa upanipāta mātreṇa eva indriya ādayaḥ iva sahakāriṇaḥ pratyaya tām pratipadyante kintu vivakṣita kārya utpāda anuguṇam pratikṣaṇam prakṛṣyamāṇam viśeṣam utpādayantaḥ tatra kāla kṣepa bhāvini kārye karttavye hetu santānaḥ apara aparakṣaṇa bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ ātma atiśaya āsādana artham saha kārīṇi pratyaya antarāṇi apekṣate na tu tad samāna kālaḥ kāraṇa kṣaṇaḥ iti tatas tebhyaḥ kāraṇa antarebhyaḥ svabhāva antarasya kārya utpāda anu guṇa viśeṣa paramparā lakṣaṇasya pratilabhyaḥ santānasya eka tvena adhimuktasya ucyate loke parama arthaḥ tu tatra api pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ pratyaya kalāpaḥ uttarottara kārya utpāda anuguṇe viśiṣṭa kṣaṇe pratiniyataḥ iti eka artha kriyā lakṣaṇam eva sahakāri tvam 
HBṬ_2.42.11–2.42.12	 anubhavati kathām punar svabhāva antara pratilambhaḥ teṣām  yatas krameṇa kāryam nirvarttayanti iti atas āha tatra svarasataḥ ityādi tatra tasmin hetu santāne ye hetavaḥ upādānakāraṇa ākhyāḥ ye ca pratyayāḥ sahakāri saṃjñitāḥ teṣām ye pūrve prathame upanipāta kṣaṇāḥ teṣām vināśa hetu anapekṣi tayā svarasataḥ nivṛttau satyām tebhyaḥ eva svarasataḥ nivarttamānebhyaḥ prathama kṣaṇebhyaḥ kārya utpāda anuguṇena viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭasya kṣaṇasya utpattiḥ tebhyaḥ anuguṇatara viśeṣavatām tṛtīyakṣaṇānām tebhyonuguṇatama viśeṣavatām caturtha kṣaṇānām evam yāvat atyanta atiśayavān antyaḥ kāraṇa kalāpaḥ jātaḥ tatas kāryasya utpattiḥ iti evam saha kāribhyaḥ svabhāva antara pratilambhaḥ kṣepavatī ca kārya utpattiḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.42.13	 atra paraḥ codayan āha sahakāriṇaḥ saha karaṇa śīlāt kāraṇāt jātau eka vacanam yat samutpanna viśeṣam anantara uktena prakāreṇa kāraṇam antya sāmagrī kṣaṇa lakṣaṇam tatas aṅkura ādi kārya utpattau iṣyamāṇāyām tasya eva viśeṣasya ādyasya kārya utpādana anuguṇasya yaḥ krameṇa abhivarddhamānaḥ kāryasya janakaḥ iṣyate tasya eva utpattiḥ na syāt prathama kṣaṇa upanipātinām para sparataḥ viśeṣa an āsādanāt kṣaṇānām avivekāt anabhyupagamāt ca 
HBṬ_2.42.14	 parasparataḥ anavāpta viśeṣāḥ eva kārya utpādana anuguṇam viśeṣam ārapsyante iti ced āha aviśiṣṭāt aviśiṣṭebhyaḥ para sparataḥ viśeṣasya kārya utpāda anuguṇasya utpattau iṣyamāṇāyām kāryasya aṅkura ādeḥ syāt viśeṣa abhāvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ tatas ca parasparataḥ viśeṣa utpāda anapekṣiṇaḥ eva sahakāriṇaḥ kāryam kurvīran 
HBṬ_2.42.15	 kim evam sati siddham bhavati iti ced āha tena yena kṣaṇikāḥ api para sparataḥ viśeṣa utpādāḥ anapekṣāḥ eva sva kāryam kurvanti eka kārya pratiniyama lakṣaṇam ca sahakāri tvam pratipadyante tena kāraṇena akṣaṇikānām api kāraṇa tā āsyāt apekṣaṇīyebhyaḥ svabhāva atiśaya utpattiḥ ca na syāt iti akṣaṇika vādī kṣaṇika pakṣeṇa sva pakṣasya sāmyam āpādayati yat āha 
HBṬ_2.42.16–2.42.21	 kaḥśobheta vadan= evaṃyadi na syāt ahnīka tā ajña tau= āyataḥ sarvaṃkṣaṇikeṣu api tad samam viśeṣa hetavaḥ teṣāṃ pratyayāna kathañcana nityānām iva yujyante kṣaṇānām avivekataḥ iti tatra etat syāt prathama kṣaṇe api kṣiti bīja ādayaḥ parasparataḥ samutpanna viśeṣāḥ eva sannidhīyante yena yasya abhisambhandhaḥ dūra sthasya api tena saḥ 
HBṬ_2.42.22	 iti nyāyāt dhi dūra deśa varttinām api hetu phala bhāvāt iti āśaṅkya āha atha sahakāriṇā ityādi sahakāriṇaḥ paraspara samparkka vikalāḥ api vastu dharma tayā eva anyonyam upakurvanti iti sahakāriṇā kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa jananāya kṛta viśeṣaḥ eva samparkka kāle upatiṣṭheta evam sati anavasthā syāt tathā hi tad viśeṣa utpattau api aparaḥ sahakāri kṛtaḥ viśeṣaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tathā tad utpattau api anyaḥ iti 
HBṬ_2.42.23	 atha na evam sahakāriṇaḥ parasparasya kārya utpāda anu guṇa viśeṣa nimittam aparam viśeṣam kurvanti svabhāvataḥ eva tatra teṣām yogya tvāt iti atas āha na ca ityādi na eva hi sahakāriṇaḥ kṣiti bīja ādayaḥ parasparasya kārya utpāda anuguṇaḥ yaḥ viśeṣaḥ tad utpādane nityam sarvakālam yogyā avasthā yena yogyā avastha tvena nitya anuśaktaḥ nitya anubaddhaḥ eṣām kṣiti bīja ādīnām kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa janakaḥ viśeṣaḥ syāt yatas aviśiṣtāt viśeṣa utpattau kāryasya api syāt iti etat api parihriyeta 
HBṬ_2.42.24–2.42.25^1	 kutas etat iti āha tad upāyaḥ ityādi teṣām kṣiti bīja ādīnām upāye yogya deśa upanipāte kārya vyakti darśanāt apāye ca paraspara samparkka virāme kārya anutpatti darśanāt yadi hi kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa utpādane sarvadā yogyā avasthāḥ syuḥ tadā saḥ api viśeṣaḥ sarvadā syāt tatas tad paramparā bhāvi kāryam iti tad upāya apāyayoḥ kāryasya utpatti anutpattī na syātām tasmāt na sahakāriṇaḥ kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa utpādane yogyā avasthāḥ sarvadā iti yatas sahakāriṇā pṛthak avasthitena anavasthā bhayāt kṛta viśeṣaḥ na upatiṣṭhate parasparataḥ ca prathama samparkkakṣaṇa bhāvinām na upeyate yujyate vā 
HBṬ_2.42.24–2.42.25^2	 tena kāraṇena ādyaḥ viśeṣaḥ kārya utpāda anuguṇaḥ saha kāribhyaḥ samāna kāla tayā nirupakārasya kṣiti bīja ādeḥ na utpadyate utpadyate ca asau iti iṣyate tena samagra avasthāvat sarveṣām vyagra avasthā bhāvinām api kṣaṇānām aviśeṣāt tad janana svabhāva tve api ajananāt samagra avasthāyām eva jananāt yathā kṣaṇikānām eka artha kriyā pratiniyama lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam tathā sthira svabhāvānām api bhaviṣyati iti kṣīṇa sarva upāyaḥ akṣaṇika vādī sāmyam eva āturaḥ iva bahu manyamānaḥ tatra eva bharam kṛtavān 
HBṬ_2.42.26–2.42.27	 siddhānta vādī bhaṅgyā param upahasan āha na asmākaṃpunar punar ityādi yadi punar punar vacane api lokasya nyāya pratītiḥ bhavati śataśas api brūmaḥ kim aṅga punar dvau trīn vā vārān  na hi para artha pravṛttānām asmākam punar punar abhidhāne kaścid udvegaḥ bhavati evam vādinaḥ ca śāstra kṛtaḥ kvacid prakāra antareṇa tam eva artham sphuṭīkurvataḥ ye punar uktā parihārāya yat ante sa teṣām asthāna pariśramaḥ eva yadi na udvegaḥ hanta tarhi ucyatām iti atas āha na viśeṣa utpādanāt eva ityādi na eva viśeṣa utpādanāt sahakāriṇām sahakāri tvam paramārthataḥ kvacid sambhavati yatas prathama kṣaṇa bhāvinām bīja ādīnām tad abhāvāt kārya utpāda anuguṇe viśeṣe karttavye saha kāritā virahaḥ syāt kintu eka artha kriyā eva sahakāriṇām pāramārthikam sahakāri tvam pūrva uktābhiḥ yuktibhiḥ sambhāvyate sā ca prathama samparkka bhājām asti eva iti kim na sahakāriṇaḥ syuḥ  
HBṬ_2.42.28^1	 paraḥ āha sā api eka artha kriyā na bhavet parasparataḥ viśeṣa rahitānām yadi punar parasparataḥ viśeṣa rahitānām api tad eka artha kriyā aṅgīkriyate tadā pratyekam tad avasthāyām tad utpādana sāmarthya abhyupagamāt tad avasthāyām iva pṛthak api sā bhavet tathā hi te tad avasthāyām api parasparataḥ nirviśeṣāḥ eva kurvanti teṣām pṛthak api tad viśeṣa kriyā katham iva na prasajyeta  na hi eṣām saṃhata asaṃhata avasthayoḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti iti bhavatu kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced tathā ca kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣasya pṛthakkaraṇa prasaṅge sati tasmāt viśeṣāt bhavana śīlam aṅkura ādi kāryam api viśeṣa vat kevalāt sahakāriṇaḥ syāt iti ced manyase atra api sarvam uktam uttaram tathā hi saṃhata asaṃhata avasthayoḥ nirviśeṣāḥ eva kṣaṇa kṣayiṇaḥ bhāvāḥ iti tat ucyate tat kim tāvat viśeṣa mātra apekṣayā āhosvit kārya utpāda anu guṇa viśeṣa janaka viśeṣa apekṣayā  yadi prācyaḥ vikalpaḥ tat ayuktam 
HBṬ_2.42.28^2	 na hi kācid viśeṣa mātra rahitā avasthā sambhavati sarvadā apara apara pratyaya yoga nibandhanasya apara apara viśeṣasya bhāvāt na hi kadācid kiṃcid ekam eva ādhāra= chāyā ātapa vāta śīta ādeḥ yathāsambhavam bhāvāt na ca tabhāve api tat tādṛśam eva kāraṇa bhedāt etāvat tu syāt kaścid viśeṣaḥ kvacid kārye anuguṇaḥ na sarvaḥ sarvatra iti etat ca prāk eva uktam iti darśayan āha pratikṣaṇam apara aparaiḥ pratyayaiḥ iti apara apara pratyaya yogena pratikṣaṇam bhinna śaktayaḥ saṃskārāḥ santanvantaḥ yadi api kutaścid sāmyāt sarūpāḥ pratīyante tathā api bhinnaḥ eva eṣām svabhāvaḥ tena kiñcid eva kasyacid kāraṇam iti kṣaṇikeṣu bhāveṣu apara apara utpatteḥ aikya abhāvāt iti ca atra saṃkṣiptataram uktam evam ca na asmākam punar punar vacanaḥ iti atra dvis punar grahaṇam yujyate yathā yena prakāreṇa bhāva santāneviśeṣasya utpattiḥ tat api uktam 
HBṬ_2.42.29	 tatra svarasataḥ pūrva kṣaṇa nirodhe tebhyaḥ eva viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa utpādāt viśeṣa utpattiḥ iti atha kārya utpāda anu guṇa viśeṣa janaka viśeṣa apekṣayā prāgvat prathama samparkka bhājaḥ parasparataḥ nirviśeṣāḥ iti abhimatam tat api ayuktam yatas kārya utpāda anuguṇasya viśeṣasya janakāḥ kṣiti bīja ādayaḥ kīdṛśāḥ ye vyavadhāna ādi rahita tvena upanipātinaḥ tad bhāvaḥ eva tasya bhāvāt etāvat mātra nibandhana tvāt ca janaka vyavasthāyāḥ te ca tathāvidhāḥ sarvadā na bhavantī katham pṛthak api kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa ārambhaḥ eṣām syāt  yatas kevalānām api kārya kriyā prasajyeta tat darśayati yogyaḥ deśaḥ yeṣām te yogya deśāḥ tad bhāvaḥ yogya deśa tā sā ādiḥ yeṣām avyavahita deśa tva ādīnām avasthā bhedānām te tathā uktāḥ te ca te avasthā bhedāḥ ca tathā uktāḥ yogya deśa tā ādya vyavahita deśatā ādayaḥ ye avasthā viśeṣāḥ 
HBṬ_2.42.30	 kṣiti bīja ādīnām upajāyante te kārya utpāda anu guṇa viśeṣa lakṣaṇa kārya karaṇa śīlāḥ na evaṃvidhāḥ sarvadā bīja ādayaḥ iti katham eṣām pṛthak api tathāvidha viśeṣa ārambhaḥ syāt  etat api prāk eva uktam tatra yaḥ avyavadhāna ādi deśaḥ rūpa indriya ādi kalāpaḥ sa vijñāna janane samarthaḥ hetuḥ iti vacanāt tasya ca udāharaṇa mātra tvāt iha api tatra yaḥ avyavadhāna ādi deśaḥ kṣiti bīja ādi kalāpaḥ sa kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa janane samarthaḥ hetuḥ iti pratīyate eva sa ca tathāvidhaḥ viśeṣaḥ sarvadā na bhavati tad janakasya hetoḥ abhāvāt paraspara upasarppaṇa ādi āśrayasya eva pratyaya viśeṣasya tad hetu tvāt etat api pūrvam eva uktam iti āha teṣām ca kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa janane viśeṣavatām yatas utpattiḥ tat api uktam asakṛt eva yaḥ teṣām paraspara upasarppaṇa ādi āśrayaḥ pratyaya viśeṣaḥ sa tad hetu janane samarthaḥ hetuḥ iti tathā yathāsvam pratyayaiḥ paraspara upasarppaṇa āśrayaiḥ 
HBṬ_2.42.31	 ye yogya deśa ādi avasthāḥ jātāḥ te saha svabhāva niṣpattyā jñāna hetu tām pratipadyante iti anena iha api gamyamāna tvāt tatas yadi api eṣām parasparataḥ anupapatteḥ viśeṣaḥ na bhavati sva hetu kṛtaḥ tu kena vāryate  na ca sva hetutaḥ eva sañjāta viśeṣāṇām bhāve parasparataḥ tad āśaṃsā yatas para sparataḥ viśeṣa ayogaḥ pratipādyamānaḥ śobheta teṣām ca kārya utpāda anu guṇa viśeṣa janakānām pratyayānām pratyekam sāmarthye api khaṇḍaśas kārya utpāda ayogāt sakalasya eva pratyekam karaṇāt yathā kevalānām akriyā kartṛ viśeṣasya avyavadhāna ādi deśa kṣiti bīja ādi kalāpasya pṛthak ekaikasya samarthasya bhāvasya abhāvāt iti etat api asakṛt eva uktam teṣām ca na pūrvam na paścāt na pṛthak bhāvaḥ iti samarthānā api pūrva apara pṛthak bhāva bhāvinaḥ doṣāḥ na upalīyante ityādi vacanāt tatas tathāvidha viśeṣasya sva upādāna mātra nibandhanasya anabhyupagamena kevalānām 
HBṬ_2.42.32–2.42.33	 aprasaṅgāt kutas kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa ārambha dvārakam kāryam api syāt iti  kutas punar ayam kāma cāraḥ labhyate yat aṅkura ādi kāryam sahakāriṇaḥ parasparasya kārya utpāda anuguṇām viśeṣa paramparām janayantaḥ kurvanti kārya utpāda anuguṇam tu viśeṣam vyavadhāna ādi rahita deśa upanipāta mātreṇa iti atas āha kārya dvaividhyaṃca yasmāt tasmāt evaṃvibhajyate katham dvaividhyam kāryāṇām iti atas āha sahakāribhiḥ avyavadhāna ādi deśaiḥ anantaram san janitāḥ parasparasya prāc avastha apekṣa viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa bhāva lakṣaṇāḥ ye viśeṣāḥ tad paramparayā uttarottara viśiṣṭa viśiṣṭa tara ādi kṣaṇa bhāva rūpayā utpattiḥ ddharmaḥ yasya tad ātmakam ekam kāryam anyat ca tad viparītam yat sahakāri sannidhi mātreṇa bhavati na paraspara kṛtām viśeṣa paramparām apekṣate atra udāharaṇam aṅkura ādi vat ādi grahaṇāt odana ādi vat tathā akṣepeṇa karaṇa śīlam yat indriyam tad vijñāna ādi vat ca prabhāsvarāt apavaraka praviṣṭa indriya nirāsa artham 
HBṬ_2.42.34	 ca etat viśeṣaṇam kutas etat iti ced kārya kāraṇayoḥ svabhāva bhedāt kiṃcid dhi kāryam kāraṇa sāmagrī sannidhi mātra janya svabhāvam tat anyat tu tad pariṇāma apekṣam iti kāraṇam api kiñcid sva sannidhi mātreṇa kārya janana svabhāvam sva kāraṇebhyaḥ eva bhavati yena paraspara kṛtām viśeṣa paramparām sva kārya karaṇe na apekṣate anyat tu tad viparīta svabhāvam yathā kiñcid eva śāli aṅkura janana svabhāvam tad viparītam ca aparam śāli aṅkuraḥ ca tat bīja janya svabhāvaḥ na yava ādi bīja janya svabhāvaḥ iti na bhāvānām sva hetu bala āyātāḥ pramāṇa adhigatāḥ svābhāvāḥ paryanuyojyāḥ ye tu yat janana svabhāvāḥ pramāṇataḥ adhigatāḥ te kim sarvadā eva tad svabhāvāḥ āhosvit tadā eva iti atra cintā pravarttate tatra sarvadā tad svabhāva tve paścāt iva prāk api tad kārya kriyā prasaṅgena para rūpeṇa ākārakasya bhinna svabhāva tā kāraka ākāraka avasthāyoḥ śāli yava bīja ādīnām iva tattva cintakaiḥ 
HBṬ_2.42.35	 ucyate sadṛśa apara bhāva nibandhanam ca ekatayā pratyabhijñānam lūna punar jāteṣu iva keśa nakha ādiṣu iti atra virodha abhāvāt iti yadā ca tad kārya kāraṇa svabhāva bhedāt kārya dvaividhyam tatra etasmin sati saha kāribhyaḥ kṣiti bīja ādibhyaḥ teṣām paraspara santāna upakāram apekṣate yat kāraṇam antyavasthā prāptam tasya yat kāryam aṅkura ādikam tad janma nimittam sahakāriṇām prathama kṣaṇa anantaram viśiṣṭa dvitī ya kṣaṇa bhāva rūpaḥ yaḥ viśeṣaḥ kārya utpāda anu guṇaḥ ādyaḥ bhavati sa teṣām sahakāriṇām prathama samparkka bhājām paraspara kṛtaḥ yaḥ viśeṣaḥ tad janmā na bhavati paraspara upasarppaṇa ādi āśrayāt eva pratyaya viśeṣāt tasya bhāvāt tatas kārya utpāda anu guṇāt ādyāt viśeṣāt prathama kṣaṇa upanipātibhiḥ sahakāribhiḥ anyatas samāsādita viśeṣaiḥ janitāt tad prabhṛti ye viśeṣāḥ 
HBṬ_2.42.36	 prakṛṣyamāṇa tad uttara uttara kṣaṇa bhāva lakṣaṇāḥ jāyante te tad janmānaḥ sahakāri kṛta viśeṣa janmānaḥ kutas tad prakṛti tvāt tasya ādyasya viśeṣasya paraspara upasarppaṇa ādi āśrayāt pratyaya viśeṣāt āsādita tad anukūla viśeṣaiḥ saha kāribhiḥ paraspara upakāra nirapekṣaiḥ janya svabhāva tvāt tad uttareṣām ca viśeṣāṇām sahakāri kṛta kārya utpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa janya svabhāva tvāt yatas evam iti tasmāt na anavasthā prāk uktāḥ atha sahakāriṇā kṣiti ādinā kuśūla ādi avasthaḥ api bīja ādiḥ tena api kṣiti ādiḥ kṛta viśeṣaḥ eva upatiṣtheta an avasthā evaṃsyāt iti tasya prakārasya anabhyupabgamāt puruṣa prayatna ādeḥ eva kṣetra prakiraṇa hetoḥ avyavahita snigdha pṛthivī bīja samparkka lakṣaṇasya kārya upāda anu guṇa viśeṣa janakasya viśeṣe asya upagamāt tatra yat uktam pareṇa yathā prathama sampartta bhājaḥ kṣiti bīja ādayaḥ parasparasya viśeṣa m anāt 
HBṬ_2.42.37	 adhānāh kārya utpāda anuguṇam viśeṣam janayanti tathā sthira rūpāḥ api bhāvāḥ tad eka kārya pratiniyatāḥ paraspara kṛta viśeṣa nirapekṣāḥ eva bhāviṣyanti iti tad abhyupagacchan āha tathā āyadi akṣaṇikaḥ api ityādi kṣaṇika vat akṣaṇikaḥ api yadi kāryam karoti karotu nāma na kaścid vārayati kintu yena svabhāvena kāryam karoti sa yadi avilambita kārya kartṛ dharmā apekṣeṇa karoti iti evaṃśīlaḥ dharmaḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ tadā pṛthak bhāvasya sambhavāt kevalaḥ api na kevalam sahitaḥ tathā āsyāt tad kārya kārakaḥ syāt iti uktam bahuśas atatsvabhāvaḥ tu akṣepa kartṛ svabhāva vikalaḥ tu tadā api sahita avasthāyām api prāgvat akārakaḥ eva para rūpeṇa kartṛ tvasya pūrvam eva niṣedhāt 
HBṬ_2.42.38	 tat evam eka artha kriyayā viśeṣa utpādanena ca akṣaṇikānām sahakāri tvam niṣidhya upasaṃharan āha tasmāt ityādi dvividhasya api sahakāri tvasya ayogāt na eva akṣaṇikasya kaścid sahakārī iti kevalaḥ api sva kāryam kuryāt iti sahakāri pratyaya apekṣasya akṣaṇikasya hetu tām bruvāṇasya kim yuktam iti darśayan āha prāyas tu ityādi yaḥ hi sthira hetuvādī tasya yadi sa hetuḥ pratyaya antarāṇi apekṣya kāryam karoti tadā vyaktam avaśyam tasya sthirasya hetoḥ pratyaya antara apekṣa kārakasya svabhāva antarasya utpattiḥ iti na akāryasya kārya tām ananubhavataḥ apekṣā iti ucyate yatas sahakāriṇām yaḥ saṃghātaḥ sannipātaḥ tad sthāyī tatra varttamānaḥ bhāva santānaḥ prāyas bāhulyena sahakāri pratyayaiḥ upajanita viśeṣaḥ san sva kāryaṃkurvan dṛṣṭaḥ bīja ādi vat tasmāt evam vibhajyate prāyas grahaṇam 
HBṬ_2.42.39	 ca ākṣepa kārī indriya ādi saṅghāta vyavaccheda artham tad sambhavinaḥ nyāyasya akṣaṇikeṣu pṛthak bhāva sambhavena kathañcid api kalpayitum aśakya tvāt prāgakārakasya paścāt kāraka svabhāva antara utpattiḥ tu na virudhyate tasya eva hi akārakasya tad ātmā kārakaḥ svabhāvaḥ na yujyate na tu atadātmā atas eva svabhāva antara grahaṇam tatra kevalam akāraka svabhāvasya svarasa nirodhitā mātram upeyam tatas sarvam sustham iti 
HBṬ_2.42.40	 atha matam kāraka svabhāva antara utpattiḥ iṣyate yadi sthirasya hetoḥ prāk api kāraka svabhāvaḥ na syāt tasya tu prāk api bhāvāt pratyaya antara apekṣā tad utpattiḥ api uktā iti atas āha kārakasya ityādi yadi hi samagra avasthāyāḥ prāk api kāraka svabhāvaḥ bhavet tadā asya akriyā na yujyate saṃhata avasthāyām api tad svabhāva tayā eva karaṇāt para rūpeṇa kartṛ tvasya prāk eva niṣiddha tvāt na ca karoti tasmāt saḥ asya svabhāvaḥ prāk na eva āsīt yadi ca pratyaya antaraiḥ api asau na kriyeta tat kim iti mudhā eva tāni apekṣate iti 
HBṬ_2.43.1	 tat evam tad svabhāvasya jananāt iti asya yaḥ yat svabhāvaḥ sa sva hetoḥ eva utpadyamānaḥ tādṛśaḥ bhavati na punar tad bhāve hetu antaram apekṣate iti asya anekānta parihārāya uktasya prakāra antareṇa anekānte udbhāvite tad parijihīrṣayā apara apara pratyaya yogena iti ādi abhihitam tatra yena nyāyena kṣaṇikānām hetu phala svabhāvaḥ tasya akṣaṇikeṣu asambhavam pratipādayitum prāsaṅgikam yat upakrāntam tat parisamāpayya prakṛtam anubadhnan āha tasmāt yaḥ yadātmā ityādi yadi svabhāvena āsthiti dharmaṇaḥ bhāvasya na nāśa kāraṇaiḥ prayojanam svabhāvena sthiti dharmaṇaḥ bhaviṣyati iti atas āha sthiti dharmaṇaḥ api ityādi sthiti dharmaṇaḥ api hi na eva nāśa kāraṇaiḥ kiñcid prayojanam tasya sva hetubhyaḥ samupajātaḥ yaḥ sthiraḥ svabhāvaḥ tad anyathātvasya asthiḥ ātma tā āpatteḥ kenacid karttum aśakya tvāt kāmam hi bhāvāḥ svayam na bhaveyuḥ na 
HBṬ_2.43.2	 tu santaḥ eva svam svabhāvam parityajanti atha sthiti dharmaṇaḥ api anyathātva pratipattiḥ iṣyate tadā anyathātva pratipattau vā tad svabhāvaḥ eva sthiti dharmā eva na syāt ātma bhūtasya āsthiti dharmaṇaḥ svabhāvasya paścāt sambhave prāk api abhāvaa ayogāt na hi tadā ātamanaḥ tasmin sannihite kadācid abhāvaḥ yuktaḥ atad svabhāva tā prasaṅgāt viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt iti uktam tathā ca sati pūrvaḥ eva vikalpaḥ svabhāvena āsthiti dharmāḥ bhāvaḥ iti tatra ca pūrva vikalpe prāk eva uktam dūṣaṇam vināśa hetoḥ vaiyarthyam iti 
HBṬ_2.43.3	 atha asau sthira svabhāvaḥ eva kevalam asya asthira svabhāva tā prāk asati vināśa hetoḥ upajāyate anyathā nivṛttya yogāt iti atas āha yaḥ ca parasmāt nāśa hetoḥ sthiti dharmaṇaḥ sataḥ anyathā bhāvaḥ asthiti dharma tā lakṣaṇaḥ bhavati sa pūrvakāt sthiti dharmaṇaḥ sva hetu samudbhūtāt svabhāvāt aparaḥ anyaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasmin niṣpanne paścāt janya tvāt bhinna hetuka tvāt ca kathaṃtasya svabhāvaḥ syāt  tad ātma tayā pratibhāsanāt iti ced sārūpyāt alakṣita vivekasya tathā pratibhāsanam syāt yadi asau pūrva svabhāve sati eva anyatas bhavet anyathā virodhaḥ katham parihriyeta  bhavatu aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti ced yaḥ ca aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa katham tasya  na hi anyaḥ anyasya svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ atiprasaṅgāt yaḥ aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ sa kim iti tasya na bhavati iti atas āha svabhāva bhedaḥ ityādi bhavatu vastu antaram eva tad apara svabhāva tayā kaḥ doṣaḥ 
HBṬ_2.43.4	 iti atas āha tathā ca vastu antara tve sati vināśa hetoḥ upajāyamānasya svabhāvasya pūrvakaḥ bhāvaḥ sva hetubhyaḥ yaḥ sthiti dharmā jātaḥ saḥ acyuti dharme sthitaḥ nivṛtti bhāj na bhavati vināśa hetoḥ vastu antara utpattau vyāpṛta tvāt iti na tasya sthiti dharmaṇaḥ anyathā bhāvaḥ nivṛttiḥ na hi mudgara ādeḥ vastu antarasya bhāve aparasya nivṛttiḥ yuktāḥ atiprasaṅgāt tad upamarddena tad utpattau ca prāk eva proktam 
HBṬ_2.43.5	 nanu ca dṛśyate eva kaṭhina ādi rūpasya tāmra ādeḥ agni ādeḥ vināśa hetoḥ drava ādi svabhāva antara utpattiḥ na ca pūrvakasya pracyuti dharma tā iti atas āha etena anantara uktena kaṭhina ādīnām ādi śabdāt drava ādīnām tāmra suvarṇa ādīnām agni śīta vāta ādibhyaḥ drava tva kaṭhina tva ādi svabhāva antara utpattiḥ vyavasthita rūpasya tāmra ādeḥ pratyuktā pratyākhyātāḥ tulya dūṣaṇa tvāt 
HBṬ_2.43.6	 katham tarhi svabhāva antara utpattiḥ pūrvasya ca apracyuti dharme sthitasya abhāvaḥ yuktaḥ iti āha tatra api kaṭhina ādi rūpe tāmra ādau pūrvakasya kaṭhina drava ādi rūpasya svarasa nirodhi tvāt vināśa hetu ayogena vināśe sati agni ādeḥ ādi grahaṇāt jala niṣeka śīta vāta ādeḥ sahakāriṇaḥ paraspara upasarppaṇa ādi āśraya pratyaya viśeṣa upajāta atiśayāt upādānāt ca yat tat kaṭhina ādi rūpam tāmra ādi svarasataḥ virudhyate tatas eva upādānakāraṇāt agni ādi sahakāri kāraṇa upādāna pratyaya upajāta viśeṣāt aparaḥ eva anyaḥ eva drava kaṭhina ādi svabhāvaḥ drava grahaṇasya upalakṣaṇa tvāt utpannaḥ na tu pūrvakam eva kaṭhina drava ādi rūpam tāmra ādi vyavasthita ātmakam drava kaṭhina ādi svabhāvena pariṇatam iti 
HBṬ_2.43.7	 atra paraḥ āha kena uktam yathā sthiti dharmaṇaḥ sataḥ vināśa hetoḥ asthiti svabhāva utpattiḥ tatas vināśaḥ iti yena yaḥ ca parasmāt anyathā bhāvaḥ saḥ aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ ityādi ucyate kintu sa svayam sthiti dharmā eva sva hetubhiḥ janitaḥ na asya asthira svabhāva tā vināśa hetoḥ upajāyate katham jñāyate yathā sva hetubhiḥ svabhāvena sthiti dharmā eva janitaḥ iti  vināśa hetoḥ agni ādeḥ asambhave avasthānāt yadi svabhāvena āsthiti dharmā sva hetoḥ jātaḥ syāt tadā tad asambhave api na avatiṣṭheta tasya svabhāvena sthiti dharmaṇaḥ sva hetubhiḥ eva ayam aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ niyamitaḥ yat uta parasmāt virodhinaḥ agni ādeḥ vināśaḥ svayaṃbhavati iti parasmāt iti karmaṇi lya plope pañcamī param apekṣyaḥ iti arthaḥ sva hetubhiḥ eva ayam niyamita svabhāvaḥ jātaḥ yathā tvayā virodhinam apekṣya svayam nivarttitavyam iti tat uktam 
HBṬ_2.43.8–2.43.10	 svabhāvaḥ api sa tasya itthaṃyena apekṣya nivarttate virodhinaṃyathā anyeṣāṃpravāhaḥ mudgara ādikam iti nanu yadi asya vināśaḥ virodhi sannidhāne svayam eva bhavati ahetukaḥ prāpnoti ahetoḥ ca deśa kāla svabhāva niyamaḥ na yuktaḥ iti atas āha na ca na eva vināśaḥ nāma vinaṃṣṭuḥ aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ yatas ayam doṣaḥ syāt kintu bhāva cyutiḥ eva vināśaḥ tasyāḥ ca niḥsvabhāva tvāt dhetumat tā na eva yujyate na hi sā tasya bhavati kevalam asau svayam eva na bhavati tatas bhavituḥ abhāvāt kasya hetumat ta upagamyate
