HBṬ_2.43.11	 siddhānta vādi āha na idam anatara uktaṃvikalpa dvayam atikrāmati kīdṛśam vikalpa dvayam  kim nityaḥ bhāvaḥ ityādi nanu ca kāla antara sthiti dharma tām upagacchataḥ na eva nitya vikalpasya avakāśaḥ na tad upagame api nityatā eva upagatā bhavati tathā hi yadi ayam saṃvatsara sthiti dharmā sva hetubhiḥ janitaḥ tadā saṃvatsara parisamāptau yaḥ asya ādau= udaya kāle saṃvatsara sthiti dharmā svabhāvaḥ yatas ayam saṃvatsaram sthitaḥ saḥ eva tad ante api tatas aparam saṃvatsaram avatiṣṭheta tad ante api prathama utpanna saṃvatsara sthiti dharma svabhāva aparityāgāt apara apara saṃvatsara sthiti prasaṅgāt kāla antara sthiti dharmatā upagame api nityatā eva upagatā bhavati iti nitya vikalpaḥ durnnivāraḥ vināśa hetu sannidhau svayam nivarttate iti ca upagamāt anitya vikalpaḥ naśvara ātma tā vikalpaḥ tathā hi vināśa hetu abhimata sannidhau svayam vinaśyataḥ yaḥ asya svabhāva saḥ eva bhāvasya eka rūpa tvāt utpanna mātrasya iti tadā eva vināśa prasaṅgāt katham asya 
HBṬ_2.43.12	 kāla antara sthiti dharma tā sambhavati  evam vikalpe kṛte pāścātya vikalpa upagame kāla antara sthitiḥ eva asya truṭyati iti nitya vikalpaḥ eva anena upagantavyaḥ tatra vināśa hetu sannidhau svayam nāśa upagame prāk nityaḥ bhūtvā paścāt anityaḥ vinaśvara svabhāvaḥ bhavati iti brūte evaṃca bruvāṇaḥ bhāva dvayaṃca āha vakṣyamāṇa apekṣaḥ cakāraḥ kīdṛśam bhāva dvayam  nitya anityau svabhāvau bhedau yasya tathā yaḥ asau nityaḥ svabhāvaḥ prāktanaḥ tasya nitya abhimatasya svayam paścāt nāśam bruvāṇaḥ sarvadā pratikṣaṇam eva nāśam prāha anyathā pūrva uktena nyāyena paścāt api na āśā sambhavāt atha pratikṣaṇam asya nāśaḥ na bhavati tadā paścāt api tad ayogāt sarva daiva anāśam prāha iti kṛtvā pūrvasmin iti ābhimate svabhāve vināśa hetuḥ asamarthaḥ akiñcitkaraḥ eva 
HBṬ_2.43.13	 nanu ca vināśa hetoḥ na eva sāmarthyam upagatam pareṇa virodhi sannidhim apekṣya svayam nāśa upagamāt na atas eva tad nibandhanatva prasaṅgāt nāśasya anyathā hi akiñcitkaraḥ kim iti asau apekṣyate  hetu bhāvasya apekṣā lakṣaṇa tvāt sva hetavaḥ eva atra aparādhyanti yat akiñcitkare api tatra apekṣāyām niyuñjate iti ced kaḥ punar ayam asthāna abhiniveśaḥ teṣām yat tatra tathā niyuñjate tasmāt upakāri apekṣāyām eva hetavaḥ niyuñjānāḥ śobhante anyathā te api kārya ātmānaḥ na eva tad niyogam ādriyeran katham ca akiñcitkaraḥ virodhī nāma  na hi asya avirodhi tva abhimatāt viśeṣaḥ kaścid iti yat kiñcid etat 
HBṬ_2.43.14	 yat api uktam yathā anyeṣām kṣaṇika vādinām akiñcitkaram api mudgara ādikam apekṣya ghaṭa ādi pravāhaḥ nivarttate tathā asmākam api kāla antara sthāyī bhāvaḥ iti tat api para samayān abhijñatayā ucyate yatas na asmākam pravāhaḥ nāma kṣaṇa vyatiriktaḥ asti yaḥ akiñcitkara mudgara ādi sannidhau nivartteta kṣaṇāḥ eva hi kevalam santi te ca sva nivṛttau na mudgara ādikam apekṣante svarasataḥ eva nirodhāt yā tu teṣām kapāla ādi vṛtti lakṣaṇā paryudāsa vṛttyā nivṛttiḥ yasyām satyām ekatva abhiniveśino lokasya sadṛśa apara bhāva rūpasya vibhrama nimittasya apagamāt nivṛttāḥ ghata ādayaḥ iti vyavahāraḥ tatra akiñcitkara tvam mudgara ādīnām na eva asti tad bhāvaḥ eva teṣām bhāvāt vegavat mudgara ādi sahakāriṇaḥ ghaṭa kṣaṇāt paraspara upasarppaṇa ādi āśrayāt pratyaya viśeṣāt sañjāta atiśayāt kapāla ādeḥ bhavana dharma tvāt tasya tad janana svabhāvāt iti 
HBṬ_2.43.15–2.43.16	 svabhāva dvaya upagama prasaṅgāt iti parijihīrṣayā paraḥ āha na prāk ityādi kutas etat  eka svabhāva tvāt sarvadā eka svabhāvasya sarvadā nitya tā eva na paścāt anitya svabhāvatā sambhavaḥ iti siddhānta vādi āha sa tarhi bhāvaḥ sarvadā nitya svabhāvaḥ svabhāvena nāśam anāviśan apratipadyamānaḥ katham naṣṭaḥ nāma  kutas tad svabhāva vināśayoḥ nitya svabhāvatāyāḥ vināśasya ca anitya rūpa tāyāḥ ca aparaspara rūpa tvāt paraspara parihāra rūpa tvāt upasaṃharan āha yatas evam sthiti dharmaṇām vināśaḥ na eva yujyate tasmāt sati asya vināśe yadi avaśyambhāvī kṛtaka rūpasya sataḥ vināśaḥ iṣyate paraiḥ tadā vināśa svabhāvena vinaśyati na avatiṣṭhate iti vināśaḥ karttari bahula vacanāt ghan sa svabhāvaḥ yasya tena vināśa svabhāvena āsthiti dharmaṇā tena kṛtaka rūpeṇa satā vastunā sva hetubhyaḥ bhavitavyam anyathā avaśyambhāvitayā upagatasya kṛtaka ātmanām satām vināśasya eva ayogāt 
HBṬ_2.43.17–2.43.18^1	 bhavatu evam iti ced āha tathā api svayam vināśa svabhāva tve api na kevalam avinaśvara svabhāva tve svabhāvānyathā tva asambhavāt vyarthaḥ vināśa hetuḥ iti prathama vikalpa upanyāsaḥ eva uktam na punar ucyate yatas evam tena ityādi sugamam tat evam vināśam pratyanapekṣām asāmarthya vaiyarthyābhyām tad hetu ayogena kṛtaka lakṣaṇasya sattvasyapūrva ācārya darśa tām pratipādya yathā asau viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa tām anubhavati tat darśayan āha tasmāt vināśaḥ ityādi prayogaḥ tu evam ye yad bhāvaṃpratyanapekṣāḥ te tad bhāva niyatāḥ 
HBṬ_2.43.17–2.43.18^2	 tat yathā antyā kāraṇa sāmagrī sva kārya utpādane anapekṣaḥ ca kṛtaka rūpaḥ san bhāvaḥ vināśe avaśyambhāvi vinā śata yogataḥ paraiḥ iti svabhāva hetu prasaṅga prayogaḥ viparyaye bādhakam pramāṇaṃpūrva ācārya pradarśitam tatas tad bhāva niyata tve nāśasyākādācitka tvāt udaya anantaram nāśaḥ iti yaḥsan kṛtaka lakṣaṇaḥ bhāvaḥ sa vināśī vinaśvara svabhāvaḥ naśvara tāyāḥ sādhya dharmasya nivṛttau ca kṛtaka lakṣaṇa sattva nivṛttiḥ iti kṛtvā kṛtaka lakṣaṇasya sattvasya kṣaṇikatāyām anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ sampadyate 
HBṬ_2.43.19–2.43.20	 anapekṣayā anya krānta sattva kṣaṇika tvayoḥ tādātmya siddheḥ tad nibandhanayoḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ api niścayāt tat evaṃpūrva ācāryān prati akṛtakasya sataḥ abhāvāt sat akāraṇa vat nityam iti nitya lakṣaṇa virahāt eva na tat nitya tvam yat tu sat utpattimat tat uktena nyāyena avaśyam nāśitayā upagatam paraiḥ kāla antara sthāyi na bhavati iti prati pāditam 
HBṬ_2.44.1	 yadā tu yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva iti sāmānyena ucyate kṛtaka akṛtaka lakṣaṇam sataḥ bhedam anapekṣya prauḍha vādi tayā kṛtakasya api ca avaśyambhāvī vināśaḥ iti para upagamaḥ na apekṣyate tadā vināśam pratyanapekṣa tvam eva sarvasya na sidhyati yeṣām hi vināśaḥ bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭa ādīnām teṣām eva tad hetu ayogāt tatra anapekṣā yujyate 
HBṬ_2.44.2	 ye tu deśa ādi vyavahitāḥ parvata ādayaḥ vā vināśam āviśantaḥ na dṛṣṭāḥ teṣām avaśyam vināśi tvā upagama nibandhana abhāvāt antye api ayam vināśam pratyanapekṣaḥ eva vinaśyan aviśeṣāt ādau api tad bhāva niyataḥ iti vaktum aśakya tvāt tad svabhāva sāpekṣa tvāt vināśam pratyanapekṣatvā siddheḥ akṛtakānām ca ākāśa ādīnām vināśi svabhāva sāpekṣāṇām iti anapekṣayā sataḥ naśvara svabhāva tā asiddheḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ tad nibandhanayoḥ ayogam utpaśyan artha kriyā virodha lakṣaṇam eva tadā bādhakam pramāṇam tādātmya prasādhakam abhidhānīyam iti manyamānaḥ pūrva pakṣam utthāpayan āha svabhāvataḥ naśvara tve api uktena nyāyena paridṛśyamāna vināśānām ghaṭa ādīnām kaścid deśa ādi vyavahitaḥ parvata ādiḥ vā anupalabdha vināśaḥ kṛtakaḥ api sat rūpaḥ ākāśa ādiḥ vā akṛtakaḥ san na atad svabhāvaḥ api avināśi svabhāvaḥ api syāt api śabdaḥ 
HBṬ_2.44.3	 sambhāvanāyām tasya vināśi svabhāva saṃsādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt āśaṅkyate etat tatas ca vināśi svabhāva sāpekṣa tvāt tad anapekṣa tvam asiddham iti tad vaśāt sādhyasya kṣaṇika tvasya sattva svabhāva tva asiddheḥ tad nibandhanā na anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ iti kim punar atra āśaṅkā nimittam yenakaścid atad svabhāvaḥ api āśaṅkyate iti āha na hi sarvaḥ sarvasya svabhāvaḥ iti vicitra svabhāvāḥ hi bhāvāḥ dṛśyante kecid sa pratighāḥ kecid apratighāḥ tathā nīla ānīla ādi svabhāvāḥ tathā kecid vināśinaḥ anye tu avināśi svabhāvāḥ śaṅkyante iti pūrva pakṣa āśaṅkā 
HBṬ_2.44.4	 na kaścid atad svabhāvaḥ api syāt iti āśaṅkanīyam tathā abhāve hi akṣaṇika tvam tasya syāt tasmin ca sati avastu tva prasaṅgāt kutas atad svabhāvatā śaṅkā  katham punar akṣaṇika tve avastu tva prasaṅgaḥ  yatas sattvasya kṣaṇika tva svabhāva tayā anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ iti atas āha śaktiḥ hi ityādi 
HBṬ_2.45.1	 evam manyate iha tāvat idam eva vicāraṇīyam kim lakṣaṇam etat bhāvānām sattvam yuktam iti tatra na sattā yoga lakṣaṇam avyāpteḥ sāmānya ādiṣu abhāvāt vandhyā suta ādiṣu api bhāvāt ati vyāpteḥ vā vandhyā suta ādīnām asattvāt katham sattā yogaḥ iti ced na itaretara āśrayāt yatas teṣām asattvam sattā yoga virahāt eva tad virahaḥ ca asattvāt iti yadi ca satām eva sattā yogaḥ evam tarhi anyat sattva lakṣaṇam abhidhānīyam sattā yogasya ca vaiyarthyam tatas eva vastunaḥ sattvāt sarva artha kriyā sāmarthya virahāt sattā yoga abhāvaḥ teṣām iti ced evam sati yat eva artha kriyā sāmarthya yuktam tasya eva sattā yogaḥ iti artha kriyā sāmarthyam eva bhāva lakṣaṇam āyātam iti apārthakaḥ sattā yogaḥ itthaṃcaḥ evam anyathā sāmānya ādīnām katham svarūpam sattvam syāt  artha kriyā sāmarthyam tu sarveṣām asti iti tat eva bhāva lakṣaṇam 
HBṬ_2.45.2	 utpāda vyaya dhrauvya yuktaṃsat iti etat api ayuktam dhrauvyeṇa utpāda vyayayoḥ virodhāt ekasmin dharmiṇī ayogāt kathañcid utpāda vyayau kathañcid dhrauvyam iti ced yathā utpāda vyayau na tathā dhrauvyam yathā ca dhrauvyam na tathā utpāda vyayau iti na ekam vastu yathā ukta lakṣaṇam syāt tatas anyasya bhāva lakṣaṇasya ayogāt śakteḥ ca antaśas sva jñāna janane api upagamāt paraiḥ anyathā ṣaṭpadārtha ādi vyavasthāna ayogāt sā eva bhāva lakṣaṇam sarva śakti virahaḥ punarbhāva lakṣaṇam 
HBṬ_2.45.3–2.45.4	 sarva grahaṇam ca sarvasya vastunaḥ vastu antara śakti viraha rūpa tvāt abhāvatā nirāsa artham yasya tu na kvacid śaktiḥ saḥ eva ekāntena abhāvaḥ ucyate śakti lakṣaṇam eva sattvam akṣaṇike syāt tatas kṣaṇikā ātma tā sattvasya na sidhyati iti kutas anvaya vyatirekau iti ced āha na ca eva akṣaṇikasya kvacid kārye antaśas jñāna lakṣaṇe api śaktiḥ asti tat kutas tasya tad lakṣaṇam sattvam atīta ādeḥ iva bhaviṣyati  yatas sattvasya kṣaṇikā ātma tā na sidhyet 
HBṬ_2.45.5	 nanu ca śakteḥ atīndriya tvāt kāraṇānām kārya ārambha niyama abhāvāt ca katham tat virahaḥ akṣaṇikasya bhavet yatas asya sarva śakti viraha lakṣaṇena asattvena virodhinā nirākriyamāṇam sattvam kṣaṇikā ātma tām eva anubhavet yatas anvaya vyatirekau syātām iti atas āha krama yaugapadyābhyām ityādi na eva pratyakṣatas kārya virahāt vā sarva śakti virahaḥ akṣaṇika tve ucyate kintu tad vyāpaka virahāt tathā hi krama yaugapadyābhyām kārya kriyā vyāptā prakāra antara abhāvāt tatas kārya kriyā śakti vyāpakayoḥ tayoḥ akṣaṇika tve virodhāt nivṛtteḥ tad vyāptāyāḥ kārya kriyā śakteḥ api nivṛttiḥ iti sarva śakti viraha lakṣaṇam asattvam akṣaṇika tve vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ ākarṣati viruddhayoḥ ekatra ayogāt tatas nivṛttam sattvam kṣaṇikeṣu eva avatiṣṭhamānam tad ātma tām anubhavati iti yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva iti anvaya vyatireka rūpāyāḥ vyāpteḥ siddhiḥ niścayaḥ bhavati 
HBṬ_2.45.6	 nanu ca prakāra antara abhāvāt kāryam aṅkura ādikam bīja ādinā krama yaugapadyābhyām eva kriyate iti ucyate saḥ eva tu prakāra antara virahaḥ kārya ātmanaḥ kutas siddhaḥ  prakāra antarasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tve katham atyanta asambhavaḥ  kevalam deśa ādi niṣedha mātram eva syāt anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tve nā asattā niścayaḥ vipra karṣiṇām iti kutas tad abhāva siddhiḥ  tatas prakāra antareṇa artha kriyā sambhavāt krama yaugapadya nivṛttau api na artha kriyā sāma rtthya nivṛttiḥ iti kutas akṣaṇika tve sati sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇam asattvam  yatas sattvasya kṣaṇikā ātma tayā anvaya vyatirekau syātām  na ubhayathā api adoṣāt tathā hi kramaḥ nāma paripāṭiḥ kārya antarāsāhityam kaivalyam aṅkura ādeḥ yaugapadyam api tasya aparaiḥ bbīja ādi kāryaiḥ sāhityam prakāra antaram ca aṅkura ādeḥ tad ubhaya avasthā virahe api anyathā bhavanam tasya ca aṅkura ādi svabhāvasya anya sahitasya 
HBṬ_2.45.7	 kevalasya vā abhāve pratyakṣa bodha gamyamāne sati upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta eva svabhāvaḥ krama yaugapadya bhāva bahis bhūtaḥ na upalabhyate vastunaḥ upalabhyasya anya sāhitye kaivalye ca apanīte tad vivikta deśa ādi pratibhāsinaḥ pratyakṣasya udayāt svabhāva anupalambhataḥ eva abhāva niścaya ādi lakṣaṇa vyavahāra vṛtteḥ tasya ca aṅkura ādi bhāvasya avasthā dvaya bahis bhāva niṣedhe kayoḥ cit deśa kālayoḥ deśa antara ādau krameṇa aṅkura ādi bhāvavatī tarasmin vā bhāve api na kācid kṣatiḥ tatas pratyakṣatas eva prakāra antara abhāva siddheḥ katham krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā śaktiḥ avyāptā syāt  śāstra kāraḥ tu yathā pratyakṣatā eva prakāra antara abhāva siddhiḥ tathā svayam etena kramākrama ādayaḥ api iti atidiśan vakṣyati 
HBṬ_2.45.8	 anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tve api prakāra antarasya krama yaugapadyayoḥ anyaḥ anya vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt eva abhāva siddhiḥ tathā hi anyonya vyavaccheda rūpāṇām eka niṣedhena apara vidhānāt tasyāḥ apratiṣedhe vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ virodhāt ubhaya pratiṣedha ātmanaḥ prakāra antarasya kutas sambhavaḥ  atra prayogaḥ yatra yat prakāra vyavacchedena yat itara prakāra vyavasthānam na tatra prakāra antara sambhavaḥ tat yathā nīla prakāra vyavacchedena ānīla prakāra antara vyavasthāyām pīte asti ca krama yaugapadyayoḥ anyatara prakāra vyavacchedena tad itara prakāra vyavasthānam vyavacchidyamāna prakāra aviṣayīkṛte sarvatra kārya kāraṇa rūpe vastuni iti viruddha upalabdhiḥ vyavacchidyamāna prakāra itara vyavasthānam ca prakāra antara sambhavaḥ ca tatas bahis bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ iti anayoḥ tattvā anyatva rūpayoḥ anyonya parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tvāt na ca atra api bādhaka antara āśaṅkayā anavasthānam 
HBṬ_2.45.9–2.45.10^1	 āśaṅkanīyam pūrva prasiddhasya virodhasya smaraṇa mātra tvāt viruddha upalabdhiṣu bahis ddharmiṇi hetoḥ sadbhāvam upadarśya virodha sādhanam eva bādhakam tat ca iha asti tatas viruddhayoḥ ekatra asambhavāt pratiyogi abhāva niścayaḥ śīta uṣṇa sparśayoḥ iva bhāva abhāvayoḥ iva vā iti kutas anavasthā  tatra na krameṇa akṣaṇikaḥ kāryāṇi karoti aviśeṣāt akāraka avasthāyām iva sahakārī apekṣā ca dvividhasya api sahakāri tvasya ayogāt anupanyasanīyāḥ sarveṣām ca eka kriyā kāle eva kriyā prasakteḥ tad kārakasya svabhāvasya tadā eva bhāvāt na api yugapad pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt punar tad kriyā prasaṅgāt ca kṛta tvāt na iti ced na sāmarthyān apāyāt anyathā prāk api akāraka rūpā viśeṣāt kriyā syāt kṛtasya karttum aśakya tvāt iti ced śakta aśakta tayā tarhi ekatra eva kārye bheda prasaṅgaḥ śāli kodrava bīja ādeḥ iva 
HBṬ_2.45.10^2	 nityaḥ ca yadā yugapad karoti tatas prāk api bhāvāt tadā eva tad kriyā prasaṅgaḥ punar tatas api pūrvataram iti evam na kadācid yugapad kriyā syāt pūrva uttara kālayoḥ ca ekadā yugapad kāriṇaḥ anyadā sarva artha kriyā sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇam asattvam syāt iti katham na kṣaṇika tā  kriyā upagame vā krama pakṣaḥ eva tatra ca uktaḥ doṣaḥ evam akṣaṇika tve sati cakṣuḥ ādi āyatanānām asattva prasaṅgāt kṣaṇikatāyām eva sattvam iti yat sat tat kṣaṇikam eva iti sataḥ naśvara ātma tā siddheḥ anvaya vyatireka rūpa vyāpti siddhiḥ iti 
HBṬ_3.1.1	 tat evam svabhāva hetau tādātmya siddhi nibandhanam anvaya vyatireka niścayam pratipādya kārya hetau kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nimitta tvāt tayoḥ tasya āś ca pratyakṣa anupalambha nibandhanāyāḥ prāk eva darśita tvāt tad gatam aparam api pareṣām bhrānti kāraṇam apanetum tad viṣayam darśayan āha artha antare hetoḥ vyatirikte vastuni gamye kāryaṃhetuḥ anartha antare tu svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ iti uktam kasmāt punar artha antare kāryam eva hetuḥ iti āha avyabhicārāt iti kāryam eva hi artha antaram na vyabhicarati na anyat yathā uktam prāk tatas kāryam eva artha antare gamye hetuḥ ucyate saṃyoga vaśāt gamaka tve 
HBṬ_3.1.2	 na ca kenacid ityādinā yaḥ sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāva prasaṅgaa ācāryeṇa uktaḥ parasya tam iha api kārya hetau paraḥ kadācid prasañjayet iti āśaṅkamānaḥ āha kārya kāraṇaḥ ityādi yadi hi kāryam hetuḥ ucyate tadā kārya kāraṇa bhāvena kāraṇena asya gamaka tvam tathā ca sati sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ prāpnoti agneḥ sāmānya dharma vat viśeṣa dharmāḥ api tārṇa pārṇa ādayaḥ gamyāḥ syuḥ dhūmasya api viśeṣa dharma vat dravya tva pārthiva tva ādayaḥ api sāmānya dharmā gamakāḥ bhaveyuḥ kutas sarvathā janya janaka bhāvāt janya janaka bhāvaḥ hi kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ucyate sa ca na agni dhūmayoḥ aṃśena api tu sarveṇa prakāreṇa tathā hi yathā agniḥ agni tva dravya tva satva ādibhiḥ sāmānya dharmaiḥ janakaḥ tathā tārṇa pārṇa tva ādibhiḥ viśeṣa dharmaiḥ api yathā ca dhūmaḥ dhūma tva pāṇḍu tva ādibhiḥ sva niyataiḥ viśeṣa dharmaiḥ janyaḥ tathā 
HBṬ_3.1.3	 sāmānya dharmaiḥ api sattva dravya tva ādibhiḥ tatas ca yathā tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tathā eva gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ prāpnoti tasya eva tad nibandhana tvāt iti pūrva pakṣa āśaṅkā atra āha na sarvathā janya janaka bhāvaḥ tatas ca kutas tathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ syāt  kasmāt iti ced tad bhāve teṣām tārṇa pārṇa tva ādīnām viśeṣa dharmāṇām abhāve bhavataḥ dhūma mātrasya tebhyaḥ eva viśeṣa dharmebhyaḥ bhavati iti evam ātmanaḥ tad utpatti niyamasya abhāvāt tathā tad abhāve agni abhāve bhavataḥ dravya tva ādeḥ sāmānya dharmasya agneḥ eva ayam bhavati iti evaṃrūpasya tad utpatti niyamasya abhāvāt kutas sarvathā janya janaka bhāvaḥ  yatas sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ syāt na hi asati tad utpatti niyame janya janaka bhāvaḥ vyavasthāpayitum yuktaḥ yatas evam tasmāt kāryam dhūma ādikam svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ dhūma tva ādibhiḥ sva gataiḥ ittham bhūta lakṣaṇā 
HBṬ_3.1.4	 ca tṛtīyā avinābhāvi vinā na bhavati kaiḥ vinā na bhavati  kāraṇe yāvadbhiḥ svabhāvaiḥ iti atra api sambadhyate kāraṇa āśritaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ svabhāvaiḥ vinā te kārya gatāḥ svabhāvāḥ na bhavanti hetuḥ taiḥ teṣām iti gamyate kva avinābhāvi  kāraṇe kāraṇa viṣaye aparaḥ arthaḥ kāraṇe ādhārasaptamī idānīm kāraṇa sthaiḥ svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ agni tva dravya tva ādibhiḥ avinābhāvi teṣām kāraṇa gatānām sāmānya dharmāṇām hetuḥ kāryam gamakam kasmāt iti āha tad kāryatva niyamāt teṣām eva kāraṇa gatānām sāmānya dharmāṇām tat kāryam iti evaṃrūpasya niyamasya sadbhāvāt na hi tān sāmānya dharmān kadācid api kāryam vyabhicarati 
HBṬ_3.1.5–3.1.6^1	 evaṃkāraṇa gatam aṃśam pāścātyena arthena nirūpya prāktanena arthena kārya gatam aṃśam nirūpayan āha taiḥ eva ca ityādi kāryam api taiḥ eva dharmaiḥ sva gataiḥ kāraṇa gatānām dharmāṇām gamakam yathā antarā sambhavinaḥ dhūma tva pāṇḍu pārṇa tva ādayaḥ viśeṣa rūpāḥ taiḥ kāraṇa gataiḥ sāmānya dharmaiḥ vinā na bhavanti atra api tad kāryatva niyamāt iti apekṣyate teṣām eva kārya gatānām viśeṣa dharmāṇām kāraṇa gata sāmānya dharma apekṣayā kāryatva niyamāt na hi te viśeṣa dharmāḥ kārya gatāḥ kāraṇa stha sāmānya dharmaiḥ vinā kadācid api bhavanti 
HBṬ_3.1.5–3.1.6^2	 tatas teṣām eva kāryatva niyamaḥ na anyeṣām dravya tva ādīnām kāraṇa stha sāmānya dharmaiḥ vinā bhavatām tat evam kāraṇasya sāmānya dharmāḥ eva gamyāḥ na viśeṣa dharmāḥ kāryasya api viśeṣa dharmāḥ eva gamakāḥ na sāmānya dharmāḥ tad kāryatva niyamāt ye tu kāraṇasya viśeṣa dharmā yaiḥ tad kāryatva niyamaḥ kārya mātrasya na asti iti na te gamyāḥ ye ca kāryasya sāmānya dharmāḥ dravya tva ādayaḥ teṣām api tad kāryatva niyama abhāvāt eva gamaka tvam na asti iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvena gamaka tve kutas sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ pareṣām iva prasajyeta  
HBṬ_3.2.1	 parasya aniṣṭa āpādanam āśaṅkya āha aṃśena ityādi yadi hi kāraṇasya sāmānya dharmāḥ eva gamyāḥ kāryasya api viśeṣa dharmāḥ eva gamakāḥ tad kāryatva niyamāt iṣyante hanta tarhi aṃśena janya janaka bhāvaḥ prāptaḥ kāraṇasya sāmānya dharmāḥ eva janakāḥ na viśeṣa dharmāḥ kāryasya api viśeṣa dharmāḥ eva janyā na sāmānya dharmāḥ iti syāt sarvathā ca janya janaka bhāvaḥ abhimataḥ iti abhyupagama virodhaḥ etat pariharati na aṃśena janya janaka bhāva prasaṅgaḥ niraṃśa tvena vastunaḥ sarva ātmanā tad abhyupagamāt gamya gamaka bhāvasya api sarvathā abhimata tvāt tat āha tat janyaḥ ityādi yadi hi kāryasya taiḥ kāraṇa gataiḥ viśeṣa dharmaiḥ janyaḥ yaḥ viśeṣaḥ sa grahītum śakyate tadā tad janya viśeṣa grahaṇe abhimata tvāt kāraṇa gata viśeṣa dharmāṇām gamya tvasya tathā liṅga viśeṣaḥ dhūma tva ādiḥ upādhiḥ viśeṣaṇam yeṣām dravya tva ādīnām sāmānyānām kārya gatānām 
HBṬ_3.2.2^1	 teṣām ca abhimata tvāt gamaka tvasya tathā hi aguru dhūma grahaṇe bhavati eva tad agneḥ anumānam dhūma tva viśeṣaṇena ca dravya tva ādinā agneḥ anumānam na hi sarvathā janya janaka bhāvaḥ asti iti eva tathā eva gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ bhavati tasya jñāna apekṣa tvāt tathā hi na sattā mātreṇa liṅgasya gamaka tvam tasya jñāpaka tvāt jñāpakaḥ hi sva niścaya apekṣaḥ jñāpyam artham jñāpayati na anyathā katham tarhi uktam tad abhāve bavataḥtad utpatti niyama abhāvāt iti  sarvathā janya janaka bhāva abhyupagame tad abhāve bhāvasya eva abhāvāt iti atas āha aviśiṣtaḥ ityādi 
HBṬ_3.2.2^2	 yadi hi tad janya viśeṣa grahaṇa rahitam aviśiṣṭam kārya mātram upādīyate liṅga viśeṣa upādhi rahitam vā dravya ādikam tadā aviśiṣṭa sāmānya vivakṣāyām kāraṇa gata viśeṣa abhāve api dhūma mātrasya bhāvāt tad aviśiṣṭasya ca dravya tva ādeḥ agni abhāve api bhāvāt vyabhicāraḥ iti sarvathā janya janaka bhāvaḥ na iṣyate tad abhāvāt gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ ca na tu viśeṣa vivakṣāyām tatra vyabhicāra abhāvāt tathā hi yadi nāma dhūma mātram tārṇa pārṇa ādi viśeṣa abhāve bhavati na tu tat janyaḥ viśeṣaḥ sa yadi grahītum śakyate tadā viśeṣasya gamya tvam asti eva niścitasya eva liṅga tvāt tathā yadi api dravya tva sattva mātram agni abhāve api bhavati na tu dhūma ātmakam iti tad viśiṣṭasya avyabhicārāt gamaka tvam api na vāryatas iti 
HBṬ_3.3.1	 atra parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkya āha kasyacid dhūma ādeḥ kadācid kasmiṃścid kāle kutaścid agni ādeḥ bhāve api sati sarvaḥ dhūma ādiḥ tādṛśaḥ yādṛśaḥ ekadā agni ādeḥ bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ tad jātīyaḥ tathāvidha janmā yathāvidhāt saḥ ekaḥ bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ tādṛśāt eva janma yasya sa tathāvidha janma iti etat kutas pramāṇāt avasitam yena ucyate kārya hetau kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhi nibandhanau anvaya vyatirekau iti tathā hi yadi nāma pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kasyacid dhūmasya agni ādi sāmagrī kārya tvam avagatam kim etāvatā anyasya api tādṛśasya tādṛśa kārya tā sidhyati tatra tad nibandhanayoḥ pratyakṣa anupalambhayoḥ avyāpārāt tatra eva hi tayoḥ vyāpāraḥ tasya eva tad kāryatā bhavatu tat anyasya tu kim āyātam yena tathāvidhāt asya janma syāt evam hi kasyāścid dhūma vyakteḥ agni ādi janya tā dṛṣṭā iti kin na ghaṭa ādeḥ 
HBṬ_3.3.2–3.3.4	 api sā abhyupagamyate anya tvena viśeṣa abhāvāt kaḥ evam sati doṣaḥ iti ced tathā ca pramāṇa abhāvena tathāvidha janma tvā niścayāt atādṛśāt api janma āśaṅkāyām tādṛśasya dhūma ādeḥ agni ādinā anvaya vyatirekau na niścitau iti kutas kārya hetoḥ ggamaka tvam  na hi yaḥ asmau ekaḥ deśa kāla avasthā niyataḥ agni viśeṣa hetukaḥ dhūmaḥ adhigataḥ pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām tasya eva anvaya vyatirekau pratipattavyau tasya deśa antara ādau asambhavāt kim tarhi  tādṛśasya sāmānya ātmanaḥ eva liṅga tvāt tasya ca atathāvidhāt api janmāśaṅkāyām kutas tathāvidhena anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā  tat uktam avasthā deśa kālānāṃbhedāt bhinnāsu śaktiṣu bhāvānām anumānena pratītiḥ ati durllabhāḥ iti 
HBṬ_3.3.5	 siddhānta vādi āha na atadbhāvinaḥ ityādi evam manyate iha ekadā dhūma ādeḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janya tayā pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām niścita rūpa tve api tādṛśasya ātādṛśāt api bhāvaḥ samāśaṅkyate yathā paridṛṣṭāt anya tvena tatra yaḥ asau agni ādi sāmagrī janyodhūma viśeṣaḥ ekadā niścitaḥ tad apekṣayā yathā anyaḥ dhūma viśeṣaḥ tādṛśaḥ yaḥ anyādṛśāt api bhāvānām vicitra śakti tayā bhavet iti śaṅkyate tathā saḥ api ekadā agni ādi sāmagrī janya tayā niścitaḥ tad anya apekṣayā tādṛśaḥ eva tatra yadi tat anyasya tādṛśasya atādṛśāt janma syāt tadā tādṛśasya svabhāvasya na agni ādi sāmagrī janya svabhāva tā iti paridṛṣṭasya api dhūmasya nā agni ādi sāmagrī kāraṇam iti āyātam tādṛśasya svabhāvasyāḥ agni ādi sāmagrī vilakṣaṇa kāraṇa janya svabhāva tvāt tatas ca agni ādi sāmagryāḥ akāraṇa tvāt yaḥ mayā ekadā 
HBṬ_3.3.6	 tatas bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ dhūmaḥ saḥ api na bhavet na hi yat yasya kāraṇam na bhavati tat tatas sakṛt api jāyate tasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt iti atadbhāvinaḥ iti tad śabdena vivakṣitam agni ādi kāraṇam parigṛhyate na tat atat tad vilakṣaṇam atādṛśam śakra mūrddha ādikam atasmāt bhavitum śīlam yasya tasya atad bhāvinaḥ tādṛśasya tad lakṣaṇasya dhūma vastunaḥ sakṛt api ekadā api tatas agni ādeḥ abhāvāt bhāva virodhāt bhavati ca tādṛśaḥ agni ādi sāmagrītaḥ tatas tādṛśasya svabhāvasya tādṛśam eva kāraṇam iti avagamyate sakṛt pravṛttābhyām eva pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām iti kutas vyabhicāra āśaṅkā  tena yādṛśaḥ dhūmaḥ agni ādi sāmagryāḥ bhavan dṛṣṭaḥ sakṛt tādṛśasya tasya tad janya svabhāvatayā tādṛśāt eva bhāvāt yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agni ādi sāmagrī iti anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ 
HBṬ_3.3.7	 athavā anyathā vyākhyāyate iha pratyakṣa anupalambha nibandhanā kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ prāk uktā tad nibandhanau anvaya vyatirekau pratipādayitum tat ca ayuktam tathā hi kasyacid dhūmasya agni ādi sāmagrī anantara bhāvinaḥ ādyasya kadācid prathama utpāda kāle kutaścid agni ādi sāmagryāḥ bhāve api utpāde api sarvaḥ tādṛśaḥ yādṛśaḥ prathama kṣaṇa bhāvī dhūmaḥ dvitīya ādi kṣaṇeṣu api tādṛśaḥ pratyakṣatas eva tasya pūrvakṣaṇa avilakṣaṇa tayā pratīteḥ tathāvidha janmā iti yathāvidhāt agni indhana sāmagrī lakṣaṇāt kāraṇāt ādyaḥ dhūma kṣaṇaḥ utpannas tathāvidhāt janma yasya sa tathāvidha janma iti etat kutas na eva tasya dhūma ādeḥ abhāvāt evam ca yadi atas dṛṣṭam tasya anyatas api bhāvasya darśanāt sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ iti anyamānaḥ āha tathā ca anagnitaḥ dhūmāt api dhūmasya 
HBṬ_3.3.8–3.3.11	 bhāve śakra mūrddha ādeḥ api tasya bhāva avirodhāt agninā dhūmasya na anvaya vyatirekau iti ced manyasaḥ iti pūrva pakṣa āśaṅkā tat uktam kṣaṇika tve kathaṃbhāvāḥ kvacid āyatta vṛttayaḥ prathama dhūma kṣaṇa janitaḥ dhūma kṣaṇaḥ tādṛśaḥ apara prathama dhūma kṣaṇa janitaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ dhūma kṣaṇaḥ na tṛtīya ādiḥ evam tṛtīya kṣaṇa ādiṣu api aṅkura ādiṣu ca sarvatra vācyam kutas punar ayam vibhāgaḥ iti ced āha atadbhāvinaḥ atasmāt anagni indhana ādi rūpāt dhūmāt bhavana śīlasya prathama kṣaṇa avilakṣaṇasya dhūmasya sakṛt api ekadā api tatas agni ādi sāmagryāḥ abhāvāt abhāva ayogāt yathā hi prathama kṣaṇa apekṣayā dvitīyaḥ tādṛśaḥ tathā tad apekṣayā prathamaḥ api iti tādṛśatva aviśeṣāt tādṛśasya anagnitaḥ bhāve tādṛśaḥ na agni janya svabhāvaḥ iti sakṛt api tatas na bhavet bhavan vā tad janya svabhāva tām ātmanaḥ tādṛśaḥ khyāpayati iti kutas anyādṛśāt bhavet tasmāt anyādṛśāt bhavan anyādṛśaḥ eva tatas na vyabhicāraḥ 
HBṬ_3.4.1–3.4.3	 nanu sarveṣām dhūma kṣaṇānām kaṇṭha kṣaṇana akṣi sruti kālīkaraṇa ādikāyām artha kriyāyām upayogāt katham tādṛśa svabhāva tā na syāt  na tasyāḥ api artha kriyāyāḥ kṣaṇa bheda upadhīyamāna rūpāyāḥ tādṛśa tva abhāvāt tatra api tulya doṣa tvāt katham tarhi loke sarvatra dhūma vyavahāraḥ iti ced sadṛśa apara bhāva nibandhana eka tva adhyavasāya vaśāt kṣaṇaiḥ vyavahāra ayogāt ca sādṛśye sati katham na tādṛśatā iti ced tādṛśāt anya tvāt sadṛśasya tathā hi go sadṛśaḥ bhavati gavayaḥ na tu tādṛśaḥ goḥ eva aparasya tādṛśa tvāt parama arthena ātādṛśe api tādṛśa abhimānaḥ manda matīnām bhavan katham nivāryeta  tathā hi tattva adhyavasāyaḥ api tāvat atasmin arvāk dṛśām vinivārayitum na pāryate kim aṅga punar tādṛśa tva adhyavasāyaḥ yathā uktam samāna varṇa saṃsthāne santāne anyatra jāyate atasmin tad matiḥ puṃsāṃkim uta ekatra saṃtatau iti 
HBṬ_3.4.4	 tattva cintakāḥ tu tādṛśātādṛśa kāraṇa bhedāt tādṛśā tādṛśatām bhāvānām anumanyante na tādṛśatām tat yadi atādṛśāt api tādṛśaḥ bhavet tadā tasya tat janyaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti atadbhāvinaḥ sakṛt api tatas bhāvaḥ na syāt amum eva artham samarthayamānaḥ āha paraspara apekṣayā ityādi kāraṇa apekṣayā hi janya svabhāvam kāryam kārya apekṣayā ca janaka svabhāvam kāraṇam yatas hi kāraṇāt yat bhavat dṛṣṭam tasya tad janya svabhāvaḥ itarasya ca tad janakaḥ iti pratīyate anyathā tasya tatas bhāva ayogāt itarasya ca tad janana ayogāt yadi nāma evam tatas prakṛte kim siddham iti atas āha tatra evasmin nyāye sati yadi dhūmaḥ yādṛśaḥ ādyaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janitaḥ tādṛśaḥ dvitīya ādi kṣaṇa bhāvī agni ādi sāmagryāḥ agni indhana ādi kāraṇa kalāpāt tad janaka svabhāva tayā nirddhāritāt anyatas agni indhana ādi sāmagrī janitād 
HBṬ_3.4.5	 ādyāt dhūma kṣaṇāt bhavet tadā tasya tādṛśasya dhūma svabhāvasya tat janyaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janyaḥ svabhāvaḥ na bhavati kintu dhūma janyaḥ eva iti kṛtvā sakṛt api tatas agni ādi sāmagrītaḥ na bhavet tādṛśasya hi svabhāvasya anyatas bhāve tad janya svabhāva tā na agni ādi janya svabhāva tā iti kutas sakṛt api tatas bhāvaḥ yujyate atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ artha antara vat iti yathā hi artha antaram atajjanya abhimatam anyatas bhavat na tad janya svabhāvam na agni ādi sāmagrī janya svabhāvam iti sakṛt api tatas na bhavati tadvat tādṛśaḥ dhūmaḥ api iti tatas bhavan anyādṛśaḥ eva asau iti gamyate 
HBṬ_3.4.6	 syāt matam agni ādi sāmagryāḥ asau atajjanya svabhāvaḥ api tādṛśaḥ balāt janyate kaḥ tasya tapasvinaḥ aparādhaḥ iti atas āha na api na kevalam svayam atajjanya svabhāva tayā tatas na bhavet kintu agni ādi sāmagrī api tam tādṛśam dhūmam yādṛśaḥ dvitīya ādi kṣaṇa bhāvī na janayet kutas  atajjanana svabhāva tvāt tādṛśasya hi anyatas bhāve saḥ eva tad janana svabhāvaḥ na agni ādi sāmagri iti tad janana svabhāva vikalā katham tam janayet  atra api udāharaṇam sāmagryantara vat iti yathā sāmagryantaram atajjanana svabhāva abhimatam na janayati tadvat agni ādi sāmagrī api tathā hi sā ātmīyam svabhāvam anusṛtya eva pravarttate tatas kutas asau sāmagrī balāt jāyeta  
HBṬ_3.5.1	 syāt matam agni ādi sāmagrī janya svabhāvaḥ api tādṛśaḥ dhūmaḥ dhūma janya svabhāvaḥ api yathā saḥ eva dhūmaḥ indhana janya svabhāvaḥ agni janya svabhāvaḥ ca ubhayatas bhavati tathā tādṛśaḥ api dhūmaḥ ubhaya sāmagrī janya svabhāvatayā ubhayatas bhaviṣyati iti atas āha na ca na eva dhūmasya tādṛśasya tat atat janyaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janyaḥ dhūmajanyaḥ ca svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ yuktyā saṅgatāḥ kutas eka svabhāva tvāt tādṛśasya dhūma rūpasya bheda abhāvāt na hi tasya kāla bhede api tādṛś rūpa tā bhidyate bhede hi anyādṛśasya anyādṛśāt bhāve vivāda ayogāt tasya yadi tādṛśā tādṛśa kāraṇa janya tā syāt tatas tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva tā eva syāt tat eva darśayan āha dhūmā adhūmaḥ ityādi dhūma śabdena yādṛśaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī janyaḥ tādṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ abhipretaḥ adhūma śabdena anya adṛśa kāraṇa janyaḥ dhūma janitaḥ 
HBṬ_3.5.2	 anya dṛśaḥ tayoḥ ca tādṛśātādṛśa kāraṇa janya tayā eva tādṛśā tādṛśa svabhāva tā avagantavyā vakṣyamāṇa nītyā tena agni dhūma lakṣaṇāt dhūmādhūma janana svabhāvāt tādṛśā tādṛśa janana svabhāvāt tādṛśā tādṛśa tayā asya bhavataḥ dhūmādhūma svabhāvaḥ tādṛśā tādṛśa svabhāvaḥ syāt kutas tādṛśaḥ eva  kutas etat iti āha kārya svabhāvānām ityādi kāryāṇām hi ye svabhāvāḥ paraspara asaṃbhavinaḥ te paraspara vilakṣaṇa kāraṇa sāmagrī svabhāva kṛtā na svābhāvikāḥ ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt tatas tādṛśātādṛśāt bhavataḥ dhūmasya tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva tā eva syāt 
HBṬ_3.5.3	 syāt matam na eva tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāvatāyām tādṛśātādṛśa kāraṇa apekṣā kāryāṇām utpatti mātraḥ eva kāraṇa apekṣaṇāt iti atas āha akāraṇa apekṣaṇe ca tādṛśātādṛśa rūpa tāyām tādṛśā tādṛśa kāraṇa anapekṣaṇe ca tādṛśātādṛśa tāyāḥ ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt na hi tādṛśā tādṛśa svabhāvayoḥ abhūtvā bhāva vyatirekeṇa anyā kācid utpattiḥ yatra tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva kāraṇa nirapekṣāṇām api tad apekṣā syāt tasmāt utpatti śabdena tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva tā eva ucyate iti tatra kāraṇa apekṣā upagame katham tādṛśā tādṛśa tāyām kāraṇa apekṣā na syāt tasmāt sāmagrīṇām tādṛśā tādṛśa tvāt eva kāryāṇām tādṛśa ātādṛśa svabhāva vibhāgaḥ iti kutas anyādṛśāt tādṛśa sambhavaḥ iti 
HBṬ_3.5.4	 yat tu uktam yathā ekaḥ dhūmaḥ agni indhanābhyām vilakṣaṇābhyām janyate tathā eka lakṣaṇam api kāryam vilakṣaṇāt api sāmagrī antarāt bhaviṣyati iti tat ayuktam yatas na asmābhiḥ vilakṣaṇānām janaka tvam vāryate janayanti eva paraspara vilakṣaṇā api sva hetu pariṇāma upanidhi dharmāṇaḥ tad avasthā niyatāḥ tat ekam kāryam tasya tu teṣām ca paraspara apekṣayā janya janaka svabhāvatā niyamāt tādṛśasya tādṛśāt eva janma ucyate na anyādṛśāt tasya atad janana svabhāva tvāt tad abhāve api anyatas bhavataḥ tad utpatti niyama abhāvāt aniyame ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva ayogāt yadi tu agniḥ iva indhana upādāna upakṛtaḥ tad upādāna upākṛtam ca indhanam iva tad avasthā niyatam atādṛśam api dhūma ādikam tādṛśam dhūmam janayet pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām ca tathā avagamyeta tadā agni ādi vat saḥ api tad janana svabhāvatā niyamāt tādṛśa janakaḥ kena na anumanyeta tad abhāve api 
HBṬ_3.5.5	 tu tādṛśasya bhāve tayoḥ janya janaka svabhāva tā niyama abhāvāt kutas kārya kāraṇa tā iti ahetu tā eva tādṛśasya anyādṛśāt bhavataḥ syāt yatas evam tasmāt saḥ agni indhana ādi sāmagrī viśeṣaḥ mantavyaḥ yaḥ ādya dhūma jananaḥ na anyaḥ sa dhūmaḥ ādyaḥ yaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī viśeṣeṇa janitaḥ na anyaḥ iti kṛtvā kārya kāraṇayoḥ evam yathā uktena nyāyena janya janaka rūpasya svabhāvasya niyamāt yādṛśam yasya karaṇam ekadā pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām eva avadhāritam tat vijātīyāt tatas anyādṛśāt kāraṇāt utpattiḥ tādṛśasya kāryasya na bhavati anyādṛśasya eva na vāryatas iti 
HBṬ_3.5.6	 tat evam tādṛśātādṛśa kāraṇa kṛtaka tvam tādṛśā tādṛśa kārya svabhāvasya pratipādya upasaṃharan āha tat tasmāt yādṛśam kāryam yādṛśāt kāraṇāt dṛṣṭam pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām niścitam ekadā tat tat na vyabhicarati tādṛśam anyādṛśāt na bhavati yana evam tena kāraṇena siddhe kārya kāraṇa bhāve tādṛśasya kāryasya tādṛśam eva kāraṇam iti niścaye sati yathā uditena nyāyena kāryasya kāraṇena vyāptiḥ anvaya vyatireka rūpā siddhā abhavati 
HBṬ_3.5.7	 na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ iti dṛṣṭa kāraṇa vijātīyāt kāraṇāt anyādṛśān na utpattiḥ iti amum artham apratipadyamānaḥ kāryasya na vijātīyāt kāraṇāt na utpattiḥ iti ayam atra arthaḥ abhimataḥ iti manvānaḥ paraḥ codayan āha nanu svatas vijātīyāt api kāraṇāt kiñcid kāryam bhavat dṛṣṭam tat katham na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ iti asya na dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ syāt katham yathā iti āha tat yathāgomaya ādeḥ ādi grahaṇāt śṛṅga candra kānta ādeḥ śālūka ādi ādi grahaṇāt śara udaka ādi tathā hi gomayāt śālūkasya bhāvaḥ śṛṅgāt śarasya candrakāntā dapām na ca gomaya ādikam śālūka ādeḥ na vijātīyam tat kim ucyate na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ iti siddhānta vādī parasya bhrāṃtatāṃdarśayan āha na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ iti yatas hi kāraṇāt yat bhavat dṛṣṭam tat tatas anya adṛśyāt na bhavati iti ayam 
HBṬ_3.5.8	 atra arthaḥ vivakṣitaḥ na tu kārya vijātīyāt iti na ca tasya vyabhicāraḥ tat āha tathāvidham eva hi gomaya ādi rūpam tādṛśām śālūka ādīnām ādi nimittam śālūka ādi prabandhasya yaḥ ādiḥ prathamaḥ ārambha kṣaṇaḥ tasya kāraṇam iti kṛtvā śālūkā di pabandhasya ādeḥ na kāraṇa bhedaḥ anyādṛśāt utpattiḥ sarvasya tadā aadeḥ ggomaya ādi nimitta tvāt yadā tu prabandhena pūrva kṣaṇa nimittānām uttara utta rakṣaṇānām santānena utpatti lakṣaṇā vṛttiḥ bhavati śarasya tadā śarāt bhāvaḥ tat evam yasya prabandha ādeḥ śṛṅga ādibhyaḥ bhāvaḥ na tādṛśasya śara ādeḥ yasya ca śara ādeḥ tad uttarottarasya bhāvaḥ na tādṛśasya śṛṅga ādeḥ iti na dṛṣṭa kāraṇa vijātīyāt kāraṇāt tādṛśasya sambhavaḥ iti kārya hetoḥ anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ 
HBṬ_3.5.9	 yadā api śālūka ādayaḥ pūrva pūrva sva jāti nibandhanāḥ anādi santāna pravṛttāḥ iṣyante tadā a pi gomaya ādibhyaḥ keṣāñcit bhāve api tādṛśatva abhāvāt na vyabhicāraḥ iti darśayan āha asti ca ityādi yasya śālūka santānasya gomaya ādi kāraṇam yasya ca sarvadā sva jāti nimitta tvam tayoḥ gomaya itarajat manoḥ śālūkayoḥ asti eva svabhāva bhedaḥ parasparam anyādṛśa tvam rūpasya abhede api sati tulya ākāra tve sati katham anyādṛśa tvam iti ced āha na hi ityādi yasmāt na ākāra tulya tā eva bhāvānām tattve tādṛśa tve nimittam yatas gomayetarajat manoḥ śālūkayoḥ ākāra sāmyāt tādṛśa tvam eva syāt na jāti bhedaḥ kutas etat iti āha abhinna ākārāṇām api ityādi yeṣām api hi samāna ākāra tā keṣāñcid bhāvānām teṣām api yatas ākārāt anyatas viśeṣāt jāti bhedaḥ dṛśyate tatas na ākāra sāmyam eva jāti eka tve nibandhanam tathā hi ākāra sāmye 
HBṬ_3.5.10	 api kvacid puṣpāt bhedaḥ dṛśyate nīla itara kusumayoḥ iva sūryayoḥ kvacid phalāt vandhyetarayoḥ iva kark koṭakyoḥ kvacid rasāt vandhyetarayoḥ iva trapuṣayoḥ kvacid gandhāt vṛkṣa itara prabhavayoḥ iva campakayoḥ kvacid prabhāvāt sparśa upayoga sraṃsinyoḥ iva haritakyoḥ iti tasmāt ākāra sāmya nibandhanam yadi api tat eva idam iti pratyabhijñānam sajātīyatām gomayetarajat manoḥ śālūkayoḥ upakalpayati tathā api vilakṣaṇa sāmagrī janya tayā tayoḥ jāti bhedaḥ eva avagantavyaḥ na eka jāti tāḥ tatas eva pratyabhijñānasya bhrānta tayā tad kalpitasya tādṛśa tvasya alīka tvāt 
HBṬ_3.6.1–3.6.2	 yadi punar gomaya itarādi janmanaḥ śālūka ādeḥ agni dhūma ādi janmanaḥ vā dhūma ādeḥ pratyabhijñā vaśāt vilakṣaṇa sāmagrī nibandhana tve api samāna svabhāva tā eva syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt iti atas āha anyathā hi ityādi yadi hi yā sva jāti lakṣaṇa pratyaya antara sahitā sāmagrī yā ca sva jāti nirapekṣā gomaya ādi rūpā śālūka ādeḥ dhūmasya vā yā agni indhana ādi lakṣaṇā yā ca śakra mūrddha ādi svabhāvāḥ dhūma ādi ātmikā tasyāḥ vilakṣaṇāyāḥ api sāmagryāḥ avilakṣaṇam tādṛśam eva kāryam dhūmaśālūka ādikam utpadyeta tadā na kāraṇasya sāmagrī rūpasya bheda abhedābhyām vailakṣaṇya availakṣaṇyābhyām kāryasya bheda abhedau vailakṣaṇyā vailakṣaṇye tad jātīya vijātīya ātmake syātām iti kṛtvā viśvasya sakalasya padārtha rāśeḥ ahetukau bheda abhedau sajātīya vijātīya tve syātām tasmāt yatra vilakṣaṇā sāmagrī tatra kutaścid sāmyāt sarūpa tve api vijātīyatā eva kāryasya iti 
HBṬ_3.6.3	 nanu dhūma indhana ādi sāmagrī bhede api dhūmasya na jāti bhedam āmanti vidvāṃsaḥ atad rūpa parāvṛtteḥ ubhayatra samā anta tvāt na eṣa doṣaḥ kṣaṇa bheda āśraya sūkṣma avāntara jāti bhede api sthūla santāna āśraya vijātīya vyāvṛtteḥ samāna tvāt śābaleya ādi avāntara jāti bhedepi ago vyāvṛtti nibandhana go jāti vat gavām sarva dhūmānām eka santāna vyavasthā api upādānakāraṇa kṣaṇa bhede api eka ākāra pratyaya nibandhana tayā samāna tvāt ādyasya indhana prabhavasya katham iti ced na indhana jāti anuvidhānāt sarva dhūmānām tathā hi aguru karpūra candana ādi jāti bhedam anukurvanti eva tad dhūmāḥ kāḥ aśvāsa ādi hara dravya nirmita vartti bhedam ca tad dhūmāḥ tad rasa vīrya vipāka anuvidhānāt na ca ākāra anyatayā vijātīya tvam yatas na ākārā abheda bheda nibandhane sajātīya vijātīya tve na hi śāli aṅkura ādayaḥ tad vīja ādi ākāram anukurvate na ca tad jātīya tām aśāli ādi vyāvṛtti nibandhanām na anubhavanti tasmāt indhanam eva tasya upādāna kāraṇam agni ādi sahakāri pratyaya āhita viśeṣam tathāvidham dhūma kāryam aṅgāra ādi bhinna ākṛti janyati iti alam atiprasaṅgena 
HBṬ_3.6.4	 nanu ca yadi nāma sāmagrī bhede api kāryasya bhedaḥ na jātaḥ tadā kāraṇa bhede sati api tasya abhāvāt tasya ahetuka tā astu abhedasya tu kim āyātam yena ubhayoḥ ahetuka tvam ucyate iti atas āha tathā hi ityādi yadā hi sāmagrī bhede sati api kāryasya bhedaḥ na jātaḥ iti tasya ahetuka tvam na hi hetau sati abhavataḥ kathañcid api hetumat ta upapadyate tadā yaḥ api asau abhedaḥ kāryasya saḥ api sāmagryoḥ bhinna tvāt asati abhede jātaḥ iti kutas tasya api hetumat tā  yathā hi hetau sati abhavataḥ na hetumat tā tathā hetau asati api bhavataḥ hetumat tā kutas syāt  hetu bhedasya evā abheda nibandhana tvāt naḥ iti ced na tarhi ayam bhedaḥ kvacid padam ābadhnīyāt śālī kodrava ādeḥ api hetu bhedasya abheda hetu tvāt nimittam antareṇa kalpanāyām viśeṣa abhāvāt pratibhāsā bhedasya ca kutaścid bhrānti nimittāt paramārthataḥ bhede api upalakṣaṇāt syāt etat yaḥ hi atādṛśāt api tādṛśa udbhavam 
HBṬ_3.6.5	 icchati tasya bheda abhedayoḥ ahetuka tvam iṣṭam eva bhāvāḥ eva kevalam hetumantaḥ iti atas āha tad vyatiriktaḥ ca ityādi na hi bheda abheda vyatiriktaḥ kaścid bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ asti yaḥ tayoḥ ahetuka tve api hetumān syāt tasya tābhyām anya tve asya imau bheda abhedau iti sambandha abhāva prasaṅgāt tad anya sambandha kalpanāyām anavasthā doṣāt ananya tve api bheda abhedayoḥ bhāva svabhāvasya ca sva ātmani eva avasthānāt anupakārāt ca kutas sambandhitā  upakāra kalpanāyām ca yadi bhāva svabhāvaḥ sva hetubhyaḥ eva na kutaścid bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā samutpannaḥ iti iṣyate tadā tad bhāve api svabhāvānyathātva abhāvāt kutas bhinna abhinna tā bhāva svabhāvasya syāt  atha avyatirikta bheda abheda vaśāt bheda abhedau svabhāvaḥ pratipadyeta tau api yadi bhinnau tadā bhāva svabhāvaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti na tasya kutaścid svarūpataḥ bhedaḥ abhedaḥ vā syāt punar tad vaśāt bheda abheda kalpanāyām bhāva svabhāvasya tad avastham tādavasthyam 
HBṬ_3.6.6	 anavasthā ca bheda abhedayoḥ atha abhinnau tadā bhāva svabhāvaḥ eva bheda abhedābhyām kriyate iti syāt tasya rūpa antareṇa karaṇa asambhavāt tasya ca hetu antarāt paścāt bhavataḥ tatas anyatva āpatteḥ na ca bhāva svabhāvaḥ kriyate tasya sva hetoḥ eva nirvṛtteḥ sva hetubhyaḥ eva bhāva svabhāvasya kutaścid bhinna abhinna ātmanaḥ utpatti kalpanāyām vā bheda abhedayoḥ vyatirekavatoḥ vayarthyam bheda abheda buddheḥ api tatas eva siddheḥ tasmāt vaiśeṣika ādi kalpitayoḥ bheda abhedayoḥ viśeṣa sāmānya ātmanoḥ ayogātbhāva svabhāva eva bheda abheda śabda vācyaḥ tayoḥ ahetuka tve bhāva svabhāvasya eva ahetuka tvam āpatitam tatas bhāvānām ahetuka tvāt nityam sattvam asattvam vā syāt ahetuka tve hi bhāvānām yadi kadācid sattvam sarvadā eva syāt atha kadācid asattvam tat api sarvadā syāt kādācid ka tvam tu sattvasya ayuktam kim kāraṇam  apekṣyasya ahetuka tve sati kasyacid abhāvāt yasmāt apekṣayāhi tasya apekṣaṇīyasya 
HBṬ_3.6.7–3.6.8	 hetoḥ bhāve bhavantaḥ abhāve ca na bhavantaḥ kādācid kāḥ kadācid bhavāḥ yujyante na anyathā iti tasmāt na vilakṣaṇāt kāraṇāt avilakṣaṇasya kāryasya utpattiḥ abhyupagantavyā yathā uktena nyāyena ahetuka tva ādi prasaṅgāt punar api vilakṣaṇāyāḥ sāmagryāḥ avilakṣaṇasya kāryasya utpattau doṣa antaram āha vyavasthāvān= ca pratiniyataḥ sādhyeṣu ghaṭa paṭa ādiṣu sādhanānām mṛd tantu ādīnām loke yaḥ niyogaḥ ghaṭa arthī mṛd piṇḍam eva tatra niyuṅkte na tantūn paṭa arthī ca tantūn eva na mṛd piṇḍam iti ādikaḥ sa na syāt kasmāt iti āha kāraṇānām sāmagrīṇām yāḥ śaktayaḥ ātma atiśaya lakṣaṇāḥ tāsām pratiniyame kācid eva sāmagrī kvacid eva kārye upayujyate na anyā anyatra iti evaṃrūpe hi yasmāt kiñcid eva mṛdā ādikam kasyacid eva ghaṭa ādeḥ sādhanāya upādīyate na aparam tad vilakṣaṇam tantu ādikam kasmāt evam iti ced tasya eva mṛd ādeḥ tatra ghaṭa ādau śakteḥ yogya tvāt anyasya tantu ādeḥ tatra aśakteḥ kasmāt tasya eva tatra śaktiḥ na anyasya 
HBṬ_3.6.9–3.6.10	 iti atas āha tayoḥ mṛd ādeḥ tantu ādeḥ ca tad janana svabhāva tvena ghaṭa ādi janana svabhāva tvena itara svabhāva tvena ca ghaṭa ādyajanana svabhāvena ca bhedāt anya tva bhāvāt na hi mṛd tantu ādi rūpa tātaḥ anyat eva tad janana itara svabhāva tvam nāma yadā tu sāmagrīṇām paraspara vilakṣaṇānām api śakti pratiniyamaḥ na iṣyate vilakṣaṇāt api avilakṣaṇa kārya upagamāt tadā tad janana svabhāva vilakṣaṇāt api dhūma ādi janana svabhāvam yat kāraṇam agni indhana ādi sāmagrī lakṣaṇam tad vilakṣaṇāt api śakra mūrddha ādeḥ kṣaṇa āśrayeṇa vā dhūma ādeḥ tasya agni indhana ādi sāmagrī janyasya dhūmasya tad lakṣaṇasya ca utpattau iṣyamāṇāyām na tad janana śakteḥ pratiniyamaḥ vivakṣita dhūma ādi kārya janana śakti pratiniyamaḥ iti tasmāt yat kiñcid kāryam yatas kutaścid kāraṇāt syāt utpadyeta na yathādṛṣṭam eva yathādṛṣṭāt sarvam sarvatas jāyeta iti yāvat tasmāt śakti pratiniyamaḥ kāraṇānām abhyupagantavyaḥ tatas vilakṣaṇa sāmagrī janmanaḥ kāryasya kutaścid sāmyāt sarūpasya upalakṣaṇe api anyādṛśa tā eva iti sarvaḥ tādṛśaḥ tathāvidha janma iti siddham 
HBṬ_3.6.11	 syāt matam vilakṣaṇāyāḥ api sāmagryāḥ tad lakṣaṇa kārya janana śaktiḥ samānā iti tad lakṣaṇam kāryam bhaviṣyati kasyāścid eva ca tathā abhāvāt na yathā udita doṣa avasaraḥ iti atas āha tad janana śakti sāmye tu ityādi uktam eva tāvat atra pūrva pakṣe na ca dhūmasya tad atad janya svabhāvaḥ iti ādikam dūṣaṇam abhyupagamya api idam āha yādṛśīhi agni sahakāriṇaḥ tad ādhīyamāna vikārasya indhanasya sva bhedena dhūma bheda hetoḥ śaktiḥ ātmā atiśayaḥ tādṛśi eva śakra mūrddhnaḥ dhūmasya vā yadi tad sāmagrī janya dhūma avilakṣaṇa kārya janana śaktiḥ ātma atiśaya lakṣaṇā tadā tad śakti sāmye tat eva agni indhana ādikam eva arthāt nāma antareṇa uktam syāt tad vilakṣaṇasya tad vilakṣaṇa ātmā atiśaya asambhavāt saḥ eva hi agniḥ yaḥ indhana vikāram ādadhānaḥ dhūmam janayati tat ca indhanam yat agninā aadhīyamāna vikāram dhūmam 
HBṬ_3.6.12	 sva jātim anukārayati yadi ca śakra mūrddha ādeḥ api evam bhavatā abhyupagamyate tadā kevalam nāmni vivādaḥ syāt artha abhedam abhyupagamya tathā abhidhānāt yatas evam iti tasmāt kāryam dhūma ādikam dṛṣṭam ekadā pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām niścitam atad rūpa vyāvṛttena ātmanā kāraṇam indhana ādikam santāna apekṣayā kṣaṇa apekṣayā vā na vyabhicarati tad vilakṣaṇāt anyatas na bhavati iti kārya hetau anvaya vyatireka niścayaḥ sidhyati iti 
HBṬ_4.1.1	 tat evam kārya hetau yatas yat bhava dṛṛṣṭaṃsakṛt pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyāṃtādṛśasya sarvasya tathāvidhāt eva janma na tad vijātīyāt iti ekasyāḥ api kārya vyakteḥ kutaścid bhāva darśane vyāptyā anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ iti pratipāditam anupalabdhau tu yathā uktāyām nimitta antara abhāva upadarśana nibandhanayoḥ na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ vipratipattiḥ svarūpaḥ eva tu pare vipratipadyante tathā hi kecid upalabdhi abhāva mātram anupalabdhim abhāvasya prasajya pratiṣedha ātmanaḥ pramāṇa antara tvena gamikām icchantii īśvara sena prabhṛtayaḥ apare tu pratiṣedhya viṣaya jñāna viṣaya rūpeṇa apariṇāmaḥ ātmanaḥ tad anya vastu viṣayam vijñānam eva vā abhāvasya gamakam pratyakṣa anumāna abhyam pramāṇa antaram āhuḥ mmīmāṃsakāḥ na hi anya vastu viṣayam jñānam pratyakṣa anumāna ātmakam 
HBṬ_4.1.2	 abhāvam pratipadyate tasya bhāva aṃśa viṣaya tvāt abhāva aṃśasya ca tatas anya tvāt bhāva aṃśa janayat iti tu na asti iti jñānam janayat tad abhāva pramāṇa ākhyam labhate yathā indriyam sva viṣaya pratipatti janaka tvena pratyakṣa ākhyām tathā anye anya bhāva lakṣaṇām tad jñāna lakṣaṇām vā anupalabdhim abhāvasya eva sādhanam āhuḥ na abhā= a vyavahārasya anupalabdheḥ liṅgāt abhāva siddhau svayam eva tad vyavahāra pravṛtteḥ naiyāyikāḥ tu na asti iti jñānam eva kevala pradeśa ādi grāhi jñāna anantara bhāvi pratyakṣam na pramāṇa antaram abhāvasya tuccha rūpasya pariccheda ātmakam ācakṣate tat eva asya ghaṭa ādeḥ pratiṣedhyasya anupalabdhi śabdena yadi ucyate na kaścid virodhaḥ iti tat evam anupalabdhau bhedam gatāḥ buddhayaḥ prativādinām iti tad nirāsa artham anupalabdhi svarūpam tāvat upadarśayan āha upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya ityādi upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ 
HBṬ_4.1.3	 upalambha pratyaya antarāṇām samanantara adhipati pratyaya saṃjñitānām sākalyam ālambana pratyayasya svabhāva viśeṣaḥ ca yaḥ svabhāvaḥ satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu san pratyakṣaḥ eva bhavati iti evaṃrūpa aśāstra kṛtā anyatra vyākhyātā naiyāyika vipratipatti nirāsa artham te hi anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpti śabdena mahattva aneka dravyavat tva rūpāṇi dravyāṇām āhuḥ mahatī iti aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ evam vacanāt iti evaṃca upa labdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ sati api vastuni sambhavati iti asat vyavahāra siddhau anaikāntikī iti ācakṣate na hi cākṣuṣasya api raśmeḥ mahattva aneka dravyavat tva rūpāṇi upalambhakāni bhavanti na ca tāvatā anupalambha api asat vyavahāraḥ tatra śakyate karttum yat āhabhāṣya kāraḥ na anumānataḥ upalabhyamānasya 
HBṬ_4.1.4	 pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ abhāve hetuḥ iti indriya tvāt tvac ādi vat kila prāpya kāri cakṣuḥ iti anumānataḥ cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ upalabhyate tasya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ katham abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet iti tat evam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhim asat vyavahāre anaikāntikīm āhuḥ naiyāyikāḥ tad nirāsa artham upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ aviparīta rūpa upadarśanena śāstra kāraḥ abhyadhāt yadā ahi upalambha pratyaya antarasākalyam svabhāva viśeṣaḥ ca yathā ukta upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ ucyate na mahat tva ādikam tadā kutas vyabhicāra avakāśaḥ  sati vastuni tasyāa sambhavāt mahat tva ādikaṃtu asambhavāt eva na upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpti śabdena vācyam na hi rūpa ādi vyatiriktam dravyam tad pratibhāsa vivekinā aakāra antareṇa sva jñāne pratibhāsate na ca apratibhāsamānam anātma rūpa vivekinā 
HBṬ_4.1.5	 rūpeṇa pratyakṣatām anubhavati atiprasaṅgāt tat kutas asyāḥ asataḥ mahat tva ādi sambhavaḥ  na ca svarūpeṇa amahataḥ tad sambandhe api asya mahat tā sambhavaḥ apara rūpeṇa vā grahaṇe kathaṃtad grāhi jñānam abhrāntam  tatas na mahat tvam dravyasya upalambhakaṃrūpam vā tasya api sva rūpeṇa grahaṇe dravya ātmanaḥ atyanta parokṣa tvāt dravya rūpasya ca tad vivekena anupalakṣaṇāt na tathā āgrāhaka tvam na ca mahat tvam rūpam vā dravya udaya kāle abhyupagamyate yatas dravyam guṇasya samavāyi kāraṇam iṣyate tat ca pratilabdha ātmakam eva tathā ātām anubhavati iti prathame kṣaṇe dravyam nirguṇam eva na ca asya dvitīye kṣaṇe prāktana rūpa tyāgaḥ asti rūpa antaram vā aavirbhavati yatas prāc apratipanna ādhāra bhāvam mahat tva ādi guṇa pratibandhāt ādhāra tām yāyāt na ca ajanakaḥ ādhāraḥ janaka tve ca kṣaṇika tā artha kriyā virodhāt akṣaṇikasya tatas 
HBṬ_4.1.6–4.1.7^1	 kutas samavāyi kāraṇasya sambhavaḥ  yatas sva utkalitaṃkāryam janayat tathā vyapadiśyate na ca etat kṣaṇika tve sambhavati akṣaṇika tve vā prāk anādhārasya paścāt ādhāra abhāvaḥ samavāyi kāraṇā sambhavāt eva aneka dravyavat tvam api asambhavi yasmāt anekam dravyam ārambhakam samavāyi kāraṇa ātmanā yasya vidyate tat evaṃvyapadiśyate dravya abhāvāt ca na aneka dravyavat tvam sattve api mahat tva ādeḥ na iyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ asmākam abhimatā 
HBṬ_4.1.6–4.1.7^2	 yā tu abhimatā na tayā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ asat vyavahāra siddhau= anaikāntikī iti śāstra kāraḥ darśayām babhūva upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya yā anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇasya vyāpakasya vā pratiṣedhyāt anyasya sā abhāva hetuḥ kāryasya vyāpyasya ca abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ ca yātu pratiṣedhyasya eva upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ sā abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ eva iti vā śabdena darśayati yā tu anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ pratyakṣa anumāna nivṛtti lakṣaṇā sā saṃśaya hetuḥ pramāṇa nivṛttau api artha abhāva asiddheḥ nimitta abhāvāt tu sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha hetuḥ iti avagantavyam 
HBṬ_4.2.1	 tatra ye tāvat upalabdhi abhāva mātram anupalabdhim icchanti vijñānaṃvā anya vastuni iti vacanāt tad anya vastu vijñānam eva vā tad nirāsa artham jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇām anupalabdhim darśayitum upalabdhim eva tāvat dvividhām darśayan āha atra anupalabdhi vākye yā upalabdhiḥ śrūyate kriyā rūpā sā yadā kartṛstha tayā apekṣyate tadā tasyāḥ upalabhamānasya kartuḥ dharma tve apekṣyamāṇe tat jñānam upalabhamānasya yat jñānam tat upalabdhiḥ ucyate upalabhamānaḥ ca buddhīndriya deha kalāpaḥ eva ca pūrva kṣaṇa saṅgṛhīta upalabdhijanakaḥ ucyate tathā hi upalabdheḥ janakaḥ āśrayaḥ vā karttā paraiḥ ucyate na ca indriya ādeḥ anyasya janaka tvam sambhavati yatas anvaya vyatireka nibandhanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva vyavahāraḥ tau ca anvaya vyatirekau na indriya ādeḥ anyasya sambhavataḥ satsu indriya ādiṣu niyamena upalabdheḥ bhāvāt yadi 
HBṬ_4.2.2–4.2.4	 hi indriyā ādiṣu satsu api kadācid upalabdhiḥ na upajāyate tadā satsu api anyeṣu sakaleṣu hetuṣu kārya anutpattiḥ kāraṇa antara vaikalyam sūcayati iti tad vyatirikta kāraṇa antaram parikalpyeta na ca etat asti tat katham ātmanaḥ tad utpattau nimitta bhāvaḥ abhyupagamyeta atiprasaṅgāt yat āha yasmin sati bhavati eva yat tatas anyasya kalpane tad hetu tvena sarvatra hetūnām anavasthitiḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.5	 āśraya tvam api janakasya eva iti tat api ātmanaḥ na sambhavati sthāpaka tvāt āśrayaḥ iti ced na kṣāṇika tve sthiteḥ abhāvāt upalabdheḥ akṣaṇika tve api svayam eva avināśāt avasthānāt tathā hi upalabdheḥ avināśaḥ eva sthitiḥ ucyate na pāta abhāvaḥ tasyāḥ guru tva abhāvāt saṃyoga abhāvena guru tvāt patanam iti capareṣāṃkṛta antaḥ samavāyāt āśrayaḥ iti ced nanu saḥ api ādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām eva iṣyate na ca āpatana dharmikāyāḥ upalabdheḥ ādhāreṇa kiṃcid samavāyāt ca āśraya tve anyasya api tad bhāva prasaṅgaḥ tasya sarva ātmasu samāna tvāt eka tvena asya upagamāt krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virodhāt ca na asya ātmanaḥ sattvam tatas asya kutas janaka tvam āśraya tvam vā iti alam kṣuṇṇa kṣodīkaraṇena iti 
HBṬ_4.2.6^1	 evam upalabdhim ādarśya anupalabdhim ādarśayan āha tasmāt upalabdhi jñānāt anyā vastu antara viṣayāḥ upalabdhiḥ jñāna ātmikā anupalabdhiḥ katham punar upalabdhiḥ eva anupalabhdiḥ ucyate iti āha vivakṣitā ityādi yathā bhakṣya abhakṣya prakaraṇe vivakṣitāt bhakṣyāt anya tvāt abhakṣyaḥ grāmya kukkuṭaḥ bhakṣyaḥ api san tad anyasya ucyate yathā ca sparśanīyā sparśanīya adhikāre vivakṣitāt sparśanīyāt anya tvāt asparśanīyaḥ cāṇḍāla ādiḥ tad anyasya sparśanīyaḥ api san ucyate tadvat upalabdhiḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ mmantavyāḥ nañaḥ pratiṣedha viṣaya tvāt katham bhāva viṣaya tā iti ced āha paryudāsa vṛttyā iti paryudāsena pratiṣedhyasya arthasya varjanena yā viśiṣṭe arthe vṛttiḥ tayā nañaḥ āgṛhīta pratiṣedhasya bhāva viṣaya tā 
HBṬ_4.2.6^2	 yatra vidheḥ prādhānyam pratiṣedhaḥ artha gṛhītaḥ vidhi bhāj sva padena na ucyate eka vākyatā ca tatra paryudāsa vṛtti tā vidheḥ ca prādhānyam vivakṣita upalabdheḥ anya upalabdhiḥ bhavati iti evam vākyena anya upalabdheḥ vidhānāt anya upalabdhi sāmarthyāt eva vivakṣita upalabdheḥ pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate vivakṣita upalabdheḥ anivarttane tad apekṣayā anyasyāḥ vidhāna ayogāt sva padena nañā vidhi bhāj na ucyate kim tarhi  anya śabdena paryudāsā āśrayeṇā anya śabdasya eva vākye prayogāt anyā upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ iti nañaḥ ca subantena sāmarthyam na tiṅantena iti eka vākya tvam naḥ upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ iti prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ punar etad viparītaḥ mantavyaḥ tatra hi pratiṣedhasya prādhānyam vidhiḥ arthāt gamyate vākya bhedaḥ sva padena nañā pratiṣedha bhāj sambadhyate 
HBṬ_4.2.7	 tat evam jñātṛ dharma lakṣaṇām anupalabdhim vyākhyāya jñeya dharma lakṣaṇām pratipādayan āha upalabhyamāna dharma tvaḥ ityādi yadā karma stha kriyā apekṣayā upalabhyamānasya vastunaḥ dharmaḥ upalabdhiḥ vivakṣyate tadā viṣaya svabhāvaḥ upalabdhiḥ mantavyāḥ kīdṛśaḥ viṣaya svabhāvaḥ iti āha sva viṣaya ityādi pratiṣedhyasya ghaṭa ādeḥ yad ā ātma viṣayam vijñānam tat janane yā yogya tā tad lakṣaṇaḥ viṣaya svabhāvaḥ upalabdhi śabdena ucyate yadi viṣaya svabhāvaḥ upalabdhiḥ katham yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ  tathā hi yogyatā dharmaḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ ca bhedaḥ eva iti atas āha yogyatāyāḥ ityādi yogya tā hi paramārthataḥ bhāva rūpā eva na vastu svarūpāt bhidyate anyathā bhāvaḥ yogyaḥ eva na syāt yogyatā asya iti ca sambandhaḥ bhāvataḥ na syāt sambandha kalpanāyām anavasthā iti ukta prāyam 
HBṬ_4.2.8	 tat evam upalabdheḥ viṣaya dharma tām pratipādya anupalabdheḥ api pratipādayan āha tasmāt anyaḥ ityādi tasmāt pratiṣedhyāt ghaṭa ādeḥ sva viṣaya jñāna janana yogyāt yaḥ anyaḥ upalambha janana yogyaḥ eva na tad viparītaḥ svabhāvaḥ ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa rūpaḥ saḥ eva ca atra anupalabdhi śabdena ucyate prāktanam eva nyāyam atra adiśan āha pūrvavat iti vivakṣita upalabdheḥ anya tvāt abhakṣya asparśanīya vat paryudāsa vṛttyā iti katham punar ayam nan anya artha vṛttiḥ sāmānya śabdaḥ san ghaṭa vivikta pradeśasya tad jñānasya eva vā ghaṭa viviktasya anupalabdhi tvam paryudāsa vṛttyā prakalpayati na punar aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣām eva anya śabda vācyānām iti atas āha yatra yasmin ityādi yatra deśe kāla avasthāyām vā avyavadhāna ādi lakṣaṇāyām yasmin pradeśa rūpa ādau upalabhyamāne niyamena avaśyaṃtayā yasya anyasya 
HBṬ_4.2.9^1	 padārthasya ghaṭra rūpa ādeḥ upalabdhiḥ bhavati sa ghaṭa rūpa ādiḥ padārthaḥ tad saṃsṛṣṭaḥ tena pradeśa rūpa ādinā saṃsṛṣṭaḥ katham ekasmin upalabhyamāne parasya api niyama upalabdhiḥ iti ced yogyatāyāḥ aviśeṣāt pradeśa ghaṭayoḥ hi sva viṣaya vijñāna janane yogyatā tulyā yadā hi pradeśa rūpam vyavadhāna vipra karṣa ādi rahitam vijñāne su a ākāram samarppayati tadā ghaṭa rūpam api tatra tathāvidham su a ākāram samarppayati eva yadi nāma yogyatā tasya tena tulyā sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ tu katham tad saṃsṛṣṭa tā iti atas āha eka jñāna saṃsarggāt iti ekatra hi jñāne dvau api tau su a ākāra dvāreṇa saṃsṛṣṭau na sākṣāt tat vijñānam padārtha dvaya ākāram ājāyamānam tayoḥ ātmani saṃsarggam darśayati kim iti punar tat jñānam padārtha dvaya ākāram avaśyam bhavati yatas tayoḥ jñāna dvārakaḥ saṃsarggaḥ iti atas āha tayoḥ satoḥ ityādi 
HBṬ_4.2.9^2	 yau etau tulya yogya tā rūpau tau yadi santau bhavataḥ tadā na eva eka ākāra niyatā pratipattiḥ bhavati kasmāt asambhavāt na hi eṣa sambhavaḥ asti yat tulya yogya tā rūpayoḥ ekaḥ eva pratibhāseta na aparaḥ iti tathā hi aviśiṣṭa tvāt yogyatāyāḥ kaḥ tatra su a ākāram na samarppayet  anubhava siddhim ca yugapad aneka pratibhāsanam na ca anubhava viruddham ācakṣaṇāḥ viduṣām avadheya vacasaḥ bhavanti laghu vṛtti tvāt yaugapadya abhimānaḥ iti ced na bādhaka pratyaya viraheṇa bhrānti kalpanā anupapatteḥ sarvatra tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt karaṇa dharmaḥ eva ayam yat ekasmin eva karmaṇi kriyām niṣpādayati na anekatra karaṇam ca indriyam tatas na aneka pratipatti hetuḥ iti ced katham pradīpa ādiḥ anekatra bahūnām pratipatti janakaḥ  kartṛ bhedāt adoṣaḥ iti ced karttṛ eka tvāt tarhi kriyā ekatra karmāṇi iti katham karaṇa dharmaḥ ityādi vacaḥ na plavate  na ca pratikṣaṇa viśara aruṣu bhāveṣu paramārthataḥ kartṛ karaṇa ādi bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.10	 kriyā vā kācid na ca sarrva kāraka anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyini kārye kasyacid atiśayaḥ asti yena ayam karttā karaṇam ca idam ityādi parikalpyeta tasmāt aviśiṣṭa yogya tayoḥ kutas eka rūpa niyatāyāḥ pratipatteḥ sambhavaḥ iti siddhaḥ eka jñāna saṃsarggaḥ tulya yogya tā rūpa tvasya ca etat eva liṅgam na hi asati tulya yogya tā rūpa tve yugapad eka indriya janita jñāna pratibhāsitā rūpa rasavat sambhavati iti 
HBṬ_4.2.11	 tatra yeṣāṃsaugatānām idam darśanam eka āyatana saṅgṛhīte anekatra api ekam eva indriya jñānam ājāyate iti teṣām mukhyaḥ eva eka jñāna saṃsarggaḥ ye tu tatra api pratyartham bhinnāni eva eka indriya nimittāni eka kālāni tad viṣayāṇām yugapad sannihitānām sva jñāneṣu sāmarthya aviśeṣāt atas eva ekatayā loke adhyavasīyamānāni jñānāni upajāyante iti varṇayanti teṣām eka indriya ja tvena eka āyatana viṣaya tvena ca eka kāleṣu eka tva vyapadeśaḥ loke tathā adhyavasāyāt aupacārikaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.12	 yadi nāma eka jñāna saṃsarggāt tad saṃsṛṣṭasya api sāmānyena sarvam anyam ayam nan kid na pratipādayati iti atas āha tasmāt ityādi yasmāt aviśiṣṭa tvāt yogyatāyāḥ yathā uktena prakāreṇa ekatra jñāne dvayoḥ api saṃsarggaḥ tasmāt aviśiṣṭam yogyatā rūpam yayoḥ tata eva eka jñāna saṃsarggiṇau tau tasmāt tayoḥ evaṃrūpayoḥ paraspara apekṣam eva na sarva anya padārtha apekṣam anya tvam iha anupalabdhi adhikāre abhipretam loke tu yadi aviśeṣa padārtha antara apekṣam anya tvam nañā kvacid ucyate vyāpti nyāya samāśrayāt tathā api tat iha na gṛhyate pratyāsatteḥ āśrayaṇāt eka jñāna saṃsargga lakṣaṇā pratti āsattiḥ āśrīyate nā anyā pramāṇa cintā adhikārāt anyathā anupalabdhiḥ anaikāntikī a iva syāt tasmāt tattva cintakaiḥ tathāvidham anya tvam āśrayaṇīyam yat anupalabdheḥ avyabhicāra nibandhanam tat ca yathoktam eva iti abhiprāyaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.13	 tat evam eka jñāna saṃsargga apekṣayā anya tvam pratipādya anupalabdhim darśayan āha sa kevalaḥ ityādi saḥ eva yadā kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ yathā ukta ghaṭa apekṣayā tasmāt anyaḥ ucyate tadā ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa jñānam vā anupalabdhiḥ na tu yathā īśvarasenaḥ manyate upalabdhi abhāva mātram anupalabdhiḥ iti vakṣyamāṇa doṣāt ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa svabhāvaḥ vā na tu tad vivikta jñānam eva yathā ahakumārilaḥ vijñānaṃvānya vastuni iti yathā hi anya vastu viṣayam jñānam anubhūyamānam pratiyogi smaraṇa apekṣam tad abhāva vyavahāra nibandhanam tathā tad viviktaḥ pradeśaḥ api tathā hi kasyacid pratipattuḥ yatas kevala pradeśa ākāram eva jñānam mayā saṃvedyate na tu ghaṭa ākāram api tasmāt atra ghaṭaḥ na asti iti evam na astita ajñānam utpadyate kasyacid tu yatas kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ ayam dṛśyate na tu ghaṭa sahitaḥ tasmāt na asti atra ghaṭaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.14–4.2.15	 evam tasmāt ubhayoḥ na astita ajñāna janmani tulyam sāmarthyam iti dvayoḥ api anupalabdhi vyavasthā yuktā iti tatra yadā tat jñānam tadā jñātṛ dharma lakṣaṇā anupalabdhiḥ kartṛstha kriyā a pekṣayā yadā tad svabhāvaḥ tadā jñeya dharma lakṣaṇā karma stha kriyā apekṣayā iti evam anupalabdhim paryudāsa vṛttyā vyavasthāpya sādhyam asyāḥ darśayan āha sāabhāvam ityādi sarva anya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta vivikte api pradeśa ādau dṛśyamāne yatra ghaṭa ādau pratiyogini arthi tva ādibhiḥ smṛtiḥ asya bhavati tasya abhāvam sādhayati abhāva vyavahāram vā kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhī abhāvam abhāva vyavahāram ca sādhayataḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ tu abhāva vyavahāram eva abhāva vyavahāraḥ ca jñāna bhidhāna pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ tatra na asti atra ghaṭaḥ iti evam ākāram jñānam evaṃvidha vastu abhidhāyakam ca abhidhānam niḥśaṅkasya ca tatra pradeśe gamana āgamana lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.16	 atra īśvara sena kumārilayoḥ vacana avakāśam āśaṅkya siddhānta vyavasthām eva kurvatā tad mate niraste api āhatya tad mata nirāsa artham āha katham anya bhāvaḥ ityādi īśvarasenaḥ hi manyate kārya svabhāva hetubhyām bhāva rūpābhyām anupalabdheḥ pṛthak karaṇāt avaśyam abhāva rūpa tvam asyāḥ anyathā pṛthakkaraṇam anarthakam eva syāt tvayā ca anyasya pratiṣedhya viviktasya pradeśa ādeḥ tat jñānasya vā bhāva rūpa anupalabdhiḥ ākhyāyate tat nūnam anya bhāvaḥ tad abhāvaḥ yena evam abhidhīyate na ca etat yujyate bhāva abhāvayoḥ virodhāt eka ātma tā anupapatteḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.17–4.2.20	 kumārilaḥ api evam manyate yā iyam jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇāḥ dvidhā anupalabdhiḥ abhāva rūpā tvayā ucyate tasyāḥ bhavatu na astita ajñānam prati sādhana bhāvaḥ kintu saḥ eva anyasya pratiṣedhya viviktasya vastunaḥ pratiṣedhya jñānāt anyasya vā tat jñānasya yaḥ bhāvaḥ bhāva aṃśaḥ sa katham abhāvaḥ pratiṣedhyasya tat jñānasya vā katham abhāva aṃśaḥ  na eva yujyate dharma rūpa tayā bhāva abhāva aṃśayoḥ bhedāt sati api dharmi rūpeṇa abhede tayoḥ ca udbhava abhibhavābhyām grahaṇa agrahaṇa vyavasthā iti yat āha dharmayoḥ bhedaḥ iṣṭaḥ hi dharmya bhede api naḥ sthite udbhava abhibhava ātma tvāt grahaṇaṃca avatiṣṭhate iti 
HBṬ_4.2.21	 ukta uttara tām asya darśayan āha uktam uttaram atra codye yathā paryudāsa vṛtti ā aapekṣātaḥ pratiṣedhyam tat jñānam vā apekṣya tad viviktaḥ arthaḥ tat jñānam vā abhāvaḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca ucyate itiīśvarasenasya prativacanam na hi prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ eva ekaḥ nañarthaḥ kin tu paryudāsaḥ api tatas anya bhāvasya abhāva rūpa tā na virudhyate prasajya pratiṣedha rūpa tā api anya bhāvasya yathā tathā uttaratra vakṣyate svabhāva hetoḥ tu anupalabdheḥ pṛthak karaṇam pratipattṛ abhiprāya vaśāt pratipattā hi svabhāva hetau vastu pratipatti adhyavasāyī anupalabdhau tu abhāva pratipatti adhyavasāyī paramārthataḥ tu pratiṣedhya abhāva vyavahāra yogya tā vastu bhūtā eva pradeśasya sādhyate iti na svabhāva hetoḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ bhidyate iti 
HBṬ_4.2.22^1	 yat tu anapekṣita artha antara saṃsarggam pratiṣedha mātram anupalabdhiḥ iti īśvarasenaḥ manyate tad nirākurvan āha na pratiṣedha mātram ityādi kasmāt iti āha tasya sādhana asiddheḥ ityādi na hi abhāvasya sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇasya sādhana tvam siddhi hetu tvam sidhyati sarva sāmarthya viraha rūpasya tad ayogāt hetu tve vā katham na sāmarthya yogitāḥ bhāva rūpa tā vā  sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt vastunaḥ abhāvasya ca anapekṣita sahakāriṇaḥ anādheya atiśaya tayā na asti iti jñāna janane nityam tad janana prasaṅgaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.22^2	 tatas ca sādhaka tva ayogāt abhāva vyavahāraḥ eva na sidhyet athavā tasya prasajya pratiṣedha ātmanaḥ upalabdhi abhāvasya sādhanam eva kiñcid na sidhyati iti sa hi abhāva tvāt apareṇa upalabdhi abhāvena sādhyaḥ syāt saḥ api apareṇa iti anavasthānam na ca indriya vat ajñātasya pratiṣedha jñāna hetu tā sadā sannihita tvena anapekṣita sahakāriṇaḥ nityam tad udaya prasaṅgāt idam ca artha dvayam katham abhāvaḥ kasyacid pratipattiḥ pratipatti hetuḥ vā  tasya api katham pratipattiḥ iti atra antare svayam eva vipañcayiṣyati 
HBṬ_4.2.23	 kumārilasya api uttaram āha tasya anyasya pratiyoginā vastu antareṇa asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya na hi asau vastu antaraiḥ saṃsṛṣṭa svabhāvaḥ eka rūpaḥ tathā tve hi abhāva aṃśaḥ api na kvacid sidhyet tasya evaṃvidhasya bhāva siddhiḥ eva bhāva aṃśa siddhiḥ eva aparasya pratiyoginaḥ vastu antarasya abhāva siddhiḥ abhāva aṃśasya tvad abhimatasya siddhiḥ astu bhāva aṃśasya eva abhāva aṃśa rūpatā upapatteḥ iti manyate tathā hi abhāva aṃśaḥ api para rūpa asaṃsṛṣṭa tayā eva abhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyate anyathā tad ayogāt sā ca bhāva aṃśasya api samānā iti saḥ eva abhāvaḥ astu tad nimittasya samāna tvāt kim anyena abhāva aṃśa upagatena  atas eva asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya iti viśeṣaṇam yatas evam iti tasmāt anya bhāvaḥ api anyasya vastunaḥ bhāvaḥ api tvad abhimataḥ bhāva aṃśaḥ api na kevalam abhāva aṃśaḥ tvad matyā abhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyate asmābhiḥ tatas bhāva aṃśasya abhāva rūpa tā saṅgatā eva iti 
HBṬ_4.2.24–4.2.25	 na kiñcid virudhyate iti yat uktam jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇayā svabhāva anupalabdhyā abhāva vyavahāraḥ eva sādhyate na abhāvaḥ iti tat paraḥ vighaṭayitum yat ca uktam na pratiṣedha mātram anupalabdhiḥ tasya sādhana asiddheḥ iti dvitīye vyākhyāne pratiṣedha mātrasya anupalabdhiḥ iti etasya sādhanam darśayitum āha anya bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ ityādi evam manyate lokaḥ hi kevala pradeśa darśanāt ghaṭa abhāvam eva prathamam pratipadyate kevala pradeśa jñāna saṃvedana dvāreṇa ghaṭa jñāna abhāva pratipattyā vā tatas ghaṭa abhāvasya vyavahāram tena loka pratīti anusāreṇa pratiṣedhyāt anyasya pradeśasya pratiṣedhya jñānāt vā tat jñānasya yaḥ bhāvaḥ tad lakṣaṇaḥ abhāvaḥ svayam pramāṇena indriya pratyakṣeṇa sva saṃvedana pratyakṣeṇa ca siddhaḥ alam ghaṭa abhāvam sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa ca yathākramam sādhayitum sa ca ghaṭa abhāva vyavahāram iti evam vyavasthāpayitum 
HBṬ_4.2.26	 yuktam na ca evam api vyavasthāpane asmad pakṣasya kācid kṣatiḥ tathā hi pāramparyeṇa api yat anupalabdheḥ tvad abhyupagatāyāḥ siddham tat tat eva siddham bhavati iti pratiṣedha mātrasya anupalabdhi tve tad sādhana pratipādane api ayam abhiprāyaḥ yathā bhavataḥ jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇāḥ bhāva rūpā dvividhā anupalabdhiḥ tathā mama api jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇa upalabdhi abhāvaḥ api anupalabdhi saṃjñitaḥ dvividhaḥ bhaviṣyati tatra jñeya dharma lakṣaṇena anya bhāvena pratyakṣa siddhena pratiṣedhya abhāvaḥ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇa upalabdhi abhāva rūpa anupalabdhi saṃjñitaḥ setsyati jñātṛ dharma lakṣaṇena ca anya bhāvena kevala pradeśa jñāna ātmanā sva saṃvedana siddhena jñātṛ dharmaḥ pratiṣedhya jñāna abhāva rūpaḥ anupalabdhi samākhyātaḥ setsyati tatas ca kutas anavasthā yena sādhana asiddhiḥ syāt iti tatra anya bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ iti pratiṣedhyāt tad jñānāt ca yaḥ anyaḥ bhāvaḥ pratiṣedhya viviktaḥ pradeśaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.27	 tat jñānam ca tad ātmakaḥ abhāvaḥ vivakṣitāt bhāvāt pratiṣedhyāt bhāvāt tad jñānāt ca anya tvāt anupalabdhi tvena bhavataḥ abhimataḥ svayam sva rūpeṇa pramāṇena indriya pratyakṣeṇa sva saṃvedana pratyakṣeṇa ca siddhaḥ saṃs tasya pratiṣedhyasya abhāva vyavahāram jñāna abhidhāna pravṛtti lakṣaṇam sādhayet tad siddhi siddhaḥ vā tasya anya bhāva lakṣaṇasya abhāvasya yathā uktasya siddhyā siddhaḥ vā tad abhāvaḥ tasya pratiṣedhyasya tat jñānasya vā a bhāvaḥ iti evam apīṣyamāṇe na kaścid viśeṣaḥ tvad abhimata anupalabdhito asmad abhimata anupalabdheḥ tatas asmat darśanam kim iti pratikṣipyate  nanu asti eva evam iṣyamāṇe viśeṣaḥ anya bhāva lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ itarayā vyavahitā tad abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet itarā tu sākṣāt iti āha sa viśeṣaḥ na asti yena viśeṣeṇa anupalabdhyā abhāva rūpayā vastu saṃsparśa rahitayā asmad abhimatayā abhāva vyavahāra siddheḥ virodhaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.28	 syāt anyasya tu viśeṣasya sataḥ api abādhaka tvāt asat sama tvam eva yat api uktam tasya sādhana abhāvat abhāva vyavahāra asiddhi prasaṅgaḥ iti tat api asat yatas saḥ eva tvad abhimataḥ anya bhāvaḥ pratiṣedhya vivikta bhū tala ātmakaḥ tad viṣayā ca upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhi tvena iṣṭā bhavatas tad abhāvasya anupalabdhi tvena asmad matasya pratiṣedhya abhāvasya tad upalabdhi abhāvasya ca kim kasmāt na sādhanam liṅgam iṣyate  tathā hi sati loka pratītiḥ anusṛtā bhavati kiṃpunaḥ kasmāt punar abhāvasya dvividhasya siddhiḥ eva tad abhāva siddhiḥ na tad sādhyā kācid anyā vidyate iti asmad mata niṣedha artham loka atikrāntam iṣyate iti pūrva pakṣaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.29	 atra āha apṛthak siddheḥ anya bhāvāt tad abhāvasya pṛthak siddheḥ abhāvāt kutas liṅga liṅgitāḥ tathā sambandha abhāvāt ca anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ na liṅga liṅgitā iti prathamam tāvat kāraṇam vivṛṇvan āha anya bhāvaḥ tad vivikta pradeśa ātmakaḥ tāvat na sādhanam liṅgam pratiṣedhya abhāvasya tad upalabdhiḥ api tad abhāvasya na sādhanam iti paścāt vakṣyate tad artham eva tāvat śabdaḥ kasmāt anya bhāvaḥ na sādhanam iti āha yad siddhau yasya vastunaḥ siddhau pratītau yasya aparasya vastunaḥ na siddhiḥ na pratītiḥ tat vastu tasya vastunaḥ liṅgam bhavati iti ayam liṅga liṅginoḥ nyāyaḥ tatra udāharaṇam dhūma agni vat iti yathā yadā dhūma pratītau na agniḥ pratīyate tadā tayoḥ lliṅga liṅgi bhāvaḥ bhavati na tu dhūma pratīti kāle eva pratīyamāne agnau yadi nāma evam tatas kim iti atas āha anyasya vastunaḥ yaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ tad siddhyā eva 
HBṬ_4.2.30–4.2.31	 tat pratītya eva tad abhāvaḥ tasya pratiṣedhyasya abhāvaḥ prasidhyati pratīyate anya bhāvasya eva tad abhāva ātmaka tvāt tad siddheḥ eva tad siddhi lakṣaṇa tvāt naiyāyikāḥ tu manyante pratiṣedhya abhāvaḥ hi prasajya pratiṣedha ātmakaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ tasya katham tad anya bhāva rūpa tā  bhāva abhāvayoḥ virodhāt tatas katham tad anya bhāva siddhyā eva tad abhāva siddhiḥ syāt iti atas āha tasya tad anya bhāvasya pradeśa lakṣaṇasya tasmāt anyena pratiṣedhyena ghaṭa ādinā asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya rahita ātmanaḥ kevalasya pratiṣedhyena śūnya ātmanaḥ anena kevala pradeśasya api prasajya pratiṣedha ātmaka tām āha katham bhāvasya tuccha rūpa tā svabhāvaḥ virodhāt  iti ced na para rūpeṇa tasya api tuccha rūpa tvāt yathā hi anapekṣita bhāva antara saṃsargaḥ prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ śūnya vikalpa pratibhāsī pratiṣedhyena tuccha rūpaḥ tad rūpa virahāt tathā tad anya bhāvaḥ api pratiṣedhya asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpaḥ tatas katham asya pratiṣedhyena tuccha rūpa tā virudhyeta  sva rūpeṇa hi ayam atuccha rūpaḥ syāt na para rūpeṇa 
HBṬ_4.2.32–4.2.33^1	 anyathā katham asya anya bhāva tvam parasya vā tatra abhāvaḥ syāt  yaḥ hi yat abhāva rūpaḥ na bhavati saḥ eva asau bhavati tad svarūpa vat tatas sarvasya jagataḥ paraspara ātma tā prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt sarva bhāvāḥ para rūpeṇa niḥsvabhāvaḥ svarūpeṇa rūpavat tve api iti anavadyam kaḥ tarhi prasajya pratiṣedhāt paryudāsasya bhedaḥ  na kaścid kevalam anapekṣita rūpa antaram abhāva mātram prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ iti loke kathyate rūpa antaram tu para rūpa śūnyam paryudāsaḥ iti na tu rūpa antaram para rūpa tuccha ātmakam na bhavati 
HBṬ_4.2.32–4.2.33^2	 anubhūyate eva ca rūpa antaram tad rūpa śūnya tayā katham tasya prasajya pratiṣedha ātma tā na syāt para rūpeṇa  sāmarthyāt tatas tad pratītiḥ iti ced na akāraṇa pratītau sāmarthya asambhavāt tādātmya abhāve hi prasajya pratiṣedhasya paryudastāt pratītau tad kāraṇa tve sati syāt pratipattiḥ na anyathā tasya tad anyā saṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya yat tattvam tasya pratiṣedhya tuccha rūpa tāyāḥ vyavasthāpakam pramāṇam pratyakṣa rūpam tat eva na tad uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ na asti iha ghaṭaḥ iti vikalpāt tasya gṛhīta grāhitayā smṛti tvena apramāṇa tvāt anyasya ghaṭa ādeḥ tatra asataḥ vyavacchedasya abhāvasya siddheḥ tad abhāva ātmakasya eva 
HBṬ_4.2.34	 pradeśasya tena grahaṇāt dvividhaḥ hi ayam pradeśaḥ ghaṭa asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpaḥ tad vyāvṛtta rūpa tayā tatas anyaḥ ghaṭavān api kevalaḥ ca ghaṭam prati apratipanna ādhāra bhāvaḥ tasya tat vivekena pratyakṣeṇa grahaṇe ghaṭāt anya tvam ghaṭa virahaḥ ca gṛhītaḥ eva bhavati iti na vastu asaṃkara siddhi artham iha idam na asti iti evam artham ca pramāṇa antaram anveṣaṇīyam vistaraḥ ca etat uttaratra vakṣyate iti āstām tāvat yatas ca anya bhāva siddhyā eva tad abhāvaḥ uktena nyāyena siddhyati tatas na anya bhāvaḥ pratiṣedhya abhāvasya liṅgam 
HBṬ_4.2.35^1	 dvitīyam kāraṇam vyācakṣāṇaḥ āha sambandha abhāvāt ca iti anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ na kaścid sambandhaḥ asti tatas kutas liṅga liṅgi bhāvaḥ iti etat ca kadā ucyate  yadā tad abhāva rūpa tā anya bhāvasya para anabhyupagatā apekṣyate tad anya bhāvāt pṛthak eva tad abhāvaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ iṣyate paraiḥ anyathā uktena nyāyena anya bhāvasya eva tad abhāva rūpa tve tādātmyāt katham sambandha abhāvaḥ  pratyakṣa siddha tā ca tadā eva na pakṣa antareṇa abhihitā tat ca tasya iti ādyasya eva vivaraṇam vyatireka mukhena eka artha samavāyaḥ iti para darśanena uktam 
HBṬ_4.2.35^2	 pareṣām hi naiyāyika ādīnāṃ vyatiriktau eva kṛtaka anitya tva ākhyau dharmau ekasmin eva dharmiṇi samavetau iti kṛtakasya anitya tvena ekasmin arthe dharmiṇi samavāyaḥ sambandhaḥ dhūmasya vā iti sambandhaḥ eva udāharaṇa antaram atra ekartha samavāyaḥ iti saṃyogaḥ saḥ eva samavāya śabdena uktaḥ saṃyoga samavāyayoḥ kalpita tvāt bhedena vyapadeśe anādarāt pareṣām tu agni dhūmau sva avayaveṣu eva samavetau iti na tayoḥ eka artha samavāya ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ vā iti dhūmasya agneḥ upari darśanāt laukikaḥ sambandhaḥ uktaḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ vā iti pāramārthikaḥ sambandhaḥ abhihitaḥ paramārthataḥ agneḥ janaka tvāt itarasya ca janya tvāt iti 
HBṬ_4.2.36	 nanu ca īśvarasenena saha vicāraḥ prakrāntaḥ tat kim iti naiyāyikā abhimatasya api sambandhasya anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ abhāvaḥ ucyate satyam prasaṅgena tu tad matasya api niṣedha artham uktam pūrvam hi anya bhāva grāhi pratyakṣa siddha tvāt pratiṣedhya abhāvasya na tad artham pratyakṣa antaram na asti iha ghaṭaḥ iti evam ākāram kalpanīyam iti prasaṅgataḥ kathitam adhunā tu prasaṅgāt idam ucyate yadā anya bhāva grāhi pratyakṣa siddhaḥ ayam tad abhāvaḥ na bhavati tadā pratyakṣa antaram na asti iha ghaṭaḥ iti evam ākaram viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva lakṣaṇāt sannikarṣāt iṣṭam bhavatā na ca asati sambandhe anya bhāva tadabhāvayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ atiprasaṅgāt tatas kutas tad lakṣaṇāt sannikarṣāt tad abhāve pratyakṣam bhavet iti 
HBṬ_4.2.37	 evam sambandha svarūpam ākhyāya tasya iha asambhavam āha na evam yathā kṛtaka tva anitya tvayoḥ agni dhūmayoḥ vā eka artha samavāya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ na evam kaścid bhāva abhāvayoḥ sambandhaḥ yena asya tad abhāvasya anya bhāvaḥ sādhanam syāt yau ekatra arthe dharmi rūpe pravarttete tayoḥ eka artha samavāyaḥ bhavati anya bhāvaḥ ca pradeśa ākhyaḥ sva avayaveṣu yeṣu varttate na tatra ghaṭa abhāvaḥ evam hi pradeśa avayaveṣu ghaṭaḥ na asti iti syāt na pradeśe na ca asya pradeśavayavaiḥ ārambhaḥ te hi dravya ātmānaḥ dravya antaram eva ārambhante na ca ghaṭa abhāvaḥ dravyam nava eva hi dravyāṇi iṣyante na ca kriyāvat ādikam dravya lakṣaṇam tatra asti na ca guṇa rūpa tayā tatra varttate catur viśatiḥ eva hi guṇāḥ iṣyante na ca ayam teṣām anyatamaḥ na api karma rūpa taya pañcasu karmasu anantarbhāvāt tad lakṣaṇa virahāt ca eka dravyam iti ādikam 
HBṬ_4.2.38	 hi tad lakṣaṇam na ca etat abhāve sambhavati iti na api sāmānya ādi rūpa tayā tad rūpa virahāt eva na api anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ saṃyogaḥ agni dhūmayoḥ iva dravyayoḥ eva tad abhyupagamāt na ca tad abhāvaḥ dravyam iti uktam na api ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ yatas saḥ api saṃyoga nimittaḥ ucyate iha kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti samavāya nimittaḥ vā iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iti na ca abhāvasya adravya ātmanaḥ saṃyogaḥ samasti na api samavāyaḥ pañcānām eva hi dravya ādīnām padārthānām samavāyi tvam iṣyate na ca abhāvaḥ pañcasu antarbhavati iti na ca tad ā ātmā anupakāre sati ādhāra vyapadeśaḥ sambhavati upakāre vā janya janaka bhāvaḥ na ca tad abhāvaḥ janyaḥ kārya tā prasaṅgāt kārya tā ca asya asambhavinī yatas sva kāraṇa samavāyaḥ sattā samavāyaḥ vā kāryatā ucyate bhavadbhiḥ anya bhāvaḥ tu pradeśa ākhyaḥ asya na kāraṇam trayāṇām eva hi dravya guṇa karmaṇām dravyam kāraṇam iṣṭam na ca abhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.39	 dravya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ iti sattā samavāye api sat pratyaya viṣaya tā tad abhāvasya syāt na abhāva pratyaya viṣaya tā pradeśa abhāve api ca ghaṭa abhāva sambhavāt kutas tad kāryatā na ca asya prativiṣayam bhedaḥ eka ākāra jñāna viṣaya tvāt sambandhi bhedāt bhede vā sāmānya ādiṣu api tad prasaṅgaḥ samavāya upi asya anantaram eva nirastaḥ iti kutas sva kāraṇa sattā samavāya rūpā kārya tā tad abhāvasya syāt  etena janya janaka bhāvaḥ pratyuktaḥ tatas sarvathā sambandha abhāvāt na anya bhāvaḥ tad abhāvasya sādhanam iti 
HBṬ_4.2.40	 paraḥ sambandha antaram darśayan āha asti viṣaya iti ādi yathā hi arthaḥ viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ viṣayi iti tayoḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ evam anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ bhaviṣyati pradeśa ākhyena anya bhāvena ghaṭa abhāvasya pratyāyanāt iti pūrva pakṣa āśaṅkā śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ syāt iti abhisambandhaḥ kim rūpaḥ  kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇaḥ katham punar artha kārya tā śabdasya  tad pratipādana abhiprāye sati artha pratipādana vivakṣāyām satyām tad prayogāt śabda uccāraṇāt tena arthena vivakṣā viparivarttinā śabdasya kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ syāt yadi api ca śabda arthayoḥ buddhi parikalpita sāmānya rūpa tā tathā api artha pratibhāsinyā vivakṣayā śabda sāmānya utprekṣā nibandhanasya śabda sva lakṣaṇasya utthāpanāt tad mukhena kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ucyate avinābhāva lakṣaṇaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.41	 vā iti para prasiddhyā ucyate paraḥ hi avinābhāva lakṣaṇaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ iti vyavaharati tatas sambandha nibandhanaḥ pratipādya pratipādaka rūpaḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ tad abhāvāni abhāvayoḥ api evam bhaviṣyati iti ced āha ayaṃca anantara ukta prakāraḥ atra tad abhāvāni abhāvayoḥ na sambhavati na hi ghaṭa abhāva pratipādana abhiprāye sati anya bhāvasya pradeśa lakṣaṇasya prayogaḥ niṣpattiḥ bhavati ghaṭa abhāva pratipādana abhiprāyāt prāk api pradeśasya sva hetubhyaḥ eva niṣpatteḥ sati api tad abhiprāye anya bhāvasya abhāvāt ca tatas ca katham tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tad dvārakaḥ avinābhāvaḥ vā syāt yatas viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ kalpyeta 
HBṬ_4.2.42	 syāt matam yathā śabda arthayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva nimittaḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ tathā anya bhāva tadabhāvayoḥ api iti etāvat mātreṇa śabda arthayoḥ dṛṣṭānta tā iti atas āha siddhe hi ityādi śabda arthayoḥ hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva nibandhanaḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ anyathā artha antara tve tad ayogāt tathā iha api yadi tad abhāvāni abhāvayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ sidhyet tadā tad mukhena sādhya sādhana bhāva dvāreṇa viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ syāt yāvatā saḥ eva sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ asati sambandhe kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādike na sidhyati sarvasya sādhya sādhana aprasakteḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.43	 katham indriyam sva viṣaya siddhi nibandhanam iti ced paraspara upasarppaṇa ādi āśrayāt pratyaya viśeṣāt indriya viṣayayoḥ eka vijñāna utpādanayoḥ udayāt tathā vyapadeśaḥ na evam iha anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ tad ayogāt liṅga liṅgi bhāva lakṣaṇasya ca sādhya sādhana bhāvasya prakṛta tvāt tasya ca sambandham antareṇa ayogāt 
HBṬ_4.2.44	 na eva sambandha antara nibandhanaḥ anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ api tu viṣaya viṣayi bhāva nimittaḥ eva iti ced āha anyathā yadi sambandha antaram na iṣyate kin tu viṣaya viṣayi bhāvāt sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ tasmāt ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ tatas itaretara āśrayam idam syāt tathā ca eka asiddhau dvayoḥ api asiddhiḥ bhavet iti kiñca anya bhāvāt ca liṅga bhūtāt abhāvasya liṅginaḥ siddhau anumitau iṣyamāṇāyām asamudāyaḥ ca sādhyaḥ syāt anya bhāvena tad abhāvasya kevalasya eva sādhanāt na kevala sambandha abhāvāt sādhya sādhana bhāva ayogaḥ samudāyaḥ ca viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva āpannaḥ dharma dharmi lakṣaṇaḥ sādhyaḥ yaḥ iṣṭaḥ tad abhāva doṣaḥ ca iti ca śabdaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.45	 sarvatra samudāyasya sādhya tā na eva iṣṭā iti ced āha tathā ca dharma mātrasya api svatantrasya sādhyatā upagame ghaṭa abhāvaḥ tad anya bhāvāt iti evaṃrūpe prayoge ghaṭasya sarvatra deśe sarvadā ca abhāvaḥ prasajyeta dharmiṇi hi kvacid dharmasya guṇa bhūtasya sādhane tatra eva tad kāle eva ca bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ na anyat ā iti sarvatra samudāyaḥ eva sādhyaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ na kevalaḥ dharmaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.46–4.2.47	 atra āha paraḥ na asamudāyasya sādhya tā anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ asambandhaḥ vā kutas  pradeśa ādi ityādi iha pradeśe ghaṭaḥ na asti iti evam ghaṭa abhāvena pradeśa ādiḥ dharmī viśeṣyate sa ghaṭāt pradeśa ādeḥ bhedena avasthāpyata iti tad viśeṣaṇa tvam prāptaḥ sādhyate na tu ghaṭaḥ na asti iti evam kevalaḥ dharmiṇaḥ kasyacid guṇa bhāvam anāpannaḥ tatas na asamudāyasya sādhyatā iti kutas tad bhāvī doṣaḥ  na ca na eva asmin pakṣe liṅgasya anya bhāva ātmanaḥ liṅginaḥ ca pradeśa ādi dharmi lakṣaṇasya asambandha doṣaḥ prasajyate kutas  anya bhāvasya ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa ādi lakṣaṇasya pradeśa ādinā dharmiṇā sambandhāt tādātmya sadbhāvāt iti tathā hi śabda ādi dharmiṇā kṛtaka tva ādeḥ tādātmya lakṣaṇaḥ eva sambandhaḥ iṣyate bhavatā saḥ iha asti iti abhiprāyaḥ tatas ca sambandha abhāvāt ca iti ayuktam iti manyate 
HBṬ_4.2.48	 siddhānta vādī tu sādhya dharma lakṣaṇasya liṅginaḥ ghaṭa abhāva ākhyasya anya bhāvena liṅgena sambandha abhāvaḥ prāk uktaḥ na dharmiṇā tatas kvadam uttaram saṃbadhyate iti manyamānaḥ dharmiṇā api anya bhāva ākhyasya liṅgasya sambandha abhāvam darśayan āha na liṅga liṅginoḥ asambandhaḥ na ca iti sambadhyate tathā na asamudāya sādhanam iti kin tu liṅga liṅginoḥ asambandhaḥ eva asamudāya sādhanam eva ca evam api bruvataḥ kutas  pradeśa ādeḥ eva dharmi tayā avasthāpyamānasya anya bhāva tvāt anya bhāva lakṣaṇa liṅga tvāt etat eva darśayati yatra eva hi pradeśa ādau dharmi tayā tvayā kalpyamāne yat ghaṭa ādikam na asti iti ucyate lokena saḥ eva pradeśa ādiḥ tena ghaṭa ādinā asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ saṃsarga rahitaḥ anya bhāvaḥ liṅgatayā iṣṭaḥ na aparaḥ kaścid yatas tad darśanāt eva ghaṭa asaṃsṛṣṭa pradeśa ādi darśanāt eva asya pratipattuḥ ghaṭaḥ na asti iti vikalpaḥ liṅgi jñāna tayā upagataḥ
