HBṬ_4.2.49	 bhavati tatas saḥ eva anya bhāvaḥ yat eva hi dṛśyamānam liṅgi jñānam janayati tat eva liṅgam ucyate ghaṭa asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ ca pradeśa ādiḥ evam tasmāt tat eva anya bhāva lakṣaṇam liṅgam upeyam tatas katham tasya eva anya bhāvasya vyāvṛttitaḥ api bhedam ananubhavataḥ liṅga liṅgi bhāvaḥ liṅga tvam liṅgi tvam vā  na hi liṅgam eva dharmī bhavitum arhati dharmi pratipattau eva sādhya pratipatteḥ anvaya ādi anusaraṇa ayogāt tatas ca anyasya dharmiṇaḥ abhāvāt katham anya bhāva ātmanaḥ liṅgasya tad sambandhaḥ samudāya sādhyatā vā  śabda kṛtaka tvayoḥ tu paramārthataḥ tādātmye api vyāvṛtti bheda nibandhanaḥ asti eva bhedaḥ tatas śabda ādi dharmi pratipattau api anitya tva ādi apratītau kṛtaka tva ādinā tat sādhyate iti yuktam 
HBṬ_4.2.50	 syāt matam sāmānya viśeṣa kalpanayā liṅga liṅgitā ekasya api bhaviṣyati iti atas āha na ca atra prakṛte anya bhāve sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva kalpanā sambhavati yena sāmānya viśeṣa vikalpena sāmānyam hetuḥ bhavet viśeṣaḥ dharmī yatas samudāya sādhyatā liṅga liṅginoḥ sambandhaḥ vā syāt kutas na sambhavati iti āha tad viśeṣa pratipatteḥ eva ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa viśeṣa pratipatteḥ eva tad abhāvasya ghaṭa abhāvasya pratīteḥ yatas ca viśeṣaḥ eva ghaṭa abhāva pratīti nibandhanam tatas kim tatra sāmānya kalpanayā kriyate iti saḥ eva viśeṣaḥ anyatra varttamānaḥ sāmānya rūpa tām pratipatsyate iti ced āha tasya ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa viśeṣasya anyatra sajātīye anvayasya anuvṛtteḥ abhāvāt kutas sāmānya ātma tā  na hi asau deśa kāla avasthā niyataḥ viśeṣaḥ anyam anveti iti atra eva upacaya hetum āha pratijñārtha ityādi yadi hi ghaṭa vivikta 
HBṬ_4.2.51	 eva pradeśa viśeṣaḥ dharmī tasya eva ca hetutā iṣyate tadā pratijñāyāḥ yaḥ arthaḥ dharma dharmi samudāyaḥ tad eka deśaḥ eva dharmi lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ syāt pratijñā artha eka deśasya ca vyāvṛttitaḥ api bhedam ananubhavataḥ hetu tvam asiddham iti atha mā bhūt eṣa doṣaḥ iti na ghaṭa viviktaḥ eva pradeśa viśeṣaḥ hetuḥ iṣyate kin tu pradeśa mātram ghaṭa vivikta tā viśeṣa rahitam iti atas āha na ca yatra pradeśa mātraṃtatra ghaṭa abhāvaḥ sa ghaṭe api pradeśe pradeśa mātrasya bhāvāt anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ syāt 
HBṬ_4.2.52	 paraḥ anyathā sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvam darśayan āha tādṛśe yādṛśaḥ ghaṭa viviktaḥ kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ agratas sthitaḥ tādṛśe sarvatra pradeśe ghaṭasya abhāvaḥ iti kutas anekāntaḥ  tathāvidha pradeśa viśeṣa pratītiḥ eva ghaṭa abhāva pratītiḥ tatas anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ liṅga liṅgitāḥ anupapanna iti upadarśayan āha nanu tasya eva ityādi yaḥ asau kevalaḥ pradeśa viśeṣaḥ dharmi tayā avasthāpitaḥ tasya eva yat kaivalyam kevalaḥ iti anena viśeṣaṇena ucyate bhavatā tat eva ghaṭa virahaḥ ghaṭābhāvaḥ iti kathyate sa ca ghaṭa virahaḥ liṅga bhūtasya kevalasya pradeśasya pratipattau eva siddhaḥ na tu uttara kālam tatas anyaḥ eva ākāra antareṇa dhūmāt iva agniḥ sidhyati tatas kasya idānīm tad pratipattau eva sādhya pratītau satyām tat liṅgam  na kasyacid jijñāsitasya ghaṭa abhāvasya siddheḥ anyasya kasyacid ajijñāsita tvāt kevala pradeśa pratipattau eva ghaṭa viraha pratītau 
HBṬ_4.2.53	 ca yat etat uttara kālam yatra yatra kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ tatra tatra ghaṭa virahaḥ iti anvayasya anugamanam anusaraṇam tat ca nirarthakam ādau eva sādhya pratīteḥ yatas evam tasmāt anya bhāvaḥ kevala pradeśa lakṣaṇaḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ bheda abhāvāt na sādhanam abhāvasya iti sthitam tat evam samudāya sādhyatām liṅgasya ca dharmiṇā sambandham pratipādayitum yat uktam pareṇa pradeśa ādi dharmi viśeṣaṇasya abhāvasya sādhanāt iti tad apṛthak siddhi dūṣaṇena eva nirākṛtam 
HBṬ_4.2.54	 viṣaya viṣayi bhāvena tu sambandha pratipādane niraste paraḥ anyathā sambandham sādhya sādhanayoḥ darśayan āha asti anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ sambandhaḥ virodha ākhyaḥ tatas sambandha sadbhāvāt anya bhāvāt abhāvasya siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti siddhānta vādī tu sādhya sādhanayoḥ virodham eva asambhāvayan pṛcchati kena kasya virodhaḥ iti na hi atra sādhya sādhanayoḥ virodhaḥ saṃbhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ paraḥ virodham abhiprāya anabhijñātayā darśayati anya bhāvena kevala pradeśa ātmanā pratiyoginaḥ yasya abhāvaḥ pramātum iṣṭaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ tasya iti 
HBṬ_4.2.55–4.2.58	 parasya evaṃvādinaḥ asambandha abhidhāyitām ādarśayan āha kiṃnu vai pratiyogī ghaṭa ādiḥ pramātum iṣṭaḥ yena pratiyogināḥ prameya tvena liṅga liṅginoḥ virodhaḥ sambandhaḥ abhidhīyate  na eva pratiyogī pramātum iṣṭaḥ kin tu tad abhāvaḥ iti ced āha abhāvaḥ tu pratiyoginaḥ yaḥ sādhyaḥ kumārilaḥ tu manyate bhāva aṃśāt bhinnaḥ ayam abhāva aṃśaḥ tatas na anya bhāva eva tad abhāvaḥ iti katham tad pratipattiḥ eva tad abhāva pratipattiḥ iti tathā hi ayam abhāvaḥ prāc abhāva ādi bheda bhinnaḥ na ca avastunaḥ bhedaḥ sambhavati atas ayam vastu rūpaḥ eva yat āha na ca avastunaḥ ete syuḥ bhedāḥ tena asya vastu tāḥ iti na ca bhāva aṃśaḥ eva abhāva aṃśaḥ yuktaḥ tasya indriya saṃyoga balena pratīteḥ itara pratīteḥ ca tad asaṃyoga hetuka tvāt yat āha tad saṃyoge sat iti evaṃsat rūpa tvaṃpratīyate 
HBṬ_4.2.59	 na asti atra idam iti itthaṃtu tad asaṃyoga hetukam iti tat katham tad pratipattiḥ eva aparasya vyavacchedanam iti tad nirāsa artham āha tasya anyasya pradeśasya kevalasya yat tat kaivalyam ekāki tvam asahāya tā tat eva aparasya pratiyoginaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ vaikalyam abhāvaḥ iti tasmāt tad anya bhāvaḥ eva bhāva aṃśaḥ eva tvat abhimataḥ tad abhāvaḥ pratiyogi abhāva aṃśaḥ na tatas pṛthak bhūtam dharma antaram iti ucyatesu gata sutaiḥ tatas ca tad pratipattiḥ eva ca tasya anya bhāvasya pratipattiḥ eva ca tad apratipattiḥ tasya pratiyoginaḥ apratipattiḥ abhāva pratipattiḥ iti yāvat evam manyate yaḥ ayam abhāva aṃśaḥ bhāva aṃśāt pṛthak bhūtaḥ vastunaḥ dharmaḥ parikalpyate sa ghaṭa ādi abhāva ātmaka tām tad rūpa vaikalyāt eva anubhavati na anyathā tat ca tad rūpa vaikalyam anya vastunaḥ bhāva aṃśasya api 
HBṬ_4.2.60	 vidyate eva tad abhāve hi tasya anya vastu tā eva hīyeta na hi yat yat rūpa vikalam na bhavati tat tatas anya tvam anubhavati yathā tasya eva svarūpam tathā ca abhāva aṃśaḥ api tasya na sidhyet sarvam ca viśvam ekam dravyam prasajyeta tatas ca saha utpatti ādi prasaṅgaḥ sarvasya ca sarvatra upayogaḥ syāt iti avaśyam anya vastunaḥ bhāva rūpa tā tad anya abhāva ātmikā eva tathā ca tad pratipattiḥ eva tad anya abhāva pratipattiḥ tad saṃyogaḥ eva ca indriyasya tad anya bhāva abhāva saṃyogaḥ iti kim ucyate 
HBṬ_4.2.61–4.2.62	 na asti atra idam iti itthaṃtu tad asaṃyoga hetukam iti  vikalpa apekṣayā uktam iti ced tat etat abādhakam eva pratyakṣeṇa tad ākāra utpattyā tad anya abhāva ātmake eva vastu rūpe pratipanne pāścāt yasya yathā gṛhīta abhilāpinaḥ vikalpasya upagamāt vistarataḥ ca ayam abhāva vicāraḥ pramāṇa dvi tva siddhau abhāvam prameyam pramāṇam ca vicārayatā vihitaḥ iti tatas eva avadhāryaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.63	 avaśyam ca tad anya bhāva pratipattiḥ eva tad abhāva pratipattiḥ tatas na vastu asaṅkara sidhi artham na asti atra idam iti abhāva vyavahāra artham ca abhāva pramāṇa parikalpanā yuktā iti darśayan āha anyathā yadi tad pratipattiḥ eva tad abhāva pratipattiḥ iti na iṣyate tadā tasya anya vastunaḥ svarūpa paricchedena tatas anyasya atad rūpasya avyavacchede anirākaraṇe tad abhāva apratipattau tad paricchedaḥ eva na syāt tasya tad anya vastunaḥ svarūpa pratipattiḥ eva na syāt kim kāraṇam tat atad rūpayoḥ tasya tad anya vastunaḥ yat rūpam pratiniyatam sakala trailokya vilakṣaṇam yat ca atad rūpam tad rūpam na bhavati para rūpam tayoḥ avivekāt avivecanāt vivekena avyavasthāpanāt asāṅkaryeṇa aprasādhanāt sakala para rūpa asaṅkīrṇam hi tad rūpam tat ced tad sāmarthya bhāvinā pratyakṣeṇa tathā na anukṛtam kevalam sammugdha ākāram eva tat utpannam tadā kathan tena tad paricchedaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.64	 syāt  na hi yat rūpam yat vastu tad rūpān anukāriṇā jñānena tad paricchedaḥ yuktaḥ yathā śukla śaṅkha rūpa an anukāriṇā kāmalinaḥ pīta śaṅkha avabhāsinā jñānena iti pratiniyata rūpa anukāre vā tad paricchedasya katham anyā avyavacchedaḥ nāma  tatas pratiniyata rūpān anukārāt eva tad anya avyavacchedaḥ tathā ca tad pariccheda abhāvaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.65	 bhavatu evam tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ iti atas āha yaḥ eṣa vyavahāraḥ sarva jana pratītaḥ kasyacid agni ādeḥ vastunaḥ darśanāt kvacid deśe tad sambandhini prāpti arthaḥ dṛṣṭasya adṛṣṭasya ca parihāra arthaḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ sa na syāt kim kāraṇam  na hi yasmāt ayam pratipattāḥ analaṃpaśyan api saṅkīrṇa tada tad rūpa pratibhāsinā pratyakṣeṇa anyathā asya darśana rūpa tā hāneḥ tathā hi asaṅkīrṇasya adarśane saṅkīrṇam api yadi na paśyet tadā loṣṭa ādi prakhyam katham kasyacid etad darśanam syāt  saḥ evaṃbhūtaḥ saṅkīrṇa darśanavān pratipattā katham analam eva paśyati na salila ādikam  kin tu saṅkīrṇa rūpa vastu pratibhāsi jñāna tayā salila ādikam api paśyati tatas katham salila arthī tatra agnimati pradeśe na pravarteta  
HBṬ_4.2.66–4.2.68	 parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkya āha anupalambhena ityādi anala pratibhāsinā hi jñānena anala svarūpan eva pratīyate yaḥ tu salila abhāvaḥ sa tatra salilasya anupalambhena tatas jñāna dvayena tad atad rūpayoḥ vivekāt loke pravṛtti nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ pratiniyataḥ vyavahāraḥ sidhyati iti siddhānta vādi āha kaḥ ayam anupalambhaḥ nāma iti kadācid paraḥ brūyāt salila upalambha viraha mātram iti atas āha yadi salilaḥ iti ādi kumārilasya tu salila upalambha nivṛtti mātram tuccha rūpam abhāva pramāṇa tayā nābhimatam eva pratyakṣa ādeḥ anutpattiḥ pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ucyate sa ātmanaḥ apariṇāmaḥ vā avijñānaṃvā anya vastuni 
HBṬ_4.2.69	 iti vacanāt kin tu yaḥ abhāva ātmanaḥ pratiṣedhya vastu pratibhāsi jñāna ātmanā apariṇāmaḥ sa tad anya vastu pratibhāsi jñāna sahacaritaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ na kevalaḥ iti param abhyupagamayitum asya upanyāsaḥ tathā ca anya vastu vijñānam eva abhāva pramāṇam astu kim apramāṇakasya ātmanaḥ apariṇāma ākhyena dharmeṇa parikalpitena  na ca tad anya vastu vijñāna pariṇāmāt anyaḥ eva tasya apariṇāmaḥ nāma bhavataḥ abhimataḥ bhāva antarasya eva abhāva tvena upagata tvāt tulya yogya tārūpasya eka jñāna saṃsarggiṇaḥ eva ca anya vastunaḥ vijñānam tathā upeyam na anyasya tad jñānāt pratiyogi abhāva siddheḥ na hi rūpa jñānāt rasa ādi abhāva pratītiḥ yuktam atī deśa ādi viprakarṣavataḥ vā anya vastu vijñānam ca pratiniyata rūpa pratibhāsi eva rūpa antara avabhāsi tve hi tasya salila upalambha abhāvaḥ eva na sidhyet evam ca pratiyogi abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa avabhāsitaḥ eva tad abhāva vyavahāre tu asmad abhimatā eva anupalabdhiḥ āyāta iti pratipādayitum asya upanyāsaḥ tatra yadi salila upalambha abhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.70	 tuccha rūpaḥ anupalambhaḥ tadā katham abhāvaḥ kasyacid pratipattiḥ paricchedaḥ iti yāvat paricchedasya jñāna dharma tvāt atha na tasya pratipatti rūpatā iṣyate kin tu tad hetu bhāvaḥ iti āha pratipatti hetuḥ vā iti na hi sarva sāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇasya abhāvasya pratipattim prati hetu bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ hetu bhāve vā tasya anapekṣita sahakāriṇaḥ nityam tad jñāna jananāt abhāva jñānam eva ekam pratipattuḥ syāt jñāna antarasya avakāśaḥ eva na bhavet 
HBṬ_4.2.71	 na ca ajñātasya asya na astita ajñāna jananam yuktam iti āha tasya api salila upalambha abhāvasya katham pratipattiḥ  atha ayam salila upalambha abhāvaḥ svayam apratītaḥ eva salila abhāva pratītim janayati tadā kasyacid api tat eva āha tasya salila upalambha abhāvasya tatas vā salilāt anyasya anala ādeḥ vijñānam vā anya vastuni iti atas ātmanaḥ apariṇāmasya pṛthak avasthāpanāt tatra api tad aṅgīkaraṇe ca ātmanaḥ apariṇāmasya tad ātmaka tvāt na tatas bhedena vyavasthāpya ita tatas ca kasyacid api tasya tad anyasya vā apratipattau api yadi abhāvaḥ salila ādeḥ pratīyate tadā svāpa ādi avasthāsu api salila ādi a bhāvaḥ kim na pratīyate  tadā api tad abhāvaḥ pratīyeta iti etat vicāri tampramāṇa viniścaye tatas eva avadhāraṇīyam vyavadhāna ādi grahaṇena ca etat darśayati anya vastunaḥ api anya tvam tad tulya yogya tā ru upāpekṣam eva na tad anapekṣam upeyam tathā ca asmat upavarṇita anupalabdhi siddhiḥ iti yadā ca evam uktena 
HBṬ_4.2.72	 prakāreṇa anupalambhena salila abhāva pratītiḥ na yujyate anala pratibhāsinaḥ ca jñānasya pratiniyata ākāra tā na abhyupagamyate tasmāt ayam anala darśī pratipattā analam paśyan api saṅkīrṇa rūpa pratibhāsinā jñānena analaḥ ayam na salilam iti na adhyavasyati anadhyavasyan ca salila rūpasya api pratibhāsanāt tad arthī na tiṣṭhet pravarteta na api pratiṣṭheta salila arthī na pravarteta tathā hi salilam nāma tat ucyate yat sarva udanyā santāpa ādi apanayana kṣamam sakala tad anya rūpā saṅkīrṇa pratiniyata ākāra jñāna avabhāsi idam tu anyat eva śabala rūpam kim api avabhāsate iti tatas ca pravṛtti nivṛttiyoḥ viruddhayoḥ yugapad anuṣṭhātum aśakya tvāt dustaraṃvyasanaṃpratipattuḥ syāt 
HBṬ_4.2.73	 atra parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkya āha tatas eva ityādi na mayā salila upalambha nivṛtti mātrāt tuccha rūpāt tad abhāva gatiḥ ucyate yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgāt kin tu yat etat ekasya kevalasya analasya darśanam tatas eva anyasya tatra apratibhāsamānasya salilasya abhāva gatiḥ bhavati vijñānam vā anya vastuni iti vacanāt 
HBṬ_4.2.74	 siddhānta vādi āha katham ekam ityādi kena punar sāmarthyena tad eka darśanam anya abhāvaṃpratyāyayati  tathā hi tasmin dṛśyamāne tat eva asti iti avagacchatu tat anyat tu na asti iti kim iti pratyeti iti tasya eva paridṛśyamānasya anala ādeḥ kevalasya salila asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya darśanāt anala jñāne pratibhāsanāt salilam na asti iti niścayaḥ san jāyate tathā hi analaḥ iva salilam api yadi tatra abhāviṣyat tat api anala vat darśane pratyabhāsiṣyata tayoḥ sva jñānam pratyaviśiṣṭa tvāt yogyatāyāḥ na ekasya pratibhāsaḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt eka pratibhāsanam anya abhāvanā antarīyakam iti anya abhāve tatas jñānam utpadyate anya vastuni ca vijñānam na asti iti jñānam janayati tathā anyat vastu para rūpa asaṃkīrṇa svabhāva tayā eva tathā ucyate tad rūpa tayā eva ca tat jñānam anyat pratiyat evam vyapadiśyate anyathā tad ayogāt iti anya pratipattiḥ eva tad abhāva vikalpa hetuḥ iti siddhānta vādi āha 
HBṬ_4.2.75	 idam eva ityādi nanu asmābhiḥ idam eva prāk abhihitam tayoḥ satoḥ na eka rūpa niyata apratipattiḥ asambhavāt iti ādibhiḥ vacanaiḥ tatas yat eva anya asaṃsa rggiṇaḥ kevalasya pratibhāsanam tat eva tad anya abhāvasya api tasya eva kevalasya tad anya abhāva ātmaka tvāt anyasya ca abhāva aṃśasya nirasta tvāt tatas pratyakṣa avabhāsita tvāt tad abhāvasya tad balāt pāścātyam vyavahāra pravartana rūpam na astita ajñānam vikalpakam ājāyate na tu tena apratipannam kiñcid avagamyate yatas tad anya vastuni vijñānam pratyakṣa ātmakam api anavagate tad anya abhāve jñānam janayat pṛthak abhāva pramāṇa tayā vyavasthāpyeta tathā hi tad anya ākāra śūnyaḥ eva tad eka jñāna ākāraḥ saṃvedyate tatas tad saṃvedanam eva tad abhāva saṃvedanam na hi vikalpa jñānasya api tad ākāra śūnya rūpa saṃvedanāt anyat tat abhāva saṃvedanam nāma kevalam asya vikalpa rūpa tā eva atiricyate tatas yathā nirvikalpa jñāna avasite kvacid 
HBṬ_4.2.76	 anale analaḥ atra asti iti pāścātyaḥ vikalpaḥ vyavahāra pravartana mātram na tatas pṛthak pramāṇam yathoktam prāk tathā na astita ajñānam api vikalpakam tad phala dvāreṇa vā anya vastu vijñānam na pratyakṣāt pṛthak abhāva ākhyam pramāṇam iti tasmāt yat eva asmābhiḥ abhihitam tad anyā bhāva pratītim prati tat eva tvayā api abhidhīyate iti kasmāt puruṣam iva ābhāti yatas tad anabhyupagamena pṛthak abhāva ākhyam pramāṇam abhyupagatam iti upahasati tathā hi agati edānīm tvayā ucyate na madhyastha tayā anyathā idam eva kim na pūrvam eva abhihitam  yatas āla jāla abhidhānena aatmā parikleśitaḥ iti upasaṃharan āha tasmāt tīrādarśinā iva ityādi yathā kila vahana ārūḍhaiḥ vaṇigbhiḥ śakuniḥ mucyate api nāma tīram drakṣyati iti sa yadā sarvatas paryaṭan= tīram na āsādayati tadā vahanam eva āgacchati tadvat etat api draṣṭavyam yatas ca avaśya abhyupagamanīyaḥ ayam pakṣaḥ tasmāt na kiñcid anayā avidyamāna pratiṣṭhā anayā 
HBṬ_4.2.77–4.2.79	 diśaḥ pratipattyā prayojanam tat evam parasya anya bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ liṅga liṅgi bhāvam icchataḥ sambandha abhāvāt asau ayuktaḥ iti pratipādite pareṇa asati sambandhe anya bhāva gatyā api tad abhāva gatiḥ na syāt iti codite na vai kutaścid sambandhāt iti ādi abhihitam tatas anya bhāvaḥ eva tad abhāvaḥ anya bhāva gatiḥ eva ca tad abhāva gatiḥ iti prasādha yata akumārila parikalpitaḥ kasyacid abhāva niścaya artham abhāva pramāṇa vādaḥ prasaṅgataḥ nirastaḥ samprati tu vastu asaṅkara siddhiḥ ca tad prāmāṇya samāśritā 
HBṬ_4.2.80	 iti etat āhatya nirākartum pūrva pakṣam utthāpayan āha yadi eka paricchedāt eva ityādi yadi hi ekasya kevalasya paricchedāt anyasya vyavacchedaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ sidhyati tadā sarvasya anyasyāḥ aviśeṣeṇa eva tatra deśe yatra asau ekaḥ paridṛśyate tatra abhāva siddhiḥ bhavet na tu viśeṣa parigraheṇa tulyā sva jñāna jananam prati yogyā avasthā yasya tasya eva iti tathā hi asau yathā tulya yogya tā rūpa padārtha vivikta rūpaḥ upalabhyate tad eka ākāra pratiniyamāt tat jñānasya tathā tad atulya yogya tā rūpapadārtha vivikta ātmakaḥ api tatas ca tad vivikta ākāra tayā tad anya abhāva sādhane viśeṣa abhāvāt pradeśa rūpa jñānam ghaṭa abhāvam iva rasa ādi abhāvam api sādhayet na vā ghaṭa abhāvam api iti 
HBṬ_4.2.81	 kiñ ca yat etat upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ abhāva sādhanī iti viśeṣaṇam uktam tat ca na vaktavyam kim kāraṇam yatas ye api anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ teṣām api tatra deśe tad eka ākāra tayā jñānasya vyavacchedaḥ bhavati eva tathā hi yathā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ tat eka ākāravati jñāne na pratibhāsante tatas ca vyavacchidyante tathā anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ api iti kim upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya iti anena viśeṣaṇena iti evam pūrva pakṣe vyavasthite yadi tad anya vyavacchedaḥ tatas pṛthak karaṇam anya tvena vyavasthāpanam abhimatam tat abhyupagamyate eva atha tad deśa kālayoḥ abhāvaḥ tat ayuktam yena hi sāmarthyena tulya yogya tārūpasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya ca abhāvam sādhayati na tad sāmarthyam atulya yogya tā rūpe anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpte vā sambhavati tayoḥ satoḥ na eka rūpa niyatā pratipattiḥ asambhavāt iti evam hi tad abhāva sādhanam na ca etat 
HBṬ_4.2.82–4.2.84	 anyatra sambhavati iti pratipādayitum eka ātma paricchedāt iti ādina upakramate yat puras avasthitam pratyakṣe avabhāsate tasya ekasya ātmanaḥ pratiniyatasya rūpasya paricchedāt tad ākāra utpattyā vidhi vikalpa utpādanena ca yaḥ tad anyaḥ tatas anyaḥ tad vyatiriktaḥ tasya sarvasya yaḥ ātmā svabhāvaḥ tatas vyavacchedaḥ bhedanam pṛthak karaṇam anya tva sādhanam asaṅkīrṇa rūpa tā pratyāyanam bhavati katham punar eka ātma paricchedāt eva tasya tad anya ātmanaḥ vyavacchedaḥ pratyakṣeṇa kriyate  yāvatā pratyakṣam puras avsthita padārtha sāmarthya bhāvi tad rūpam eva pratipadyatām yat tu tad vyatiriktam aśeṣa padārtha jātam tadātmanaḥ tasya puras avasthitasya katham tat vyavacchedakam atas tad vyavaccheda artham abhāva pramāṇam abhyupeyam yatas vastu asaṅkara siddhiḥ ca tad prāmāṇya samāśritāḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.85–4.2.86	 atas āha tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānāt iti yatas puras avasthitasya ekasya vastunaḥ para rūpa asaṅkīrṇaḥ ātmā sarva bhāvānām svabhāvataḥ eva sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ para rūpeṇa asaṅkīrṇa svabhāva tvāt anyathā katham abhāva pramāṇataḥ api asāṃkaryam eṣām sidhyet  saṃkīrṇa rūpāṇām asāṅkarya sādhane tasya bhrānta tā prasaṅgāt tasmin para rūpa asaṃkīrṇe svabhāvataḥ eva tad ātma niyataḥ yaḥ pratibhāsaḥ para rūpa pratibhāsā saṃkīrṇaḥ tad eka padārtha sāmarthya bhāvini pratyakṣe para rūpa pratibhāsā yogāt tasya bhrānta tā āpattyā pratyakṣatā ha aneḥ tat uktam tat dhi artha sāmarthyena utpadyamānaṃtad rūpam eva anukuryāt iti tasya tad ātma niyata pratibhāsasya jñānāt pratyakṣeṇa sva saṃvittyā saṃvedanāt tad saṃvedanam eva hi pratyakṣasya ātad rūpāt vyavacchedanam pṛthak karaṇam tat balena eva ca pāścātyaḥ anya ātmakam etat na bhavati iti asāṃkarya vyavasthā pratyayaḥ vikalpakaḥ saṃjāyate gṛhīta grāhī na tena apūrvam kiñcid pratīyate para rūpa asaṃkīrṇasya ātmanaḥ pratyakṣeṇa eva tad ākāra anukāriṇā paricchedāt iti 
HBṬ_4.2.87	 yadi nāma tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānam tathā api katham anya ātmanaḥ tasya pṛthak karaṇam iti atas āha na hi tad ātma ityādi yasmāt tasya vastunaḥ yaḥ ātmā para rūpa asaṃkīṛṇnaḥ sa tad anyasya śeṣasya vastunaḥ ātmā na bhavati sarvasya tatas anya svabhāva tvāt anyathā tad anyatva hāneḥ iti tasmāt tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānam eva tad anyebhyaḥ nivarttanam na hi jñānena arthaḥ haste gṛhītvā anyatas nivarttanīyaḥ kevalam anya rūpa asaṃkīrṇasya ekasātmanaḥ anukaraṇam eva asya anyatas nivarttanam ucyate iti atha anya ātmanaḥ sva viṣayam na nivarttayet tadā asya viṣayasya anya ātmanaḥ sakāśāt avyavacchede pṛthak avyavasthāpane para ātmanaḥ api tatra paricchedaḥ syāt anyathā tad aparicchedasya eva eka ātma pariccheda ātmanaḥ tat nivarttana rūpa tā syāt tatas ca avyavacchede anya ātmanaḥ tad pariccheda prasaṅgāt pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ abhāvaḥ iti pūrvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ na hi ayam analam paśyan= 
HBṬ_4.2.88–4.2.89	 api iti ādikaḥ na kevalam anya ātmanaḥ tat nivarttayati tadātmanaḥ api aśeṣam anyat iti darśayan āha taṃca agratas sthitam deśa akāla svabhāva avasthā niyatam tad anya deśa ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛtta ātmanaḥ sva hetubhyaḥ eva asya bhāvāt tad ātmanā deśa ādi niyatena ātmanā tathāvidha svabhāvasya eva anukārāt upalabhamānā buddhiḥ tathā tva pracyutim anya deśa kāla svabhāva avastha tām asya sva viṣayasya vyavacchinatti tatas pṛthakkaroti kasmāt punar anya deśa āditām tatas pṛthak avasthāpayati iti atas āha evaṃhi yasmāt anya deśa tā ādeḥ tatas pṛthak karaṇe sati tad deśa ādi niyataḥ padārthaḥ paricchinnaḥ bhavati tad rūpasya eva anukārāt yadi anyathā bhāvaḥ anya deśa āditā tad rūpān anukārāt vyavacchinnaḥ bhavati tathātvam ca tad deśa ādi niyata tvam ca tadā tasya eva dṛśyamānasya bhavati na anyasya anya deśa ādimataḥ yatas evam iti tasmāt anyathā bhūtāt anya deśa ādimataḥ tathābhūtam 
HBṬ_4.2.90	 tad deśa ādimaṃtam vyavacchindati eva nivarttayanti eva tat paricchinatti iti pūrvakasya upasaṃhāraḥ tathā tathābhūtāt anyathā bhūtaṃvyavacchindati eva iti dvitīyasya upasaṃhāraḥ kāryaḥ iti evam uktena nyāyena ekasya pramāṇasya pratyakṣasya anumānasya vā tasya api evam eva sva viṣaya paricchedāt vṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ sarva bhāvān dvairāśye tattve anya tve ca vyavasthāpayati tatas tad paricchedaka pramāṇa balena eva asāṅkarya siddhiḥ kim tad arthikayā api abhāva kalpanayā iti  
HBṬ_4.2.91	 nanu ca vikalpa vyāpāraḥ eṣaḥ idam anya ātmakam na bhavati anyathā etat ātmakam iti pratyakṣam ca nirvikalpakam iṣyate tat katham asāṃkarya siddhiḥ tatas iti atas āha tasya anvaya ityādi tat dhi pratyakṣam vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpau yadā sva viṣaye janayati tadā eva asya sāphalyam tadā eva ca pramāṇam iṣyate na anyadā atas eva ekasya artha svabhāvasya apratipanna aṃśa abhāvāt sarva ātmanā paricchede api bhrānti kāraṇa sadbhāvāt kṣāṇika tā ādau= anvaya vyatirekabuddhī janayitum asāmarthyāt tatra asya prāmāṇyam na iṣyate iti 
HBṬ_4.2.92	 syāt matam dvairāśya sādhane api asāṃkarya siddhi arthāḥ mā bhūt abhāva pramāṇa kalpanā kin tu prakāra antara abhāva siddhi arthāḥ bhaviṣyati na hi tad abhāva siddhau pratyakṣasya kaścid vyāpāraḥ pratipāditaḥ iti atas āha tad vyatiriktā ityādi tasmāt paridṛśyamānāt vyatiriktasya aśeṣasya vastunaḥ vyavacchedena tatas pṛthakkaraṇena anya tvena yā vyāptiḥ tad sādhanāt eva prakāra antarasya tattva anyatva bahis bhūtasya abhāvaḥ sidhyati tatas tad artham api na abhāva pramāṇa kalpanā yuktā iti 
HBṬ_4.2.93–4.2.94^1	 atha matam sarvasya aparidṛṣṭasya dṛśyamānāt anyatayā vyāptim na eva pratyakṣam sādhayati tat kutas tṛtīya rāśya bhāvaḥ pratyakṣatas eva syāt yatas abhāva prāmāṇya kalpanā vyarthā bhavet iti atas āha tasya tṛtīya rāśi tayā kalpyamānasya tatas dṛṣṭāt anyatayā vyapti abhāve tena pratyakṣeṇa tatas arthāt sva viṣayasya avyavacchedāt apṛthak karaṇāt tad arthasya ca rāśi antara tvena kalpyamānasya sva viṣayāt avyavacchedāt apṛthak karaṇāt punar api bhāvasya sva viṣayasya apariccheda prasaṅgāt sa hi tad viṣayaḥ sakala para rūpa asaṃkīrṇa ātmā yadi tena ātmanā na paricchinnaḥ katham tena tasya paricchedaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.93–4.2.94^2	 tena ātmanā paricchede vā katham sarvasya tad anyatayā vyāpti asādhanam anyathāikasya api tad anya tvam na syāt nimittasya samāna tvāt iti yatas evam tasmāt kvacid vastuni pramāṇam pratyakṣa ādikam pravṛttam tat vastu pratiniyatena ātmanā paricchinatti tatas anyat tad rūpa vikalam vyavacchinatti tad anyatvena vyavasthāpanāt tṛtīyasya ca tattva anyatva bahis bhūtasya prakārasya abhāvam sūcayati sarvasya anyatayā vyāpti sādhanāt tad viruddhasya vā sarva vastunaḥ dvaividhyasya sādhanāt iti 
HBṬ_4.2.95	 evam ekasya pramāṇasya vyāpāraḥ eṣaḥ anantara uktaḥ iti tam eva upasaṃhṛtya sukha pratipattaye darśayan= āha tathā hi kvacid vastuni pramāṇam pratyakṣa ādi pravṛttam tat eva vastu tad anyasmāt para rūpāt vyavacchinatti tatas pṛthakkaroti tad asaṃkīrṇa rūpa tayā pratipadyate paramārthataḥ tasya tad rūpa tvāt yathāvastu ca pratyakṣeṇa rūpa anukārāt kim iti para rūpāt vyavacchinatti  tasya eva para rūpa vikalasya eka rūpasya paricchedāt tathā tat anyat eva ca tasmāt dṛśyamānāt anyat eva ca vyavacchinatti kutas  tasmāt sva viṣayāt na kevalam sva viṣayam paratas vyavacchinatti param api sva viṣayāt iti kutas etat  anyasya para rūpasya tatra sva ālambane aparicchedāt avaśyam eva aparicchinnasya paricchinnāt anya tvam bhavati yatas evam atas tat eva pramāṇam eka vastu paricchedakam prakāra antara abhāvam sādhayati na abhāva ākhyam kutas etat  tasmim dṛśyamāne 
HBṬ_4.2.96	 vastuni dṛṣṭa tad anya tvena tasya anyasya tatra aparicchidyamānasya anya tvam tad anya tvam dṛṣṭāt tad anya tvam dṛṣṭa tad anya tvam tena sarvasya tad vyatiriktasya vyavasthāpanena atat anyasya eva ca yat anyat na bhavati puras avasthitam sakala para bhāva vyāvṛttam tasya eva tattvena dṛśyamāna prakāra tayā vyavasthāpanāt iti 
HBṬ_4.2.97	 amum eva nyāyam anyatra api atidiśan āha etena kramākrama ādayaḥ ityādi etena anantara uktena nyāyena pratiniyata eka padārtha rūpa anukāriṇī buddhiḥ upajāyamānā tad viparīta rūpam sarvam sva viṣayāt vyavacchindatī dvairāśyam tṛtīya prakāra abhāvam ca sādhayati iti ye kecid anyonya vyavaccheda rūpāḥ kramākrama nityān ityādayaḥ te vyākhyātāḥ tathā hi kāryasya kramam ananya sahāya tām pratiyati eva buddhiḥ tasya ākramam kārya antara sāhityam tatas pṛthakkaroti tatas krama ākrama tayā dvaita siddheḥ tṛtīyasya prakārasya sambhavaḥ nirastaḥ bhavati krama bhāva vyatirekiṇaḥ sarvasya kārya janmanaḥ tad anyatayā dvitīya prakāra tayā avasthānāt evam udaya anantara dhvaṃsitā kṣaṇikatā ucyate iti pratīyatī vyavasthāpanā kālaḥ eva buddhi s tad viparīta rūpa tāyāḥ sva viṣayāt apākaraṇāt tatas anya tvena prakāra antare avasthāpanāt rāśi antara abhāvaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.2.98	 tat evam eka pramāṇa nibandhanām asāṅkarya siddhim pratipādya upasaṃharayan āha tat evam uktena nyāyena ekasya pratiniyata ātmanaḥ upalambhāt tasya upalabhyamānasya yaḥ tatas anyaḥ tad tulya yogya tā rūpaḥ tad viparītaḥ vā tad rūpa vikalaḥ tad ā ātmanaḥ vyavacchedaḥ pṛthak karaṇam tasya upalabhyamānasya anupalabhyamāna svabhāvāt rūpa antareṇa pratibhāsanāt tathā tasya sva viṣayasya tad anya ātma tāyāḥ bhāva pradhāna tvāt nirdeśasya vyavacchedaḥ bhavati asāṅkaryam sidhyati 
HBṬ_4.2.99	 tat yadi etat aviśeṣaṇāni asya sarvasya tatra abhāva siddhiḥ syāt iti atra abhimatam tadā siddha sādhanam yatas sarvam aviśeṣeṇa eva tat eka ākārayā budhyā tad rūpa vikalam sva viṣayāt avacchidyate sarvasya anya rūpasya tatra apratibhāsanāt atha tad deśa kālayoḥ abhāvaḥ sarvasya tad viparīta rūpasya vyavacchedaḥ abhimataḥ sa na yuktaḥ iti darśayati na tad deśa kālayoḥ yatra asau pratiniyata ātmā sakala trailokya vilakṣaṇaḥ padārthaḥ upalabhyate tatra sarvasya anyasya bhāvasya tad tulya yogya tā rūpasya itarasya vā vyavacchedaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yena hi kāraṇena tad tulya yogya tā rūpasya tatra apratibhāsamānasya pratiṣedha s tasmin sati tat eka rūpa niyatāyāḥ pratipatteḥ asaṃbhavāt tat abhāvanā antarīyikā sā bhavantī tat pratiṣedham gamayati iti tad kāraṇam anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpte tad atulya yogya tā rūpe ca na sambhavati iti katham tad abhāvaḥ sidhyet 
HBṬ_4.2.100	 etat eva upasaṃharan āha tasmāt atada ātmā ca sarvaḥ tad viparīta rūpaḥ tad eka ākārayā buddhyā prasādhitaḥ syāt tad deśa kālaḥ ca tasya pratibhāsamānasya yau deśa kālau tau yasya sa ca syāt kiṃvat  rasa rūpa ādi vat iti na hi rūpa pratibhāsinā jñānena tad rūpa vikalasya rasasya sva viṣayāt pṛthakkaraṇe api tat asāṃkarya sādhane api tad deśa kālayoḥ abhāvaḥ sidhyati tatas ca katham sarvasya atulya yogyā avasthasya api tatra abhāvaḥ syāt  upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya iti viśeṣaṇam vā na ucyeta yatas evam tasmāt kvacid kadācid kasyacid abhāva siddhiḥ yathā uktāt eva anupalambhāt upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya tad tulya yogya tā rūpa upalambha ātmanaḥ ca iti evaṃrūpāt na tu sāmānyena yathā aahuḥ pare 
HBṬ_4.2.101–4.2.105	 pramāṇa pañcakaṃyatra vastu rūpe na jāyate vastu sattā avabodha arthe tatra abhāva pramāṇa tā iti na hi anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpte pramāṇa pañcaka apravṛttau api tad abhāvaḥ sidhyati sati api tasmin svabhāva ādi viprakarṣeṇa pramāṇa pañcaka apravṛtti sambhavāt iti tat evam prāsaṅgikam parisamāpayya yat uktaṃpareṇa saḥ eva anya bhāvaḥ tad viṣayā ca upalabdhiḥ tad abhāvasya kim na sādhanam iti tatra anya bhāvasya tad abhāvam prati liṅga tve niraste tad viṣayāyāḥ upalabdheḥ nirākurvan āha anya bhāva viṣaya ityādi yat punar uktam anya bhāva viṣaya upalabdhiḥ tad abhāvasya kin na sādhanam iti sā tad abhāvasya sādhika iṣṭā eva asmākam na tu liṅga tvena yathā uktavān asi kim kāraṇam  yatas tatra api anya bhāva viṣayāyām upalabdhau abhāvasya pṛthak anya bhāvāt sādhya tve kalpyamāne sambandha abhāvasya tad abhāvena tulya tvāt na hi tasyāḥ api anya bhāva rūpāyāḥ tad abhāvena kaścid eka artha samavāya ādi rūpaḥ sambandhaḥ asti iti 
HBṬ_4.2.106	 apṛthak siddheḥ iti asya api tulya tām darśayan āha liṅga āvirbhāva ityādi yā iyam anya bhāva viṣayāḥ upalabdhiḥ lliṅgatayā ucyate tasyāḥ tad vivikta pradeśa ākārāyā āvirbhāva kāle eva janma kāle pratīti kālaḥ eva vā tad abhāva siddheḥ ca tathā hi tad pratibhāsa viviktānya bhāva pratibhāsa buddhi saṃvedanam eva tad abhāva saṃvedanam iti tat eva sādhayati na hi anyasya tad viviktasya bhāvam pratipadya pratipattā punar uttara kālam tat pratipatteḥ anya bhāva pratipatteḥ tad abhāvena anya vyatirekau prasādhya pratibindha sādhakena pramāṇena tad abhāvam pratipadyate kim tarhi  tad anyam tad vivikta rūpam pratipadyamānaḥ eva tasya pratiyoginaḥ abhāvam pratipadyate tasya eva tad abhāva ātmaka tvāt tathā hi sa ghaṭa pradeśa asaṃkīrṇa rūpasya kevala pradeśasya darśanam eva ghaṭa abhāva darśanam na hi ghaṭaḥ atra na asti ghaṭavān ayam na bhavati sa ghaṭāt anyaḥ iti artha bhedaḥ 
HBṬ_4.2.107	 kaścid tatas sa ghaṭāt anya tayā kevala pradeśasya darśanam eva ghaṭa abhāva darśanam iti ghaṭaḥ atra na asti iti jñānam gṛhīta grāhitayā smṛtiḥ eva iti katham jñāyate iti ced darśana anantaram anvaya vyatireka sādhana lakṣaṇena vyavadhānena vinā idam ghaṭa viviktam pradeśa vastu asti idam tu ghaṭavastu na asti iti pāścātyena vikalpa dvayena vyavasthāpanāt tatas na anvaya vyatireka anusaraṇam atra asti iti 
HBṬ_4.2.108	 kiñ ca dṛṣṭa antara asiddhe sva ātmani abhāva viṣaya upalabdhiḥ tad abhāvasya sādhanam tat eva vyatireka mukhena darśayati tat ca tasya ityādi iha api asti eva anvayaḥ iti ced āha na hi evaṃśakyam ityādi kasmāt na śakyam darśayitum  tat eka upalabdheḥ tasya ekasya ananya saṃsarggiṇaḥ yā upalabdhiḥ viśeṣa rūpā tasyāḥ kvacid api anyatra abhāvāt atha tad vivikta upalabdhi sāmānyam hetuḥ ucyate yatra yatra ghaṭa vivikta bhūta la upalabdhiḥ tatra tatra ghaṭa abhāvaḥ yathā pūrva anubhūte ghaṭa vivikte pradeśaḥ iti āha sāmānyena pradarśane kriyamāṇe dṛṣṭānte api pūrva anubhūta ghaṭa vivikte pradeśe ghaṭa abhāvasya prasādhakam pratyakṣa ādikam pramāṇa antaram anya bhāva viṣaya upalabdheḥ na asti kim tu sā eva tad anya bhāva upalabdhiḥ sādhya dharmasya tad abhāva lakṣaṇasya sādhikā sā ca yathā sādhya dharmiṇi tad abhāva siddhaye dṛṣṭāntam apekṣate tathā 
HBṬ_4.2.109	 dṛṣṭānte api tathā tatra api tat anyatra api iti anavasthā dṛṣṭāntānām iti anavasthāyām ca apratipattiḥ sarvatra tad abhāvasya yatas evam tasmāt na kutaścid lliṅgāt tad anya bhāvāt tad upalabdheḥ vā tad abhāva siddhiḥ iti yadi tad anya bhāvaḥ tad abhāvam na sādhayati kim punar lliṅga tayā sādhayati  iti atas āha saḥ anya bhāvaḥ pratyakṣa lakṣaṇena pratyakṣasya eva vivakṣita upalambhāt anya tvena anupalambha tvāt tad lakṣaṇena anupalambhena siddhaḥ san abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet karma stha kriyā apekṣāyām tad anya bhāvasya anupalabdhi rūpa tvāt kva punar asau abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet  mūḍha pratipattau sādhyāyām yaḥ tu amūḍhaḥ viṣaya pratipattau viṣayiṇam smarati eva tasya abhāva vyavahāraḥ pratyakṣa nibandhana eva iti na tatra anupalabdheḥ liṅgatā iti su carccitam eva anyatra iti iha alam prasaṅgena iti 
HBṬ_4.3.1	 tat evam anupalabdheḥ aśeṣa vipratipatti nirākaraṇena svarūpam avasthāpya prabheda nirddeśa artham āha seyaṃyata uktā tridhā anupalabdhiḥ katham  siddhe tad prasādhakena pramāṇena kārya kāraṇa bhāve sati kāraṇasya anupalabdhiḥ kīdṛśasya  siddhābhāvasya tathā vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau satyām tad prasādhana pramāṇa balena eva siddhābhāvasya eva vyāpakasya na anyasya vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ eva asiddha tā prasaṅgāt yathā uktā svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ ca iti evam trividhā anupalabdhiḥ katham punar kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ abhāva vyavahāraḥ sidhyati yatas tayoḥ siddhābhāva tā ucyate iti āha tatra kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ api na kevalam yasya sākṣāt abhāva vyavahāraḥ sādhyate svabhāva anupalabdhau svabhāvasya asat vyavahārasya siddhiḥ anyasya tad viviktasya bhāva siddhiḥ yā sā eva asat vyavahāra siddhi hetu tvāt evam ucyate sa kāraṇa vyāpaka abhāvaḥ tathā asiddhaḥ 
HBṬ_4.3.2	 anya bhāva siddhyā pratyakṣa rūpayā siddhaḥ abhāva vyavahāraḥ kārya vyāpyayoḥ pratiṣedhyayoḥ yadā anayoḥ virūpa viṣaya tayā sa viśeṣāṇām upalabdhiḥ na sidhyati tadā abhāvam abhāva vyavahāraṃvāsādhayati samuccaya arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ atha kim svabhāva anupalabdhau api abhāvaḥ liṅga tayā sādhyate iti āha svabhāva anupalabdhau tu ityādi abhāva vyavahāraḥ eva na abhāvaḥ api tasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt 
HBṬ_4.3.3	 atra parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkya āha yadi tarhi kāraṇa vyāpakau siddhaḥ asat vyavahāraḥ yayoḥ tau santau kena  tad anyasya karaṇa vyāpaka viviktasya bhāvasya siddhiḥ yā pratyakṣa ātmikā tad rūpayā anupalabdhyā anyasya kāryasya vyāpyasya vā abhāvam abhāva vyavahāram ca sādhayataḥ sā ca anya bhāva upalabdhiḥ tayoḥ kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptau eva satyām asat vyavahārasya sādhikā na anyathā iti evam iṣyamāṇe sati katham tayoḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka an upalabdhyoḥ parokṣe arthe viṣaye prayogaḥ yadā kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ vyatireka prayogaḥ kriyate yatra yatra agniḥ na asti tatra tatra dhūmaḥ api na asti tathā yatra yatra vṛkṣaḥ na asti kṣaṇikatā vā tatra tatra śiṃśapā na asti sattvam vā iti aśeṣa padārtha parigraheṇa vyatireka prayoge sati na hi tadā agni vṛkṣa vyatiriktāḥ sarve arthāḥ pratyakṣakṣāḥ akṣaṇika tā vā tatas ca katham 
HBṬ_4.3.4	 tad vivikta upalabdhi lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ pratiyoginaḥ na upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tā siddhāḥ  tathā ca katham aśeṣa upasaṃhāreṇa vyāptyā kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ vyatirekaḥ sidhyet  tad asiddhau vā katham anayoḥ ggamaka tvam  tasmāt kvacid adarśana mātrāt eva vyatirekaḥ eṣṭavyaḥ kvacid ca darśana mātrāt anvayaḥ tathā ca pratibandha ghoṣaṇā anarthikā iti manyate paraḥ 
HBṬ_4.3.5	 siddhānta vādi āha na eva parokṣe arthe kāraṇa vyāpaka an upalabdhyoḥ prayogaḥ vyatireka upadarśana kāle pramāṇa tayā kāraṇasya vyāpakasya vā anupalabdhiḥ pramāṇa bhūtā na eva prayujyate kasmāt  liṅgasya kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhi lakṣaṇasya tad abhāva lakṣaṇasya vā aniścayāt tad anupalabdhyoḥ sandeha rūpa tvāt tad abhāvasya ca sandigdha tvāt katham tarhi tadā anayoḥ prayogaḥ iṣyate iti āha kevalam ityādi kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva prasādhakena pūrva uktena pramāṇena vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva sādhakena ca tad utpatti lakṣaṇe tādātmya lakṣaṇe ca sambandhe sādhite siddha sambandhayoḥ yadi abhāvaḥ yatra yatra abhāvaḥ syāt parasya api kāryasya vyāpyasya vā avaśyam niyamena abhāvaḥ anyathā ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt niḥsvabhāvatā prasaṅgāt ca tad dvāreṇa pratibandha prasādhake pramāṇe smṛtiḥ katham nāma 
HBṬ_4.3.6	 syāt iti etasya arthasya darśana artham ete kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhī prayujyeta iti darśana adarśana balena tu sādhane yatra eva eka darśane paraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ adarśane vā na dṛṣṭaḥ tatra eva tasya bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā bhavatu sarvatra tu kasmāt bhavati  na hi apratibaddha ātmanām gavāśu ādīnām kvacid tathā abhāva darśane api sarvatra tathā abhāvaḥ bhavati puruṣasya tu sarvadā kvacid eka bhāva abhāvayoḥ aparasya bhāva abhāva darśanam yadṛcchā saṃvādaḥ sambhāvyeta asati pratibandhe tathā ca āha 
HBṬ_4.3.7–4.3.8	 deśa ādi bheda at ṛṛṣyante bhinna adravya iṣu śaktayaḥ pramāṇa siddhe sati avaśyam eva yatra yatra kāryam tatra tatra kāraṇam yatra yatra tad abhāvaḥ tatra tatra ca kāryasya api abhāvaḥ anyathā kāraṇam antareṇa kāryasya bhāve tasya ahetu tā eva syāt tatas ca nityam sattva ādi prasaṅgaḥ tathā yatra yatra yat svabhāvaḥ tatra tatra tad bhāvaḥ anyathā tasya nairātmyam eva syāt iti vyāptyā eva anvaya vyatireka upadarśane pratibandhaḥ khyāpayitum śakyate na anyathā iti prāk eva vistarataḥ vipañcitam 
HBṬ_4.4.1^1	 evam kāraī svabhāva anupalabdhi lakṣaṇe eva pakṣa dharme tad sādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāvāt anvaya vyatireka sadbhāvaḥ na anyatra iti pratipādya upasaṃharan āha iti eṣaḥ eva svabhāva kārya anupalabdhi lakṣaṇaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ anvaya vyatirekavān pratibandha sadbhāvāt yatas ca anvaya vyatirekavān pratibandha prasādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāvāt uktena nyāyena iti tasmāt tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ anvaya vyatireka niścayena eva tad aṃśa vyāpteḥ niścayāt yathoktam prāk tatas ca tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanāt tri lakṣaṇaḥ eva trirūpaḥ eva trividha eva hetuḥ ggamakaḥ na anya lakṣaṇaḥ anyaḥ vā yathā ukta trairūpya sadbhāve rūpa antarasya vaiyarthyāt yathā ukta trairūpya abhāve ca rūpa antara kalpanāyām api avyabhicāra abhāvena āgamaka tvāt 
HBṬ_4.4.1^2	 kasmāt tri lakṣāṇaḥ eva trividhaḥ eva hetuḥ ggamakaḥ na anya lakṣaṇaḥ anyaḥ vā iti darśayati sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārāt iti tri lakṣaṇasya eva sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārāt sva sādhya dharma avyabhicāraḥ eva ca gamaka tvam iti rūpa antara kalpanā vyarthāḥ pratibandha nibandhana anvaya vyatireka apagame ca rūpa antara kalpanāyām api sva sādhya dharma avyabhicāra abhāvāt tat anena tridhā eva saḥ iti asya tri lakṣaṇaḥ eva sa hetuḥ avinābhā= asya sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārasya niyamāt avaśyan tayā sadbhāvāt pratibandha nimitta tad aṃśa vyāpti anabhyupagame ca rūpa antara kalpanāyām api hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare yathā ukta tri lakṣaṇāt apare rūpa antara yogi tayā vikalpyamānā hetvābhāsā avinābhā= asya sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārasya teṣu abhāvāt iti aparaḥ arthaḥ darśitaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.1	 yat uktam tri lakṣaṇaḥ eva hetuḥ na anya lakṣaṇaḥ iti tatra pareṣām vipratipattim darśayan āha ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ iti aparena eyāyikamīmāṃsaka ādayaḥ manyante kāni punar ṣaṣ rūpāṇi hetoḥ taiḥ iṣyaṃte iti āha trīṇi ca etāni pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatireka ākhyāni tathā abādhita viṣaya tvam caturtham rūpam abādhitaḥ pramāṇena anirākṛtaḥ viṣayaḥ sādhya dharma lakṣaṇaḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam aparam rūpam tathā vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam rūpa antaram ekā saṃkhyā yasya hetu dravyasya tat eka saṃkhyam vivakṣitam eka saṃkhyam hetu dravyam āśraya tvena yasya hetu sāmānyasya tad vivakṣita eka saṃkhyam tad bhāvaḥ aparam rūpam yadi eka saṃkhyā vyavacchinnāyām pratihetuḥ ahitāyām hetu vyaktau hetu tvam bhavati tadā gamaka tvam na tu pratihetu sahitāyām api dvi saṃkhyā yuktāyām iti yadi viruddha avyabhicārya param 
HBṬ_4.5.2	 hetu antaram na upadarśyate iti yāvat tathā jñāna tvam ca jñāna viṣaya tvam ca na hi ajñātaḥ hetuḥ sva sattā mātreṇa gamakaḥ yuktaḥ iti tatra eteṣu rūpa antareṣu yat etat abādhita viṣaya tvam nāma tat tāvat pratibandha nibandhana anvaya vyatireka ātmakāḥ avinā abhāva sambhave sati tatas pṛthak anyat lakṣaṇam na bhavati tad ātmakam tu tat vacanena eva uktam iti na vaktavyam iti kasmāt pṛthak lakṣaṇam na bhavati bādhāyāḥ avinā abhāvasya ca virodhāt iti tathā hi sati api avinā abhāve yathā ukte bādhā sambhavam manyamānaiḥ abādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaram ucyate sā ca iyam tad sambhāvanā na sambhavati bādhāyāḥ avinā abhāvena virodhāt saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇāt tam eva virodham sādhayan āha avinā abhāvaḥ hi ityādi sati eva hi sādhya dharme bhāvaḥ hetoḥ avinā abhāvaḥ ucyate pramāṇa bādhā tu tasmin= asati yadi hi sati eva tasmin tad abhāva viṣayam pramāṇam pravartteta tadā asya bhrānta tvāt apramāṇa tā eva syāt 
HBṬ_4.5.3	 iti kutas bādhā  tatas sa hetuḥ tad lakṣaṇaḥ sādhya avinābhāvī dharmiṇi syāt atra ca sādhya dharmaḥ kathaṃ na bhavet yatas bādha avakāśaḥ syāt tasmāt avinā abhāvasya pramāṇa bādhāyāḥ ca saha anavasthānam avinā abhāvena upasthāpitasya dharmiṇi sādhya dharma bhāvasya pramāṇa bādha upasthāpitasya ca tad abhāvasya paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇa tayā virodhena ekatra dharmiṇī asambhavāt iti 
HBṬ_4.5.4	 tam eva virodham saṣṭīkartum para upahāsa vyājena āha pratyakṣa anumāne hi ityādi sādhya dharmam hi bādhamāne pratyakṣa anumāne taṃgrīvāyāṃgṛhītvā dharmiṇaḥ sva āśrayāt niṣkāsayataḥ tasmin ca sādhya dharme sati eva tad avinā bhāvi tvāt dhetuḥ bhavan tam sādhya dharmam niṣkāsyamānam gale gṛhītvā haṭhāt tatra eva dharmiṇī avasthāpayati iti param prakṛṣṭam vata bhāvānām sādhya dharma lakṣaṇānām asvāsthyam vartate tathā hi yantra dvaya niyantritānām nirucchvāsitayā maraṇam eva prāptam iti 
HBṬ_4.5.5	 paraḥ bādhā avinā bhāvayoḥ viṣaya bhedāt avirodham darśayan āha anyatra sādhya dharmiṇam parihṛtya dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sādhya dharmeṇa avinābhāvī hetuḥ na punar sādhya dharmiṇī eva tatas kutas bādhā avinā bhāvayoḥ virodhaḥ anyatra bādhayā sādhya dharma abhāva sādhanāt anyatra ca hetunā tad bhāva sādhanāt tathā ca evaṃvidhe sati api avinā abhāve bādhā sambhavāt abādhita viṣaya tvasya rūpa antarasya sambhavaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.6	 evaṃvidhāvinā abhāva upagame sati api abādhita viṣaya tva ādike rūpantare hetvābhāsāḥ tatas a pare rūpa antara sambhavinaḥ iti āpāditām hetvābhāsa tām vivarītum para upahāsa pūrvakam āha tat kim ayam sādhya dharmī tapasvī varākaḥ śaṇḍham udvāhya tasmin sādhya dharma sādhana śākti vikalam hetum pariṇāyya sādhya dharma lakṣaṇam putraṃmṛgayate  etat eva vyanakti yasya hetoḥ ddharmiṇī asati api sādhya dharme bhāvaḥ iṣyate sādhya dharmiṇaḥ anyatra āvinābhāva upagamāt tam tathāvidham sādhya dharmiṇī upadarśya katham dharmī sādhya dharmavān iti ucyate  na hi ambhaḥ tu asya samudre lavaṇa tvena āvinābhave api tad vyatirikte ambhasi lavaṇa tayā sādhya tvena iṣṭe ambhaḥ tu abhāve api lavaṇa tva siddhiḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.7	 parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkhyā āha atas eva ityādi etat eva vivṛnoti syāt etat bhavataḥ matam yatas eva hetuḥ anyathā api sādhya dharmam antareṇa api dharmiṇi bhavet ambhaḥ tu ādiṣu tathā adarśanāt sādhya dharmi parihāreṇa ca avinābhāa upagamāt atas eva kāraṇāt pramāṇābhyām abādhita dharmāḥ dharmī iti ucyate yadi pratyakṣa anumānābhyām sādhya dharmiṇi hetoḥ viṣayaḥ sādhya dharmaḥ na bādhyate yathā ambhaḥ tu asya lavaṇa tvam tadā tasya gamaka tvam na anyathā iti tatas anyatra avinābhāva mātreṇa sādhya siddheḥ anabhyupagamāt na yathā uktaḥ doṣaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.8	 siddhānta vādi āha tat kim idānīm yadā hetoḥ dharmiṇī avinābhāvita anabhyupagamāt sādhya siddheḥ abhāvāt tad siddhaye rūpa antaram abādhita viṣaya tvam ucyate tadā hetoḥ na kiñcid sāmarthyam kasmāt abādhayā eva hetum antareṇa api sādhya siddheḥ akiñcitkaraḥ eva hetuḥ tathā hi atra kalpanā dvaiyam bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttau sādhya abhāvaḥ niyataḥ vā syāt aniyataḥ vā  tatra yadi pūrvaḥ vikalpaḥ tadā sādhya abhāvaḥ hi bādhaka pramāṇasya vṛttau niyataḥ tadā eva bhāvāt tad abhāve ca abhāvāt iti tasmāt abādhāyām bādhaka pramāṇa vṛtti abhāve tat niyatasya sādhya abhāvasya api abhāvāt sādhya siddheḥ bhavati eva iti vyarthaḥ eva hetuḥ iti na upanyasanīyaḥ eva tatas kasya ābādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaraṇ bhavet  syāt matam mā bhūt bādhaka pramāṇa vṛtti abhāve hetoḥ sāmarthyam yadā tu sādhyasya bādhakam pramāṇam dharmiṇi varttate tadā hetoḥ sādhya sādhane 
HBṬ_4.5.9	 sāmarthyam bhaviṣyati iti atas āha bādhāyām api iti yadi bādhakam pramāṇam varttate tadā tena sādhya abhāvasya dharmiṇi sādhanāt punar brahnaṇā api tad bhāvasya karttum aśakya tvāt kim aṅga punar śaṣṭhena hetunā iti kutas sādhanasya hetoḥ sāmarthyam  atas eva hi bhavadbhiḥ abādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaram ucyate iti 
HBṬ_4.5.10	 atha bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttau sādhya abhāvaḥ na niyataḥ tad abhāve api bhāvāt iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣyate tat api abādhāyāḥ sāmarthya virahaḥ iti darśayan āha aniyame bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttau sādhya abhāvasya iṣyamāṇe sati idam āpatitam na ca bādhakam pramāṇam syāt sādhya abhāvasya ca sambhavaḥ iti na sādhya sādhane sāmarthyam abādhāyāḥ satyām api sādhya abhāvasya smbhavāt iti tad yoginaḥ api hetvābhāsa tā eva iti 
HBṬ_4.5.11–4.5.12	 yat uktam abādhayā eva sādhya siddheḥ vyarthaḥ hetuḥ iti tatra anyathārtham abādhāyāḥ darśayan hetu sāmarthyam pratipādayan āha paraḥ na bādhāyāḥ abhāvaḥ samābādhā abhimatā kim tarhi  bādhāyāḥ anupalabdhiḥ sā ca tad anupalabdhiḥ puruṣasya śakti vaikalyāt kvacid deśa ādau bādhāyāḥ sambhave api syāt tatas bādhā anupalabdhi mātreṇa sadhya siddheḥ abhāvāt tad siddhye avaśyam hetuḥ abhidhānīyaḥ iti sa hetu prayogasya viṣayaḥ tadā hi hetuḥ sva sādhyam sādhayan katham asamarthaḥ syāt iti siddhānta vādi āha kim nu vai hetuḥ bādhāyāḥ yā upalabdhiḥ tasyāḥ bibheti na punar bbādhāyāḥ yena bādhām sambhavantīm api anādṛtya tad anupalabdhau satyām prayoktavyaḥ iṣṭaḥ bhavataḥ 
HBṬ_4.5.13	 kadācid paraḥ brūyāt kim kariṣyati vidyamānā api bādhā tapasvinī tad upalabdhiḥ eva rākṣasī tasmāt tatas eva hetoḥ bhayam tad abhāve hetuḥ prayoktavyaḥ eva iti atas āha sa tarhi ityādi evam tarhi parama arthena bādhā kim asti na asti iti etat anapekṣya bādhāyāḥ anupalabdhau satyām prayoktavyaḥ iti kā akvā pṛcchati kadācid paraḥ brūyāt uktam eva etat kim artham pṛccyate iti āha kim arthaṃprayujyate iti bādhā anupalambhe api tad sambhave sādhya sdhana ayogāt iti abhiprāyaḥ paraḥ anavagata abhiprāyaḥ āha sādhya siddhi artham iti bādhaka pratyaya abhāve prāmāṇyasya iṣṭa tvāt tatas sādhya siddhiḥ avirūddhā eva iti manyate siddhānta vādī satyām bādhāyām tad anupalambhe api sādhya siddhim asambhāvayan pṛcchati sa kiṃkvacid ityādi kim punar asau hetuḥ satyām api bādhāyām sādhyam sādhayet iti sambhavyate bhavatā yena asyāḥ bādhāyāḥ abhāva viniścayam prati yatnaḥ na kriyate 
HBṬ_4.5.14–4.5.15^1	 hetuḥ ca prayujyate iti evam etat iti ced tathā satyām api bādhāyām sādhya sādhana sāmarthya upagame sati abādhita viṣaya tvam na bhavati kim kāraṇam  bādhāyām api satyām asya hetoḥ sāmarthyāt sāmarthya upagamāt tat dhi hetoḥ lakṣaṇam ucyate yena vinā sādhyam na sādhayet iti syan matam anupalabhyamāna bādha tvam hetu lakṣaṇam parama arthena na ābādhita viṣaya tvam iti atas āha tathā ca ityādi evam sati bādhāyāḥ sadbhāva sambhave api tām abhyupagamya tad anupalambha mātreṇa hetoḥ prayogaḥ prāptaḥ 
HBṬ_4.5.14–4.5.15^2	 yadi hi bādhām abhyupagamya hetu prayogaḥ na abhimataḥ syāt tadā anupalambha mātreṇa bādhāyām saṃśayāt satām api keśāñcid kathañcid anupalambha sambhavāt saṃśayitasya hetu prayoge pravṛttiḥ eva na yujyeta tasmāt yaḥ yat saṃśaye api pravartate sa tasya bhāva pakṣam abhyupetya eva pravarttate tathā ca yathā bādha anupalabdhau tām abhyupagamya hetuḥ prayujyate tathā tad upalabdhau api prayujyatām bādhāyāḥ sadbhāva abhyupagame sati tad upalambha anupalambhayoḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt iti na anupalabhyamāna bādha tvam api hetu lakṣaṇam yujyate iti kutas bādhaka pratyaya virahe api asati pratibandhe prāmāṇyasya sambhavaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.16	 parasya vacana avakāśam āśaṅkhyā āha na bādhāyām ityādi na eva hi bādhāyām satyām hetoḥ sāmarthyam iṣyate tat katham tad upalambhe api prayogaḥ syāt  siddhānta vādi āha yadi evam bādhāyām satyām hetuḥ asamarthaḥ yadi iṣyate tadā anirṇītaḥ adhāyā asaṃbhavaḥ yasya hetoḥ sa tathāvidhaḥ prayogaṃbādhāḥ anupalambha mātreṇa na arhati kim kāraṇam  mā bhūt bādhāyāḥ sambhava pakṣe prayuktasya api hetoḥ sādhya siddhau asāmarthyam iti pūrva pakṣa vādī āha bādha anupalambhe sati bādhāyāḥ ābhāvāt sat upalambhaka pratyaya abhāve sati avaśyam arthānām asattvāt dhetoḥ sāmathyam iti ced manyase siddhānta vādi āha kim upalambhaḥ bādhām ityādi upalambhaḥ hi arthānām kāryam na ca kāryam kāraṇam vyāpnoti na hi avaśyam kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti pratibandha vaikalya sambhavāt tat katham avyāpakasya upalambhasya 
HBṬ_4.5.17–4.5.18	 nivṛttau bādhāyāḥ nivṛttiḥ  yatas hetoḥ bbādhāyāḥ sambhava kṛtam asāmarthyam na sambhavet iti etat ca paraiḥ api iṣyate eva pramāṇa tayā upagatasya api udaya kāle anupalabdha bādhasya kāla antareṇa bādhaka pratyaya utpāde sati aprāmāṇya upagamāt atha avyāpakasya api upalambhasya ivṛttau bādhā nivarttate nivarttate hi mithyā tvaṃda uśa ajānāt ayatnataḥ 
HBṬ_4.5.19–4.5.20	 iti anena eva nyāyena jñāna nivṛttyā bādhā nivṛtteḥ iti āha tathā api vyarthaḥ hetuḥ kutas  bādha anupalambhāt eva hetu pa yoga rahitāt sādhya siddheḥ kim kāraṇam  anupalambhe bādhāyāḥ asambhavāt tathā hi yatra bādhāyāḥ anupalambhaḥ tatra paramārthataḥ eva sā na vidyate iti manyase yatra ca asau paramārthataḥ na asti tatra sādhya dharmasya abhāvaḥ api parama arthena eva na asti anyathā parama arthena bādhāyāḥ abhāva ayogāt tatas ca sādhya dharmasya abhāva abhāve sati bhāvaḥ iti bhavat matya sādhya pratīteḥ vyartha tā hetoḥ iti atha mā bhūt yukti virodhaḥ iti na upalambha nivṛttau bādhā nivṛttiḥ iṣyate tatra āha upalambhasya nivṛttau api satyām bādhāyāḥ anivṛttau iṣyamāṇāyām tad avastham hetoḥ asāmarthyam yat avastham bādha upalambhaḥ iti hetoḥ aprayogaḥ iti kasya ābādhita viṣaya tvam rūpa antaram syāt  
HBṬ_4.5.21	 etat eva upasaṃharan āha tasmāt sva sādhyaḥ ityādi yatas evam vyāptya hetoḥ sarvatra sādhyena āvinā abhāva abhyupagame bahis vyāpta viṣayamāṇāyām vaiyarthyam hetu prayogasya āpadyate tasmāt sva sādhya bhāva abhāvābhyāṃanyathā api svasādhya bhāve api abhavat na abhāve api ca bhavan hetuḥ dharmiṇi kiñcid sādhyam na bhāvayati na sādhayati na vibhāvayati tad viparītam na niṣedhayati iti tasya vidhi pratiṣedhauvakurvata upakṣepaḥ prayogaḥ na samarthaḥ iti avaśyam hetu prayogam icchatā sva sādhya avinābhāvaḥ sarvatra hetoḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ sa ca pratibandha nibandhanaḥ eṣa ca darśana adarśana mātra āyattaḥ yathoktam prak tasmin ca abhyupagate bādhāvinā bhāvayoḥ virodhaḥ siddhaḥ iti upasaṃharan āha tat naḥ ityādi yatas evam tena kāraṇena ābādhā rūpa antaram na bhavati 
HBṬ_4.5.22	 yadi nāma bādhāvinā abhāvayoḥ saha avasthāna abhāvāt avinā abhāve sati abādhā gamyate rūpa antaram tu kim iti na bhavati iti atas āha tat nāma ityādi tat dhi tasmāt viśeṣaṇa antaram bhavet vastu sthitayā lakṣaṇa kāraiḥ ca rūpa antara tvena upādānam arhati yasya viśeṣaṇasya bhave api yasya aparasya abhāvaḥ syāt yatas svabhāve vyabhicāre ca viśeṣaṇa viśeśya bhāvaḥ na sambhavaḥ eva kevale udāharaṇam āha tat yathā ityādi sati api hi śrāvaṇa tva ādeḥ sa pakṣe bhāvaḥ na asti sati api ca cākśuṣa tva ādeḥ sa pakṣe bhāve sādhya dharmiṇi śabde sambandhaḥ na asti tatas anyoḥ sambava vyabhicārayoḥ bhāvāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ lakṣaṇa antara tvena ca upādānam ihā api evam bhaviṣyati iti ced āha na ca etat anantara uditam abādhāyāḥ avinā abhāve sati sambhavati sati avinā abhāve niyamena ābādhāyāḥ sambhavāt vyabhicāra abhāvāt kutas viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ 
HBṬ_4.5.23	 lakṣaṇa antara tvena ca upādānam arhati iti na hetoḥ sādhyāvinābhāvinaḥ viruddhasya ca sādhya viparyaya avinābhāvinaḥ viṣaye bādhā sambhavati uktena prakāreṇa viparyaye samyak hetuḥ eva aviṣaye tu prayogāt dhetu ābhāsaḥ ucyate yatas evam iti tasmāt na tad abhāvaḥ bādhā virahaḥ pṛthak avinā abhāvāt anvaya vyatireka ātmanaḥ anayoḥ hetu viruddhayoḥ lakṣaṇa antara tvena vācyaḥ vyabhicāra abhāvena rūpa antara tva ayogāt yatas ca āvinā abhāve sati bādhā na sambhavati virodhāt tasmāt dhetoḥ yathā ukta lakṣaṇasya prayoge sati gamya arthāyāḥ api pratijñāyāḥ doṣāṇām pratyakṣa viruddha ādīnām sambhavaḥ na asti hetu lakṣaṇena eva teṣām nirasta tvāt tat katham bādhā virahaḥ hetoḥ rūpa antaram ucyate asambhavinām ca teṣām upavarṇanam niṣphalam iti ākūtam 
HBṬ_4.5.24	 kevalāyāḥ prayoge asti sambhavaḥ iti ced āha na api ityādi hetu prayoge hi asati kevalā pratijñā eva na prayujyate hetu viṣaya tvena tad abhyupagamāt tatas caśāstrakāraiḥ na pratijñā doṣāḥ pratyakṣa viruddha ādayaḥ vācyāḥ iti diṅnāga pādaiḥ tu sādhya asādhya viparyayeṇa vipratipatti darśanāt aprayoga arhasya api pakṣasya lakṣaṇa vidhāne nyāya prāptam eva apakṣa tvam nirākṛta padena pramāṇa viruddhasya ākhyānam na tu ati prasaktam pakṣa lakṣaṇam vyavacchinnam sandigdhasya eva sādhya tvāt pramāṇa bādhite sādhaka pramāṇa āvṛtteḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.25–4.5.26	 tat evam abādhita viṣaya tvam nirākṛtya rūpa antaram nirākurvan āha etena avinā abhāve sati bādhāyāḥ asambhava darśanena eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā a pi viruddha avyabhicāri doṣa vipakṣeṇa ucyamānā pratyuktā pratyākhyātāḥ paraḥpṛcchati katham iti kena prakāreṇa yathā bādhāvinā abhāvayoḥ saha anavasthānam tathā pratihetu avinā bhāvayoḥ api  yena eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā tadvat eva pratyākhyāyeta iti 
HBṬ_4.5.27	 siddhānta vādī sāmyam darśayan āha ekaḥ ityādi ekaḥ hi hetuḥ lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ sva sādhya avyabhicārī katham bhavati  yadi sva sādhya bhāvaḥ eva bhavet anyathā tad lakṣaṇam avinābhāvaḥ nāma hīyeta atra eva dharmiṇi sa tad lakṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ bhavati tatra eva dharmiṇi tasmāt anyaḥ api pratihetuḥ viruddhaḥ tena hetu lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ katham bhavati  ekasya hetoḥ yat sādhyam tat bādhakasya tat viruddhasya aparasya dharmasya bhāvaḥ eva na abhāve bhāvāt avinā abhāvāt iti bādhayā samānam bādhā sambhavena samānaḥ pratihetuḥ iti nirastaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.28	 atra eva dūṣaṇa antaram abhidhātum vikalpayan āha api ca ityādi vastutas paramārthataḥ yasya pratihetuḥ na sambhavati kim asau samyak jñānasya viparyayasya vā upanyasta sādhya viparīta jñānasya vā hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ yatas vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam tat lakṣaṇam ucyate āhosvit yasya pratihetuḥ tad sādhya viparīta sādhakaḥ na pradarśitaḥ paramārthataḥ san api iti paraḥ doṣam apaśyan āha kiñcataḥ ityādi yadi nāma pūrvaḥ vikalpaḥ uttaraḥ vā tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.29	 siddhānta vādi āha yadi asambhavan pratihetuḥ yasya sa samyak jñāna ādi hetuḥ iṣyate tadā alakṣaṇam etat vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam kasmāt aśakyaḥ niścayaḥ yasya vastutas asambhavat pratihetutvasya sa tathā uktaḥ parama tāpekṣayā ca etat ucyate paraḥ hi darśana adarśanābhyām asati api pratibandhe avinābhāvam icchati paraḥ hi darśana adarśanābhyām asati api pratibandhe avinābhāvam icchati tatas tasya pratihetoḥ evaṃvidhasya sambhavaḥ asti sa ca anupalabhyamānaḥ api kadācid syāt iti vastutas tad abhāvaḥ niścīyate pratibandha nibandhanāvinā abhāva vādinām tu asmākam pratihetu asambhavaḥ su niścitaḥ eva na hi tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇe pratibandhe pramāṇataḥ siddhe tad nimitta avinā bhāvitayā ekena hetuna sva sādhye sādhite punar tatra eva dharmiṇi tad lakṣaṇasya tad viruddha artha sādhakasya pratihetoḥ sambhavaḥ śaṅkhyate bhāvānām viruddha svabhāva dvaya ayogāt viruddha dharma sādhaka sambhave ca tasya eva 
HBṬ_4.5.30–4.5.31	 sva sādhya avinābhāvinaḥ prathamasya tatra pramāṇataḥ bhāva siddhi ayogāt iti syāt matam yadi nāma prastutaḥ pratihetu asambhavaḥ asmābhiḥ niścetum aśakyaḥ tathā api asambhavat pratihetu tvam vivakṣitta eka saṃkhya tva pratipāditam hetu lakṣaṇam kasmāt na bhavati iti āha na hi aniścita ātmanaḥ ityādi pratipādakaḥ yaḥ dharmaḥ hetoḥ tasya aniścita svabhāvasya yasmāt tad lakṣaṇa tvam pratipādaka dharma tā na bhavati yathā saṃdigdhasya pakṣa dharma tvasya iti pūrvakasya sādhanam na api sandigdham lakṣaṇam yasya sa hetuḥ bhavati iti na kaścid hetuḥ bhavet iti hetu abhāvaḥ vā iti asya samarthanam tatas ca hetvābhāsāḥ tatas api iti atra api yojitam iti 
HBṬ_4.5.32–4.5.33	 syāt matam yasya pratiyogī dṛśyate tasya eva pratihetu bhāvāt ahetu tvam bhavatu yasya tu pratiyogī hetuḥ na dṛśyate sa vastutas eva asambha vat pratihetuḥ na hi tatra vastutas pratihetusambhavaḥ śaṅkyate bādhaka pratyayam antareṇa bādhā śaṅkāyāḥ ayogāt tat uktam bādhā jñāne tu anutpanne na āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikāḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.34	 atas āha tulye lakṣaṇe hi ityādi śaṅyamāna pratihetunā tulyam lakṣaṇam darśana adarśana mātra nimitta avinā bhāva rūpam yasya tasmin dṛṣṭaḥ pratiyoginaḥ pratihetoḥ bbādhakasya sambhava sa yeśām api tad tulya lakṣaṇānām pratiyogī na dṛśyate teṣu api śaṅkām pratihetu sambhava viṣayām utpādayati kim kāraṇam  adṛṣṭa pratiyoginaḥ dṛṣṭa pratiyoginaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt na hi tasya itareṇa kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti yatas tad sambhavaḥ na śaṅkyeta puruṣa śakti vaikalya ādinā tu tad adarśanam sambhāvyeta iti kim ucyate na āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikāḥ iti atha viśeṣaḥ pratibandha lakṣaṇaḥ avinā abhāva niścāyakaḥ dṛṣṭa pratihetor adṛṣṭa pratiyoginaḥ iṣyate yatas pratiyogi sambhava āśaṅkā astam upaiti tadā sati vā viśeṣe sa viśeṣaḥ hetoḥ lakṣaṇam kim kāraṇam  yatas tatas viśeṣāt dhetuḥ ekāntena niścayena nirasta pratipakṣaḥ tathāvidhe dharmiṇi pratihetu asambhavāt 
HBṬ_4.5.35	 sva sādhyam niścāyayati iti yaḥ tathāvidhaḥ na bhavati tad viśeṣa virahāt dṛṣṭa pratihetuḥ saḥ atad lakṣaṇaḥ na hetuḥ syāt tathā ca yadi nāmā ahetau pratihetuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hetoḥ kim āyātam yena tad nivṛttaye tatra eka saṃkhyā vivakśā kriyate yathā ukta āvinā bhāva vacanena eva tad nivṛtteḥ iti āha tathā ca hetau tad viśeṣa yogini pratihetu asambhave sati vyarthāḥ niṣprayojanam eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā iti yathā ukta viśeṣa aṅgīkaraṇe tad lakṣaṇasya pratihetoḥ asambhavāt kasya eka saṃkhyā vivakṣayā vyavacchedaḥ kriyate yatas asya kāryaka tvam syāt iti 
HBṬ_4.5.36	 viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ ca hetvābhāsasya vyavaccheda artham eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā hetu lakṣaṇe kriyate vastutas asambhavat pratihetu tva siddhye ca pratibandha lakṣaṇe viśeṣe hetau iṣyamāṇe viruddha avyabhicārī api hetvābhāsaḥ na bhavati tatas vyavacchedya abhāvāt kim eka saṃkhyā vivakṣayā iti darśayan āha atas pratibandha lakṣaṇa viśeṣa upagamāt viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ hetvābhāsasya yat lakṣaṇaṃtat dhīyeta na sambhavet kim punar tad viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ lakṣaṇam iti āha sva lakṣaṇaḥ ityādi hetoḥ yat ā ātmīyam lakṣaṇam tad yuktayoḥ hetvoḥ ekatra dharmiṇi virodhena paraspara viruddha sādhya sādhaka tvena upanipāte sati viruddha avyabhicārī iti viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ lakṣaṇam na ca tat pratibandha aṅgīkaraṇe sati sambhavati na hi tādātmya tad utpattibhyām svasādhya pratibandhavatī ekatra hetau kvacid dharmiṇi saṃbhavati dvitīyaḥ tad lakṣaṇaḥ tatra eva hetuḥ sambhavet bhāvānām viruddha svabhāva dvaya asambhavāt viruddha dharma adhyāsasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt tat avyabhicāriṇaḥ hetoḥ dvitīyasya tatra kutas sambhava avakāśaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.37	 nanu yadi tathāvidha viśeṣa sambhave sati viruddha avi abhicāri lakṣaṇam hīyate eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā vā vyārthāḥ tathā api na eva hetu abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tat kim uktam hetu abhāvaḥ vā iti atas āha na ca na eva tasya viśeṣasya pratibandha lakṣaṇasya yatas vastutas asambhavat pratihetu tvam niścīyate svarūpam tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇam nirddeśyate bhavadbhiḥ yathā asmābhiḥ nirdiṣṭam ydrūpam pratītya pratipadya pratiyoginaḥ sambhava asambhavāu utpaśyāmaḥ yatra sa viśeṣaḥ na asti tatra pratiyoginaḥ sambhavaḥ kalpitaḥ āgama āśraye anumāne yatra tu asti sa viśeṣaḥ vastu bala pravṛtte anumāne tatra pratiyoginaḥ asambhavaḥ iti yatas evam tasmāt na asti eva bhavatām sa viśeṣaḥ bhavadbhiḥ na jñāyate eva sa viśeṣaḥ iti tasmāt sarvatra yatra api pratiyogī na dṛśyate tatra api ṣāṅkyā pratiyogi viṣayayā bhavitavyam tām eva śaṅkhām draḍhyan āha 
HBṬ_4.5.38	 dṛṣṭa pratihetoḥ api ityādi yasya api hi pratihetuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasya api prāk pratiyogi darśanāt itareṇa sarvakālam adṛṣṭa pratiyoginā kaścid viśeṣaḥ lakṣyate yad darśanāt jñāyeta atra pratiyogī sambhavati nyānyatra iti darśana adarśana mātra nibandhanayoḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sarvatra samāna tvāt tathā api paścāt tatra pratiyogī dṛṣṭaḥ iti sarvatra tad tulya lakṣaṇe pratiyogi sadbhāva śaṅkā na vivarttate iti 
HBṬ_4.5.39–4.5.41	 syāt matam yeṣu pratiyogī sambhavati teṣu aśyam eva kadācid asau upalabhyate yeṣu tu puruṣa āyuṣeṇa api na upalabhyate trṣu asau na asti eva tatas sa tathāvidhaḥ hetuḥ bhaviṣyati tat katham hetu abhāvaḥ asmākam iti atas āha na ca ityādi yeṣām api hi pratihetuḥ sambhavati teṣām api na eva sarvadā tasya pratihetoḥ upalabdhiḥ pratipad tṛṛṇām na hi asarva darśinām upalabdhiḥ sarva bhāva sattām vyāpnoti pratibandha vaikalya sadbhāvāt nanu ca yatra sarvadā eva pratipattrā pratiyogī na dṛśyate tatra tad āśaṅkā katham kriyate  tathā ca āha bādhā jñāne tu anutpanne na āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikāḥ iti tathā aparam 
HBṬ_4.5.42	 śiṣya paramparayā kumārila utpādāt prāk dṛṣṭa pratiyogiṣu upanyasteṣu tena eva prajñā atiśaya śāktinā pratihetavaḥ utprekṣitāḥ tatas tad darśanāt yāvat jīvam adṛṣṭa pratihetuṣu api tad āśaṅkā nivarttate tatas katham āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikā ucyate  tulya lakṣaṇe hi iti ādikam api pratiyogi sambhava āśaṅkā kāraṇam uktam eva na ca pratiyogi sambhavam āśaṅkamānaḥ tad nimitta saṃbhavāt utprekṣeta hi iti ādi ākrośa mātrea nivarttayitum śakyate tena asya pratiyogi āśaṅkā apanodakṣam kiñcid kāraṇam abhidhānīyam yathā asmābhiḥ abhihitam svabhāva hetoḥ viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa vaśāt ātmya niścaye sati anvaya vyatirekayoḥ tatra nirṇaya kārya hetau ca yathā ukta pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ kārya kāraṇa siddheḥ tad niścayaḥ iti yatas evam sarvatra pratiyogi āśaṅkā na nivarttate bhavat darśane tena kāraṇā niścayaḥ pratiyoginaḥ sambhavayoḥ iha pratiyogī sambhavati iha tu na sambhavati iti evaṃrūpaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.43–4.5.44	 tasmāt vastutas asambhavat pratihetu tvam yat lakṣaṇam hetoḥ tasya aniścita tvāt eka saṃkhyā vivakśau ādinām na kaścid hetuḥ syāt na hi aniścita lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ bhavati iti upasaṃhāraḥ iti tat evam kim yaḥ vastutas asambhavat pratihetuḥ sa samyak jñāna viparyaya hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ iti amum vikalpam nirākṛtya dvitīyam vikalpam nirācikīrṣuḥ āha atha apradarśita pratihetuḥ samyak jñāna viviparyaya hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ iti sambandhaḥ ayam ca pakṣaḥ kila diṅnāga ācāryasya api abhimataḥ iti paraḥ upadarśayan āha yathā āha diṅnāga ācāryaḥ kim āha yadātarhi ityādi śrāvaṇa tvasya hi na kathañcid vyavaccheda hetutvam iti diś nāga ācāryeṇa ukte pareṇa abhihitam yadātarhi vaiya akāraṇaḥ śabda tvaṃsāmānya viśeṣaṃnityam abhyupagacchati tadā ayaṃśrāvaṇa tva lakṣaṇaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ hetuḥ eva syāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt śabda tva vat iti evam pareṇa ukte satya ācāryeṇa uktam yadi atra śabda ākhye dharmiṇī anitya tva hetuṃkṛtaka tva prayatna ānantarīyaka tva ādi lakṣaṇam kaścid vaiśeṣika ādiḥ na darśayet tadā ayam pradarśita pratihetuḥ hetuḥ 
HBṬ_4.5.45–4.5.46	 eva bhavet iti tat evam ācārya āpadaiḥ sākṣi tve datte mujam utkṣipya śāstra kāraḥ pūtkurvan āha idam idānīm ityādi yadā hi ācāryasya api etat abhimatam iti kaiścid vyākhyāyate tat idam su mahat vyasanam āyatam gurubhiḥ abhihita tvāt aprakāśyam na hi gurūṇām doṣaḥ prakāśayitum yuktaḥ nyāyam anupālayadbhiḥ asaṃvaraṇīyam apracchādanīyam tat kim gurūn dūṣayāmaḥ uta nyāyam api upekṣāmahe iti ubhayam api aśakyam iti kaṣṭa taraṃvyasanaṃkatham nirvoḍhuṃśakyeta  na kathaṃcid iti kaḥ punar atra doṣaḥ yena idam kaṣṭataram iti āha sa tāvat ayam śrāvaṇa tva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ vastuni śabda ādīni sva sādhyam tattvam nitya tvam tad prakṛtīni tad ātmakāni kṛtvā tat śrāvaṇa tvam pramāṇam yeṣām 
HBṬ_4.5.47	 puruṣāṇāṃmī māṃsaka vaiyākaraṇa dīnām tān abhyudayena svarggeṇa niḥśreyasena ca apa varggeṇa yojayitvā tathā hi vastu tattvam yāvan kleśāt na prajahāti tāvat svargam āsādayati kleśān tu prajahan nirvāṇa parāyaṇaḥ bhavati athavā śabda nitya tva pratītau veda prāmāṇyāt tad vahita agnihotra anuṣṭhānāt svarggaḥ vedānta niṣevaṇāt apavarggaḥ punar uttara kālam pratibhāvatā prajñā jātīyena vaiśeṣika ādinā puruṣeṇa hetu antarasya pratihetoḥ nidarśanena yat asya nitya tva sādhana sāmarthya pratihetu anupadarśane satya āsīt tat tad upadarśanena utkīlitam apanītam iti tāni vastūni nitya tva sampadaḥ pracyāvya tān ca tad pramāṇakān puruṣān svargga apavargga sampadaḥ pracyāvya śrāvaṇa tva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ śakti vaikalyāt paritrātum aśaktaḥ bhraṣṭa rājyaḥ iva rājā tapaḥ vanam gacchati 
HBṬ_4.5.48–4.5.49	 svaiḥ eva duścaritaiḥ iti kim atra vayam brūmaḥ  tat evam upahasya etasmin pakṣe doṣam upadarśayan āha puruṣa pratibhā ityādi yadā hi apradarśita pratihetuḥ hetuḥ iṣyate tadā puruṣa pratibhā akṛtam sādhana tvam abhyupagatam bhavati tatas ca vastutas na kiñcid sādhanam asādhanam vā prāptam tathā hi yadā pratihetuḥ na upadarśyate tadā sādhanam yadā tu upadarśyate tadā na sādhanam iti puruṣa pratibhā akṛtam sādhana tvam āyātam iti 
HBṬ_4.5.50	 api ca apradarśita pratihetoḥ hetoḥ hetu tve aṅgīkriyamāṇe vikalpa dvayam kim paramārthataḥ hetuḥ tad dharma bhāvī utā atad dharma bhāvi iti  tatra ādyam vikalpam adhikṛtya āha sa ca hetuḥ yaḥ asau prathamam upādīyate sa yadi svabhāvataḥ eva tasmin sādhya dharme sati eva bhavati iti evaṃśīlaḥ asmat upavarṇita pratibandha upagamāt yadi iṣyate tadā akatham anyathākriyeta hetu antareṇa ātad dharma bhāvī katham kriyate  na kathañcid kim kāraṇam  vastūnām hetu lakṣaṇānām yaḥ svabhāvaḥ sati eva sādhya dharme bhavana ātmakaḥ tad anyathā bhāvasya tad viparyayasya abhāvāt ubhayoḥ ca sva sādhya dharma avinābhāvi tve svabhāvataḥ eva dharmiṇī ekatra tayoḥ bhāve viruddau ubhau svabhāvau ekasya syātām na ca ekasya viruddhau svabhāvau sambhavataḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsena tasya ekatva hāni prasaṅgāt atha dvitīyaḥ vikalpaḥ tadā atad dharma bhāvīca 
HBṬ_4.5.51–4.5.52	 asati api sādhya dharme bhavana śīlaḥ pratibandha anabhyupagamāt katham anyadā api apradarśita pratihetu avasthāyām api sādhanam kasyacid  na eva tadā api sādhanam na kevalam pradarśita pratihetu avasthāyām iti upasaṃharan āha tasmāt savabhāvataḥ ityādi yatas evam bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ anyathā kartum na śakyate viruddha ubhaya svabhāvaḥ ca ekaḥ na sambhavati tasmāt paramārthataḥ svena svena sādhyena avinābhāvinoḥ yathā ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ tad lakṣaṇasya kārya svabhāva lakṣaṇasya pratihetoḥ asambhavāt alakṣaṇam eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam lakṣaṇam na bhavati kim kāraṇam iti āha vyavacchedya abhāvāt iti pratihetuḥ hi vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvasya vyavacchedyaḥ varṇyate sa ca pratihetuḥ sva lakṣaṇa yuktayoḥ kārya svabhāvayoḥ na bhavati eva iti katham tad hetu lakṣaṇam syāt iti tat evam anayoḥ dvayoḥ rūpayoḥ yaḥ sambhavaḥ yathā uktau= inā abhāvāḥ asambhave sati iti rūpa antara upagame api hetvābhāsa tā eva iti hetvābhāsāḥ tatas aparaḥ iti iti asya arthaḥ vivṛtaḥ iti 
HBṬ_4.5.53	 jñāta tva nirākaraṇāya āha jñānaṃpunaḥ ityādi abādhita viṣaya tvam vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam ca kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ eva āvinā abhāve sati bādhā pratihetvoḥ asambhavāt vyavacchedya abhāva tvena sati api liṅga dharma tve tad lakṣaṇam na bhavati iti uktam jñānam tu jñāta tvam tasya eva bhāva pratyayena abhidhānāt tathā hi jñāna śabda pravṛtti nimittam jñāta tvam ucyate tat ca jñānam eva tad utpāde sati jñātaḥ iti vyavahārāt na ca tat liṅgasya ātma rūpam iti katham liṅga lakṣaṇam bhaviṣyati  yadi api vikalpa pratibhāsī sāmanya ākāraḥ liṅgatayā avasthāpyate tathā api na jñānasya liṅga dharmatā na hi asau svatantraḥ eva liṅgam yat āha vikalpa bhedān asvatantrāṇām anvartha āśrayaṇāt tad kalpita viṣayāda artha pratipattau anartha pratilambhaḥ eva syāt iti tamāt bāhya vastu upādānasya eva asya liṅgatā avasthāpyate sādhya sādhana saṃkalpe 
HBṬ_4.5.54–4.5.56	 vastu darśana hāneḥ sva lakṣaṇasya kvacid ananvayāt ca tad dharma tām eva tu anusmarantaḥ vikalpāḥ nānā eka vyatirekān saṃdarśayantaḥ vastuni paramparayā pratibandhāt avisaṃvādakāḥ kārya ādi liṅga vyapadeśa nibandhanam ca iti ukta prāyam na ca tasya kārya ādeḥ ātma rūpam jñātam vikalpa avabhāsī ca sāmānya ākāraḥ na eva vikalpasya ātma bhūtaḥ tasya nīrūpasya vastu rūpa virodhāt tad rūpasya ca vikalpa pratibimba cakrasya sāmānya ātma tā virahāt yasmāt abāhya asya api bāhya tayā vyavasitasya ananuyāyinaḥ api anuyāyitayā sāmānya āmaka tvam tathātve ca asya vikalpa rūpa tayā kutas yadā aaha jñānāt avyatiriktaṃca katham artha antaraṃvrajet  
HBṬ_4.5.57	 tasmāt mithyā avabhāsaḥ ayam artheṣu eka ātma tā grahaḥ iti na jñānasya liṅga dharmatā etat eva sādhayan āha kiṃrūpāt ityādi kim ātmakāt hetoḥ anumeyaḥ arthaḥ jñātavyaḥ iti cintāyām prakṛtāyām pratipattuḥ puṃsaḥ yat avisaṃvādakam liṅgam tasya svarūpam abhidhīyate śāstra kāraiḥ yasya rūpasya darśanāt ayam pratipattā yatra tad rūpa sambhavaḥ tat sādhanam tad rūpa vikalam asādhanam iti pravibhāgena vyavasthāpya yat tatra sādhana tvena vyavasthāpitam tasya iṣṭa artha sannidhāna sampratyayāt pravṛttim avalambate tathā etasmin ca nyāye vyavasthite yat asya liṅgasya ātma rūpam tat lakṣaṇam bhavitum arhati pakṣa dharma ādi vat na tu yat para rūpam 
HBṬ_4.5.58–4.5.61	 syāt etat jñātasya liṅgasya sādhaka tvāt yuktā eva sādhya siddhi upayoginaḥ jñānasya liṅga lakṣaṇa tā iti atas āha pratipatti janmani ityādi yadi anumeya pratīti janmani upayujyate jñānam iti tanmātreṇa liṅgasya lakṣaṇam iṣyate tadā ati prasaṅgaḥ prāpnoti tam eva āha evaṃpratipatti janmani upayoga mātrāt liṅga lakṣaṇa tve prameyasya arthasya puruṣasya pramātuḥ adi śabdāt saṃyoga samavāya ādīnām āloka manaskāra ādīnām liṅga lakṣaṇa tvam bhavet atra kāraṇam āha na hi teṣu api prameya ādiṣu asatsu liṅgini jñānam bhavati iti kṛtvā atra paraḥ aniṣṭam āpādayan āha niścita grahaṇaṃtarhi ityādi yadi para rūpa tvāt jñānam liṅga lakṣaṇam na bhavati tadā ca yat etat ācāryeṇa anumeye artha tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ na astitā asati niścitā iti niścita grahaṇam kṛtam bhavataḥ ca abhimatam tat na karttavyam tathā hi niścayaḥ hi liṅgasya para rūpam eva sa ced tad lakṣaṇam jñānam kim iti na īśyate yatas niścayaḥ vijñānam eva tad viśeṣa tvāt asya iti 
HBṬ_4.5.62	 siddhāntavāy āha na na karttavyam kintu kartavyam eva tasya niścita grahaṇasya liṅga rūpa pratipādanāt anya artha tvāt tām eva anya artha tām darśayan āha sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ ityādi pare hi sa pakṣe darśana mātreṇa āsapakṣe ca adarśana mātrataḥ gamakam hetum icchanti teṣām na eva darśana mātreṇa sādhya siddhau samarthaḥ hetuḥ bhavati iti jñāpana artham niścita grahaṇam kṛtam yatas satoḥ vidyamānayoḥ api darśana adarśanayoḥ agamaka tvam hetoḥ dṛśyate sa śyamaḥ tad putra tvāt ityādau yatas evam tena kāraṇena sa pakṣe bhāvena vipakṣe sarvatra abhāva viśiṣṭenā asapakṣe ca sarvatra abhāvena sa pakṣe tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa bhāva viśiṣṭena gamakaḥ hetuḥ iti asya arthasya jñāpana artham lakṣaṇa vākye niścita grahaṇam kṛtam boddhavyam etat uktam bhavati yau eva sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvau pratibandha sādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā niścitau tābhyām 
HBṬ_4.5.63–4.5.64	 eva hetuḥ gamakaḥ bhavati na tu yathā kathañcit darśana mātreṇa iti asya arthasya jñāpanāya niścita grahaṇam kṛtam iti prakṛtam upasaṃharan āha tena ityādi yena viśiṣṭayoḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ eva khyāpanāya niścita grahaṇam kṛtam na rūpa antara abhidhānāya anātma rūpasya ca lakṣaṇa tā na yujyate tena para rūpam liṅgasya lakṣaṇam na bhavati yatas tena jñāna ādinā para rūpeṇa liṅgasya na kiñcid rūpa viśeṣaḥ abhidhīyate iti 
HBṬ_4.5.65	 nanu ca pare api sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvābhyām gamakam hetum icchanti darśana adarśane tu tayoḥ eva sādhake tat kim artham niścita grahaṇam iti atas āha tau hi ityādi yadi api pare bhāva abhāvābhyām eva gamakam hetum icchanti tathā api sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ asapakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva iti bhāva abhāvau darśana adarśana mātrataḥ vyavasthāpayanti na ca tatas tau tathāvidhāu sidhyataḥ pratibandha vikalānām api athānām kvacid bhāva abhāvayoḥ kathañcid darśana adarśana sambhavāt tasmāt yau hetoḥ sa pakṣe eva bhāvaḥ asapakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva iti evam ātmakau bhāva abhāvau tau tad bhāvasya sādhakam yat pramāṇaṇ tādātmya tad utpatti sādhana viṣayam tad vṛttyā boddhavyau kutas upāya antarasya abhāvāt tad anabhyupagame hi hetoḥ sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ sarva īśām hetumatām bhāvānām sādhyena anugama darśane sati vipakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva sādhya vikalānām sarva arthānām 
HBṬ_4.5.66–4.5.68	 hetu viviktānām upalambhe sati syāt na ca etat asarva darśinaḥ sambhavati iti yatas upaya antaram na asti tena kāraṇena tayoḥ viśiṣṭayoḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ pratipādanāya niścita śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ lakṣāṇe lakṣaṇa kāeṇa iti nanu ca bhāva abhāva vacana mātrāt eva pramāṇataḥ niścayaḥ labhyate anyathā tayoḥ eva sattā na prasidhyet iti atas āha yadi api ityādi anumeye artha tat tulya sadbhāvaḥ na astitā asati 
HBṬ_4.5.69	 iti anena eva sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāva vacana mātreṇa niścita grahaṇa nirapekṣeṇa tayoḥ bhāva abhāvayoḥ yat sādhanam pramāṇam tasya vṛttiḥ yadi api ākṣipyate katham punar niścita grahaṇam antareṇa bhāva abhāva vacana mātrataḥ tad vṛtteḥ ākṣepaḥ iti āha anyathā yadi tad sādhana pramāṇa vṛttiḥ na ākṣipyeta tadā tayoḥ eva sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ eva bhāva abhāvayoḥ yā sattā svarūpa vyavasthā tasyāḥ aprasiddheḥ kasmāt aprasiddhiḥ iti āha jñānasya upalabdheḥ yā sattā utpattiḥ tad nibandhana tvāt jñeyasya bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇasya sattā vyavasthāyāḥ svarūpa vyavasthiteḥ na hi upalambham antareṇa svatas eva arthāḥ sidhyanti sarvasya sarva siddhi prasaṅgāt tasmāt idam evaṃrūpam na evaṃrūpam iti tad ākāra jñāna udayāt eva vyavasthāpyate yatas evam tasmāt sarvatra śāstre loke vā jñeya sattā vyavasthā eva niścita grahaṇam vinā api tad sādhanam 
HBṬ_4.5.70	 tad sattā sādhanam pramāṇam ākarśati ākṣipati iti kiñ ca para artha tvāt ca śāstra praṇayanasya tad sādhana pramāṇa vṛttiḥ ākṣipyate iti sambandhaḥ kīdṛśam punar tad śāstra praṇayanam yat para artha rūpa tayā sva vyavasthāpita jñeya sattā sādhanam pramāṇam ākṣipati iti āha trirūpaṃliṅgaṃvaḥ saṃvāda kaṃprāpakam vā āñcitasya arthasya iti yadi nāma evaṃrūpam para artham śāstra praṇayanam tathā api katham tat sādhana pramāṇa vṛttim ākṣipati iti āha tad rūpam tasya liṅgasya trirūpasya rūpam svabhāvam śāstra uktam ye pratipattāraḥ na vidanti na teśām tatas tri rūpāt liṅgāt śāstra uktāt vā āñcite arthe pravṛttiḥ bhavati ajñātasya arthasya jñāpakasya sva sattā mātreṇa pravartaka tva abhāvāt yatas evam iti tasmāt para upalakṣaṇa tvāt eva pareṣām jñāpaka tvāt eva pravarttake trirūpa liṅge jñānam siddham iti yadi api niścita grahaṇam atiricyate tathā api tau eva 
HBṬ_4.5.71	 liṅgasya sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvau viśiṣṭau śastra uktau sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ asapakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva iti evaṃrūpau kecid naiyāyika prabhṛtayaḥ pare darśana adarśana mātreṇa ye darśana adarśane pratibandha sādhake na bhavataḥ tanmātreṇa vyavasthāpayanti yatas eva iti tasmāt teṣām vādinām niśedha arthaḥ ayam lakṣaṇe niścita śabdaḥ prayuktaa ācāryeṇa asmābhiḥ ca abhyupagataḥ iti yadi tu para vipratipattiḥ na syāt tadā na eva asau prayujyeta iti 
HBṬ_4.5.72	 kim iti punar darśana adarśanābhyām bhāva abhāva viśayābhyām sa pakṣa āsa pakśayoḥ viśiṣṭau bhāva abhāvau anvaya vyatireka ātmakau neṣyeta iti āha satoḥ api ityādi sati api kvacid sa pakṣe bhāva darśane hetoḥ kvacid ca āsapakṣe abhāva darśane sa śyamaḥ tad putra tvāt iti ādau anvaya vyatirekayoḥ saṃśayāt tathā hi anvayaḥ nāma sarvatra sati eva sādhye hetoḥ bhāvaḥ vyāptyā ca asati sādhye hetoḥ abhāvaḥ vyatirekaḥ na ca kvacid sati sādhye hetoḥ bhāva darśane api tanmātreṇa tathā abhāvaḥ sarvatra bhavati apratibaddha svabhāvānām sahabhāva niyamāḥ abhāvāt tathā kvacid sādhya abhimatasya abhāve sati abhāva darśane api hetoḥ sarvatra tad abhāve avaśyam abhāvaḥ tat anāyat tasya tad nivṛttau niyamena nivṛtti abhāvāt tasmāt pratibandha prasādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā eva yathā uktau sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvau sidhyataḥ na anyathā iti vipratipatti nirāsa artham eva niścita grahaṇam 
HBṬ_4.5.73–4.5.74	 kṛtam iti upadarśayan āha tasmāt ityādi asmābhiḥ iti ācārya kṛte niścita grahaṇe anyatra asmākam abhimata tvāt asmābhiḥ iti āha tat evam vipratipatti nirāsa artham niścita grahaṇam asatyām tu vipratipattau tat na kartavyam eva iti pratipādya atas eva nyāyāt jñāta tvam rūpa antaram na bhāvati iti darśayan āha yatas api ityādi pṛthak atas iti pakṣa dharma tva ādeḥ trairūpyāt kutas  tena eva trairūpya vacanena eva tad sādhana pramāṇa ākṣepataḥ avagata tvāt pratipanna tvāt iti kiṃvat upanaya artha vat pakṣa dharma tvāt iti yathā pakṣa dharma tva vacanena eva hetoḥ upanayasya arthaḥ avagataḥ tasya dharmiṇi hetoḥ sadbhāva pradarśana ātmaka tvāt pakṣa dharma vacanasya ca tad rūpa tvāt tatas pṛthak upanayaḥ rūpa antaram na bhavati tathā trairūpyāt jñānam tat vacanena eva avagata tvāt iti 
HBṬ_4.5.75	 atra paraḥ aniṣṭam āpādayan āha anvaya vyatirekayoḥ api ityādi yadi trairūpya vacanena eva sāmarthyāt jñānam labhyate iti tat tatas pṛthak na vaktavyam hanta tarhi anvayāt pṛthak vyatirekaḥ na vaktavyaḥ vyatirekāt ca pṛthak anvayaḥ kim kāraṇam  ekasya anvayasya vyatirekasya vā prayogāt ubhayasya gateḥ kṛtam ca tayoḥ pṛthak vacanam tathā jñāta tvasya api trairūpyāt gamyamānasya api pṛthak vacanam karttavyam iti 
HBṬ_4.5.76	 siddhānta vādi āha na hetoḥ ityādi na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ na pṛthaktvam kintu bhinna rūpa tā eva tathā hi anvayaḥ hetoḥ sa pakṣe bhāvaḥ ucyate vyatirekaḥ punar abhāvaḥ asapakṣe na ca tau parasparam ākṣipataḥ parasparam antarbhavataḥ vidhi pratiṣedha rūpayoḥ bhinna svabhāva tvāt na ca yaḥ yatas bhinna svabhāvaḥ sa tatra antarbhūtaḥ yuktaḥ nanu ca yadi anvaya vyatirekayoḥ bhinna rūpa tā katham tarhi trairūpam liṅgam ucyate  na hi paraspara bhinnau ātmānau eva asya yujyate svabhāva bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt vastu bhedasya na eṣa doṣaḥ yatas yathā anvaya vyatirekau vyavasthā apyete tathā tayoḥ anantarbhāvaḥ ucyate na anyathā katham ca etau vavasthā apyete  vyāvṛtti kṛtam bhedam upādāya tathā ca anayoḥ bhinna rūpa tā eva vyāvṛtti bhede api ca paramārthataḥ bhedaḥ na asti iti ekam liṅgam trirūpam iti ucyate iti 
HBṬ_4.5.77	 katham tarhi prāk uktam na anayoḥ arthaḥ kaścid bhedaḥ anyatra prayoga bhedāt iti atas āha ekaṃvākyam ityādi anvaya mukhena vyatireka mukheṇa vā prayuktam ekam vākyam ubhayam anvayam vyatirekam ca bhinna lakṣaṇam eva gamayati iti ucyate asmābhiḥ na ekaḥ arthaḥ svabhāvaḥ dvitīyasya ucyate paraspara bhinnayoḥ eva eka vākya artha rūpa tvāt 
HBṬ_4.5.78	 atra paraḥ āha nanu tatra eva ityādi ayam abhiprāyaḥ lakṣaṇa vākya pratipāditau anvaya vyatirekau āśritya paraspara antarbhāvaḥ codyate sa ca vidyate eva tathā hi tatra eva bhāvaḥ iti atra lakṣaṇa vākye tad artha tayā tad abhāve abhāvaḥ gamyate atad abhāve avaśyam abhāvaḥ iti ca atra tad bhāve bhāvaḥ na hi asati pratibandhaḥ eka abhāve aparasya abhāvaḥ pratibandhaḥ ca tādātmya tad utpattibhyām tad bhāve bhāva rūpaḥ eva tatas ca ekena eva sa pakṣa āsa pakṣyoḥ bhāva abhāva pratipādakena prativiśiṣṭena lakṣaṇa vākyena ubhaya gateḥ dvitīya vacanam na karttavyam iti tathā ca eka vākya artha antarbhāvāt bhinna svabhāva tā api anayoḥ durllabhā tatas ca yat uktam anvaya vyatirekayoḥ api tarhi na pṛthaktvam iti tat tad avastham eva iti 
HBṬ_4.5.79	 siddhānta vādi āha vacanam etat tatra eva bhāvaḥ ityādi rūpam ubhayam ākṣipati pratipādayati kutas  sāmarthyāt ubhaya pratipādana śaktasya  niyamaḥ vyāpakasya sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ asapakṣe ca abhāvaḥ eva iti sa avadhāraṇasya dvitīya ākṣepana antarīyaka tvāt dvitīya pratipādanana āntarīyaka tvāt na ca tāvatā eka vākya pratipādana mātreṇa ubhayoḥ eka svabhāva tā bhinna svabhāvānām api athānām eka vākyena pratipādanāt ekena eva ca lakṣaṇa vākyena ubhaya gatau api yat pṛthaa bhidhānam tat prayoga niyama artham sādharmya prayoge vaidharmya vacanam na karttavyam vaidharmya prayoge ca sādharmya vacanam iti na punar eka abhidhānena anavagatasya rūpa antarasya pratipādana artham na ca tathā trairūpya vacanena jñāna nibandhanena jñeya sattā vyavasthāyāḥ para upalakṣaṇāthena ca śāstra praṇayanena āśrita jñānasya eva trairūpyasya pratipāda nāl 
HBṬ_4.5.80–4.5.81	 labdhasya jñānasya punarvacane na kiñcid prayojanam asti iti na asya pṛthak vacanam yuktam iti syāt matam kevalau api tarhi eka vākya artha anantarbhūtau para sparama abhinna svabhāvau bhaviṣyataḥ tatas eva eka vākya artha antarbhāvāt iti atas āha na punar kevalau eka vākya artha anapekṣau tad antar bhāva mātreṇa sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhāva abhāvau parasparam ākṣipataḥ antarbhavataḥ bhinna rūpāṇām api arthānām eka vākya antar bhāva darśanāt nanu ca niyamavantau api bhāva abhāvau kevalau eva tayoḥ paraspara ākṣepe kevalayoḥ api tad prasaṅgaḥ iti atas āha niyamavantau ca sa avadhāraṇa vākya pratipāditau na kevalau kintu sahitau eva kutas  niyamasya sa avadhāraṇasya vākyasya ubhaya rūpa tvāt bhāva abhāva pratipādana ātmaka tvāt 
HBṬ_4.5.82	 tat evam sāvadharaṇena vākyena na eva kevalaḥ anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā abhidhīyate tad antar bhāvāt tu dvitīya gatiḥ kintu paraspara anantarbhūtau eva sahitau ekena vākyena abhidhīyeta iti pratipādya upasaṃharan āha tasmāt tatra eva sa pakṣaḥ eva bhāvaḥ iti anena vākyena na sa pakṣe bhāvaḥ eva ucyate kim tarhi  asapakṣe abhāvaḥ api tathā ca itareṇa api asapakṣe abhāvaḥ eva iti vacanena na abhāvaḥ eva kevalaḥ ucyate kintu sa pakṣe bhāvaḥ api yena kevala vacanena bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā tad ātmaka tayā dvitīyam ākṣipet yatas anayoḥ pṛthak vacanam na syāt tasmāt yadā anvaya vyatirekau bhāva abhāvau abhipretau tadā tau bhinna rūpau eva iti katham tayoḥ na pṛthaktvam  atha niyamavatā vākyena abhihitau tadā eka vākyāt eva ubhaya gateḥ pṛthak vacanam na karttavyam eva tat tu kṛtam na apratipanna pratipattaye kintu prayoga niyama artham iti uktam etat iti 
HBṬ_4.5.83	 syāt matam yathā anvaya vyatirekau bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇau na paraspara ātmakau tatas ca tayoḥ parasparataḥ rūpa antara tvam evam para upalakṣaṇa śastra pratipāditāt trailakṣaṇyāt bhidyate eva jñānam na tatra antarbhūtam tatas rūpa antaram bhaviṣyati iti atas āha na evam yathā anvaya vyatirekau bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇau parasparam anantarbhūtau na tathā jñānam para upalakṣaṇa śāstra pratipādite trailakṣaṇye anantarbhūtam kutas  para upalakṣaṇāt pare upalakṣyante upalakṣaṇam trairūpya viṣayām pratītim kāryante yena śāstreṇa tatas yat trailakṣaṇyam pratīyate āgṛhīta jñānam tasmāt avyatirekāt āgṛhīta jñāne trailakṣaṇye antarbhāvāt iti yāvat iti tasmāt na lakṣaṇa antaram trairūpyāt iti tat ayam atra samudāya arthaḥ yadi jñāta tvam jñāna śabda pravṛtti nimittam uktena prakāreṇa jñānam eva ucyate tadā tad liṃgasya anātma bhūtam iti 
HBṬ_4.5.84–4.5.90	 na tad lakṣaṇam atha api jñāna apekṣaḥ karma bhāvaḥ jñāta tvam ucyate tadā api jñeya sattā vyavasthāyā jñāna sattā nibandhana tvāt trairūpya vyavasthā eva tad sattā vyavasthāpakam jñānam ākṣipati tatas tad apekṣaḥ api karma bhāvaḥ anukta siddhaḥ iti na tat vacanam pṛthak karttavyam tathā para upalakṣaṇa artha śāstra pratipādita agṛhīta jñānāt trailakṣaṇyāt avyatirekāt iti tat evam abādhita viṣaya tva ādikam rūpa trayam nirākṛtya nigamayan āha tasmāt na hetuḥ ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ kim tarhi  trailakṣaṇyaḥ eva iti imam kṣata aśeṣa kutarka mārgam muni īśarāt dhāntannaya pradīpam vitatya puṇyam yat upārjitam tat parām viśuddhim jagataḥ vidheyāt hetu binduṭīkā samāptāḥ
